# Getting Started | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoGKMsPBXU74hxlmjew7q%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%2828%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5676e432-694f-4e19-92c8-8c07ffe792ea&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbd3a6d2&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS is a new-age HR solution with ease of access and extensive features. Its intuitive features give you the advantage of simplifying your daily HR activities while keeping the fun alive.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FdaHT31vH2JLNz6sgYde7%252FHRMS-Software-banner.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56355375-a4ed-4d02-a99c-ab4e884be39c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7eeb4877&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS is a fully scalable HR software, which aims to bring about a change in the working dynamics of the HR department. Our HRMS Solution takes HR steps ahead by introducing revolutionary features like automated [ChatBotarrow-up-right](https://www.pockethrms.com/hr-chatbot)
, interactive dashboards, mobility, customizable modules, etc.

Real-time updates and automated report generation are a few things that HR experts crave. These features help them make better decisions and curb errors.

Cloud-supportive Pocket HRMS is the perfect pick-me-up [HRMS software for businessesarrow-up-right](https://www.pockethrms.com/hr-management-software)
 of all sizes and verticals.

# ESS Portal: Manager's Guide | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6VZNF1d0lnvlmxDyUyC1%252FManager%25E2%2580%2599s%2520Guide.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd537a3d1-8c2a-4c28-ac30-6c0157b352ae&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3db32c8d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-managers-guide#ess-guide-for-managers)

ESS Guide for Managers

Through approval matrix Admin can configure different managers for various modules such as leave, regularization, expense and more.

Whenever an employee submits any request the respective manger (The manager who has approval rights configured by the admin) will be notified about the same on an email as well as on their ESS. The manager can act (Approve/Reject) on these requests through

*   ESS portal
    
*   Email
    

According to the Pocket HRMS configuration the respective manager need to approve / reject the entries so the details will be updated in the system against the employee.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-managers-guide#notification-for-approval-requests)

Notification for Approval Requests

Once an employee submits any request their respective manager will receive notification about it in their ESS portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fi2zH5cg7EYFmUPYch5kq%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2596b329&sv=2)

You can view these notifications once you click on the ‘Bell’ icon at right-hand corner of the screen. Click on the notification to reach the respective approval page.

Checking for Pending Approvals

To approve a request, you need to follow the path for particular module for example,

*   On duty
    

Leave > Approval > Approval > On Duty

*   Attendance Regularization
    

Leave > Approval > Attendance Regularization

You can check on the ‘Details’ button

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4yuE27MrewKsLhzJVHVz%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42977f01&sv=2)

The manager may approve / reject multiple entries at a single go also.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-managers-guide#email-for-approval-request)

Email for Approval Request

Apart from the notification in the ESS, the manager will also receive an email notification for employee’s request. So, as a manager you can approve or reject reject requests from email itself.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7SHzrmjQ9psErSiwc3yW%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ccf8025&sv=2)

On the successful approval or rejection of the request the respective employee will be notified about the same on their ESS as well as via email.

**Note**:

In the multi-level approval, the request will go to Manger 1 and only after approval it goes to Manager 2 and so on according your configurations made by the Admin.

**Checking Team’s Attendance** As a manager you may check the attendance details of you team through the below path:

1.  Leave > My Team Report > Punch In Out Report
    
2.  Leave > My Team Report > In Out Details _(Note , here the attendance data will be updated after processing of attendance)_
    
3.  Leave > My Team Report > Monthly Attendance Summary
    

[PreviousESS Portal: Employee's Guidechevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide)

# ESS Portal: Employee's Guide | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkIOa67zdplJ2cXcfEebU%252FEmployee%25E2%2580%2599s%2520Guide.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe9f9f32-72ec-41ef-904c-77c1a6b582d8&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80ad2d64&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS Employee Self-service Portal allows employees to take care of their day-to-day tasks such as applying for a leave, downloading salary slips and submitting with ease. Employees seamlessly enter and edit their personal details according to the rights provided by the Administrator.

This guide will walk you through the steps you need to follow for various tasks.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#how-to-log-in-to-the-ess-portal)

How to log in to the ESS portal?

Go to [ess.pockethrms.comarrow-up-right](https://ess.pockethrms.com/)
 and enter the ‘Company Code’, ‘Employee Code’ and ‘Password’ that you received from you via email.

Once you click on the ‘Sign In’ button, it will take you to the ESS dashboard Screen. You should start by creating a new password.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCh1Tj8gg9z3zoXMuhC6P%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D880d2ad4-0c75-4f14-9aa3-d7450df33023&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6767508&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#how-to-reset-password)

How to Reset Password?

Go to the upper right-hand corner of the screen and click on the ‘Profile Icon’ as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fd57L5wESkiSvKw8StSQf%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D047abceb-dcee-4f4e-8f8a-aeeeda9f3e91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbcdd67a&sv=2)

Here you need to click on the change password menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FelVPicbcZXugfDy0eGvF%252FFrame%25201%2520%2833%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48354c48-158e-4ba8-beaa-e3ad8d016db3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21dfdb4c&sv=2)

That will take you to the password reset screen. Enter ‘Old Password’ and ‘New Password’ in the respective fields. Ensure that the password you enter in the ‘New Password’ and ‘Confirm Password’ fields are the same. Click on the ‘Change Password’ button to set the new password.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFFb82ZwkEZ6L9KKr1XMX%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D341013ba-5168-45ae-bc6f-cd457e86072e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9efbb0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#how-to-use-ess-dashboard)

How to use ESS Dashboard?

Once you login to the ESS portal it will take you to the ‘Dashboard’. The intuitive Dashboard is designed to provide employees with quick access to essential information. This single screen allows you to perform multiple activities through this easy-to-understand single screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvJwXlvimqtmjyRSsi6sa%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D811bde32-645a-48b6-804a-9a2ba1d6f7f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e0cceff&sv=2)

The evident card at the top of the screen will show you your name. Employee code as well as designation you are working at.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzDq7wRy8A2jdhWMdwxAr%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8afbfb4a-352e-4892-b4cd-dc90d022c4ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffe9d6e7&sv=2)

Click on the ‘View Manager Details’ buttons to view your approval manager’s name for respective processes such as ‘Leave’ or ‘Expense’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FD03CKHmMpkYtEsAzaQR1%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ab6ddb3-ad95-444a-bc9c-42de3e2225ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35dea0a5&sv=2)

In the ‘Attendance Statistics’ section, you will get easy-to-grasp data about your attendance.

Starting with your Punch entries for the present day the top section also shows the shift schedule for the next day that way you get timely reminders and plan accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FeQvgGszXsquDpJCgQmqp%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da82a4e49-720b-453d-a766-8b6abef28006&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56ff6a17&sv=2)

You can click on the ‘Holiday this Year’ to view details about the same.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBgogb7TuTq5V5xTjxyMk%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2202b0e2-0ae8-4af4-863b-c607993348c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f68b47&sv=2)

Similarly, you can view respective details when you click on the other tabs in the section such as late marks and unpunches.

We also have dedicated sections for news as well as upcoming birthdays and anniversaries in the company so you can stay informed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrpOCmnW3Fj7KbxzkgRM7%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1a11570-1d36-43af-8b00-a49188025303&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3fc441a&sv=2)

The graphical representation of the leaves you utilize helps you to easily grasp the information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXNxm3bJ5eTJb5j4R5beb%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfafcb2a2-bcad-49e6-884c-b57c656b8a84&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18effc97&sv=2)

You can click on the ‘Last Salary Processed’ to download your pay slip. Similarly, the section gives you tac details, the last increment date as well as used leaves and leave balance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCbT1tsWllQYz5MW94Qol%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D447976aa-2571-4fad-86cc-472fe7ec6941&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=377e7314&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#id-4xtv78n3tj3b)

How to view employment details?

Go to the ‘Profile’ menu and select ‘My Profile’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7W3auwiX74KZPxEK8dTv%252FHow%2520to%2520view%2520employment%2520details1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3743bc77-8fc2-46ac-b71f-354a76defb53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=875bf497&sv=2)

Go to the ‘Employee Details’ tab to view your profile, where you can view your personal information such as name, date of birth, date of joining, PF account number and more. You can also access the ‘Personal Details’ and ‘Additional Details’ tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUDuQkZdjgY5rkTfuXUQc%252FHow%2520to%2520view%2520employment%2520details%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e8cd054-6e31-4439-83b0-8b116b665c25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5addde3d&sv=2)

Under the ‘Other Details’ you can able to update or view Family, Academic, joining documents, nominee details, employee history, Language details and Training details based on the rights given to you.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAzowksNXbI5DJ0oTCS6a%252FHow%2520to%2520view%2520employment%2520details%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D175458de-1146-43e5-8168-6412c7bd3a7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a080eb67&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7Akrl3Mej5OomZKxQgOZ%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f6d2f62-3562-4827-9476-2a64f8a53e63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e5488d9&sv=2)

To access HR-related information, go to the ‘HR Tools’ submenu under the ‘Profile’ menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2YPcx5n88FdEvvjvHLp7%252F16.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8606bd4d-0842-4ca8-8c4a-0fa1249f2a4e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c3d9f23&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgbPj8Uea4pc8HtBS6xdU%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbdfccde1-3632-49a7-af3c-6c1a46004bf5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d2d13af&sv=2)

*   Contact Info: Contact information of the HR and administrator can be seen here
    
*   Policies: Company policies which are shared by the HR team can be downloaded from this option
    
*   General Info: General Information about the company can be downloaded through this option
    

To access details related to their salary go to the ‘My Salary Details’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwG68w7ECwcFHvingSvbE%252F17.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2201fb8-3f64-430b-8a44-fba7a8f5ffae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b2a631e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVG4UCWaEFZCyCJgpS78z%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deacb0112-a9f0-412e-951c-5487cbafeece&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9bbb2ee&sv=2)

*   My Pay slip: You may download your Pay slip from this option
    
*   My Provident Fund Details: You may check your PF details from this option
    

You can access your tax-related details by going to the ‘My Tax Details’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJgqYZW82Ne6oGxGXVJMW%252F18.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5692d74-8434-4f12-a027-4a3953f5f7f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54e4abac&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAGu517SOQ2lC9dneiymS%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81eab8fc-9bdf-4632-b099-f847cc5c41dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b61dbe29&sv=2)

*   Work Sheet – TDS: You may download your Income Tax worksheet through this option
    
*   TDS Declaration Entry: You may enter your TDS declaration entries through this option
    
*   TDS – Proof Entry: You may enter your TDS declaration entries through this option
    
*   Tax Calculation: You can able to calculate your annual tax using this option
    
*   Form 16: You can able to download your form 16 using this option
    

You also get easy access to your loan information under ‘My Loan Details’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbrCvNFBEutJXJduVpTUr%252F19.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4d6c3e7-f6c2-4a11-8313-afa6beb27ce1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=629fc01e&sv=2)

*   My Loan Details: You can able to see your loan details using this option
    
*   Loan Request: You can make a loan request using this option if applicable
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9CS336BgLD7KKwEwMkoM%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd82d7cad-7c76-4186-aa1b-d9ebdb26b845&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ddc9541c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#how-to-apply-for-leave)

How to apply for leave?

From the left-hand side menu bar click on the ‘Leave’ menu followed by the ‘Request’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJp1MR2ksZDclfPC7Q0G3%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6dbc7b83&sv=2)

Click on the ‘Leave’ tab and,

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJnFch6fOUYS7MdYTTqD1%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=423492bc&sv=2)

select ‘Type of Leave’ from the drop-down.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGgtrbqpz0P4zad6WQiBT%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c1f1b58&sv=2)

Once you select the ‘Type of Leave’ the respective leave balance will be displayed in red colour.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2NX5Td6QCaXH4fjig6Dn%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c38025a&sv=2)

Select ‘Reliever - Employee Name’ who is going to take care of your work responsibilities while you are on leave.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FS0czIpPGARoBhIx8wpAt%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df6dbdd0&sv=2)

Select the duration of your leave. Choose whether it is a full day or half day from the drop-down options for both ‘From Date’ and ‘To Date’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEhffejhY4eGavjIuhoaQ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4326b4f&sv=2)

Fill in the other essential information such as ‘Reason’ for the leave, whether you are going to ‘Leave Station’, as well as ‘Vacation Address’ and ‘Contact Number’ in the respective fields.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9QilBwDlRQX3ENIzTmOJ%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e7d4c3f&sv=2)

Once you click on the ‘Add’ button you will see the summary for your leave request.

You can click on the ‘Delete’ icon if there are any mistakes and you want to create a new request. Click on the ‘Confirm Leave’ button to submit the leave request.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FerA5kGPB5yhe7cICuf0A%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0a2c3ea&sv=2)

You can see your leave request under the ‘Previous Leaves’ section along with the ‘Status’.

You can also delete your leave application by clicking on the ‘Cancel’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOXFC7VuWEIVH4Zrazyjo%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71ddb7ab&sv=2)

Once the manager approves your leave you will be notified about the same by an email as well as mobile notification for Pocket HRMS app.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#hlk160441358)

How to RequestOn-duty or Work from Home?

Click on the ‘Leave’ menu from the sidebar followed by ‘Request’ sub-menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0uLRzH9MPM4mq8paPmKm%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=82eaa026&sv=2)

Click on the ‘On-duty or Work from Home’ tab and select the ‘Start Date’ & ‘End Date’ in the respective fields.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fn0WLNC7rmIsZGWHLxOct%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f999d96&sv=2)

Select the ‘Day Type’ from the drop-down.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLB4lgn8mmdXUvf7ODzZF%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=716a0f09&sv=2)

Enter ‘In Time’ and ‘Out Time’ according to 24-hour format.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fx2JRm43oz1wt7TSwJzuC%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33951182&sv=2)

Choose your ‘Remark’ and click on the ‘Save’ button to submit your request.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRLaVOJ5GOYK3NzsLj3yz%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5fd3540&sv=2)

The request will go to your Manager for approval. The respective and you will get an email and app notification after the approval.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#hlk160459094)

How to regularize your attendance?

Select ‘Leave’ from the left-hand sidebar followed by the ‘Request’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzRFMdEaaNbHh3Xzycybh%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4bf046b&sv=2)

Go to ‘Attendance Regularization’ tab. Select the ‘From Date’, ‘To Date’ and click on the ‘Search’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0TlSOuXUnfKD3Y9GQQUO%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa2af547&sv=2)

In the search results, you will be able to see your in and out items along with status and remarks for your previous attendance regularization request. You can also choose to ‘Re-Updte’ your request.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fz7pxdiRkgNNugnIq9k33%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bca8889b&sv=2)

Click on the ‘Update’ button for the entry you want to regularize.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fra7FQrLDtGUkcaQ1L24l%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7107b6a&sv=2)

Modify the ‘In Time’ or ‘Out Time’, add ‘Remark’ and click on the ‘Save’ button to submit your attendance regularization request.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyfKs1dM8PZfoJ5CZaIqO%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e71e0f51&sv=2)

Once the manager approves your request you will be notified about the same by email as well as mobile notification for Pocket HRMS app.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-employees-guide#how-to-upload-pictures-for-face-recognition)

How to upload pictures for face recognition?

Select ‘Leave’ from the left-hand sidebar followed by the ‘Face Recognition’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXuAKY9npR80Y6z99Zqih%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3afe8716&sv=2)

Go to the ‘Face Recognition’ tab. Click on the 3 boxes individually one-by-one to upload your high-resolution pictures with clear background and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fc58OS9YSzf4CYJIfKODE%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41a01f42&sv=2)

After you click on the ‘Save’ button your pictures will be sent to HR for approval and the ‘Face Recognition’ feature will be activated for attendance once HR approves your pictures.

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#7a090f0a0a15080e3a0a1519111f0e1208170954191517)

[PreviousESS: Beginner's Guideschevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides)
[NextESS Portal: Manager's Guidechevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/introduction-pockethrms-help-document/ess-beginners-guides/ess-portal-managers-guide)

Last updated 3 months ago

Pocket HRMS software is designed to empower the human resource department for better productivity. We believe HR is crucial for the growth of any organization and should spend their time in strategic planning. So, we constantly work towards streamlining administration and automating processes.

Every month we incorporate several exciting features to provide you with a better user experience. With every software update, you will get a more intuitive and user-friendly interface, making navigation and task execution smoother than ever. # September 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FpZ74Abpai22wEqfaxueR%252FSeptember%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3f2aaed-9fa7-445e-acb4-5445e3c00e65&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c80e696f&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS continuously strives to improve the end-user experience, and in this pursuit, we have made further enhancements to your beloved HRMS software.

In this update, we present the brand-new training dashboard, which will provide an overview of employee training. We have also optimized the roster management system for a smoother roster setup. Finally, our users can enjoy the added usability of Single Sign On (SSO), which helps improve the login experience.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/september-2022#all-inclusive-training-dashboard)

All-Inclusive Training Dashboard

Introducing our groundbreaking feature, the 'Training Dashboard' in our HRMS software! Now, employees can effortlessly access a comprehensive overview of their training activities in one streamlined interface. It consists of vital information such as:

*   Assigned training sessions
    
*   Training Schedule
    
*   Completion status
    
*   Certifications Achieved
    
*   Monthly Training Report and more.
    

This dashboard helps in boosting productivity and empowering employees. It ensures seamless training management, enhancing both individual and organizational growth.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FfpxHX3R7m9FBHkbxwVOT%252FAll-Inclusive%2520Training%2520Dashboard.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14639a0f-cfbc-43b8-8ffb-b1eac6d6b524&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27da0afe&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoBCecmJYWXhl6UkRLabu%252FAll-Inclusive%2520Training%2520Dashboard1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ddcf7b9-d467-4015-946b-d94d44dfc157&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afc4ed6d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/september-2022#revolutionize-work-schedules-instantly)

Revolutionize Work Schedules Instantly

Now you will get an advanced Roster Management System with this cutting-edge feature, managers can effortlessly apply complete rosters for their teams, streamlining the scheduling process. Meanwhile, our Admin/HR users gain the power to apply new rosters for all employees, accommodating various shifts and even managing week offs seamlessly.

This functionality ensures optimal workforce organization, reducing managerial workload and enhancing overall productivity. Experience hassle-free scheduling and empower your team with our HRMS software.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHQv7ycvW2owm7RP8aiik%252FRevolutionize%2520Work%2520Schedules%2520Instantly.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8abafbf7-4c5e-4535-a736-c8d87565e191&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a8ed393&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqU1fbNkPOaAiUC8YqTws%252FRevolutionize%2520Work%2520Schedules%2520Instantly1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2d9d0d9-dbcd-4615-b15c-dc9b53dfa929&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12377928&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/september-2022#simple-access-with-enhanced-security)

Simple Access with Enhanced Security

With this update, we are introducing our seamless Single Sign-On (SSO) feature powered by Microsoft Account integration. With just one click, employees can enjoy password-less sign-ins, streamlining their access to our HRMS platform effortlessly.

By granting initial access to their Microsoft Account, employees ensure a hassle-free login experience every time. This not only enhances security but also boosts productivity, eliminating the need to remember complex passwords.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ff2aocwTVDZPXPgEOYPcK%252FSimple%2520Access%2520with%2520Enhanced%2520Security.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96c6cabe-9b1a-44c4-b2ec-6f229ae0e502&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cba50801&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3WcJJRXtdocA1KTUHaaV%252FSimple%2520Access%2520with%2520Enhanced%2520Security1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe01d07d-b2b1-4970-88a5-b6b6ca450d7e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2823668&sv=2)

# August 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFNZGyHdO1MpJ9PpY3tyu%252FAugust%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97963a1c-8f96-4480-bf1b-13909e1d25e2&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8cde53e4&sv=2)

August 2022


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Pocket HRMS team is always passionate about upgrading the user experience and providing more significant help for our clients. In our pursuit of excellence, we are introducing a few enhancements.

Here is an overview of all the major and minor enhancements made in August 2022

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/august-2022#custom-display-of-appraisal-total-ratings)

Custom Display of Appraisal Total Ratings

With our new update Admins and HR professionals can now effortlessly enable ratings to be displayed on both employees' and managers' screens. This innovation promotes transparency and empowers employees by allowing them to view the ratings of their appraisals firsthand.

It fosters open communication and clarity, ensuring a transparent and accountable work environment for everyone involved.

Configurable Pay Scales for Efficient Payroll

Pocket HRMS now offer slab-wise Pay Scales Configuration. With this, Admin and HR teams have seamless control over employee salaries. Define and adjust pay scales effortlessly, ensuring fair compensation across the board. Instantly update salaries based on predefined increments and PayScale structures. Plus, set effective dates for changes, ensuring accuracy and transparency. This feature streamlines payroll processes making your HR tasks smoother and more efficient.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5jsvpwuhfK759lVcjYBS%252FConfigurable%2520Pay%2520Scales%2520for%2520Efficient%2520Payroll.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64fbdce8-e4a7-4eb6-a27d-2702ebaae048&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2046697&sv=2)

This streamlined feature ensures quick access to essential information, enabling efficient tax compliance and payroll processing while saving valuable time.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMHU7D3EA0rV3Qrk0jqEI%252FSimple%2520Team%25E2%2580%2599s%2520TDS%2520View%2520for%2520Managers.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4359ded2-2552-4cdb-a876-53c8bb9498cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c0c0db8&sv=2)

# 2024 Major Highlights | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fc8LRP1tlS2He0K3mM47f%252FHighlights%25202024%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c61a1f7-9f27-422c-a363-2222ec944c92&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e59c9fe9&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our most remarkable updates, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the year 2024, here are some of the most remarkable enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#lop-deduction-in-sandwich-rule)

Leave

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#lop-deduction-in-sandwich-rule-1)

LOP Deduction in Sandwich Rule

The sandwich leave setting now includes LOP leave within the leave deduction options. You can select the LOP leaves with ease from the dropdown and improve leave management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkE6ClZo5pTLh0qsZEECq%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e29b26fb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#effortless-bulk-lop-credit-entry)

Effortless Bulk LOP Credit Entry

Now you can do bulk LOP credit input, making it easier than ever to manage Loss of Pay. No more manual entry for each employee - simply enter credits in bulk for multiple employees at once. This saves time, improves efficiency, and enhances workflow management. As an HR professional or organization, you'll enjoy smoother processes and increased productivity.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOpTivOf1M8dfZQaP7QBz%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2df6b1f0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#customize-week-off-scheduling)

Customize Week-Off Scheduling

The week-off setting is now more flexible than ever before. Now you have more control and select whether the 1st, 2nd, 3rd, 4th, or 5th occurrence of a day (like Sunday) should be your week-off for a certain date range.

Once you save the settings, your choices will be clearly shown on the screen for easy reference and full transparency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FObdBVUvzuFVqTkkbsVlU%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e09e0364&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#comp-off-leave-now-with-a-deadline)

Comp Off Leave, Now with a Deadline!

Admins can now restrict employees from applying for Comp Off leave after a specific timeframe from the Comp Off date. That ensures policy compliance and prevents misuse of leave.

**For example,** If the Comp Off date is 13th September and the limit is 30 days, leave can only be applied between 13th September and 12th October. Requests outside this range will be denied.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYoeevjpquw73IBoxqMqx%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f242cfa3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#improved-monitoring-with-geolocation)

Attendance

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#improved-monitoring-with-geolocation-1)

Improved Monitoring with Geolocation

The ‘In Out Detail’ report now features two new columns, 'IN geolocation' and 'OUT geolocation,'. These columns show where employees enter and exit specified areas, aiding in tracking their movements. This enhancement offers a detailed overview of employee activities based on geolocation data, enhancing monitoring.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fq6Zy4NlCY9lXV8rq7cOz%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9255b146&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#late-mark-deductions-with-customizable-settings)

Late Mark Deductions with Customizable Settings

We've upgraded the late mark customization to now include deductions for late days, which are determined by shift settings and prioritize different types of leave. Admin/HR can now save specific settings for various shifts, enabling them to prioritize the deduction of certain types of leave before others.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FX8RG0tGw6ZnxJLhNdxjp%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b29aa050&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#priority-based-time-range-leave-deductions)

Priority-Based Time Range Leave Deductions

Pocket HRMS offers flexible settings of leave deductions based on employees' attendance punch times. You can do the following customizations with ease.

*   Define auto deduction criteria for individual shifts
    
*   Set multiple time ranges of deductions for each shift
    
*   Set priorities with multiple leave types for deductions for each time range
    
*   Delete settings for individual time ranges without disturbing other settings
    
*   Delete all the custom settings for the particular shift when you no longer need it
    

These settings provide better control and efficiency for attendance and leave management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTg2twgCOAORbMJnekdM9%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d77e23ff&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FH6NsC9ZtlovGXC86VTO3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22311af0-b88d-4676-883a-1476dcdefdd2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46ac2cb5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#optimized-sandwich-leave-rule-based-on-leave-taken)

Optimized Sandwich Leave Rule Based on Leave Taken

Sandwich Leave deductions now follow the order in which employees apply for them and not the predefined order. If an employee lacks the balance for a particular leave type, Loss of Pay (LOP) will be applied.

**Example**,

*   Employee requests 'Paid Leave' for Friday and 'Sick Leave' for Monday.
    
*   Resulting leave pattern: Paid Leave, Week off, Week off, Sick Leave.
    

**Scenarios**:

*   **If the remaining Paid Leave balance is 2 or more** - Both week off are deducted as Paid Leave.
    
*   **If the remaining Paid Leave balance is 1** -First week off as Paid Leave; the system checks Sick Leave for the second week off.
    
*   **If there is no remaining Sick Leave balance** - The second week off will be considered LOP.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYJKTrKLrDxr1Wp6AIjKk%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12a668b9&sv=2)

Employee


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#streamline-employee-access)

Streamline Employee Access


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We have introduced a new module named Employee Access. Here, the managers have been given an option to raise requests on behalf of their subordinates to grant or revoke access on various events like New Joining, Promotion, Separation, etc. Access forms can be created in Form Master and the requests can be raised by Managers in ESS and approved by the IT Team.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRcRk96ha5yma9Gfgqx7F%252FFrame%252097.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7616ad13-e800-47a5-857c-b7c8fac9aa48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67608cab&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#integrated-training-period-with-confirmation-module)

PMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#bell-curve-flexibility-tailor-your-appraisal-process)

Bell Curve Flexibility: Tailor Your Appraisal Process

The Appraisal module has been enhanced to provide greater flexibility and configuration options for the Bell Curve functionality.

**Rating Type Configuration**

Users can select ‘Scale’ with a default range of 1-5 or ‘Weightage’ which displays the Grade % as the rating type for appraisals.

**Define Bell Curve Screen**

The graph dynamically updates based on the first three values entered. Users can display either Rating Scale or Grade % in the first column. Strict validation ensures the first three values are in ascending order, with the total Expected % equaling 100%.

**Rating Normalization Screen**

The Rating Normalization screen will now adapt its columns based on the selected rating type (Scale or Grade %). Normalization calculations align with the chosen configuration. An additional "Count to be Normalized" column provides further insights.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fin6KgDeTsSzOjjbN4FEa%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4ac1b41&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FR5QqnSuAMKJetd2lZPvY%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54ef3dcc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#integrated-training-period-with-confirmation-module-1)

Confirmation

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#integrated-training-period-with-confirmation-module-2)

Integrated Training Period with Confirmation Module

Our new training period configurations allow you flexibility to add training period before probation and ensures that employee receives adequate training with better user experience.

*   To set a training period by defining the ‘End Date’ as the ‘Joining Date’ is considered as the start date.
    
*   Probation begins right after the training period ends.
    
*   Extend the training by adding more days.
    
*   Both the employee and manager will be notified of the new end date.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FI4ZBG1ty0Oecu4Bpo1Pv%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1b8f1a4&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#exit)

Exit

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#optimized-employee-separation)

Optimized Employee Separation

Pocket HRMS will block the separation if the employee has any pending requests for

Leaves, On-Duty, Regularizations, Expenses, Reimbursements, or Loans. The system will display the 10 most recent pending requests in each category and also provide you with an option to download an Excel report. That makes the process of reviewing pending requests and taking the necessary steps to proceed with the separation, quick and effortless.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCA24qWdLl3M5XYa1fYDs%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fd13126&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#streamline-resignation-requests-with-mobile-app)

**Streamline Resignation Requests with Mobile App**

Experience the seamless exit process from the mobile app. Employees can now submit their resignation requests directly from their mobile apps. Managers and Department Heads can approve or reject these requests right from their phones as well. This feature is available on both Android and iOS, and it works just like it does on the web. Providing consistent & uniform experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FaPY7G0bzgL4wlSQCnCZP%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9423b24f&sv=2)![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYKOTkmT0IsKy9afyMX8C%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cefaa8a2&sv=2)![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRnfIHKkjT3pQ6XZtVWbR%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1dafcc7e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#customizable-job-offer-approval-flow)

Recruitment

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#customizable-job-offer-approval-flow-1)

Customizable Job Offer Approval Flow

We’ve created a flexible approval process for job offers. The system allows two options:

*   Serial Approval: Both the Job Offer Approval Manager and Department Head approve the offer one after the other.
    
*   Single Approval: Either the Job Offer Approval Manager or Department Head can approve the offer on their own.
    

With customizable approval settings, multiple managers or department heads can be included. Each approver can:

*   Approve the offer as is.
    
*   Reject the offer.
    
*   Modify details like the offer letter, salary, or validity before approving.
    

The final approver can send the offer directly to the candidate, without needing further input from the recruiter.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMqmSJm97MkhUbxHk4QLu%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=386ba5f0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#flexible-header-footer-options-for-recruitment-pdfs)

Flexible Header/Footer Options for Recruitment PDFs

We’ve introduced a new Header/Footer feature for Recruitment Email and CTC Templates, allowing users to choose how to display headers and footers in generated PDFs:

*   **No Header/Footer**: PDFs will be created without any headers or footers.
    
*   **System-Generated Header/Footer**: Automatically includes a header with the company logo and name, and a footer with the company name and address.
    
*   **Custom Header/Footer**: Users can upload their own header and footer images to be included in the PDFs.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvLq08KCySe8WYm0uqvTR%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6443e0&sv=2)

e-Posh

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#e-posh-empowering-action-against-harassment)

e-POSH: Empowering Action Against Harassment

The e-POSH (Prevention of Sexual Harassment) module is now available on web and mobile. It allows female employees to report sexual harassment incidents at the workplace, either for themselves or co-workers, with an option to keep their identity anonymous. A Complaint Committee can be set up, including a Committee Head and members, who can monitor and take necessary actions through the ESS portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWKgWZwvYwLhW9XaRwNE2%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cfb2b8b8&sv=2)

UI/UX Improvements

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/2024-major-highlights#all-new-dashboard-for-easy-access-to-work-essentials)

All New Dashboard for Easy Access to Work Essentials

We’ve created a new, all-in-one employee dashboard that gives a clear view of everything important. Employees can easily check their profile details, shift schedules, upcoming events, leave history, monthly attendance, and company news. With a fresh, easy-to-use design, we’ve also made it simpler for employees to apply for leave, view salary details, and connect with their managers.

# January 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9Y7NMO4FlOuR4pNNZSVz%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%287%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a158c9c-66c9-4022-be9a-1a0f99d070e3&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b2c4a0a&sv=2)

Introducing our latest HRMS software upgrades tailored to enhance workplace efficiency. Experience seamless attendance tracking streamline hiring access real-time attendance tracking and regularization requests. Elevate support with the revamped 'Help Desk,' ensuring swift issue resolution and superior user satisfaction. For the month of January, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/january-2023#single-punch-shift-attendance)

Single Punch Shift Attendance

The feature offers a flexible and efficient way for employees to record their attendance. The HRMS software allows the HR manager or administrator to enable the 'Single Punch' feature for multiple employees or specific categories of employees. Once enabled, employees can punch their attendance at any time between their designated 'in' and 'out' timings.

The system automatically assigns shifts to employees based on their recorded punch time. This ensures accurate tracking of working hours and adherence to the assigned schedules. That accommodates flexible work hours, remote work, or staggered shifts, catering to the modern workforce's needs and reducing administrative burden with automation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBnHUedb1Quz4LGyY6uyS%252FPicture1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D721363aa-b2b3-4be7-8103-27ea4949f2c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=825ea2d0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/january-2023#id-2.-bulk-admin-ratings-for-hassle-free-stage-settings)

2\. Bulk Admin Ratings for Hassle-Free Stage Settings

Introducing our latest software update, designed to empower HR managers. With the new 'Bulk Admin Ratings' feature, you can now effortlessly upload large volumes of 'Admin Ratings' at once, simplifying the importing process stage-wise.

It saves valuable time and effort by uploading multiple Admin Ratings in one go, eliminating manual entry hassles. Minimize data entry errors, ensuring accurate and reliable stage-wise settings for a seamless workflow.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FmXXPEKVPbDUCbhD0mLkE%252FPicture2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35bcd1c9-ac95-430e-bfdd-6ff49f039995&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=828e1473&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/january-2023#id-3.-streamline-hiring-with-external-invites)

3\. Streamline Hiring with External Invites

Recruiters can now effortlessly invite external interviewers by simply entering their email IDs into the system. HR teams can extend invites to candidates without the hassle of juggling multiple platforms. That helps to simplify your recruitment process and elevate your HR capabilities.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fd4WMQPoVdOc8YUPo0gk2%252FPicture3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91c6863e-055c-472d-8e3d-02d4cbd3075d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18e2a56&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/january-2023#id-4.-effortless-time-tracking-with-mobile-app)

4\. Effortless Time Tracking with Mobile App

The enhanced 'My Calendar' feature on the ESS mobile App. Now, employees can effortlessly track in and out timings, monitor completion of total work hours, and instantly identify invalid attendance punches—all in one place.

The app also prompts employees to apply for regularization directly from 'My Calendar,' simplifying the entire process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fi7EdJpVy1wZaYFaqqv9V%252FPicture4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D479bdcbb-7333-470b-a3b5-3c06010af522&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15c6b217&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/january-2023#id-5.-discover-the-enhanced-help-desk-experience)

We're thrilled to introduce the revamped 'Help Desk' features with sleek and modern UI tailored for an unmatched user experience. This means streamlined issue resolution, faster ticket handling, and an intuitive interface that enhances productivity.

With our enhanced Help Desk, your team can provide swift, accurate assistance, ensuring employee satisfaction and smooth operations.

# February 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5RnXm1DB0NDQVXpmyTgE%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcfd62496-7ea6-47b2-a305-918ec06d4cde&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e39cf144&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#effortless-bulk-lop-credit-entry)

Effortless Bulk LOP Credit Entry

Now you can do bulk LOP credit input, making it easier than ever to manage Loss of Pay. No more manual entry for each employee - simply enter credits in bulk for multiple employees at once. This saves time, improves efficiency, and enhances workflow management. As an HR professional or organization, you'll enjoy smoother processes and increased productivity.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOpTivOf1M8dfZQaP7QBz%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2df6b1f0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#efficiency-upgrade-detailed-leave-balance-view)

Efficiency Upgrade: Detailed Leave Balance View

Now, users can select the 'Summary' checkbox in the Leave Tracker report to access a more detailed view. This includes additional columns like 'Credit' and 'Debit,' alongside existing ones such as 'Opening,' 'Used,' and 'Balance.' This enhancement offers a comprehensive overview of leave balances and transactions, enabling informed decision-making for better leave management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAzavVQ6GjVLunWzEUjk8%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4565f87f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqqHQNlF1VZ8IGp3P8QCw%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c45d7869&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#flexible-requirements-for-leave-attachments)

Flexible Requirements for Leave Attachments

Pocket HRMS enables you to set attachment mandatory for the leaves exceeding specified number of days based on a certain group of dates, such as retirement or confirmation. This feature offers flexibility and control in managing attachment requirements for different leave types, ensuring compliance and proper documentation making leave management hassle-free.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3mogJfWz1jUBOBCaHXoN%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cea8791&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#streamlined-multi-company-ess-access)

Streamlined Multi-Company ESS Access

Our HRMS now allows users to access and perform actions across multiple companies. With defined roles or groups, users can view data, make changes, or initiate transactions across entities. This enhancement ensures efficient operations and data security, enabling seamless management across multiple company contexts. It gives you streamlined processes and improved data segregation, enhancing overall productivity.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvRtGdZPiMYMtVdg8h9oP%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1227e365&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#hlk160701859)

Geolocation with Easy Access & Tagging

You will get easier access to geolocation data with a global search option. Employee tagging within locations is also simplified with a dedicated search feature, displaying the count of tagged employees. This enhancement streamlines location management, making it easier to track and manage personnel across different locations. Providing improved accessibility and efficiency in geolocation settings for smoother HR operations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjdzMvb5pmZ1VrxDOQqQO%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=562f4647&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6EVaJUXLbJUhmtRA0Fbd%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=461b4f11&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#geolocation-integration-enhanced-reporting)

Geolocation Integration: Enhanced Reporting

Now, geolocation fields are included in the data export wizard, covering aspects like name, radius, longitude, and latitude. This enhancement empowers users to include location-specific data in their reports, aiding analysis and interpretation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8ktLJypgMboLzv4toQHn%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fa3e19&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#improved-monitoring-with-geolocation)

Improved Monitoring with Geolocation

The ‘In Out Detail’ report now features two new columns, 'IN geolocation' and 'OUT geolocation,'. These columns show where employees enter and exit specified areas, aiding in tracking their movements. This enhancement offers a detailed overview of employee activities based on geolocation data, enhancing monitoring.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fq6Zy4NlCY9lXV8rq7cOz%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9255b146&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#accountability-in-attendance-with-ip-address)

Accountability in Attendance with IP Address

Pocket HRMS now records employees' IP addresses when they punch in and out, included in both individual and team reports. This enables managers and administrators to review attendance records thoroughly, ensuring greater oversight and accountability within the organization.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4gguLQlja8A72ES0nvzD%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5585c75&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#improved-collaboration-in-offer-management)

Improved Collaboration in Offer Management

Recruiters can include managers in CC while sending offers to candidates. This keeps managers informed about offers sent out, streamlining communication, collaboration and transparency in the offer process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FX7ADnKGHowlFu5voork8%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eab3d5e1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#flexible-job-approval-settings)

Flexible Job Approval Settings

Pocket HRMS offers three enhanced flexibility in job approval workflows, ensuring efficient management of job creation and modification requests.

1.  **Approval Required**
    

All new job creation and modifications will need approval from assigned job manager. If a job manager is not assigned, job creation or modification will not be allowed.

1.  **Approval Not Required**
    

All new job creation/modification requests will be directly approved by the system, irrespective of whether a job manager is assigned.

1.  **As per the assigned Job Manager**
    

All new job creation/modification requests will be sent for approval to the assigned job manager. If no job manager is assigned, requests will be directly approved by the system

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGh0M59NBW4Lp5kipgUrM%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=361705ee&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fj0gL12aFOHIkap0QMO39%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2eb93168&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#effortless-module-selection-across-companies)

Effortless Module Selection Across Companies

We provide you 'Select/Deselect All' option for module selection in Cross-Company Manager. Modules not applicable will be automatically deselected and disabled. This streamlines module management, ensuring only relevant options are available, saving time and improving user experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8a28A2kotp2QgWpnRTYL%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1926150f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#improved-oversight-for-job-requisition-approval)

Improved Oversight for Job Requisition Approval

Our HRMS now allows Super Admins to approve or reject Job Requisition requests directly. A new screen named 'Job Admin Approval' displays all pending requests for quick review and action. Notifications inform employees of approval or rejection by the admin. This increases oversight, and ensures efficient management of job requisitions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FM9Kp4CVOpuEiY6NFIaHI%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea3604aa&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#efficient-onboarding-approval-across-companies)

Efficient Onboarding: Approval Across Companies

Now new hires can be approved across different company entities. This simplifies the approval process, enabling administrators to review and approve new employee requests efficiently, regardless of their organizational affiliation. Ensuring efficient new hire onboarding, regardless of their specific company or department within the organization.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWmAPmEc0Oc7PtonLcu7p%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=438a80ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/february-2024#enhanced-flexibility-in-expense-details)

Enhanced Flexibility in Expense Details

Users now are allowed to edit expense modes and purposes, offering greater flexibility and accuracy in expense management. This enhancement simplifies the process, enabling users to make necessary adjustments as needed, improving overall control and accuracy in expense tracking.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F71kHmjOfDoRaqrp8qE3V%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af88668d&sv=2)
