# March 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGGNvHjpKxYmwsDj5Lt3i%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ccab0a2-9454-47f5-a61a-b77b86c6b5ac&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad94e9aa&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#late-mark-deductions-with-customizable-settings)

Late Mark Deductions with Customizable Settings

We've upgraded the late mark customization to now include deductions for late days, which are determined by shift settings and prioritize different types of leave. Admin/HR can now save specific settings for various shifts, enabling them to prioritize the deduction of certain types of leave before others.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FX8RG0tGw6ZnxJLhNdxjp%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b29aa050&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#shift-permissions-set-once-apply-everywhere)

Shift Permissions: Set Once, Apply Everywhere

We've simplified permission settings for employees working different shifts. Now, you can set permissions once for an employee to apply across all their shifts. For example, if an employee is allowed 2 hours monthly for both Morning and Evening shifts, the system ensures this limit isn't exceeded even if he requests different hours for each shift.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbsC0fHufKUUyJGl9IhOB%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f16d809f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#streamlined-punch-out-automation)

Streamlined Punch-Out Automation

If the shift setting is 'Current In-Tomorrow Out' and there's no punch-out recorded, perhaps due to reasons like a holiday, a day off, an unassigned shift, or a modified punch, activating this setting will make the system automatically fill in the punch-out time when the 'In-Out Import' operation is carried out.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrrWIII0VxIlkP7rIUPTd%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2a687a8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fqjhj9MGleJS9pejssdCn%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a705c03b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#enhanced-travel-alerts-with-instant-updates)

Enhanced Travel Alerts with Instant Updates

We've introduced a new email template and app notifications for our travel modules. The template makes it easy to communicate travel plans and updates clearly, while app notifications provide instant alerts for any changes to the itinerary. These improvements simplify our processes, increase efficiency, and enhance the overall user experience within our organization.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvfGEHV5yPeCPCfVZILke%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b4254cf&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fann4CBoRq6ld7VSFglxb%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=632df40f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#simplify-pending-employee-confirmations)

Simplify: Pending Employee Confirmations

The ‘Employee Confirmation Pending’ tab shows tasks awaiting employee feedback for approval or rejection, while the ‘Action Pending’ column indicates how long the task has been awaiting confirmation when the manager extends the confirmation period, streamlining communication and ensuring timely task completion.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAvXn7B7lds23ZUN6u57j%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acdd5f48&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#approval-menu-boosts-mobile-app-convenience)

Approval Menu Boosts Mobile App Convenience

In the mobile app an Approval menu is added to the Profile section, matching the web ESS functionality. This update allows for Shift and Permission approvals. It streamlines mobile experience with essential approval features.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FxVJMylRo8f0Fnqnr8KnT%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67645539&sv=2) ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyJ3GzuQUphKXvzczprWg%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a590c0f&sv=2) ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoJFg9XOpjfTth7IUBMuO%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66768612&sv=2)

*   **Permission Approval – Hourly based**
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBRUsfLkqZUsYpddfRTq1%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f81d0d5c&sv=2) ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvSiFLNyJGo1UZ4zErAAH%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a63bfbbc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#simplified-employee-task-breakdown)

Simplified Employee Task Breakdown

The Task-Based Employee Work Hour Report offers a comprehensive breakdown of individual work. It includes essential information such as employee names, task/project details, dates and total hours worked per task. That helps managers in resource optimization, project tracking, and productivity enhancement while promoting transparency, accountability, and compliance with labor regulations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FT8zsHIIcWvpf6UtPjWg2%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2535c36f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#enhanced-training-insights)

Enhanced Training Insights

The learning reports now provide detailed breakdown, including pre-test and post-test percentages, and success statuses for the both. This thorough report offers clear insights into learners' progress and performance, enabling more accurate assessment of training effectiveness and individual proficiency. Administrators can use these added metrics to make informed decisions, optimizing learning outcomes and customizing future training programs.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkkV2O8tKtuQpNUqbcRar%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7d7785f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FH0b26duH3beJAlCGeXhO%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0b7bae4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#clear-company-hierarchy-chart)

Clear Company Hierarchy Chart

Our system's organization chart visually displays the company's hierarchy, detailing departments and job titles for each employee; users can easily access comprehensive information on any individual, fostering clear communication and collaboration across the organization.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMkKB5GoeEa91hTE1lZkJ%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6787053&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#cross-company-employee-separation)

Cross Company Employee Separation

Employee separation platform now incorporates a Cross-Company feature, enabling managers to approve requests from employees in different departments or subsidiaries, streamlining coordination and decision-making across the organization. With this feature integrated into employee profiles, ensures secure management of cross-company operations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FV8nA4Vt53fw7U6ZPe5jw%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8896edd6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#clear-reimbursement-insights)

Clear Reimbursement Insights

Before, rejected reimbursement reports didn't show up in travel reports, but now users can see reimbursement details regardless of rejection, enhancing transparency and facilitating better tracking and management of travel expenses.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVpspE7EegPlWu3kmjV68%252F21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8f705d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#simplify-candidate-management-prioritize-and-exclude)

Simplify Candidate Management: Prioritize & Exclude

Our upgraded recruitment module now allows recruiters to blacklist or whitelist candidates, streamlining candidate management. Blacklisting bars undesirable candidates from future consideration, while whitelisting prioritizes preferred candidates, optimizing recruitment efficiency by focusing on the most suitable candidates for available positions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F32CHOy3HehbEWKUG2At7%252F22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d563fca&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#job-insights-made-easy)

Job Insights Made Easy

We've introduced a new 'Job Report' within the Hire Module of ESS, offering Admins, HR, and Recruiters comprehensive insights into company job listings. With the ability to download the report based on selected filters, users can efficiently gather and analyze job-related data.

• Job Code

• Job Title

• Hiring Manager

• Added By

• Department Name

• No of Positions

• Requisition Date

• Published Date

• Closure Date

• Job Status

• Position Type

• Job Type

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrhIPHwq4k7l41sVkLUaj%252F23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3dd9ccd2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#enhanced-reapplication-management)

Enhanced Reapplication Management

A new feature allows companies to control how often candidates can reapply for a position, preventing the reuse of Mobile, Email ID, and Aadhar ID by default across all jobs. Admin/HR can set waiting periods of 30, 60, or 90 days, or customize the duration before reapplication is allowed, either for specific jobs or all. The system ensures candidates fill in required parameters to prevent skipping, notifies them of waiting periods, and prompts updates if duplicate profiles are detected after the waiting period. This feature ensures fair and efficient candidate management, preventing spam and encouraging updated candidate information.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/march-2024#streamlined-job-modifications-approval)

Streamlined Job Modifications Approval

Admins now have the ability to directly approve or reject Job Modifications, similar to Job Requisitions, with notifications promptly informing the Recruiter of the decision from the Admin Profile, ensuring smoother and more efficient workflow management.

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#bfcccacfcfd0cdcbffcfd0dcd4dacbd7cdd2cc91dcd0d2)

# December 2025 | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#product-update-december-2025)

Product Update December 2025

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of December 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#leave-lapse-configuration)

Leave Lapse Configuration

Leave Credit settings have been enhanced with a Leave Lapse option, allowing admins to decide whether unused leave should automatically lapse as per company policy. Currently, this applies to leaves credited on the 1st of the month across all credit frequencies, helping prevent unintended accumulation of leave balances.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FWoCCnNM865j582skc19X%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=102d5ce6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#age-based-leave-credit)

Age-Based Leave Credit

An Age Criteria for Leave Credit has been introduced, allowing admins to define a maximum employee age for leave eligibility. Leave will be credited only to employees who meet the configured age requirement.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F0srIzzz59k1FRWMk214G%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=455647a1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#custom-maternity-leave-categories)

Custom Maternity Leave Categories

Earlier, the system supported only a single maternity leave category. This has now been enhanced to allow multiple maternity leave categories, giving organizations the same flexibility available for Paternity Leave and enabling more tailored maternity leave policies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FtMTZud81naA9so2BtMdK%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a3d8b6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#contextual-remarks-for-punch-imports)

Contextual Remarks for Punch Imports

A Remarks field has been added to both Unpunch Import and Invalid Punches Import. Any remarks entered during import are now saved and reflected in the Employee Profile on the Cloud portal, improving auditability and providing clearer context for attendance corrections.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FUPTLLD3SIU5ZQnZqJCJN%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a34e718f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FgB1a3RP1tVRUTSIVZ5VY%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8ac24f6&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FW4nRZU5iD59P9uBAuaEG%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cd10f93&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#real-time-shift-update)

Real-Time Shift Update

Employees can now receive real-time notifications on both web and mobile whenever a manager updates their shift through Roster Management. The notification includes updated shift details along with the manager’s name, ensuring clear visibility and timely awareness.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F3dAxgBdq0dKg98aXD4xb%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3cdc4ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#smarter-employee-report-filtering)

Smarter Employee Report Filtering

Leave and Attendance reports—including Leave, On Duty, Permission, and Regularization—now come with a Generic Filter option. Users can apply advanced, condition-based filters using employee master fields, enabling more precise analysis and easier, more effective reporting.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FxtqUP6yzX2YeTNn4zs2K%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=279f4a9b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/december-2025#proactive-unpunch-monitoring)

Proactive Unpunch Monitoring

The Continuous Unpunch Report has been enhanced to provide deeper insights. In addition to employee code and name, the report now includes Category, Department, Location, and Reporting Manager details, helping HR teams analyse unpunch patterns more effectively.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fw5JnQ7TWZ01I3ISX8QWG%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11d75567&sv=2)

# May 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIWlsXWgqesK4pMSt3asI%252FMay%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8378a12-e877-468c-909e-5d404ac2b46c&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=182668bd&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of May, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#priority-based-time-range-leave-deductions)

Priority-Based Time Range Leave Deductions

Pocket HRMS offers flexible settings of leave deductions based on employees' attendance punch times. You can do the following customizations with ease.

*   Define auto deduction criteria for individual shifts
    
*   Set multiple time ranges of deductions for each shift
    
*   Set priorities with multiple leave types for deductions for each time range
    
*   Delete settings for individual time ranges without disturbing other settings
    
*   Delete all the custom settings for the particular shift when you no longer need it
    

These settings provide better control and efficiency for attendance and leave management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTg2twgCOAORbMJnekdM9%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d77e23ff&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9mMQ4IYhFnr3WLntuO33%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9934a7a4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#extension-for-leave-and-attendance-requests)

Extension for Leave and Attendance Requests

Our new feature allows employees to submit requests such as, Leave, Attendance Regularization, On-duty, and Permission requests up to 5 days after the previous leave cycle ends.

**Example:**

*   **Current Date**: 30th May 2024
    
*   **Current Leave Cycle**: 26th May to 25th June
    
*   **Previous Leave Cycle**: 26th Apr to 25th May
    

Employees want to submit a request for dates that fall under the previous cycle such as 24th May.

**Case A**:

If you select the check box for ‘Limit requests to current and future date range only’ and set ‘5’ as ‘Extended Days’, employees can submit requests for dates within the 5-day buffer. That means employee can submit request for 24th May on current date of 30th may.

**Case B**:

If you select the check box for ‘Limit requests to current and future date range only’ and set ‘4’ as ‘Extended Days’, the buffer ends on 29th May, so employees cannot submit requests for 24th May on present date 30th may.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fd84bnnEYKuJKpFqOvVKr%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1da4a461&sv=2)

Optimized Sandwich Leave Rule Based on Leave Taken

Sandwich Leave deductions now follow the order in which employees apply for them and not the predefined order. If an employee lacks the balance for a particular leave type, Loss of Pay (LOP) will be applied.

**Example**,

*   Employee requests 'Paid Leave' for Friday and 'Sick Leave' for Monday.
    
*   Resulting leave pattern: Paid Leave, Week off, Week off, Sick Leave.
    

**Scenarios**:

*   **If the remaining Paid Leave balance is 2 or more** - Both week off are deducted as Paid Leave.
    
*   **If the remaining Paid Leave balance is 1** -First week off as Paid Leave; the system checks Sick Leave for the second week off.
    
*   **If there is no remaining Sick Leave balance** - The second week off will be considered LOP.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYJKTrKLrDxr1Wp6AIjKk%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12a668b9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#simplified-appraisal-reports-in-modern-pdf-format)

Simplified Appraisal Reports in Modern PDF Format

We've revamped the PMS module with major upgrades. You can now get clearer and more readable appraisal reports in a modern PDF format. Also, we've introduced a new ‘New Detailed Report’ type with a user-friendly layout, making it easier to understand and enhancing your overall appraisal experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQ8gvFbvwVHmfYyOg3WBk%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c81c26fa&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBzc5WIRmJPgUJ2HRUs7T%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39cd2958&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#streamlined-peer-appraisal-interface)

Streamlined Peer Appraisal Interface

We have enhanced the Appraisal Peer Screen with several UI improvements and new features to make it easier to use,

*   Send emails to multiple peers at once
    
*   Delete individual or multiple entries simultaneously with proper validation to prevent errors
    
*   Auto-fill for email IDs for better accuracy
    
*   Edit auto-filled email IDs if needed.
    

These updates streamline the peer appraisal process and improve the overall user experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbRUjII2ijrJbLLL4SxIR%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1258bee5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#offer-letter-and-ctc-break-up-in-single-pdf-attachment)

Offer Letter & CTC Break-up in Single PDF Attachment

Our new feature in the 'Make an Offer' function allows you to send an offer letter and CTC break-up as a single PDF when you select the 'Attachment File' option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgdiJHFuDjHTgb64LC67a%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50e7d77&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#travel-report-in-summary-and-detailed-format)

Travel Report in Summary and Detailed Format

We have introduced two new reports to better manage and analyze travel data:

1.  **Travel Detailed Report**: Provides a detailed view of each travel entry, including reimbursement details, approval status, travel dates, and more.
    
2.  **Travel Summary Report**: Offers a summary of travel activities, highlighting key details for quick insights.
    

These reports enhance travel data tracking and streamline reimbursement processes.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FNBJj8CGPiEPK8iKc7FmP%252Fa.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d41d960-fd90-4ee1-a7cd-7e76d6add4f2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4867fdca&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#integrated-training-period-with-confirmation-module)

Integrated Training Period with Confirmation Module

Our new training period configurations allow you flexibility to add training period before probation and ensures that employee receives adequate training with better user experience.

*   To set a training period by defining the ‘End Date’ as the ‘Joining Date’ is considered as the start date.
    
*   Probation begins right after the training period ends.
    
*   Extend the training by adding more days.
    
*   Both the employee and manager will be notified of the new end date.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FI4ZBG1ty0Oecu4Bpo1Pv%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1b8f1a4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#bulk-approval-and-rejection-for-expense-entries)

Bulk Approval & Rejection for Expense Entries

Our new ‘Approve All’ and ‘Reject All’ features let you approve or reject all expense entries at once, across all pages. This saves time by eliminating the need to review each entry individually.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDe53qszaKNycZyPLGTYI%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a759f339&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024#improved-project-tracking-with-timesheet-attachments)

Improved Project Tracking with Timesheet Attachments

The new "**Attachment** **Option**" for timesheet entries in the project module allows users to attach files directly to their timesheet entries. This enhancement, enables better documentation and support for timesheet data, improving project tracking and record-keeping.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAXzrctNZrA2waJsdb75v%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae75dec3&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0b787e7b7b64797f4b7b6468606e7f6379667825686466)

# December 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbMYhMtmPO7TEdZ6eZzaF%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%289%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f6507d8-53e7-48a6-b910-834cb6c5b492&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d7eedb6&sv=2)

We are excited to announce the deployment of the ‘smHRt Payroll’ Process with the December 2022 update, which is one-of-a-kind feature wherein we have provided additional checks to ensure your payroll runs smoothly. It even uses machine learning to understand your company and suggest modifications and remove outliers from the data.

With the latest update, the HR and Administrator will also be able to identify modified attendance entries. Additionally, they can create custom ESS roles and enable email notifications to the managers and other stakeholders if the HR edits the ‘last working day’ of an employee. We have also added the option to create dynamic email tags for emails. Another major update is the integration of WhatsApp, using which you can send pay slips directly to the employees.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/december-2022#smhrt-payroll)

smHRt Payroll

The smHRt Payroll Process ensures that the HR or Administrator can process payroll with pre-process checks that helps them identify errors in the configuration and formulae and avoid any outliers in the data. It also assures the users that all pre-requisites for processing the payroll are completed, by giving an overview, which includes the total gross salary processed, income tax processed, payroll count vs employee count, and more.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0UwYlVwNEn1XUD9BjSUm%252FPayroll-Process-1536x828.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a30d2d6-bd69-4daa-82c5-a249e3db4c92&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34295898&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/december-2022#identify-modified-attendance-entries)

Identify Modified Attendance Entries

The HR and Administrator can identify the ‘In’ and ‘Out’ entries modified by the employee or another HR or Admin as it get flagged after being modified. This functionality gives you transparency and mitigates fraud as flagging modified entries makes it easier to identify any unauthorized entry.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUbGPoURYlFbnWtBPYV6G%252FIn-Out-Core-Details.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc8a7f30-0685-4343-a47e-b9c234f96fa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=185d778a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/december-2022#seamless-designation-creation)

Seamless Designation Creation

The HR or Administrator can create multiple custom ESS roles which can be used for different designations of users. This feature allows HR administrators to define specific access and permissions for different employee groups. This flexibility allows a more organized approach to access to information and leads to a productive work environment.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrI7kyvBu1pBk5xJDHXQP%252FSelf-Service-Roles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D288a23be-d929-4891-a53d-3b1ebea70afc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a29a18&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/december-2022#notification-for-last-working-date-edits)

Notification for ‘Last Working Date’ Edits

The software now enables you to send email notifications for edits in the last working date provided. The notifications can be sent to HR, managers, the resigning employee, and external email IDs. This ensures seamless communication, enhancing transparency and accountability within the organization. It aids in keeping all relevant stakeholders informed about employee departures, facilitating smooth transitions and maintaining professional relationships.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKqnU7yMrC9azo52g842M%252FReminder.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc116f0ee-502c-4dee-ad48-6729375aa3db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3432199e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/december-2022#dynamic-email-fields)

Dynamic Email Fields

With our latest update HRs can create dynamic email template fields which can be used while sending offer letters to candidates.

For example, an HR can create a dynamic tag as ‘Address’ and the same will be used in the offer letter email template. While sending the offer letter, the ‘Address’ field will be replaced with the mapped dynamic tag.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FE3QK4E7WSK8PZ9AnmRfO%252FEmail-Template.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd468c127-29bd-4d9f-bd8d-0c0e5ee429b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18a89e33&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FL0wOy0RlnNmKoT7Vgk7m%252FEmail-Tags.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cc031c4-a882-4607-b0be-338a42752404&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb31b65b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/december-2022#whatsapp-integration)

WhatsApp Integration

The HR or Administrator can enable WhatsApp integration to directly send pay slips on the employee’s WhatsApp mobile number. This direct and instant delivery enhances efficiency, ensuring timely access to crucial information. By leveraging this functionality, businesses can enhance their employee experience, fostering trust and transparency within the organization. It not only saves time and effort for both HR professionals and employees but also demonstrates the company's commitment to embracing modern, convenient communication channels.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYbcvVWUmlhWWPlgftcA6%252FPay-Slip.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D392b3e2f-95d5-4c70-9cac-e7683790bb1f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=526f2cbd&sv=2)

[PreviousUpdates 2022chevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022)
[NextNovember 2022chevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/november-2022)

# November 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fm7wUEMX0Dau6CzqlT95H%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%2810%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62123402-08d1-466c-a9b9-3c79950e430b&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94e78e33&sv=2)

With this update, we have introduced the option to attach documents with leave requests and restrict employees from making leave requests beyond a certain date. We have also added the option to allocate the duties of the leave day with a colleague while applying for leave. We have also enabled the option to view previous appraisals of employees for both the manager and employees as well as the option to download detailed performance review reports or a summarized version.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/november-2022#mandatory-supporting-leave-document)

Mandatory Supporting Leave Document

The HR or Administrator can enable the option to make it mandatory to attach documents with leave requests. By making it obligatory for employees to attach relevant documents such as medical certificates or official approvals, the company can validate the authenticity of leave requests. This feature streamlines the approval process, reducing the likelihood of false claims and ensuring compliance with company policies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FI0TckH1tAFzrbIuN3zJe%252FMandatory%2520Supporting%2520Leave%2520Document.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad62c02b-0035-4f3d-8a01-c969aa6bb05f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=add4a00&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwCuFJTzHo1tsTEhUqmb9%252FMandatory%2520Supporting%2520Leave%2520Document%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1d3a3b3-8432-418d-8f5d-0aa8bc7e1393&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7366757&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/november-2022#limiting-retroactive-leave-requests)

Limiting Retroactive Leave Requests

We are implementing a leave restriction feature, where you can limit employees from applying for leave for past dates based on the number of days specified in the leave configuration. It facilitates fair leave management, prevents misuse, and encourages employees to adhere to leave policies, thereby promoting a cohesive and efficient workplace.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtsNkksql7wZDOERkrxTe%252FLimiting%2520Retroactive%2520Leave%2520Requests.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4fb5aeb-ae74-4574-8086-c92f672dac7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20edbfa7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/november-2022#consistency-with-leave-task-delegation)

Consistency with Leave Task Delegation

Pocket HRMS now enables employees to allocate their tasks to colleagues while applying for leave. This feature helps to foster seamless workflow continuity and ensure that the company functions efficiently even when team members are on leave. That leads to operational effectiveness enabling you to manage fluctuations in staffing without compromising productivity or project timelines.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlhKmIWRC8NdDftn9jpYB%252FConsistency%2520with%2520Leave%2520Task%2520Delegation.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd15f81bf-4632-4238-b101-2bf030c12eed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=90497782&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbRrOR1TTc8J3zxvaAvmC%252FConsistency%2520with%2520Leave%2520Task%2520Delegation1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6c033f7-d67e-4eaf-8527-5466f4ae33ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a98871a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/november-2022#holistic-performance-insight)

Holistic Performance Insight

Our software now offers the ability for employees and managers to access past performance reviews and feedback enabling employees to track their progress and understand expectations. When manager transitions occur, the new manager's access to prior ratings and feedback ensures a seamless transition, continuity in performance assessment, and a holistic understanding of the employee's journey.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPvhTLnY8FYjJbAFD4K0e%252FHolistic%2520Performance%2520Insight.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cba6e12-47df-47fe-9d56-c20b9852fdcb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4ef9f98&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzCxJrAqIzPhWKVHm0Pqb%252FHolistic%2520Performance%2520Insight1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca9706f7-13f7-440d-a67b-0197e2f059e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=617318fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/november-2022#convenient-performance-review-downloads)

Convenient Performance Review Downloads

The employees can download their performance review reports either as a summary or in a detailed report format. That will make it easy to understand the performance highlights, key feedback, and achievements in a concise summary. Understand your strengths and areas for improvement at a glance. Employees can also dive deep with detailed feedback to understand the context behind evaluations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fll16E4SL2R5UctygeO1a%252FConvenient%2520Performance%2520Review%2520Downloads.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddba96113-97c1-4561-9722-8a7b4808fb9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1839729&sv=2)

# July 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FD5rUUFkQMvg1qveL0jPM%252FJuly%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7e71354-52c8-4a1b-8929-2bb72280f0f6&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c475d5d&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of July, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#instant-department-visibility)

Instant Department Visibility

Now it’s easier to get a complete view of employee details, as alongside the employee's designation, you will also see their ‘Department’ on the top section of their profile. This means you can instantly know both their role and the department they belong to, all in one glance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwZmqUJtiikkyifEVKpEZ%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbe6eb8e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#pre-configured-joining-documents)

Pre-configured Joining Documents

Pocket HRMS streamlines your onboarding process with a pre-configured list of the employee joining documents. That gives you,

*   **Simplified Employee Mapping -** Our pre-configured list makes document mapping quick and easy, saving you time and effort.
    
*   **Seamless Cross-Company Integration -** If a field is missing in your cross-company setup, a pop-up alert will appear. You can simply click on the 'Proceed' and the system will automatically create the necessary field.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5QP0GSVsGYNoApJKIunQ%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b19760f5&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#in-depth-trip-report)

In-depth Trip Report

Now you can get all the trip details in expense with our new ‘Trip Detailed Report’. It enables you to get employee information, including their location and shift times. Plus, you get all the trip-specific information you need—like Start KM, End KM, and Total KM in a single report making it easy and time-efficient to analyse all the details.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUv2Gfo5XwSQP6WqAc9Z7%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53d618d0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#leave-cycle-reflected-in-attendance-settings)

Leave Cycle Reflected in Attendance Settings

Now the ‘Maximum Count’ for the Regularization and On Duty will be aligned with existing leave calendar configurations i.e. ‘Month-wise’ or ‘Date-wise’. The option to set the maximum leave calendar will also reflect the leave configurations.

For example,

1.  Let’s consider a case where leave calendar is set ‘Date-wise’, from 21st of current month to 20th of next month. Then the system will show this specific this date range in the option to set ‘Maximum Count’ for Regularization and on Duty. The system will also the consider the value you put in maximum count feature for this specific date range only.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3MhvbXwvhtykvsFvBM50%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae6419b6&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fh96nIuqQUWIr7uOlfZ0E%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=805b4713&sv=2)

In case, the leave calendar is set ‘Month-wise’, the maximum Regularization and On Duty count will be set and considered according to the respective months. (Standard Calendar Month).

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUMDWmMUrrJ4hFkfp3IZS%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d37e34ba&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3Xy4G8PMuWnGC1jkFLdX%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c987a2bd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#effortless-email-composition-with-new-placeholders)

Effortless Email Composition with New Placeholders

Now, you can quickly draft comprehensive Recruitment and CTC emails with new & efficient placeholders. That enrich the email templates and makes your communication seamless and precise. Our newly introduced placeholders include:

*   Job Title
    
*   Job Code
    
*   Job Department
    
*   Job Type
    
*   Job Cost Center
    
*   Job Grade/Level
    
*   Job Position
    

Along with that, you get Annual and Monthly CTC placeholders in both words and numbers format making the template more convenient than ever before.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWz8CPFPwedJyXPMtYgyl%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c81e496d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIK0ZybcD5XmXlZEtzhTV%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=517beaf0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#lock-resignation-date)

Lock Resignation Date

Managing employee resignation is now made easier with the ‘Lock Resignation Date’ feature. That makes the resignation date non-editable for employees. So, the day on which an employee requests separation from the ESS portal, the same date will be considered as a resignation date for them and they can’t change it later. That gives more structured approach to the separation management process and improve efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWPNuOpvRVh7iRL1yLxEI%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=51ccc415&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#separation-report-includes-pending-requests)

Separation Report includes Pending Requests

With our latest update, when you go to Data Wizard go get a Separation Report, it gives you a complete view. As, now along with the approved entries you will also get details for requests that are pending for approval. So, you get informed about a complete picture and then you can act quickly on any pending requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F86sbSYsMZ8p9tEqdTdqB%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6bc84c49&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024#simplified-leave-credits-with-ui-enhancements)

Simplified Leave Credits with UI Enhancements

Pocket HRMS now provides you with greater flexibility. You can configure leave credit based on attendance, using various date parameters, such as the Date of Confirmation, Date of Joining, and more.

In addition to that, we made UI improvements such as:

*   Explanation of how the leave credit works in attendance-based scenarios
    
*   Option to choose leave credit based on leave balance or credited days
    
*   An easy-to-access guide with a 'How it Works' link
    

These UI enhancements provide more flexibility and accuracy in managing leave credits.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbRJaQ3bhdpLrgsiQCiAR%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cbf6ccd&sv=2)

# October 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqinS7wMP2XuPEkrVXcUw%252FSeptember%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06439204-7223-4ac9-aa3f-024b7a6ba4ab&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a334d91&sv=2)

In our pursuit to improve the end-user experience, we have made further enhancements to your beloved HRMS software.

In this update, we have introduced the option to assign training to employees in bulk. We have also developed the option to save ratings for employees and save it as a draft instead of submitting it. As for the recruiters, there is a new option to whitelist domains before posting jobs online. Finally, we have introduced a robust employee filter to manage their roster effectively.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/october-2022#seamless-bulk-training-assignments)

Seamless Bulk Training Assignments

Our latest feature ‘Bulk Training Assignment’, allows HR professionals and administrators to effortlessly assign training to all employees in one go. This streamlined process eliminates the tedious task of manual allocation, saving valuable time and effort.

By simplifying the training assignment for multiple employees simultaneously, our software ensures efficient workforce development, allowing businesses to focus on strategic goals while ensuring every team member receives the necessary training. Boost productivity, enhance employee skills, and streamline your HR tasks.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbZXgDLDl2e9PDvbeVeTR%252FSeamless%2520Bulk%2520Training%2520Assignments.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De108e168-7d5a-44c6-862e-f524589d17bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=356ad166&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/october-2022#convenient-performance-reviews)

Convenient Performance Reviews

We empower users to effortlessly ‘Save as Draft’ their performance reviews or ratings at any moment, regardless of whether all parameters are completed. This unique feature grants employees the flexibility to work on their performance reports at their own pace and convenience. By eliminating the pressure of completing all fields in one go, we enhance efficiency and reduce stress.

Employees can now focus on their tasks without worrying about stringent deadlines, ensuring a more relaxed and productive work environment. Experience the freedom to manage your performance evaluations seamlessly, promoting a healthier work-life balance and fostering enhanced employee well-being.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRMljqeDfgQF6dliQtP41%252FConvenient%2520Performance%2520Reviews.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2357b23-33db-419b-a60b-8ac866455bd4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e3faaa3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/october-2022#boost-recruitment-reach-by-domain-whitelisting)

Boost Recruitment Reach by Domain Whitelisting

Introducing domain whitelisting feature that provides recruiters the ability to whitelist their company's website or any preferred domain before posting jobs. This streamlined process guarantees that job listings are seamlessly published on the whitelisted domains, ensuring maximum visibility and outreach.

This simplifies the posting procedure and enhances control, recruiters can save valuable time and find the perfect candidates swiftly and effortlessly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FE7Azp8KxbSKPhxnpXoxJ%252FWhitelist%2520Domains%2520for%2520Job%2520Posting.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16687fb3-88e4-40d2-b0fc-485164d42077&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf590b97&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/october-2022#streamline-roster-management-with-filter)

Streamline Roster Management with Filter

With our latest update, you will get an Employee Filter on our Roster Management page in the cloud and the Employee Self-Service (ESS) portal. Now HR/Administrators and managers can effortlessly streamline their workforce management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fx1AlYDs0VEBpd26nYThQ%252FStreamline%2520Roster%2520Management%2520with%2520Filter.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe18e210-0544-4a49-9b77-b94468ec50b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=69b48dae&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgVaZM2eISMizbkxjrIRY%252FEmployee%2520Filter%2520in%2520Roster%2520Management1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D680ad943-aa9c-416b-9da2-9a84d600214c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5584b5c&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#eb989e9b9b84999fab9b8488808e9f83998698c5888486)

# April 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvLi0sw6aZ2cISeqr8nPu%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%2822%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0103aba5-5056-4e40-88e3-e93c646d014a&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5bfddcb9&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of April, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#maximize-efficiency-with-candidate-tracker)

Maximize Efficiency with Candidate Tracker

Now, the candidate tracker can be used to retrieve all the candidate-related information that is included in the candidate report. You can use multiple filters to get up to 100 entries per page with the ability to get up to 6 months of data. Furthermore, you can use the 'Export To Excel' button which has no limit for a date range.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FADKoK1aJBFQHohfjETnf%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=485cd32e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#automated-state-selection)

Automated State Selection

With our latest enhancement in the hire module, you don’t need to manually enter the sate name while adding or editing the job. Once you select the ‘Country’ the system will fetch the state names accordingly making the process hustle-free.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F53VlkKZDAGclh0VO7zOo%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=704ba071&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#bulk-pop-up-data-import)

Bulk Pop-up Data Import

Pocket HRMS now enables you to import the Pop-up Data for multiple business units at once using the Excel sheet. That avoids a lot of repeated data entry saving you plenty of time and effort.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9hsb1sBN6Jpm9a9aXHmG%252FFrame%252023.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c7912a4-111a-4115-be76-0926866b2798&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95fd32aa&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FaPEhgKNxuYrMOexHKMXe%252FFrame%252024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0edc249-03d0-4725-9a7a-b0b937d60023&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da4689c3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#seamless-separation-across-companies)

Seamless Separation Across Companies

Now you can assign a cross company manager for employee separation. The cross-company employee separation feature is now fully functional for the admin portal as well as the self-service portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZARzXaUKrt4eY66GcbDY%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afcbbf0d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#predefined-remarks-for-on-duty-applications)

Predefined Remarks for On-duty Applications

While applying for on-duty applications now employee can select their remark from the predefined field. You can also customize these remarks according to the requirements. If employee don’t select any of the predefined remarks they also have an option to type in their reason, ensuring adaptability to various situations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FghNEjXMc2JEiEIljkOKu%252FFrame%252025.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c65ed5c-6f1d-4455-8e68-c06d408ce564&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d4f890e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvaT0qtB5L5sVAKwqn7lm%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed49a81d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#flexible-leave-deductions-for-invalid-punches)

Flexible Leave Deductions for Invalid Punches

The system now enables you to use the leave deduction feature for invalid punches. For example, if the system detects Invalid Punch i.e., single punch entries after the time consolidation process has been executed, leave deductions will be executed based on your configurations for Invalid Punch.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fl4A6lomSCWWo2SpYdlrh%252FFrame%252026.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe61ae7f-7043-4695-8b03-eda6ce3d572a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d36db15f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/april-2024#specific-leave-credits-for-your-probation-period)

Specific Leave Credits for Your Probation Period

You can customize leave credit configurations for the probation period. Now you can tailor various leave types with specific credit counts for the probation period. Additionally, dependency can be added for probation period completion i.e., probation completion depends on the Confirmation date. Furthermore, HR can specify whether unused leaves should be Elapsed or Carried Forward upon confirmation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFDBnPKXjxzv1DgpjMuGE%252FFrame%252027.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf6c3592-e7ca-4f53-b670-324a0c83fbfc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=705db8c0&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#196a6c6969766b6d5969767a727c6d716b746a377a7674)
