# 2025 Major Product Highlights | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDUH4D0CIWJl2TnKf6ROl%252FHighlights%25202025%2520Docs%2520Banner%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d3e4f8a-c19e-42c4-8563-48cee332cd4b&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d95a9ec6&sv=2)

2025 was about strengthening the foundation of everyday HR operations.Across payroll, compliance, attendance, exits, expenses, budgeting, performance, and employee experience, Pocket HRMS focused on one thing: helping HR teams move faster with confidence, accuracy, and control.

Here’s what’s new and why it matters.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.-everyday-hr-tasks-made-noticeably-easier)

1\. **Everyday HR Tasks, Made Noticeably Easier**

Small improvements create big wins in day-to-day HR operations. These updates reduce clicks, reduce confusion, and improve speed across commonly used workflows.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FiJplJJ1DEKi82LIIH4dL%252F1%2520Everyday%2520HR%2520Tasks%252C%2520Made%2520Noticeably%2520Easier.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd46f941-8fb6-4f16-b160-8eb60bd20f8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4bd4f29&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.1-bring-structure-to-appraisal-conversations)

1.1 **Bring Structure to Appraisal Conversations**

HR teams can now control the order of appraisal questions so evaluations follow a clear flow. This improves the manager experience, encourages better responses, and reduces missed or inconsistent inputs.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.2-a-more-intuitive-pms-experience)

1.2 **A More Intuitive PMS Experience**

Performance screens now have been refined to feel cleaner and easier to navigate. This reduces effort for managers during reviews and helps HR teams manage cycles with fewer support queries.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.3-create-a-professional-career-page-in-minutes)

1.3 **Create a Professional Career Page in Minutes**

Organizations can now launch a fully branded, modern career page in just a click—no technical setup required. Hiring teams go live faster, while candidates enjoy a smooth, professional experience from their very first visit.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.4-instant-access-to-tax-details)

1.4 **Instant Access to Tax Details**

Tax details are now available instantly in a quick pop-up view, so teams can review information without navigating away from the screen. This speeds up payroll processing and enables faster, more confident responses to employee tax queries.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.5-hr-letters-your-way)

1.5 **HR Letters, Your Way**

HR teams can now design and manage custom letter formats with ease, ensuring consistent communication while still supporting organization-specific templates and dynamic data fields.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.6-quick-in-out-summary)

1.6 **Quick In–Out Summary**

In-out reports now give a clearer summary view for faster daily review. This reduces the need to open multiple screens just to confirm punch timelines.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.7-in-app-ess-announcements)

1.7 **In-App ESS Announcements**

Important announcements are now delivered directly to employees through ESS pop-ups, ensuring higher visibility and reducing the chances of missing critical HR or policy updates.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.8-better-control-over-approval-chains)

1.8 **Better Control Over Approval Chains**

Approval workflows are now clearer and more streamlined, giving HR teams better visibility and control at every stage. This reduces approval bottlenecks and makes it easy to see exactly where requests are pending.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.9-more-secure-user-friendly-password-resets)

1.9 **More Secure, User-Friendly Password Resets**

Password reset emails are now clearer and easier to follow, helping employees regain access faster while reducing confusion and support requests related to login issues.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.10-protected-document-delivery)

1.10 **Protected Document Delivery**

Sensitive documents can now be shared securely through ESS, strengthening confidentiality and minimizing the risks associated with manual or unsecured sharing methods.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-1.11-ctc-that-adapts-to-global-teams)

1.11 **CTC That Adapts to Global Teams**

CTC structures now support multiple currencies, making compensation management smoother and more consistent for organizations operating across regions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-2.-learning-that-goes-beyond-attendance)

2\. **Learning That Goes Beyond Attendance**

Training effectiveness depends on engagement and outcomes, not just completion.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FG4xNkqaR0XT0XLzRklkE%252F2%2520Learning%2520That%2520Goes%2520Beyond%2520Attendance.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db980ebb1-439e-4f5a-abd7-48b4b3f88774&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac1ce12b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-2.1-learning-programs-that-listen)

2.1 **Learning Programs That Listen**

Now, with the built-in surveys within learning programs it is easy to capture participant feedback, helping organizations measure effectiveness and continuously improve future learning initiatives.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-2.2-smarter-trainer-identification)

2.2 **Smarter Trainer Identification**

External trainers can now be tagged to training sessions, improving visibility, tracking, and reporting for vendor-led learning programs.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-2.3-multi-trainer-sessions-simplified)

2.3 **Multi-Trainer Sessions, Simplified**

Training sessions can now include multiple trainers with enhanced attendance tracking, making it easier to manage larger and more complex learning programs with confidence.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-2.4-measure-engagement-beyond-courses)

2.4 **Measure Engagement Beyond Courses**

Track how learners engage with shared reference materials to gain deeper insights into participation and learning impact beyond attendance alone.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.-employee-exits-finally-under-control)

3\. **Employee Exits, Finally Under Control**

Exits require structure, visibility, and coordination across teams.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKff8fdWBgaxAILk2EFfH%252F3%2520Employee%2520Exits%252C%2520Finally%2520Under%2520Control.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D107f799c-4370-4fa0-907e-1fb9f03cc5d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6854536a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.1-approve-early-exit-exactly-on-the-last-working-day)

3.1 **Approve Early, Exit Exactly on the Last Working Day**

HR teams can now approve separations in advance while ensuring the employee is officially separated only on their actual last working day. This allows smoother exit planning without triggering early payroll actions, access changes, or compliance processes.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.2-exit-with-clarity.-re-hire-with-confidence)

3.2 **Exit with Clarity. Re-Hire with Confidence.**

HR teams can now capture re-hire eligibility directly during the exit process, creating a clear and structured outcome that supports future hiring decisions and removes reliance on informal notes or memory.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.3-group-wide-fnf-approvals-streamlined)

3.3 **Group-Wide FnF Approvals, Streamlined**

FnF approvals can now be managed centrally for employees linked to multiple legal entities, reducing duplication, speeding up approvals, and ensuring consistent exit handling across group companies.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.4-clear-notifications-at-every-exit-stage)

3.4 **Clear Notifications at Every Exit Stage**

Automated notifications keep HR, managers, finance teams, and employees informed at every stage of the separation workflow, reducing follow-ups and ensuring no critical exit step is missed.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.5-smarter-resignation-and-lwd-management)

3.5 **Smarter Resignation and LWD Management**

Resignation and last working day tracking is now clearer and more structured, giving HR teams better visibility into notice periods, timelines, and status. This helps manage exits with confidence and avoids confusion during the closure process.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-3.6-dedicated-hr-ownership-for-exits)

3.6 **Dedicated HR Ownership for Exits**

Each exit case can now be assigned to a dedicated HR owner, bringing clear accountability, smoother coordination, and timely completion of FnF activities.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-4.-more-accurate-work-hours-even-for-complex-shifts)

4\. **More Accurate Work Hours, Even for Complex Shifts**

Accurate attendance becomes critical when work patterns are not linear.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUzn5zTiJaO5qeZbgNK0j%252F4%2520More%2520Accurate%2520Work%2520Hours%252C%2520Even%2520for%2520Complex%2520Shifts.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b8d95d7-2f32-4060-ac8c-a988bf1a310a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73670dd6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-4.1-work-hour-precision-for-break-based-shifts)

4.1 **Work Hour Precision for Break-Based Shifts**

Now you can define structured breaks and split shifts within a workday using Break Shift functionality. Productive hours are calculated automatically by excluding defined breaks, ensuring attendance reflects actual working time. This delivers fairer work-hour evaluation and payroll-ready attendance data without manual adjustments.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-5.-expense-and-travel-without-the-back-and-forth)

5\. **Expense and Travel, Without the Back-and-Forth**

Expense processing becomes smoother when automation replaces manual checks.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FErzn4NDz3gvYf0NVDrUz%252F5%2520Expense%2520and%2520Travel%252C%2520Without%2520the%2520Back-and-Forth.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc71bb841-4ae1-4bcd-adac-7c2dac68511f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7f69438&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-5.1-consistent-daily-expense-governance)

5.1 **Consistent Daily Expense Governance**

you can set daily expense caps that are enforced automatically at the time of submission. This reduces rejections, minimizes manual validation, and keeps expense claims aligned with company policy from the start.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-5.2-fair-travel-distance-every-time)

5.2 **Fair Travel Distance, Every Time**

Now you can track trip distances automatically using location-based kilometre calculation, eliminating manual entries and calculation errors. Claims are submitted faster, visibility improves with smart indicators for exceeded limits, and exceptions can be managed through controlled overrides.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-5.3-handle-exceptions-without-breaking-policy)

5.3 **Handle Exceptions Without Breaking Policy**

You can now allow authorized users to override expense eligibility rules in justified cases, maintaining structured policies while enabling the flexibility needed to handle real-world exceptions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-6.-promotion-updates-made-simple-and-quick)

6\. **Promotion Updates Made Simple & Quick**

Promotions without paperwork chaos.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUdXljlrZL5oWbNiJpFze%252F6%2520Promotion%2520Updates%2520Made%2520Simple%2520%2526%2520Quick.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5c6d6f3-c4ac-44ec-9293-8652a0fb65cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f848030f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-6.1-quicker-promotions-less-admin-effort)

6.1 **Quicker Promotions, Less Admin Effort**

Designation, role, and related updates are now handled faster through structured system workflows, reducing manual effort and ensuring timely, accurate changes.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-7.-payroll-that-feels-safer-and-more-predictable)

7\. **Payroll That Feels Safer and More Predictable**

Payroll accuracy is not just about calculations. It is about governance, accountability, and trust across HR, finance, and leadership.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFSpqApb9dsW5c84hyItc%252F7%2520Payroll%2520That%2520Feels%2520Safer%2520and%2520More%2520Predictable.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bf98361-a424-4ef8-b10f-7d0327755154&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b7270ea&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-7.1-payroll-approvals-you-can-trust)

7.1 **Payroll Approvals You Can Trust**

Now you can run payroll with enterprise-grade approval and control. Once payroll is prepared, it flows through a clearly defined, multi-level approval process where authorized stakeholders review and validate details before finalization. Salaries are released only after all required approvals are completed, helping identify discrepancies, compliance risks, and calculation issues early for a more reliable payroll cycle.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-7.2-secure-attendance-for-error-free-payroll)

7.2 **Secure Attendance for Error-Free Payroll**

Now you can lock attendance data as soon as payroll processing begins, preventing changes to punches, leave adjustments, or work hours. This keeps payroll figures consistent throughout the cycle and eliminates rework caused by last-minute edits.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-7.3-faster-hassle-free-salary-disbursement)

7.3 **Faster, Hassle-Free Salary Disbursement**

Disburse salaries directly through bank integration once payroll is finalized. Pocket HRMS automatically generates a secure, bank-compliant pay-out file with verified employee details and accurate net pay amounts. This eliminates Excel-based salary files, reduces errors, strengthens data security, and ensures faster, more reliable salary pay-outs.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-8.-performance-that-directly-impacts-pay)

8\. **Performance That Directly Impacts Pay**

Performance outcomes should translate clearly into compensation decisions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1drKSjURQ3iQHOyjwYT5%252F8%2520Performance%2520That%2520Directly%2520Impacts%2520Pay.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72a5b240-7fe1-49b3-83aa-a35f7cf8fc06&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba5913b0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-8.1-performance-linked-increments-automated)

8.1 **Performance-Linked Increments, automated**

Automatically derive increment percentages from PMS outcomes, reducing manual intervention and ensuring consistent, fair salary revisions driven by appraisal results.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-8.2-pms-feedback-process-overview)

8.2 **PMS Feedback Process Overview**

Now you can run appraisals on a structured feedback framework that brings greater clarity and consistency across cycles, making evaluations more transparent and easier to understand for both employees and managers.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-9.-budgets-that-tell-you-whats-really-happening)

9\. **Budgets That Tell You What’s Really Happening**

Managing budgets across multiple companies should not require multiple spreadsheets.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHNostHws0FQ5ov2hQtcT%252F9%2520Budgets%2520That%2520Tell%2520You%2520What%25E2%2580%2599s%2520Really%2520Happening.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D253b3253-59e2-4add-a349-de0c766ece1c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2185cefd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-9.1-data-driven-budgeting-made-simple)

9.1 **Data-Driven Budgeting Made Simple**

Now get a clear, consolidated view of turnover, budgets, and workforce data across group companies through intelligent dashboards. With simple summaries, easy data updates, and role-based access, HR teams and leadership can review group-level insights with clarity and confidence.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-10.-compliance-built-into-everyday-hr)

10\. **Compliance Built into Everyday HR**

Compliance becomes easier when visibility and control are built into the system.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnONAHz3OAQFKVZ2lnFL9%252F10%2520Compliance%2520Built%2520into%2520Everyday%2520HR.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55cff97f-fe92-480c-a824-79caad1e79e2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a121eb7c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-10.1-compliance-management-fully-centralized)

10.1 **Compliance Management, Fully Centralized**

Manage statutory compliance from a single, consolidated dashboard. The Compliance Dashboard brings PF, ESIC, PT, TDS, salary registers, and other statutory reports together in one secure screen, making it easy to access, download, and store filings for any selected period. This improves audit readiness while reducing operational complexity.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/2025-major-product-highlights#id-10.2-trusted-ekyc-for-compliance-ready-payroll)

10.2 **Trusted eKYC for Compliance-Ready Payroll**

Now verify employee identity using Bank, PAN, and Aadhaar validation, improving the authenticity of master data while strengthening compliance readiness. This reduces issues during audits and statutory checks and builds greater trust in employee records.

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c7b4b2b7b7a8b5b387b7a8a4aca2b3afb5aab4e9a4a8aa)

# September 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFbyCQhM2SZvzhN47LXO5%252FSeptember%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a0acdf0-a8fd-4f9f-8191-399a641bbf22&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fdc9644&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of July, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#track-actual-vs.-regularized-times-with-ease)

Track Actual vs. Regularized Times with Ease

The Attendance Regularization Report now shows both the actual IN/OUT times and the regularized IN/OUT times. This gives you a complete view of attendance records. The enhancement is reflected in My Report, Team Report, as well as Employee Report.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fiixeix2e7lofFA5S729g%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1bb90e2&sv=2)

**My Report:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlR4t2oRY5lNPRynuyr1H%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c397a4d&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer **My Team Report/Employee Report**

Remark Configuration for Regularization and On Duty

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHEyBL1e4ecqVwXapBrOI%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49973c24&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#flexible-remarks-in-regularization-and-on-duty)

Flexible Remarks in Regularization and On Duty

Now, HR can choose whether to make it mandatory for employees to provide remarks while submitting the regularization & on duty requests or not. If you make remarks mandatory, employees will have to provide them. If it is kept optional, employees can choose to submit their requests with or without remarks.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC10GRfqZjfwtXIHiNMGN%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=797cc897&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#on-duty-type-option-for-greater-clarity)

On-Duty Type Option for Greater Clarity

With our new enhancement along with the On-duty Remarks you can also configure the dropdown values for the ‘On-Duty Type’ field. The configured values will be visible to employee in dropdown options for easy selection. Providing greater ease, segregation and keep comprehensive information.

Some Examples for reference,

**On Duty Type:** Work from Home, Field Work, Client Meetings, External Training Sessions, Site Visits, etc.

**On Duty Remarks:** Equipment Maintenance, Client Follow-up, Project Coordination, Research and Development, etc.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZkPeSbDuaFgHTsl1lInH%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e603064&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#complete-comp-off-reports-at-your-fingertips)

Complete Comp Off Reports at Your Fingertips

Pocket HRMS allows you to download a detailed Comp Off Elapse Report. The report includes dates when comp offs were credited, how many have been used, the remaining balance, manager approvals, and details about expired comp offs.

To get this report, make sure the Elapse Feature is set up in the Leave Configuration screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvuPQ7sVTIUjRw4mYlJ2m%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=239e5098&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMi08UhxLJCSOaYfvuEpk%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1db2270c&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#customize-week-off-scheduling)

Customize Week-Off Scheduling

The week-off setting is now more flexible than ever before. Now you have more control and select whether the 1st, 2nd, 3rd, 4th, or 5th occurrence of a day (like Sunday) should be your week-off for a certain date range.

Once you save the settings, your choices will be clearly shown on the screen for easy reference and full transparency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FObdBVUvzuFVqTkkbsVlU%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e09e0364&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#automatic-alerts-for-incomplete-shift-hours)

Automatic Alerts for Incomplete Shift Hours

Employees who haven't finished their scheduled shift hours will now automatically receive an email notification. The email will include details like how many hours are missing, the actual shift hours, and other important information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLZyTWqSvf2iwds6AO6yj%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0784592&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer Description automatically generated

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#all-new-dashboard-for-easy-access-to-work-essentials)

All New Dashboard for Easy Access to Work Essentials

We’ve created a new, all-in-one employee dashboard that gives a clear view of everything important. Employees can easily check their profile details, shift schedules, upcoming events, leave history, monthly attendance, and company news. With a fresh, easy-to-use design, we’ve also made it simpler for employees to apply for leave, view salary details, and connect with their managers.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPCzsYbpkWeJuchrb3hSo%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eefa1b4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#faster-company-selection-in-a-single-click)

Faster Company Selection in a Single Click

We’ve made it easier to select and switch between companies. Now, when you click on the company field, start typing the company name, and it will instantly appear, allowing you to switch companies with just one click. This update makes navigation faster and reduces the number of steps needed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FB7qmmhwVKy1gfkFz67cs%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31dbc9f7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#upload-multiple-expense-files-with-ease)

Upload Multiple Expense Files with Ease

You can now upload multiple files at once when submitting expenses. Now, you can add several files, and they will be downloaded together in a ZIP folder. The system has a size limit—each file can be up to 5MB, and for multiple files, the total size can be up to 20MB. This new feature is available on both the web and mobile apps, saving a lot of time and effort.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FV8BBfwgEqhbN4zd8R7Fo%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21ac5fb7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#quickly-edit-and-resubmit-travel-advance-requests)

Quickly Edit and Resubmit Travel Advance Requests

We've added a new page where employee can easily see all the pending travel advance requests. The user can also view any rejected requests on this page and use the new EDIT option to make changes and resubmit them, or simply resubmit without any changes. Eliminating the need to create a new request from the scratch if the previous one is rejected, making the process faster and more efficient.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fs6CyfjC9YRNdlDTadnUP%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7c57ac6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#informative-and-efficient-learning-cards)

Informative and Efficient Learning Cards

Get better clarity with our new simpler and easy to understand cards. Now, the Learning Card layout also gives you quick options to easily edit, archive, copy, or delete cards

The Learning Card shows important information, including:

*   Trainer details
    
*   Learning mode
    
*   Learning period
    
*   Duration in hours and days
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fvf6GeTUTf4uPndXaak83%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d95824f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#sort-fields-by-module-and-order-with-ease)

**Sort Fields by Module and Order with Ease**

Pocket HRMS now provides is an option to sort fields by module name and order number. Making it quicker to identify which fields were created for each module and simpler to find the information you need.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FH7vChRjGn6Qe8XizqqIP%252Fkkkk.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db01c9819-4ab0-45ab-950e-c1a63441cd97&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1db48c79&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#more-clarity-in-probation-and-training-decisions)

**More Clarity in Probation & Training Decisions**

Now in addition to the Extend and Confirm button, we’ve added a separate **Reject** button in the probation and training decision interface. Managers can easily reject an employee during their probation or training period, change their status, and send a notification. The confirmation page will also show if an employee has been rejected.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5dBQ4YD6dPkiCEhagOY5%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3e1c814&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#user-friendly-employee-confirmation-form)

**User-Friendly Employee Confirmation Form**

Now we make it easier to use Employee Confirmation Form. The new design is clearer and better organized, helping HR managers and team leads evaluate employee performance more effectively. This updated form incorporates your feedback and follows best practices from the previous version.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Frf8y9SRSNKgE6W1cKUdk%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b79a8942&sv=2)

Previous Format

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtErrV7qj7OMNWfLq2lqq%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d5e79c0&sv=2)

New Format

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#streamlined-separation-process-for-managers)

**Streamlined Separation Process for Managers**

With our latest update HR can now let managers change the Last Working Date when they approve an employee’s Separation request. The request for change will be communicated to higher-level managers, department heads, and HR during the approval process.

The access can be easily controlled from the ‘Exit Notification Settings’ page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMYOEJE0uyzDmqQJRRScL%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a836b35&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQshDZ1gA5dPDrIPPEpYv%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc5cc2fb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVxqoDMgX3KUt1s5QwefP%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4f28f3e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#customize-your-exit-reports-with-new-fields)

**Customize Your Exit Reports with New Fields**

We’ve added new fields to the Separation Module in Data Wizard! Now, HR can easily create a customized Exit Report based on their needs. This way you always get complete exit report as per your company policies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYRkNNSwPxTPomteAevW8%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a69e528c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#streamline-resignation-requests-with-mobile-app)

**Streamline Resignation Requests with Mobile App**

Experience the seamless exit process from the mobile app. Employees can now submit their resignation requests directly from their mobile apps. Managers and Department Heads can approve or reject these requests right from their phones as well. This feature is available on both Android and iOS, and it works just like it does on the web. Providing consistent & uniform experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FaPY7G0bzgL4wlSQCnCZP%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9423b24f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYKOTkmT0IsKy9afyMX8C%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cefaa8a2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRnfIHKkjT3pQ6XZtVWbR%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dafcc7e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#personalize-headers-and-footers-effortlessly)

**Personalize Headers and Footers Effortlessly**

Admins and HR can now change the Header and Footer in each Email and CTC template for the recruitment module. If the main Header and Footer are set to Custom, they can update the images in each template without affecting the primary setting. You can also delete images from individual templates if needed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVzQOIDZB40d5L0XNI83x%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a85025&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#easily-add-attachments-to-your-fnf-settlement)

**Easily Add Attachments to Your FnF Settlement**

Now, Admins and HR can easily add custom attachments when handling the Full and Final Settlement. They can upload one file at a time or several files together in a .zip format, with a maximum size of 5 MB. Later, these files can be downloaded using the ‘Preview’ option, which will include both the files and the FnF checklist.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjBDidPiuw2bLT9cXGqJV%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=106f2b6a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/september-2024#clear-salary-tags-for-easy-understanding)

Clear Salary Tags for Easy Understanding

The system will now display tags on the Salary Details screen to show how salaries were processed. For instance, if the salary includes Income Tax, a tag will appear to indicate this. This feature will help HR easily understand how each salary was calculated. You’ll also see these tags on the Salary Summary page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJcDEt31rTYps1s3zSY5T%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=462a76ed&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAnXcRV2kCU3ZKv7sYs2o%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65241e32&sv=2)

# July 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FY7p297zgNwTDIE53qdom%252FJuly%25202025.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2529507-0793-4d12-a5fd-1363efa72479&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d9e919&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of July 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#regularization-and-on-duty-limits-by-bu-employee-wise-via-rule-engine)

Regularization & On-Duty Limits by BU/Employee Wise (via Rule Engine)

The system now allows flexible Regularization and On-Duty limits by enabling configurations at two additional levels — Business Unit-wise and Employee-wise — in addition to the existing Company-wise setup. Previously, limits could only be defined at the company level, but now users have greater control and flexibility.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#id-1.-business-unit-wise-limits)

1\. Business Unit-wise Limits:

Admins can assign different limits for each Business Unit based on roles.

Example:

*   Manager: On Duty – 1, Regularization – 1
    
*   HR: On Duty – 2, Regularization – 3
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#id-2.-employee-wise-limits)

2\. Employee-wise Limits:

Specific limits can be set for individual employees.

Example:

*   EMP0004: On Duty – 2, Regularization – 1
    
*   EMP0900: On Duty – 1, Regularization – 1
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#id-3.-rule-engine-controlled)

3\. Rule Engine Controlled:

All configurations are handled through the Rule Engine. Setup details can be shared with the Development Team for implementation as needed.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#apply-category-based-l-and-a-rules-via-rule-engine)

Apply Category-Based L&A Rules via Rule Engine

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#whats-new)

What’s New:

*   Previously, Leave & Attendance (L&A) restrictions were company-wide with only one attendance cycle (either Month-wise or Date-wise like 26–25).
    
*   Now, multiple attendance cycles can be configured per employee category, as long as they match the Month Days setting.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#category-specific-restriction-days)

Category-Specific Restriction Days:

Admin/HR can now set different L&A submission cut-off periods for each category.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#examples)

Examples:

*   Category 1: Cycle – Month-wise | Restriction – 5 days after month-end
    
*   Category 2: Cycle – 26–25 | Restriction – 10 days after 25th
    

After the restriction period, employees cannot submit L&A requests for the previous cycle.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#benefits)

Benefits:

*   More flexible attendance cycle management across employee categories
    
*   Stronger payroll compliance by preventing post-cycle changes
    
*   Controlled entirely through the Rule Engine for accuracy and customization
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#customize-ot-remark-settings)

Customize OT Remark Settings

Now you can set mandatory OT remarks with dropdown options to ensure consistent and standardized approvals.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#whats-new-1)

What’s New:

*   OT approval can now include mandatory remarks.
    
*   HR/Admin defines dropdown values for managers to select from.
    
*   In ESS, managers must choose a remark from the dropdown (if mandatory) while approving OT.
    
*   This ensures consistency in justification for OT approvals.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXciJi99Em8pLOUAL9pek%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f912ce4a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhbFfAyiyIoY46VCl4nwi%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f08709c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#improved-week-off-export)

Improved Week Off Export

*   Users can export week off data for a selected date range.
    
*   Export is available for employee-wise week off settings only.
    
*   The data is downloaded in Excel format.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0U0jBE5yPdWtxERYPV4E%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ceca153&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#pms-review-workflow)

PMS Review Workflow

PMS Feedback Process – Overview

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#features-overview)

Features Overview:

*   Admins can set custom feedback fields for each appraisal stage.
    
*   Fields may include questions or inputs like Activities and Recommendations.
    
*   Option to add Instructions to guide can be added to the feedback form.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#manager-access)

Manager Access:

Managers can view their team and fill feedback forms via ESS.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#the-form-includes)

The form includes:

*   Title & Feedback Period
    
*   KPI-based questions under KRAs
    
*   Input areas for Activities, and Recommendations
    
*   Manager Remarks
    

**Supports daily, monthly, quarterly, and yearly cycles.**

*   New form auto-generates daily.
    
*   Latest feedback is shown by default; older ones can be viewed via Feedback History tab.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#additional-features)

Additional Features:

*   "Copy to All Stages" option for quick field setup.
    
*   Feedback reports are accessible to both managers and admins from ESS.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#email-confidential-docs-via-ess)

Email Confidential Docs via ESS

We’ve added a secure way to send sensitive documents like Payslips, TDS Worksheets, and Form 16 via ESS.

*   Files are emailed to employees’ personal IDs in encrypted format.
    
*   Even downloads from ESS (My Salary Details / My Tax Details) stay encrypted for security.
    
*   This protects confidential financial data from unauthorized access.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#to-enable-encryption-and-secure-delivery)

To enable encryption and secure delivery:

*   Open the Payslip tab and go to "Other Options" while editing settings.
    
*   Turn on encryption based on your company’s policy.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4JqAwXssax8HfGWsEWw7%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b474bfa&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#daily-expense-claim-limit-setup)

Daily Expense Claim Limit setup

A new ‘Per-Day’ approval option is now available in Expense Eligibility settings to control duplicate claims. This prevents employees from submitting multiple claims of the same type on the same day.

*   Now available along with existing Claim-Wise and Monthly option.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#validation-logic)

Validation Logic:

*   Employees are allowed to submit only one claim per expense type each day.
    
*   If they try to submit another claim of the same type on the same date, the system will block it and show a validation message.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ft6e3FRwWPKaGwdbulTxK%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8676aba9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/july-2025#view-edit-validations-in-monthly-input)

View/Edit Validations in Monthly Input

Smart validations have been added to help Admin/HR use the View and Edit options correctly in the Monthly Input screen.

*   If data isn’t saved yet, the system prompts:
    

“Please click 'View' and save the Monthly Input first before editing.”

*   If data is already saved, it prompts:
    

“Please click 'Edit' to overwrite the saved data.”

*   These validations prevent accidental overwrites or incorrect actions.
    
*   Helps avoid mistakes and makes the process smoother and more user-friendly.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOURHGH8zjUL4rpfD1CAO%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96136512&sv=2)

Control Visibility of Limits in Tax & Income Heads

A new checkbox has been added to let Admin/HR control whether deduction/income limits are visible to employees in ESS.

*   New Option: "Do not show Limit in TDS Declaration & Proof"
    
*   Available for both Tax Sections and Other Income Heads, similar to Tax Sub Sections
    
*   Helps Admin/HR hide limits to avoid confusion or bias during employee declarations
    
*   Provides a cleaner and more focused declaration experience for employees

Email Alerts for FnF Approval/Rejection by Department Head

# November 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7wGP8IS7H4yuZTiQs2bg%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%2811%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87e41d1f-1eb8-4dbe-8f97-726c0c616362&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27e2c273&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of November, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#streamlined-certificate-management-in-employee-profiles)

Streamlined Certificate Management in Employee Profiles

This enhancement lets an employee upload certificates in the Training section of his profile. This section is where you find info about the education and training of employees. Now, it's all in one place, making it simpler for an employee to upload, download and delete all the important training and education details.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4o9rfsWCz3VSePYLzZV4%252F1%2520Certificate%2520Upload%2520Option%2520in%2520Training%2520Details.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debf28dfd-cf9a-473f-b6c1-570d89a5de95&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a9c3b91&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#shift-centric-leave-deductions)

Shift-Centric Leave Deductions

The system now allows for setting up attendance and leave deductions based on different shifts. This means you can customize how leave is deducted for employees depending on the specific shift they are working.

This feature provides flexibility in managing attendance and leave policies, allowing you to tailor deduction rules according to the varied schedules and working hours of different shifts. It simplifies the process of handling leaves by aligning deduction practices with the unique characteristics of each work shift.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvN5JtZMIsdAsWBXfvegs%252F2Working%2520Hours%2520Setting%2520Shift%2520Wise1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbee3ce41-ea84-4245-8167-9d461ccf8363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df804ad3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FiYVDDHGpbIaUDM09PzYi%252F2Working%2520Hours%2520Setting%2520Shift%2520Wise2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40a2988c-f88f-4e39-83c5-0f70708241df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3029143&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#flexible-week-off-overtime-settings)

Flexible Week-Off Overtime Settings

The updated HRMS software now lets you set specific rules to easily manage overtime for employees during their week off. In addition to the minimum and maximum working hour eligibility for overtime, the system also allows you to specify the start time after which overtime work hours will be counted.

For example, if you set,

*   Overtime on week off will start at 15 hours (according to the 24-hour Clock)
    
*   Minimum time to be considered as 1 minute &
    
*   Maximum working hours as 6
    

If an employee works past 3 pm (15 hrs) on a weekend, even just for one minute, it's considered overtime (OT). However, only up to 6 hours of overtime is allowed. So, if an employee works 6 hours and 30 minutes on the weekend, only 6 hours will be counted as overtime.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#customize-deletion-access-for-joining-documents)

Customize Deletion Access for Joining Documents

The new feature in the software allows you to control the deletion of employees' joining documents. In simpler terms, you can now choose whether or not to show the delete button to employees for Joining Documents. You can opt to hide the delete button adding an extra layer of control and preventing accidental or unauthorized removal of crucial joining documents.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5r3WJAJmy1JnQFXLpmSA%252F4Delete%2520Option%2520Hide%2520for%2520Joining%2520Document1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba2d56ed-7181-4810-96e7-44244755f1c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a54e6ef7&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fx5TIyIGt3UXZjYh1mhY5%252F4Delete%2520Option%2520Hide%2520for%2520Joining%2520Document2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11555ed3-c58d-4e5d-a9fa-42d02a126a4b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=565af793&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#payroll-dashboard-with-versatile-component-selection)

Payroll Dashboard with Versatile Component Selection

Now, when you're setting up your payroll dashboard, you have a broader selection of earning and deduction components at your disposal. This enhancement provides a comprehensive list that makes the dashboard creation process more flexible and reflects the organization's payroll data.

So, you can more accurately represent different aspects of compensation and deductions in your payroll dashboards. This simplifies and enhances your ability to manage and analyze payroll information effectively.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3DdWck68PzSiRdcjon1w%252F5Payroll%2520Components%2520Updated%2520in%2520Dashboard.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf5e0606-1464-421f-8a1f-2b8482f5d26f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4193ab3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#appraisal-bell-curve)

Appraisal – Bell Curve

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#bell-curve-normal-distribution)

Bell Curve – Normal Distribution

The Bell Curve Screen displays employee performance. It's a visual tool that displays their performance and potential ratings in a standard and default non-editable format. It helps illustrate how ratings are distributed in a workforce. In a typical bell curve shape most employees are in the average range, with fewer at the high and low extremes of performance and/or potential.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDOGNirDhYUeDNtSqhRKz%252FBell%2520Curve%2520%25E2%2580%2593%2520Normal%2520Distribution.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0b6a028-4d1d-49d1-8b26-5e37cbaa5c54&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f7fc2c4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#rating-normalization)

Rating Normalization

In simpler terms, the Rating Normalization feature allows you to adjust final ratings based on different filters like job categories, departments, locations, and grade percentages This customization ensures a more accurate representation of performance distribution within specific segments of your workforce.

The calibrated curve is visible only when predefined conditions are met which are essential to form a meaningful visual representation of how well employees are performing within selected segments. This feature enables you to make more informed decisions about talent management, promotions, and training.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/november-2023#graph-representation)

Graph Representation

Our HRMS software now provides three helpful views allowing HR professionals to easily visualize and compare employee performance.

*   The Expected Bell Curve View helps you see how performance is ideally distributed across your workforce.
    
*   The Actual Graph View provides a real-time display of current performance levels.
    
*   The Calibrated Curve View enables you to fine-tune and adjust performance expectations.
    

These views empower you to make informed decisions, identify areas for improvement, and recognize top performers. By having a clear visual representation of your workforce's performance, you can enhance talent management strategies, address skill gaps, and ensure a fair and calibrated evaluation process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWewvrTjJzBWud9wqOE4I%252FGraph%2520Representation1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32e74b56-af4f-402a-84e0-00e01cce9c4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5af93dc&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLRlFGawjIK5PHhHV7Hh0%252FGraph%2520Representation2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ac8ef34-bf7a-48ac-8175-b1f5ea979105&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84678c45&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2c5f595c5c435e586c5c434f474958445e415f024f4341)

# March 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbJS8BB9M1qKatTLO9bgn%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%286%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5cd11467-bdd4-4741-bbe4-b9df295b163f&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcddf070&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS has always been dedicated to providing our users with the best possible features and continuously improving the user experience. Aligning with our commitment to being the best in the company here we showcase some major and minor improvements in March 2023, to enhance the efficiency further.

Here is the key highlight of the features we are going to discuss in the blog,

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#id-1.-streamline-employee-confirmation)

1\. Streamline Employee Confirmation

With our new update, remarks and recommendations of ‘Manager 1’ will be visible to ‘Manager2’ about confirming employees or extending their probation period. That keeps the transparency for the level 2 manager and helps them to make an informed decision. It contributes to effective probation management ensuring that the company has the right employees for efficiency

For example, if an employee's performance needs improvement, 'Manager 2' can

extend the probation period based on the feedback from 'Manager 1,' ensuring that the right decisions are made for the company's growth.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0vyznZHf2VU6T0L0MYT3%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82cc1968-05e5-4201-b3ff-a0ca61dff859&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=374e963c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#id-2.-half-day-leave-tracker-effortless-half-day-tracking)

2\. Half-Day Leave Tracker / Effortless Half-Day Tracking

This update makes tracking partial-day leaves and attendance much easier! If an employee takes half a day off, we display '0.5' in the leave column. Similarly, the 'Physical Present' column shows '0.5' when they are present for the other half of the day. This simple update ensures accurate leave records and attendance tracking, ensuring employees use their entitled leave days effectively.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKJ1Ks29clSezwnmiEW3D%252F2.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab5d8d9e-7848-4e98-b105-0ca99ddbfc77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc9e2b9e&sv=2)

Muster’s report showcases a present-day 0.5 for his attendance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbfNU4B9Uh4fLddJ5FG5M%252F2.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7cd79e1f-75c5-46fb-91e8-79a33c18c295&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63985285&sv=2)

ESS employee portal showcases No. of days 0.5 for half-day leave.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#a3wu5gds28r2)

3\. Comprehensive Time Card Tracking

This feature helps you to easily download a detailed staff time card report. This report includes essential employee information like their Shift Time, Punch Time, Late By, and any additional Remarks about their shift including Absent and Present, making tracking and managing workforce attendance a breeze.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fafd2iPnkgA3CiapheVZ5%252F3.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e2e4340-eb2c-439c-8fcb-729acceb9bf7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdd194b4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FfWq7gXwvO23Sz0PaFGYc%252F3.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da641748d-ba13-4196-9a1f-5bd6d16c7bf1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b912fe5c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#id-4.-flexible-late-arrival-deductions)

4\. Flexible Late Arrival Deductions

HR can set rules specific to the different time ranges in the late arrivals. This means there can be different rules for the deductions for corresponding time ranges.

For example, if an employee is late by 15 minutes, half an hour will be deducted. If an employee is late by 30 minutes, one hour will be deducted from the total working hours. These rules can be seamlessly applied to payroll calculations, ensuring accurate deductions.

HR professionals can use this feature to enforce fair and consistent late arrival deductions. Setting specific rules helps in ensuring a level playing field and maintaining discipline in the workplace. By automatically applying the defined rules to latecomers, payroll calculations become precise, saving time and resources for the business.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0Ah38OtfiBoO5pIDmNP0%252Fmarch4.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38965105-7e4c-4aa9-8cf2-38555c9543f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ce30c5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIMPpuzW4pKrAZf6ESxvH%252F4.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dceb2f7ec-7843-424b-b9c5-3e44123974a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=185dd0b5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#id-5.-accessible-ratings-and-feedback)

5\. Accessible Ratings and Feedback

Using the Employee Self-Service (ESS) portal, employees can view detailed reports on the ratings they receive and download them, providing transparency and feedback at their fingertips.

Making ratings transparent and accessible to employees, makes it easier for employees to understand their strengths and areas for improvement.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAB2qCbpeLh5LjUWqJ2o0%252F5.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5026f5d4-f0f6-4749-8d72-bac7e2057596&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6251ab7f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqGLXLvLwhSdhAJzVkU83%252F5.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decccde65-525e-4379-bfd2-c5baef467b4b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eacd5c5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#hwd13lixlaja)

6\. Easy to Access HR/Admin Ratings

Now Admin/HR can easily download and review employee ratings given by them to employees from the Cloud Portal. This feature simplifies performance evaluation, making it convenient to track and assess employee performance.

By analyzing ratings given to employees over time HR can conduct data-driven performance reviews, enabling them to make informed decisions about training, promotions, and recognition programs.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPjHTESuLOdTymzCNyvTq%252F6.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D929d47ca-9d86-46da-923f-ccf2ea6055bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3185fd27&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#id-7.-simplified-filters-for-attendance-export)

7\. Simplified Filters for Attendance Export

Our new update allows HR/Admin to easily filter and generate monthly attendance reports. You can filter by various criteria like job title, department, location, bank name, and more. Once filtered, the reports can be exported effortlessly, simplifying attendance tracking for your team.

Filtered attendance data based on location or cost center, HR can identify areas with fluctuating attendance, enabling them to redistribute resources effectively. This ensures that all departments have adequate staffing levels, enhancing productivity and customer service.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAKnR3YWI11S0VR9Etg3z%252Fmarch7.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6ca3986-27c9-4c20-bd8c-d74a356e4e15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36df693d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/march-2023#id-8.-customizable-late-mark-indicator)

8\. Customizable Late Mark Indicator

Our latest update makes it easier to track late marks. Late times are shown in black, but if someone exceeds allowed late marks (configurable based on company rules), it's displayed in red. This customizable feature helps maintain workplace punctuality standards and makes it easier to grasp the late marks information.

The red colour indicator highlights violations, allowing HR to address attendance issues promptly. This maintains a professional work environment, setting a standard for employees and fostering a culture of accountability.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2g8OtdfipBPKRxrQAOFS%252F8.1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96e74e1f-9ff6-42bc-a4af-314ea65d8b6d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0018986&sv=2)
