# February 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgcBUDYd40hsvvMJK7RTG%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%288%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D004ad543-a4fe-465b-8946-114167ac8bfd&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c6f8a25&sv=2)

Introducing our latest enhancements designed to optimize your HR processes. HR professionals and Administrators can now effortlessly download candidate documents with a single click, streamlining the hiring process. Explore a range of job types, enhancing job role alignment with expertise and company needs.

Additionally, simplify interview scheduling by sending invitations to multiple recipients at once, saving valuable time for both recruiters and applicants. For the month of February, we have the following Updates that promise to enhance operational efficiency and streamline your recruitment efforts.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#automated-shift-assignments)

Automated Shift Assignments

Our latest update introduces the 'Auto Assign Shift Import Time' option, making shift management effortless for HR and Administrators. Now, you can easily set 'In' and 'Out' punch time ranges, automating the shift assignment process with just a few clicks.

Business owners can automate shift assignments, eliminating the need for manual adjustments. HR professionals can define precise shift timings, ensuring employees' schedules align seamlessly with business needs. This accuracy prevents scheduling conflicts and enhances overall workforce efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLizt7ZsLruu875IXqNM2%252F1.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3cd6e5e2-595b-4af7-bd30-41d827d21410&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87b65e1a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fm7Ta1VYjcaTQQ0bUXGxw%252F1.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22be924a-5a57-4f0e-a447-6cc1e218e79c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7566d3dd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#automated-shift-adjustments-for-single-punch)

Automated Shift Adjustments for Single Punch

With our intuitive Auto-Scheduler feature, Pocket HRMS simplifies shift management effortlessly. When an employee arrives within their designated shifts and makes a single punch, the system automatically synchronizes their time, reducing administrative workload.

For example, if an employee arrives somewhere in the middle of their assigned shift hours (for instance, 09 AM – 05:30 PM) and records a single IN/OUT punch, our system automatically updates the shift timing against the employee’s Time IN/OUT punch. This smart automation eliminates the need for manual adjustments, ensuring precise time tracking without the hassle.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FI8cuyvmnSLSq7QY8LGF5%252F2.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf9205f5-5138-4db4-92a2-86fec47f41fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85fe14b6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#multi-manager-approval-system)

Multi-Manager Approval System

The Auto-Scheduler feature simplifies leave approvals. Now, you can assign multiple managers at the same level, each with unique leave approval responsibilities. For instance, one manager can handle approvals, while others supervise the process, ensuring efficient leave management without complications.

This flexibility prevents bottlenecks and ensures that leave requests are processed promptly and employees experience faster responses to their requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6qgq1VVzVpRpke4CBwBR%252F3.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81b470d4-574a-4a2a-9d2b-91aebe351882&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3e971c3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXfyO7xVLF8kRhmtjHKAE%252F3.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83ae8d7c-0a8c-4d6f-a07d-a20d2fc59c69&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dc91571&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#managers-notes-in-travel-requests)

Manager's Notes in Travel Requests

Now, managers can leave comments while sending travel requests to employees via email.

That helps to maintain clear communication as managers can provide specific instructions through comments, ensuring everyone is on the same page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FT2tLexouLzX8pahrDSMQ%252F4.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55d31645-4d8f-453b-8f3e-70273ee32ac8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=535a2ca8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#quick-feedback-download-from-ess)

Quick Feedback Download from ESS

Now, employees can easily download ratings given by Admin/HR via the ESS Portal. This allows them to view their performance feedback conveniently.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FxNmK5INsuT5kzCxSEHKZ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66e3ca6e-74c6-425f-ad38-378174dfb406&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f6f0210&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#streamlined-attendance-regularization-reports)

Streamlined Attendance Regularization Reports

With our latest update, HR professionals and administrators can now easily download the Attendance Regularization Report making your HR tasks more efficient and hassle-free.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEwZ60rskIEovvxmwBl6K%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8da6d3b3-4ab2-4428-9ed3-c1fdf8ac0586&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20a9edcb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#state-wise-statutory-reports-made-simple)

State-wise Statutory Reports Made Simple

With our new update HR/Admins can access and manage report status on our Cloud Portal. The data is presented in a simple calendar format, making tracking important dates and updates effortlessly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwffrRm4o8exFyc9rtK9t%252F7.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85d2cf05-b89b-4ae9-b5f1-5515ea4ce9ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac7b330c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#compliance-tracker)

Compliance Tracker

Our new Compliance Dashboard simplifies reporting. Easily choose states and get a monthly summary of pending and submitted reports. Stay ahead with upcoming deadlines displayed prominently.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUfDuJCCE8htzfR6WfFtr%252F7.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6007609f-08d4-4d29-bc2f-616c9480d615&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3077528&sv=2)

It will provide in-depth details such as applicable Form no, frequency, upcoming deadline, etc. It has multiple filters (Month/Year) on the basis of which we can download the report and check the last downloaded report history.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoTAZ4Li7qSwARmFjrCpS%252F7.3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7222d17-3103-4bb7-bc06-e69ef4dc92c8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=418261f3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#automated-escalation-solutions)

Automated Escalation Solutions

The Administrator or HR can now define a reporting and escalation matrix without changing the reporting manager for an employee. The Reporting Matrix and Escalation Matrix has four options:

· Employee Code

· Reporting Manager

· ESS Role

· Department Head

The features of Escalation Matrix include:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#auto-approval-flow)

Auto Approval Flow:

Easily set multiple-level approval mechanisms in your company. The requests would be automatically approved after a set number of days, ensuring requests are managed efficiently, saving time and reducing manual errors.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#approval-with-escalation-workflow)

Approval with Escalation Workflow:

A powerful new feature that allows you to configure a detailed approval workflow with an escalation mechanism. Precise notifications ensure that no request is left unanswered to help improve employee engagement.

The system can automatically escalate pending approvals to higher authorities, guaranteeing timely responses. This not only improves efficiency but also enhances employee satisfaction by ensuring their requests are promptly addressed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEzxkv8OYFgeBwJp3DtnF%252F8.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def2668bb-1ba8-4c02-b1a2-5167a9e2042e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9c1a57f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#gkp3em9pyhpv)

Avoid Repeated Candidate Application

Since the PAN number is unique a candidate can not apply twice. When someone applies for a job, the system will validate their PAN number with pre-existing data and won’t allow repeated applications.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBBoVjeNMLPXd0xJhnr72%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De658c831-4c77-4b52-ab0c-98107dc5b76a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff4b77f0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#effortless-bulk-asset-management)

Effortless Bulk Asset Management

Now, HR professionals effortlessly map assets in bulk in one go, ensuring accurate tracking and minimizing the chances of loss. This simplifies inventory management, saving time and resources.

During employee onboarding, HR can quickly assign necessary assets to new hires in bulk. This ensures that employees have the tools they need from day one, enhancing their productivity and satisfaction.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FACpgg5QYj4Et2qJgD1xA%252F10.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1648e387-ac8b-4d26-9c80-9bdaec79f14d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=220a4bf0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#instant-candidate-report-access)

Instant Candidate Report Access

With our latest update, HR professionals and administrators can effortlessly download detailed candidate reports from Pocket HRMS. Access to detailed candidate data helps in evaluating qualifications, experience, and suitability for specific roles. This swift access to candidate reports streamlines the hiring process, allowing HR to acquire talent promptly and maintain a competitive edge in the market.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLZw6oCcmzWdE8Lf1NsGt%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def8bfa23-0d92-4266-b24b-ddd89523b0dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb414371&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#instant-candidate-document-retrieval)

Instant Candidate Document Retrieval

In our latest update, HR professionals and Administrators can now effortlessly download all candidate documents with just one click, streamlining your hiring process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1ce45MDVAwX8pZELfk0M%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e928027-3ee5-4cb2-9036-64f745015284&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c9a3bbe&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#diverse-job-type-options)

Diverse Job Type Options

Now, HR and Administrators can easily choose from various job types as we added multiple Job Types to make the hiring process more effective. This customization ensures job role alignment with the expertise, and company requirements enhancing overall productivity and job satisfaction.

By easily selecting from multiple job types, HR professionals can efficiently plan their workforce. They can identify skill gaps and optimize staffing levels to meet business demands effectively, leading to improved operational efficiency and cost savings.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQRPb87S71LAue0Gyw2QB%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D313c3cb9-5166-489e-9c8f-0c309f836dce&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92088309&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/february-2023#multi-recipient-interview-invitation)

Multi-Recipient Interview Invitation

With our latest update, recruiters can now effortlessly schedule interviews by sending emails to multiple recipients at once.

HR professionals can send interview invitations to multiple candidates, hiring managers, and team members simultaneously. This streamlines the scheduling process, saving valuable time for both recruiters and applicants and ensuring everyone is on the same page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFtkqVv25rvdNnMBkJjJw%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a5f15ad-5570-44be-8218-b073d60711e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5257678c&sv=2)

# May-June 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPe1NcausvVebGESTTeLf%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1ff7a24-cf83-4413-8d8a-8d6b1ee02925&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db1363c9&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS understands that technology is all about giving the best possible experience and productivity to users. That drives us to constantly improve our software, so you get enhanced quality of work and increased productivity.

We take this opportunity to present you our latest and most significant updates for the month of June so you can benefit from them.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#simplifying-attendance-summary-with-colours)

Simplifying Attendance Summary with Colours

With this update, you will get a custom monthly attendance summary report in a more engaging format. Our user-friendly interface allows you to configure colours for different shifts, transforming complex data into a visually appealing view. Allowing you to grasp attendance patterns swiftly, promoting instant understanding without diving into intricate details.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHefCjYfSF6md1fn8sXwt%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfeee68a5-07d6-4c18-b164-3fa7e58c688e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=615fc48e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#graphical-shift-attendance-insights)

Graphical Shift Attendance Insights

This feature provides a clear and visual representation of shift attendance. You can easily compare actual punch counts with expected employee numbers for each shift, all presented in a graphical format.

This visual overview offers immediate insights into attendance patterns, enabling informed staffing decisions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7q8Y10eQt2JV50AKoE7M%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5877c9f7-cdcd-4fc5-8291-8610ce26b6af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8b54690&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#seamless-image-uploads-for-emails)

Seamless Image Uploads for Emails

You can upload photos, essential documents, and visual materials with just a few clicks, making communication more efficient. Along with ease of uploading this feature also makes HR communication more engaging.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhyMC7wwtRh2ViBfMsoQw%252F3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0bff53dc-db1a-4952-a6cd-350aac6acdb0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87351e0a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#hassle-free-merged-entries-for-on-duty-and-half-day)

Hassle-Free Merged Entries for On-Duty and Half-day

With this enhancement, employees can now request an on-duty when they work half day. The system will be showing only a punch entry until acceptance of the request. Once the request is accepted, a single entry will be shown which is a merged punch entry and on-duty entry. It simplifies the process by showing all the information in one entry after approval.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRWXKMIyheKo2WGxcedQC%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7af06407-0c1b-42b5-8605-57d0bb927f4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37076e45&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#smart-customization-for-comp-off-credit-eligibility)

Smart Customization for Comp Off Credit Eligibility.

This enhancement allows you to set rules for comp off eligibility based on predefined working hours. This means employees will only earn comp off credits when they complete the specific working hours. That ensures transparency and simplifies the comp off management process making it a hassle-free and efficient experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fo9WZvdqyCOcdg2ORG5lY%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd0f5c88-2833-4b7b-b039-493a2fe03294&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc9566c6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#optimized-leave-overview-for-strategic-leave-planning)

Optimized Leave Overview for Strategic Leave Planning

With our new tracker report you get a snapshot of crucial' leave data such as opening and closing leave balances along with numbers for leaves credited, used, and debited in a single report. This detailed tracker report helps you spot trends in leave utilization for smarter, more efficient workforce management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvYWtV9PLcyWj33ru91Ar%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6711b4a-f921-4718-a298-c226403267d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21032b2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#fast-track-stop-payment-entries)

Fast-Track Stop Payment Entries

The feature simplifies the process of adding stop payment entries in bulk. Instead of selecting employees one by one, you can now import these entries in bulk, saving a significant amount of time and energy. That helps you to reduce manual errors and also enhance data accuracy.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FE9TA5JTasaLCqpBZwkqy%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43cae392-8c58-49b3-ac22-e924271bbc90&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60b8ae27&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#empowering-managers-with-project-wise-timesheet)

Empowering Managers with Project-wise Timesheet

Now managers can download detailed reports that show how much time employees spend on specific projects after approvals. This means managers can see exactly how many hours are dedicated to each project.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjEmO0J28ORFM9R47Bnx6%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daddf8540-14a3-4d9f-8c5c-d8bb59b37b2f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b89a0740&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/may-june-2023#crystal-clear-attendance-details-with-raw-punch-data)

Crystal-Clear Attendance Details with Raw Punch Data

The feature allows managers to get detailed raw data for in-and-out punches by their team members. This functionality is accessible through My Team Reports and Employee Reports. Managers can use the detailed punch information to identify the pattern and optimize shift schedules.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQuw22FY34qfMrstLlOhW%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5cc6e0a2-7bd3-4dea-89d3-bcc60b7f614d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef31027&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLILWkbWG8ehZCaL1GRJC%252F10.2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8ad8c74-7d71-45f2-a1ec-fe82b0c3ca51&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28d3edbf&sv=2)

# August 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPhuaKBs5jzBWghLZgiYJ%252FPocket%2520%2520Updates%2520August%25202023.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd97b6c62-0696-4c30-a00c-f85e68a05e75&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11f2ddb4&sv=2)

We’re excited to introduce a powerful new update to Pocket HRMS that will greatly benefit our users. The introduction of these updates showcases our commitment to continually improving and refining Pocket HRMS for better user experience and productivity.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#enhancing-privacy-and-transparency-through-cc-and-bcc-fields)

Enhancing Privacy and Transparency through CC and BCC Fields

Now you can use CC (Carbon Copy) and BCC (Blind Carbon Copy) fields in HR letters. These fields allow additional recipients in an email improving communication by ensuring that the right people stay informed. It also increases efficiency allowing you to send a single email to multiple recipients saving time and effort.

CC helps to keep everyone in the loop, sharing information widely, or documenting who has been informed about a specific matter. It is a great tool to build accountability for being informed.

BCC offers an extra layer of privacy keeping recipients' email addresses and identities hidden from the other recipients. This is valuable when sending sensitive or confidential information. Recipients in the BCC field won’t receive replies from other recipients, reducing email clutter of unnecessary responses.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXMej8P1XLotwZxNeA1HN%252FAug1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D887693fc-b718-4915-94b5-95590e3e2663&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7dd6aee6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#simplified-break-shift-report)

Simplified Break Shift Report

The reports enable you to download the details for multiple IN-OUT punches. To maintain accuracy and consistency in tracking attendance, the Total Punch Count should be even. The system intelligently assigns the first punch as IN, the second punch as OUT, and so on, making it easy to interpret attendance records.

That increases comprehensiveness as it includes fields such as productive hours, permitted hours, additional hours and short hours. That results in simplified monitoring working hours. The report becomes especially important for companies where we break working shifts into small bunches of working hours such as in the hospitality industry.

**1\. Productive Hours**

The column makes it seamless to track and calculate the total working hours of each employee, providing a number for total working hours through various shifts.

**2\. Permitted Hours**

The value indicates the ideal working hours for the employees. That makes it easier to understand if employees are adhering to the assigned shift hours.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#id-3.-additional-hours)

**3\. Additional Hours**

This field helps show value for extra hours the employee worked, making it easier for you to identify and compensate for their effort.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#id-4.-short-hours)

4\. Short Hours

Detect differences between the permitted hours and actual productive hours. This can be crucial for addressing attendance issues and improving scheduling accuracy.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPVrraDdU1bBCtNWmV0Ha%252FAug2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07712643-1529-4033-be59-1fec2a1a527e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cec60af0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTEAOBw5y2qtH6iQ0md4Z%252FAug3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0eee4715-d68c-44b1-bfe4-439781ae7632&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b892e3e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#flexibility-in-leave-remark)

Flexibility in Leave Remark

In the leave configuration page, you make it mandatory or keep it optional for employees to mention ‘Leave Remarks’ to submit a leave request providing you better flexibility over the leave request process.

*   Mandatory Leave Remark
    

It promotes transparency in the leave request process and helps in making informed decisions regarding approval. It improves communication as managers can discuss any potential issues or concerns related to the leave request.

*   Optional Leave Remark
    

This simplifies the leave request process and makes it more user-friendly and less cumbersome for both employees and HR personnel. It also shows respect for employee privacy which can lead to a more positive work culture and higher job satisfaction.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrqPuHGgc0hoyWJ5LTOIe%252FAug4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a6950a2-cfaf-4974-9d55-3c58fe51b699&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eddc604&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#insightful-in-and-out-reports)

Insightful IN and OUT Reports

Now you can look into the IN and OUT details of employees with the Detailed Report and Status Report. The four new columns In Location, Out Location, Attendance, and Status enhance understanding and the status report makes it easier to take a glance.

The Detailed Report provides more comprehensive insights into attendance as it shows you data for columns In Location, and Out Location making it easier to monitor if the employee were at the location that they were expected to be.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#status-report)

Status Report

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQiB6YAENHr23teQyRxXu%252FAug5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D750a6b3e-8f73-4d51-9128-5e782c44f13a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f530c67&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#detailed-report)

Detailed Report

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbQQU3AC9KiJ0qHA6vkty%252FAug6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dddcc6fa7-fe38-4b68-a14f-1e0302a5fd5c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d20d43c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#detailed-report-1)

Detailed Report

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FF0qr1XzmpTCilOZKN48k%252FAug7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee4ce69b-abea-4212-a043-a358ac9cef8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1831f5e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fj3XrbHMMWBehUpqk1kIh%252FAug8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe36a752-703d-45ba-afdf-bc3c9d31b796&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f095849&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#detailed-attendance-report)

Detailed Attendance Report

Pocket HRMS upgraded all types of reports within the attendance report wizard with new insightful columns such as working hours, attendance and status.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#id-1.-working-hours)

1\. Working Hours

This column shows the cumulative duration of hours worked for each recorded attendance entry. The working hour column allows HR and management to track employee attendance more closely.

This can help identify trends such as late arrivals, early departures, or excessive absences, enabling proactive management interventions. It also makes it easy to identify overtime done by the employee.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#id-2.-status)

2\. Status

The “Status” column shows the attendance status marked as ‘Present’, ’Absent’ or the other relevant status accordingly. The “Status” column allows you to track employee attendance by quickly glancing at this column.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#id-3.-attendance)

3\. Attendance

The “Attendance” column showcases the attendance status in short abbreviations for each individual entry, for example; FH/Leave Type/Shift Name – FH/CL/GS. This gives you details on the shift they are working in or additional information such as if the employee is working outside the office.

Similarly, the attendance column also shows the type of leave the employee is taking with abbreviation which can help in workforce adjustment immediately.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FdgTW4oHbt7JHeriCdlhI%252FAug9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e2b9a1a-a7b7-459b-842b-f05133b76f61&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3841d293&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6eHFw8JzCJZtme3Mhs68%252FAug10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da31969aa-2365-4bc6-8c3a-177e692100ef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6c1b3e7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#over-time-can-be-claimed-as-comp-off)

Over Time can be Claimed as Comp Off

Now you can allow your employees to accumulate their overtime working hours on weekends to be claimed as compensatory time off or comp off. That way employees can get a comp off when they complete a set number of overtime hours.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOkf1OhujCYRngy7XrmQ9%252FAug11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1fd96c2-6ceb-4ff1-8ae5-5fe28f3c44e5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce698de4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLSuUSewpTuXzAq60vuHs%252FAug12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc71cc545-b8f2-4ed6-9ee4-9ca86d25c533&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5814c2a7&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7C0Wit6ygViH2AyD1tt2%252FAug13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3aa5207-1bc8-4a83-92ce-7264589eb3db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b52c486e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlySAuHieOVJ7GcQmrILo%252FAug14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e1c4e8f-8f6b-4501-8167-2a1bd407ad31&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c748412&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/august-2023#enhanced-control-over-leave-request)

Enhanced Control Over Leave Request

The Leave Lock Feature is a valuable addition to our leave management system that empowers administrators to enhance control over employee leave requests.

When the “Leave Lock” checkbox is enabled in the leave configuration settings, it introduces a set of restrictions and options that govern how employees can apply for leave within the defined leave cycle. This feature provides flexibility while ensuring compliance with organizational leave policies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FsENvGPwlr7pSWX8Isa8l%252FAug15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7dbffe72-15c0-4881-a375-270e6be10d6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3d2c33&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEn0SycDffR5LtN0xTS7N%252FAug16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72d16d21-0b9a-4b21-80e1-7d1180220187&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9b0677d&sv=2)

# Jan, Feb & Mar 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5qkjmJGaj8xFa4bN32OK%252FJan%252C%2520Feb%2520%2526%2520March%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65e5be9a-13ea-42d5-9f6e-71c211732fed&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=469d0be2&sv=2)

Guided by invaluable feedback from our esteemed clientele, we've focused on refining user interfaces and design elements, embodying our steadfast commitment to a 'user-first' approach. These developments showcase our dedication to enhancing every user's experience. For the month of March, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#revolutionary-interface-for-recruitment-management)

Revolutionary Interface for Recruitment Management

Our recruitment module has undergone a transformation, empowering users to take swift actions without navigating away from candidate profiles:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#candidate-list)

Candidate List

*   Candidate List: Easily manage and view all candidates in one place.
    
*   Schedule Interviews: Efficiently plan interviews, saving time for both recruiters and candidates and ensuring a smooth and timely hiring process.
    
*   Add Candidate Feedback: Enabling better decision-making and ensuring alignment among team members regarding potential hires.
    
*   Assign Interviewers: Seamlessly delegate interview responsibilities, distributing the workload among team members, and facilitating diverse perspectives in the evaluation process.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFlLacWLS1IorMMQLTwFR%252Fcandidate%2520List.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51da4db8-ab5f-497c-8ecf-fd8e0812e891&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70662c2d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#job-stage-visibility)

Job Stage Visibility

We now have enhanced Job Stage Visibility with a New Colour Palette. Visual cues through colour-coded job stages simplify tracking, allowing for efficient candidate management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHA5wQC0PCLqvW6nUvFPq%252FJob%2520Stage%2520Visibility.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34872c80-3d64-47b7-813f-bf61c0c4b28b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9873281&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#job-list)

Job List

*   View Number of Vacancies: Instantly assess hiring needs, ensuring timely recruitment to fill crucial positions.
    
*   Assigned Recruiters: Clearly assigned responsibilities streamline communication, avoiding confusion and enhancing efficiency in the hiring process.
    
*   Interview Panel Details: Transparency in panel composition ensures effective collaboration, leading to more informed hiring decisions.
    
*   Set Job Closure Date: Clear deadlines promote prompt decision-making, ensuring timely closure of job postings and efficient use of resources.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ftiz5GVsSWaaigSE6nVIC%252FJob%2520List.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4735ea26-5a71-4504-8f54-a227aae3f882&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6fb41e8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#personalize-news-section)

Personalize News Section

The Latest News section now supports Rich Text Formats (RTF). You can add text with the following parameters:

· Colours

· Fonts

· Hyperlinks

· Alignment

· Timestamp

& other features supported by RTF enhance your news viewing experience by creating visually engaging. This enhances user experience, making news more interactive and appealing for your team.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQTwJgymhVF1hryRpjUwF%252FPersonalize%2520News%2520Section.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96ea573e-40bc-487f-83b6-7b6f6122e0ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9f95189&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#attendance-snapshot-data-at-a-glance)

Attendance Snapshot: Data at a Glance

Experience enhanced visibility in the Attendance Dashboard with precise data on present and absent counts presented both numerically and as percentages. Gives you valuable insights at a glance enabling quick decisions with simpler representation of information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FeSR0rNyiNMuTSdYD4Uja%252FAttendance%2520Snapshot-Data%2520at%2520a%2520Glance.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc712b205-33f4-4741-ade2-bceb01415b48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=345082b8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#dynamic-ctc-calculator)

Dynamic CTC Calculator

In our recruitment module, configure formulas for job profiles and create diverse templates. Upon entering the CTC amount, the system provides a detailed breakdown of the employee’s salary, which can be conveniently shared with candidates via email.

Our recruitment module streamlines the hiring process by allowing you to create tailored job profiles and templates. It simplifies salary negotiations by instantly generating detailed salary breakdowns based on the entered CTC amount, making communication with candidates clear and efficient.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1AZwQDAg7r8I7DcKCZMp%252FDynamic%2520CTC%2520Calculator.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03b1e889-51f1-4ec5-888f-a33b2e8f77d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b444f138&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#fostering-transparency-with-employee-remarks)

Fostering Transparency with Employee Remarks

Encourage open communication by enabling employee remarks after the final Manager rating in the appraisal process. These comments foster transparency and understanding, visible to both Managers and Admins.

This feature promotes openness in appraisals by allowing employees to share feedback after their manager's assessment. It enhances transparency and understanding among employees, managers, and admins, fostering a collaborative work environment.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F64K5l38dKqA7GtiDvCgr%252FFostering%2520Transparency%2520with%2520Employee%2520Remarks.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D007ecae2-2c4d-4d36-b233-d7ffd43526bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3fa16340&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FddehQiqJ3A3v6h8vF3n7%252FFostering%2520Transparency%2520with%2520Employee%2520Remarks1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce03bbbd-b5ee-4f75-bb10-3b08128a4c91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dae77ea&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/jan-feb-and-mar-2022#efficient-payslip-management-with-emails)

Efficient Payslip Management with Emails

Now experience enhanced ease using the Payslip Email Log feature. Understand the status of sent payslips and seamlessly resend them in case of email failure with the 'Retry' button. Additionally, download logs for in-depth analysis using the 'Download' option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fgi8ZFs5TT90ZGI7x4Bqv%252FEfficient%2520Payslip%2520Management%2520with%2520Emails.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9dafa443-28f2-4929-8261-d49e60744001&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36cb8958&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0f7c7a7f7f607d7b4f7f606c646a7b677d627c216c6062)

# January 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fk5k9eUh0SxpE89Gaimoq%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7648400-7013-4828-ad06-3c6c20ea3610&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bd5b64&sv=2)

This document describes the release notes for major and minor enhancements released for Pocket HRMS in the month of January 2024.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#precision-in-travel-requests-with-unique-ids)

Precision in Travel Requests with Unique IDs

For each travel request the system will assign a unique 'Travel ID,' which acts as a digital signature to track its journey from initiation to approval. This ID ensures smooth monitoring, offering a clear reference point throughout the request process, ensuring precision and efficiency until formal approval.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRz1tVAQyAsCFhIKqAFQG%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19d2e1be&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#modify-expenses-securely)

Modify Expenses Securely

The expense eligibility feature lets users edit certain values in an expense record while keeping expense types fixed. Users can adjust numerical values like amounts or quantities for accuracy and customization, without altering predefined expense categories.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjzpM2YJWt7CPQHfa1uJO%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c407d88&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#instant-approval-self-service-permissions)

Instant Approval: Self-Service Permissions

Now we have a self-service permission option integrated into the manager/admin approval page. This provides managers and administrators greater convenience by allowing them to easily approve permission requests directly from the interface, simplifying the process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBSo04wGImoKYsyeh9Aml%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a016d91&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#simplify-log-in-toggle-your-password-visibility)

Simplify Log in: Toggle Your Password Visibility

The login screen now includes a 'Show/Hide Password' option for improved user experience. Users can toggle between revealing and hiding their password as they type it in, helping them ensure accuracy and reducing login errors.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FdCWJedgiXhdCECNOKPtq%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e22eb5a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjFpcTPKMesFNUtx5MLUS%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3fec274&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#delete-auto-approved-projects-entries-with-ease)

Delete Auto-Approved Projects Entries with Ease

We introduce a key administrative function for project management. Admin users can now directly delete auto-approved project entries from the admin panel. This enhancement offers improved control and flexibility in project administration by allowing efficient removal of auto-approved entries.

_**For example**__: An employee has no approval manager_

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgVGs0JpqBe1elAwZRP4O%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35b15161&sv=2)

_The Person with admin approval credits can delete these entries with ease._

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7ztGKvwJKNM39kk3EtDA%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=889abdf3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#streamlined-time-tracking-with-leave-integration)

Streamlined Time Tracking with Leave Integration

The Auto Time Sheet Project now incorporates Leave settings directly within the Project Menu. Approved leaves are seamlessly integrated into timesheet entries, while unconfigured leave settings are excluded. This integration simplifies reporting and tracking by aligning with the existing timesheet integration with leave.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyiORo6nsIl94MMw0fWSU%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6a71533&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9ZyZfelZnF4iMppCvTIg%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2a40ead&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#lop-deduction-in-sandwich-rule)

LOP Deduction in Sandwich Rule

The sandwich leave setting now includes LOP leave within the leave deduction options. You can select the LOP leaves with ease from the dropdown and improve leave management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkE6ClZo5pTLh0qsZEECq%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e29b26fb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#efficient-staff-scheduling-bulk-assignment)

Efficient Staff Scheduling: Bulk Assignment

Managers can efficiently assign shifts and week offs to employees using Bulk Import feature. Instead of manual entry, they can download a template for the selected date and make assignments as needed. The feature includes a grocery sheet listing configured shifts for easy selection.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5bERNYgC07S8EHoQAWI3%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c2a0573&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FdsXKpUnxVLXBl5Xd37aM%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b410d552&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#efficient-shift-management-across-companies)

Efficient Shift Management Across Companies

Roster Management's Cross-Company Integration allows managers to combine multiple companies, assigning shifts and days off to employees across different entities. It supports bulk import and seamlessly integrates with the shift schedule approval process for efficient approvals.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRaPdGM8q2QV88uuzbv4Z%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a13aeb6a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fzdqif0SW5adMzbduvXgF%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2798b7ef&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/january-2024#versatile-uploads-resumes-in-word-and-pdf-accepted)

Versatile Uploads: Resumes in Word & PDF Accepted

Now, in the hiring module, you can upload resumes in both MS Word along with PDF formats, providing more options for applicants and hiring personnel. This allows individuals to submit their resumes seamlessly in either format, making the recruitment process within the system more inclusive and versatile.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fc8TWF5LGPbFc0EeUYjCZ%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ea9691f&sv=2)

# June 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJ2vKbRlEdk2e4o53pvUm%252FJune%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D338ce1b6-d723-4b89-8126-42043013d391&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2112f902&sv=2)

At Pocket HRMS, our commitment to providing an unparalleled user experience drives us to continually enhance our technology. We are thrilled to introduce our latest updates, such as detailed split shift attendance reports, simplified account management, streamlined project approvals, and swift compensation processing, designed to empower both employees and HR teams with increased efficiency and performance. For the month of June, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/june-2022#enhanced-attendance-insights-for-split-shift)

Enhanced Attendance Insights for Split Shift

We understand the importance of detailed insights, which is why our new split shift attendance report format offers a comprehensive view. Now, you can download reports configured to display information such as Casual Leave (CL) in the first half and Presence (P) in the second half, providing a clear overview of your employees' attendance patterns for managers. It also makes it easier for employees to understand their attendance details.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKPAMeKVxKbRxTOQ5POXa%252FSplit%2520Shift%2520Attendance%2520Report.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e4c4f68-56b8-428e-a254-2470ad27897f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=69642fb4&sv=2)

Managing multiple accounts within sub-companies just became seamless. HR/Admin can now merge accounts, ensuring a consolidated view. Employees gain easy access to merged accounts directly from the ESS homepage, simplifying their experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FClTXi9n8CuVYkj3lyvbs%252FMerging%2520ESS%2520Accounts%2520with%2520Ease.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc6aa65c-ca1c-44d4-9382-48f1711b5b05&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66b90e3c&sv=2)

# August 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEWroDwjtuNzCQGluhes4%252FAugust%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43c8b0ff-0df4-483f-91a5-a86cb743e208&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94f3b25a&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of August, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#easily-manage-job-openings-with-job-tracker-report)

Easily Manage Job Openings with Job Tracker Report

Our new and improved Job Tracker Report offers a complete view of all job openings in one place. It includes key details like Job Code, Title, Location, Department, Salary Range, Experience Requirements, Recruiters, Interviewers, Hiring Managers, and Candidate Progress (from application to hiring). Plus, we've unified all recruitment trackers into one, making everything easier to access and manage. You can search for data on-screen or export it to Excel for in-depth analysis.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAYMkllsPcUmkBOASjaeQ%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef534334&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#effortlessly-track-employee-departures)

Effortlessly Track Employee Departures

The Exit Tracker helps HR create detailed reports on employee exits. It includes important details like employee code, resignation date, notice period, last working day, approval statuses, and HR remarks. This tool streamlines the exit process and approval tracking. You can easily search, filter, and export the data to Excel for further analysis.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fq0SNrwq8qqw5ni9eTUfm%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dbb6fc5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#automatic-question-migration-for-exit-interviews)

Automatic Question Migration for Exit Interviews

With the new 'Form Master' system, all existing exit interview questions will automatically move from the old 'Dynamic Form' to the new setup. If a Form Master doesn’t exist, the system will create one and transfer all questions and options without any extra effort. This update removes the need to manually recreate questions, saving time and reducing manual work.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAv3AqwTciA254xyBY22o%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6fa9dc7b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FF4siCBzHfBtUiHOFd7gU%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=468adfdd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#clear-workforce-insights-with-head-count-report)

Clear Workforce Insights with Head Count Report

We've added a Head Count Report that gives you a clear view of your workforce during a specific period. It shows key details like how many employees were added or left, changes in total headcount, and important rates like retention and attrition. You can also generate a list of all employees for more detailed analysis.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLysGEkK8LRulXWRbLKPq%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd2427a1&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAha3vCs8o5bPFt6tzX02%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=51594a0f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#customizable-job-offer-approval-flow)

Customizable Job Offer Approval Flow

We’ve created a flexible approval process for job offers. The system allows two options:

*   Serial Approval: Both the Job Offer Approval Manager and Department Head approve the offer one after the other.
    
*   Single Approval: Either the Job Offer Approval Manager or Department Head can approve the offer on their own.
    

With customizable approval settings, multiple managers or department heads can be included. Each approver can:

*   Approve the offer as is.
    
*   Reject the offer.
    
*   Modify details like the offer letter, salary, or validity before approving.
    

The final approver can send the offer directly to the candidate, without needing further input from the recruiter.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMqmSJm97MkhUbxHk4QLu%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=386ba5f0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEjZo0Ik9LaQm7V5uJyY9%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab111ca2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqvDbAoxUREC1KZgpiUoO%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d381c80c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVdw4c3cumXEqV7Kem0xO%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58c6f8cb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#select-all-for-faster-stop-payment-reports)

‘Select All’ for Faster Stop Payment Reports

You can now choose all stop payment types at once when downloading reports. Previously, you had to select each type individually. This new option saves time by letting you include all stop payment types in a single report.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIPXlhu7EW8xn3mMJmWFO%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd12bfe9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#compact-pending-joining-document-report)

Compact Pending Joining Document Report

We've updated the Pending Joining Document Report to show all document details in a single row. Now, each document's name appears in the heading, with its status (Received or Not Received) listed below. Previously, each document was displayed across multiple rows, but the new format makes it easier to view all details at once.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJBDNu8qcA4aSnsRbDvhh%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94562c58&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#flexible-date-range-selection-week-for-off)

Flexible Date Range Selection Week for Off

Now you can set custom week offs using the new date range option in the Week Off Setting screen. Instead of being limited to the default financial year, you can choose any start and end date to manage week offs more flexibly.

*   **Custom Date Range:** Define your own start and end dates for week offs.
    
*   **Enhanced Flexibility:** No need to set week offs for the entire financial year; adjust them for your preferred dates.
    
*   **Easier Management:** Save time by setting week offs only for the period you need.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIcY6YbA3kRHUPX0iinOP%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44c9d31d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#count-based-leave-debit-functionality)

Count-Based Leave Debit Functionality

Users can now debit leaves by simply entering the number of days instead of picking a date range. This makes leave management easier and more flexible.

*   **Count-Based Leave Debit:** Enter the number of days (e.g., 0.5, 1, 2), and the system automatically calculates the dates within the leave year.
    
*   **Automatic Date Adjustment:** The system selects the start and end dates based on the number of days entered.
    
*   **Simplified Interface:** No need to manually select a date range for standard leave deductions.
    
*   **Complex Adjustments:** For advanced options like Fractional or Split Hours, use the 'Import Debit' tool for precise entries.
    
*   **User Guidance:** Hover over the 'i' icon for detailed leave debit instructions.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3XHHIMaMf2oQ01eqdtS7%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ec16c55&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8qGfurLDYuLaLJ6jI8hy%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bff5d22&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#flexible-header-footer-options-for-recruitment-pdfs)

Flexible Header/Footer Options for Recruitment PDFs

We’ve introduced a new Header/Footer feature for Recruitment Email and CTC Templates, allowing users to choose how to display headers and footers in generated PDFs:

*   **No Header/Footer**: PDFs will be created without any headers or footers.
    
*   **System-Generated Header/Footer**: Automatically includes a header with the company logo and name, and a footer with the company name and address.
    
*   **Custom Header/Footer**: Users can upload their own header and footer images to be included in the PDFs.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvLq08KCySe8WYm0uqvTR%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6443e0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#auto-20-tax-for-unlinked-pan-with-aadhar)

Auto 20% Tax for Unlinked PAN with Aadhar

The system allows user deduction of 20% tax if an employee's PAN is not linked with Aadhar. Admin/HR can define in employee’s profile whether the PAN is linked with Aadhar or not and taxes will be calculated based on this during payroll processing.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F47Ldg7ATXy9bL3svtgyl%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f0daf5e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FmH3wlDFTCuYoLcGa9uep%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3337ec52&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#toc177340854)

The tax slabs and the standard deduction for the new regime has been updated as per the Union Budget 2024.

**Revised Tax Slabs (New Regime)**

**2023**

**2024**

**Tax Rate**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/august-2024#simplify-employee-tax-details-with-descriptions)

Simplify Employee Tax Details with Descriptions

HR/Admin can now add descriptions to Tax Sections, Sub Sections, and Income Heads. These descriptions appear as tooltips (on the 'i' button) on employees’ TDS Declaration and Proof pages, helping them understand the details.

Also, HR/Admin can choose which Sub Sections and Income Heads to show when an employee selects the New Regime by toggling the 'Include in New Regime' setting to ‘Yes’ or ‘No.’

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSEhEnqRxwLbfaA8TJo05%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10597117&sv=2)
