# June 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fy2aQMpjRGrNZrwoeqJRg%252FJune%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fd1eb50-6789-4b69-a054-6fd00c56ca66&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6532602f&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of June, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#clarity-with-data-segregation)

Clarity with Data Segregation

Pocket HRMS now offers you better flexibility while exporting reporting manager details from the Data Wizard. You can choose whether you want to keep the Manager’s name and Manager’s code in a single column or segregate these two in the separate columns.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRGwpztnRPVesUwBvFvad%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2072cb1c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#date-range-based-passwords-generation)

Date-Range Based Passwords Generation

Pocket HRMS allows you to generate passwords for new employees who joined in a particular date range. You also get an option to overwrite the existing password for comprehensive coverage. Make it easier to generate password for new employee with a well-organized system.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlrNYxAZ19SeOfgyfzyWt%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4b46ec7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#multiple-smtps-for-birthday-e-mails)

Multiple SMTPs for Birthday E-mails

Now, you can create and manage multiple SMTP configurations for birthday email templates. You can now define several SMTP settings with unique server details and authentication credentials. The required the SMTP setting option can be selected from the ‘Sender's Email’ field during template creation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRj0GGK92QymQsF6MZzJX%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=150a4d6b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTHVDrWHDacdl0BivCudC%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59d034ef&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#effortless-exit-form-and-enhanced-flexibility)

Effortless Exit Form & Enhanced Flexibility

Now, exit forms can be generated directly from the general form creation page by simply selecting the ‘Exit Management’ option. Pocket HRMS provides you the flexibility to add multiple questions and customize those to gather relevant feedback making it more convenient.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhUktcsRlIct1gcqqjbRS%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b13333ab&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#optimized-employee-separation)

Optimized Employee Separation

Pocket HRMS will block the separation if the employee has any pending requests for

Leaves, On-Duty, Regularizations, Expenses, Reimbursements, or Loans. The system will display the 10 most recent pending requests in each category and also provide you with an option to download an Excel report. That makes the process of reviewing pending requests and taking the necessary steps to proceed with the separation, quick and effortless.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCA24qWdLl3M5XYa1fYDs%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fd13126&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6fNetcO7OaKxUyTy68Md%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4671ce94&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fd0JMcRjGb4Ovqt6pjOHF%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eb533a2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#inclusive-marital-status-options)

Inclusive Marital Status Options

We've updated the marital status field to offer employees more choices that better reflect their situations. This change provides greater flexibility and inclusivity, allowing employees to accurately represent their status.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FaZwNn6ZML7JmEcO6B97F%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=721ae355&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#recruitment-templates-with-candidate-info)

Recruitment Templates with Candidate Info

We have enhanced our recruitment templates with master fields so you can get essential candidate information with ease. This includes job code, job position, job cost centre, Aadhar number, PAN (Permanent Account Number) long with the ‘additional information’ fields allowing to add other relevant details.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQnVBqECZTaOvhnN4UX6T%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d4879ed&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#hassle-free-document-uploads)

Hassle-Free Document Uploads

Now we enhanced the user-experience for the bulk employee document upload page contains a dedicated drop zone for easy uploads. If files don’t meet criteria the system will show an error and the files won't be uploaded so you can make the necessary corrections.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fi7zschEBGpM3sfpkyZ4L%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=320780a1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#hlk170910702)

Adjust the Last Working Day with Ease

If an employee's Last Working Day (LWD) falls on a weekend or holiday, use the 'Last Working Day Adjustment' setting to shift the LWD based on the following options:

• Move to Next Working Day

• Move to Previous Working Day

• Stay on Holiday/Weekend

This feature allows better alignment with company policies and simplifies exit formalities for employees.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FsDbsOqIhmTyUrPrDtViE%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=509a2999&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC6qxJw7aa7tnafZXKUKt%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d9dccff&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#effortless-shift-assignment-on-week-offs)

Effortless Shift Assignment on Week-Offs

The Pocket HRMS roster management screen enables you to assign shifts on week-offs without replacing the week-off. This ensures accurate calculation of compensatory offs.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F17jMSGO4XebjUet2U4Wz%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=600f235e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#show-only-relevant-leave-option)

Show Only Relevant Leave Option

Pocket HRMS now allows you to make your employee’s leave application experience clutter-free. You can choose to show gender-specific leave options only to the relevant users. For example, you can choose to show the ‘Maternity Leave’ option to only ‘Female’ users and the male users won’t see options that isn’t applicable to them.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7lsJpx2aBb9BUctEQL2w%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0a108db&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#flexible-attendance-summary-display)

Flexible Attendance Summary Display

You can customize how to show the ‘Annual Attendance Summary’ to employees offering greater flexibility and makes it easier to grasp the information. You can now choose from three options:

*   **Default View**: Shows summaries from the 1st to the 31st of each month.
    
*   **Leave Calendar View**: Reflect summaries based on leave calendar settings, like from the 26th to the 25th of the next month.
    
*   **Month Days View**: Shows the summary based on the number of days in the month. This setting is category-specific, so the view on the employee screen will reflect the appropriate category.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FpQSRDIJcp7OS4WcTL6if%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fc16335&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#effortless-grace-time-adjustments)

Effortless Grace Time Adjustments

We have enhanced time-based leave deductions with an option for additional flexibility.

*   **Set grace time bypass limit**\- Allows users to specify how many times employees can bypass the limit without getting penalized.
    
*   **Review grace time settings** - The link quickly redirects you to the ‘Late Setting’ screen where you can manage grace time configurations.
    
*   **Allow grace time bypass** - Selecting this checkbox allows to apply grace time bypass limit for the individual custom Range.
    
*   **Consider Half Day Deduction if Less than Grace Time** – If deduction ‘Full Day’ is selected for any range. Selecting this checkbox allows the system to deduct the ‘Half Day’ if the employee has arrived in the grace time but did not cross the grace time bypass limit.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnpBc88vlfo8KewJoQ0qV%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=698b1048&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#bulk-peer-uploads-transform-appraisal-process)

Bulk Peer Uploads Transform Appraisal Process

Pocket HRMS now saves you a lot of time in the appraisal process with a bulk upload feature. Now, users can upload multiple peers at once, making the appraisal process much smoother.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fx8rTufjLU0pUET94EhFg%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=564f0be&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#precise-break-shift-reports-defined-in-out-flags)

Precise Break-Shift Reports: Defined In/Out Flags

Now, the user can download the break-shift reports based on specific In/Out flags. You can choose whether the alternate punches should be classified as In and Out in the report or to generate the report according to defined In/Out flags, ensuring to reflect accuracy in punch received.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FifeRXjs15ecuCmElR8X6%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=69b07d7b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/june-2024#boosted-appraisal-flexibility-quick-data-transfer)

Boosted Appraisal Flexibility: Quick Data Transfer

Experience improved flexibility and efficiency in the appraisal process through a quick transfer of all configured data. This includes stages, parameters, questions, and the approval matrix for the new year, ensuring greater efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKp0bbtEDWkjTG5kPHPpW%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be0a335f&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3744424747584543774758545c52435f455a441954585a)

[PreviousJuly 2024chevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/july-2024)
[NextMay 2024chevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/may-2024)

# November 2025 | Pocket HRMS

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of November 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-1.-out-time-based-leave-deduction)

1\. Out-Time based Leave Deduction

A new enhancement allows leave deduction based on the employee’s Out-Time range for each shift. This is configured through the Go Rule Engine, where different deduction rules can be set per shift.

Based on the defined Out-Time windows, the system will auto-apply Full-Day or Half-Day Leave. If the employee has already used their permission limit, the deduction will move to Half-Day as configured. Out-Times beyond shift end will not trigger any deduction.

This provides shift-wise flexibility and accurate attendance handling.

**Example – Morning Shift (09:00 to 17:30):**

Out Time Range

System Action

09:00 AM – 12:59 PM

Full-Day Leave Deducted

13:00 PM – 17:29 PM

Half-Day Leave Deducted

After 17:30 PM

No Deduction

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-2.-priority-based-leave-application)

2\. Priority-based Leave Application

A new Leave Consideration Matrix decides the order in which employees can apply for leave. Based on the priority configured in the Go Rule Engine, the system will automatically allow only the highest-priority leave type with available balance. Lower-priority leave types will be disabled and shown in grey. Leave types not covered in the matrix will continue to work as usual.

Current validations like “Leave limit exceeded” and non-priority confirmation pop-ups remain the same. This enhancement ensures policy-based leave usage and a smoother experience on both ESS and Mobile App.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FQOeAta0IGJKBM8TxUjbt%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c7634dc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-3.-allowance-via-go-rule-engine)

3\. Allowance via Go Rule Engine

The Allowance feature now supports client-specific rules through the Go Rule Engine. Clients can share their allowance policies, and the Pocket HRMS team will configure the rules accordingly.

Below are examples of how different allowance types can be set up:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FHkimkE8a3nYiX4xTkRrS%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4e42321&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-4.-punctuality-pay-via-go-rule-configuration)

4\. Punctuality Pay via Go Rule configuration

A new Punctuality Pay feature allows companies to give monthly incentives for regular and on-time attendance. The Pocket HRMS team will configure it through the Go Rule Engine based on the client’s policy. The system checks punctuality for the full L&A cycle, allows limited grace time and permissions, and stops the pay-out if any leave, deduction, on-duty entry, or early exit occurs.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fn6WSLTG1W0YPVDFwtDBk%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=759dd59c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-5.-pms-ui-enhancements)

5\. PMS UI Enhancements

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#a-improved-employee-search)

a) Improved Employee Search

Employee Search has been improved across all PMS screens to correctly detect and match Employee Code and Name, similar to the updated behaviour in the Weekly Off screen under Leave Settings.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FGBOlu3BLALYAu5HbRSih%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9575ad69&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#b-parameter-refresh-enhancement)

b) Parameter Refresh Enhancement

Earlier, the screen refreshed after every add or edit, which interrupted the process. Now the screen refreshes if you search for different employees, allowing users to add or edit multiple parameters without reloads.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#c-parameter-and-question-progress)

c) Parameter & Question Progress

A new Stage-wise and Employee-wise Progress widget has been added to show:

*   Employees **Not Yet Started**
    
*   Employees **Partially Completed**
    
*   Employees **Fully Completed**
    

The widget lets users jump directly between Questions and Parameters and shows how many employees still have pending parameters, helping HR track and close appraisals faster.

**Parameter-wise widget:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fih96MlmUtQp506uLyAQc%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=426b74ca&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FUTEEPEwvyxQRjCw3SqIf%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc64a145&sv=2)

**Question-wise widget:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FArQM2MKG1aximhV78dNu%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5bc09f8e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FoyGSjF0ix4xjtBfSVFgh%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=695ff7b9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#d-consolidated-appraisal-import)

d) Consolidated Appraisal Import

All appraisal import options are now combined under one menu called \*\*“Appraisal Import.”\*\*Users can select the required template from a dropdown instead of using multiple separate import menus.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FkO20CVnEBiF6ErhrX2YJ%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=decaaf41&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#e-re-grouping-approval-menu)

e) Re-Grouping Approval Menu

Earlier, all approval options were shown under the Request section in ESS. Now, based on the user’s role (Manager/Admin), the related appraisal approval options appear under the Approval section, making navigation cleaner and more organised.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F2zxqEtAYI0Cl3rmdF6eC%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d202cc8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#f-new-ess-status-labels)

f) New ESS Status Labels

The ESS action button now changes based on the appraisal status:• For **Up for review**, it shows **Add rating**• For **Yet to be submitted**, it shows **View details**

This gives clearer next steps for the manager.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FfuSJEVFcdPUVLd6TuoO5%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4a7df49&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-6.-auto-pms-driven-increment-percent)

6\. Auto PMS Driven Increment percent

The increment percentage is auto-calculated from the Go Rule Engine based on Final Score, Department, or Business Unit. The Admin starts the cycle, the Manager reviews and confirms the percentage, and final approval stays with the Admin. If re-submitted, the Admin can revise the percentage and resend the flow.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F94qyTrixWePJDTWq1WC9%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ca26988&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FY3dT7VTUseixTbpKHsIi%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f92e49fb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FFzwLyulroBAh01NS0bpq%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36ef23d4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-7.-fnf-all-departments-acceptance-notification)

7\. FnF – All Departments Acceptance Notification

A new event has been added in Exit Notification Settings. The system will now send an email once FnF No Dues is approved by all Department Heads, making it easier for HR to proceed with final clearance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqZw3xFOKYKcytOPWjlfL%252F7%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4895a87c-5e8e-4ed5-a434-14f1068c2167&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6605cb9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-8.-custom-fields-in-emails-templates)

8\. Custom Fields in Emails Templates

HR can now add custom Job and Candidate fields in recruitment email templates. Two new placeholder sections let HR drag and drop these custom fields into email templates and attachments.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FCKraHtS42dCnku6zZma3%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd890c2c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/november-2025#id-9.-corrective-increment)

9\. Corrective Increment

Three new automation fields—Increment %, Increment, and Correction—have been added along with a Recalculate button for instant percentage-based calculation. The system now applies the percentage to eligible components, updates new values, and auto-splits the difference between Increment and Correction.

This replaces the earlier manual updates and ensures accurate and consistent salary revisions. HR now gets a clear post-save view and an updated Increment Register with Increment and Adjustment Summary, making the process faster, error-free, and easier to control.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXAbbJAOrso3UbxNx15FC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc0869fb-7147-4be4-aa4a-3894115b29d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c307c91f&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b8cbcdc8c8d7caccf8c8d7dbd3ddccd0cad5cb96dbd7d5)

# July 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPXxt0paKnh3FuVIdo9hI%252FJuly%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2bf977c6-f86b-40cc-b41d-3990aa87def2&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11b646de&sv=2)

Embrace effortless HR management with our latest enhancements to the HRMS software. From a comprehensive Employee Timeline to an intuitive Experience Field and Manager Overtime Updates, these features redefine efficiency. Dive into a world of streamlined processes, ensuring precise tracking, informed decisions, and enhanced collaboration for your team. For the month of July, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/july-2022#career-milestone-overview)

Career Milestone Overview

Our latest update brings you the Employee Timeline feature, providing Administrators and HR professionals with a comprehensive view of an employee's journey. From the date of joining and confirmation to increments, designation updates, and department changes, this feature offers a holistic understanding of an employee's career progression. It enables better decision-making by offering insights into the historical context of an employee's role within the organization.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMoMBgPVPMGlVBWuBZbxP%252FCareer%2520Milestone%2520Overview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D869b8db2-70e0-4b9e-b098-666d1717ed54&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cef5db9c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/july-2022#employee-expertise-peek)

Employee Expertise Peek

Incorporating user feedback, we’ve enhanced the Experience Field on the employee card. Now, by hovering over the information icon 'i' next to the 'Total Experience' field, users can instantly access a pop-up displaying the employee's previous work experience. Understanding backgrounds helps in the delegation of tasks for the managers.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F33JFRHUmD5KIXLvcvQKj%252FEmployee%2520Expertise%2520Peek.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0478dd94-b67e-4f5d-8858-73ebbb909f20&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9faf14e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/july-2022#effortless-overtime-adjustments)

Effortless Overtime Adjustments

We understand the need for flexibility in managing work hours. With our latest update, managers can now manually update employee overtime hours. This feature allows managers to tailor overtime records to reflect the actual work done, ensuring accurate compensation and work-hour tracking. It’s designed to simplify HR processes, providing managers with the tools they need to efficiently oversee their team's workload.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSjm9qNNqsEdeeENh03ix%252FEffortless%2520Overtime%2520Adjustments.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34184715-940d-4197-b3d6-ceffcca3f2d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4fae096&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSkKbn7KQFmazqLrZFpUv%252FEffortless%2520Overtime%2520Adjustments%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c03bd78-a4ea-4d04-bc3f-b9d253b2be2a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d7a4d15&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/july-2022#focused-appraisal-access)

Focused Appraisal Access

Ensuring data confidentiality, we’ve introduced the 'View Only' access rights for specific managers regarding employee appraisals. This feature maintains data integrity while allowing managers to assess their team's performance comprehensively. It’s a natural progression toward more streamlined appraisal processes, promoting a collaborative work environment.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FpylQaunjsZ9dbaiV8Z9S%252FFocused%2520Appraisal%2520Access.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6ea991c-5cae-4e62-82f4-4dc47ecf2481&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5048acd0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4q7GzG66EUTSi8WjBwhv%252FFocused%2520Appraisal%2520Access%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3008b38a-3aca-4a6b-9807-b8d6cbb54d0f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1cf7d87b&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#65161015150a171125150a060e00110d1708164b060a08)

# April-May 2022 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKMMuARxokfIMS9Gj3E60%252FApril-May%25202022.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5d14f22-2f19-412f-9df7-1b1a327d158c&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2501c662&sv=2)

At Pocket HRMS, our dedication to enhancing user experiences remains unwavering. In our continuous pursuit of excellence, we are thrilled to announce a series of exciting enhancements. Our latest upgrades redefine HR management. The upgrades are intended to personalize and simplify use experience. For the months of April & May, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#personalized-log-in-screens)

Personalized Log in Screens

Personalization meets professionalism with our latest feature. Admins can now add up to four images and a group company logo to the ESS Portal Login screen, creating a tailored and branded experience for every user.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1R7RaqoZKag7idOgchJd%252FPersonalized%2520Login%2520Screens.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81993dc3-ffda-4f32-a1fc-ae266786be74&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8407408&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWKQ5QjKg8TrinU0m7san%252Fpersonalized%2520Login%2520screens1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d235c4d-7daf-474f-b98e-2085e9d3c71e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e24c54ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#unified-approval-system)

Unified Approval System

Managing approvals across multiple companies has never been simpler. Admins can configure approval matrices for employees based on cross-company criteria. For example, suppose, Sam is an employee and Rakesh is a manager in XYZ Company. There is another employee Rajesh who is a manager at ABC Company. With Pocket HRMS, Sam’s approval matrix can be set as Approver 1 (Rakesh) and Approver 2 (Rajesh).

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnTyI5iq8GKH8CBB6nabC%252FCross%2520Company%2520wise%2520Manager%2520Setting.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff7fd109-83f4-4586-87c5-e8cb4289f99f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=440232ce&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#understanding-monthly-variance)

Understanding Monthly Variance

Understanding your data is key to informed decision-making. Now, admins can effortlessly download variance reports for consecutive months using Pocket HRMS, enabling in-depth analysis and strategic planning.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FygTSHINJPPvMZ5CS68ew%252FUnderstanding%2520Monthly%2520Variance.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd62dc5fc-be94-464e-9f0b-cc43400d35b6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8605513&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#streamlined-appraisals-deleting-hassle-free)

Streamlined Appraisals: Deleting Hassle-Free

Our appraisal module has been enhanced for comprehensive performance evaluation. Admins can now delete various types of appraisals, including those with KPIs and stage-wise appraisals. Additionally, the introduction of Appraisal Peer Ratings allows for a nuanced evaluation process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKWV5vNGWHdXNHR27eLSn%252FStreamlined%2520Appraisals-Deleting%2520Hassle-Free.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1560037-94e0-4ea1-9f3c-8898e6720b9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f323b8d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#peer-contributions-for-appraisals)

Peer Contributions for Appraisals

The admin can create new users for the sole purpose of Appraisal Peer ratings for the employees. The new user will only have access to the appraisal module. The admin can define various parameters, questions and assign managers as well for the appraisal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEgrdk4LM6TIWu1pktVGm%252FPeer%2520Contributions%2520for%2520Appraisals.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b38952d-58de-4326-b32f-354c8f33c631&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5e06f4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#quantifiable-objectives-kpis-as-integers)

Quantifiable Objectives: KPIs as Integers

Precision is paramount. Users can define KPI fields with numerical values, ensuring accurate assessment based on predefined KRA marks in the Appraisal Parameters. This feature maintains clarity and consistency in performance evaluations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbD5ztxvxk9uDuMlqAiSh%252FQuantifiable%2520Objectives-KPIs%2520as%2520Integers.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded8fab0f-391f-4917-a472-2a551ebfdcca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd3e6c1e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYJXaXYDEY6RjMl84gl5I%252FQuantifiable%2520Objectives-KPIs%2520as%2520Integers1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5d7f2b6-001f-4d8e-ae0e-7e9f46278ce4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c42fdd8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#flexible-managers-attendance-control)

Flexible Managers' Attendance Control

Flexibility for managers and admins is at the heart of our updates. Managers can manually mark attendance and update overtime hours for their teams, streamlining the process for present and backdated dates. Admins, too, can efficiently manage attendance records with this functionality.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9CTPDYvW67BEDwUXi259%252FFlexible%2520Managers%27%2520Attendance%2520Control.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16b1524c-ec49-4a5b-94ce-da67b3f853ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c702d742&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2022/april-may-2022#transparent-claim-approval)

Transparent Claim Approval

Financial transactions are made effortless. Finance approvers can now enter the final claim amount to be disbursed to employees, accompanied by remarks. This transparent process ensures clarity for employees initiating requests, fostering trust and efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FuWy01NMEjPcnCzpeaX5K%252FTransparent%2520Claim%2520Approval.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2ae3c51-34c9-419c-be0f-b3b2e0102540&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63000eef&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fkw3yjyXAO3gBLo2RUS1I%252FTransparent%2520Claim%2520Approval1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db28f9435-3b90-432b-bd24-3bb1118338be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e56abe4a&sv=2)

# December 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjwbEPjPOyGTzA1iT4pz9%252FDecember%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d523a52-711b-45d8-a8a4-df7a81429cc2&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7c25314&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of December, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#flexibility-in-payroll-posting-calendar-or-date-range)

**Flexibility in Payroll Posting: Calendar or Date Range**

Now you can process payroll postings with greater flexibility. The payroll posting can now be processed using specific date ranges. Based on your setup, you can choose to post payroll data either calendar-wise or by selecting date-wise option with ease.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FN1ucRhhTRJxh4y15YOtp%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac8a38e9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#smart-shift-management-with-smooth-new-year-transfer)

Smart **Shift Management with Smooth New Year Transfer**

Assign shifts to multiple employees at once, and easily edit or delete assigned shifts. Now, the system will automatically transfer selected shifts to the next year based on your leave calendar. We have also added a filter to easily sort the data based on business unit, category, or shift name. Also, you can easily find employee using their name or employee. Making your shift management swift and well-organized.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFwmoNDEHAqwY6jmhbP8k%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d89d106e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIv0KapjENxXY1fajFzyE%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f986d7d6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#advanced-filters-in-admin-approval)

**Advanced Filters in** Admin Approval

The Admin Approval screen now features a new Filter button. You can click on it to open a pop-up where you can set filter conditions using various Employee Master fields like Bank Name, Blood Group, Branch, Department, and more.

The system allows you to combine multiple conditions and add additional criteria by clicking the "Insert Row" button. Once your conditions are set, you can save them or close the popup without saving them. You also get the flexibility to remove individual filter rows. This enhancement streamlines data management and helps you find information quickly and efficiently.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvFINyEeuuVrBLxqeI0sC%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4dde657&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMKZojJLGw3lbDkWzFvXK%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5b2c97a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#consistent-colour-coding-across-web-and-excel-reports)

**Consistent Colour Coding Across Web and Excel Reports**

Now the exported Annual Summary, Monthly Summary, My Report, My Teams Report, and Employee Reports visually retain the same colour-coding as the web interface. This gives you better consistency and ease of understanding the information.

Each attendance status has a unique colour:

**Absent (A)**: Red

**Present (P)**: Green

**Holiday (H)**: Pink/Light Red

**Other statuses** (e.g., On Duty, Week Off, Invalid Punch) retain their specific colours.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMBM8BG4VGSvAG3oC2Tna%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf03b043&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FObVjckcSWztx8KmGWwFW%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b269cc1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#flexibility-to-mark-incomplete-punches-as-on-duty)

**Flexibility to Mark Incomplete Punches as On-duty**

Our latest update lets you decide whether you want to allow employees to apply for "On Duty" even if their punch entries are incomplete or invalid. This makes it easier for employees to submit their on-duty requests if they work in multiple locations in the same day and enhances attendance management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBxtrQGhfeVHvb9RbrmQL%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab29b05e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#enhanced-search-tools-for-employee-data)

**Enhanced Search Tools for Employee Data**

Now in the ‘Employee Eligibility’ screen, you get filter options to easily search and sort records using predefined fields. We also provide the option to multi-select dropdowns for fields with multiple values. Along with that, a search field helps you to find results based on keywords. These features will not only reduce the time & effort but also elevate your user experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGdRh7MnzDfxlxM2bWXSy%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4cf4bba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#focus-on-what-matters-hide-empty-columns)

**Focus on What Matters: Hide Empty Columns**

Now you can simply tick a checkbox to hide the empty columns. The columns with new values will be removed from the screen as well as from the Excel report. This makes it easier to read and focus on the relevant information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6poHoVlApEmvx6aaoqt6%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0a8be11&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#set-up-future-holidays-ahead-of-time)

**Set Up Future Holidays Ahead of Time**

With our latest update you can set holiday dates for future calendar years, even if the leave calendar for those years is not active yet. These holidays for future years will stay inactive until the respective calendar year is activated. So, you can prepare in advance with ease without impacting the current year configurations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fbb3nsZEcd1wXGZKuMZZ7%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7238b7b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#automated-employee-code-generation-across-scenarios)

Automated Employee Code Generation Across Scenarios

Now, based on the selected business unit, the system will automatically generate employee code during importing multiple employees, adding new employees as well as during the candidate onboarding. This reduces the manual effort and adds convenience to employee management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FNocuwOGzljQAoL9OpUV4%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9590f55&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fmg12yY8mG5BFVgOMNNnr%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6a43a1d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3mFOYmsr11Dny0SNDzyF%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ca6dea0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FmFgNnKzWAMQbYKvjIFki%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d773b7e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FynLWLJ8TSQ3Ki8d1tsNY%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a2d42bb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbjMxe9Btgnh3r9B0dk9o%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db9de0b7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#identify-and-manage-duplicate-claims-instantly)

**Identify and Manage Duplicate Claims Instantly**

Now, the system will spot and flag duplicate expense entries based on the **expense type** and **expense amount**. System will notify employee about it and they can easily **edit** or **delete** duplicate entries directly from the pop-up notification. This improves efficiency in expense management and saves time.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6UfkAHac7nmW9C3ZunP2%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e710c70f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#quickly-choose-hr-letter-templates-with-a-dropdown)

**Quickly Choose HR Letter Templates with a Dropdown**

Now you can experience faster template creation by simply selecting the template tags from the dropdown. This reduces the effort to manually enter the template and improves efficiency by eliminating the possibility of error.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fngm1Uo9yCgFKOtcIIYjX%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e972d0af&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#manage-fnf-department-heads-faster-with-import-and-export)

**Manage FnF Department Heads Faster with Import & Export**

No more tagging the department heads one by one. Simply import department heads details and priorities at once using the Excel sheet in the FnF Department Head Manager. You can also generate an Excel sheet with a list of all department heads saved so far, reducing time and effort as well as bringing precision to the process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBOnOlZc0L5MIanc9UfcG%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f67cc2f1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#simplify-department-head-assignments-in-fnf-department-head-manager)

**Simplify Department Head Assignments** in FnF Department Head Manager

Now you get the flexibility to assign a single manager to all departments. This will save a lot of time during manual entry. You also get an option to replace the current manager with a new one, in the FnF Department Head Manager with a single click, making the process hustle free.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlxkN2auOje5vrW6NYzsL%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6ceec42&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#easily-notify-department-heads-for-exit-and-fnf-events)

**Easily Notify Department Heads for Exit and FnF Events**

Admin/HR can now send email notifications to Department Heads for Exit and FnF-related events, such as when an employee submits their separation request or when FnF forms are activated. You can easily choose the type of event, either 'Exit' or 'FnF', to specify which department heads should receive the email notification.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoGog3xl8ObADoAHjeHv4%252F14.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24b588ed-ec59-4495-8e2f-d8c54513cf21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c370aff&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/december-2024#custom-field-tracking-now-available-in-recruitment-module)

**Custom Field Tracking Now Available in Recruitment Module**

The trackers in the Recruitment module now capture data from all custom fields for both Candidates and Jobs. Previously, only default fields were tracked. This improvement will provide more detailed data analysis by capturing all relevant information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ft0QQVBFP9uVkymDRWaiY%252F15.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2f26a6d-35f0-4550-9a4f-94f9517ab079&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7251402f&sv=2)

# E Posh | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#e-posh-detail-guide)

E-Posh (Detail Guide)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.-what-is-e-posh)

1\. What is E-Posh

E-Posh refers to a **digital or online system** designed to help organizations comply with India’s Prevention of Sexual Harassment (Posh) Act, 2013 by managing all related processes electronically.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.1-how-to-set-up-e-posh-in-pocket-hrms)

1.1 How to Set-up E-Posh in Pocket HRMS?

To set E-posh in Pocket HRMS, please follow the path and process mentioned below:

**Path:** Cloud Login > ESS Setting > E-posh > Set-up > Fill In details > Save.

**Step 1:** Log in to the '**Cloud**' portal and go to '**ESS Setting**' menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FKBzbb45cXzQwphftQbRQ%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbb4623d&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select '**E-posh**' tab and click on '**Set-up**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FHZOvLD3rR7N4f9ltoedG%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b1e7167&sv=2)

**Step 3:** '**Fill In details**' Such as:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FcPQ3LlvExUpj1xtIaij0%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a58f39f5&sv=2)

*   **Chairperson/Presiding Officer**\- Fill the name of the chairperson you want to appoint for E-Posh Committee
    

(**Note-** According to Posh Act, the chairperson or residing Officer should be a Female. But you can assign the chairperson as male/female per your convenience in Pocket HRMS). System will however prompt you if a male employee is being appointed as a Chairperson.

*   **Committee Members**\- Fill the names of the committee members apart from the chairperson.
    

(**Note-** As per POSH committee, there should be more than 50percent female employees in the committee. But you can assign the members male/female per your convenience in Pocket HRMS). System will however prompt you if a more than 50% male employees are being appointed as Committee Members.

**Please note**\- There has to be one Chairperson and at least two committee members in the E-Posh Committee.

*   **Complaint Committee ID**\- It is the email ID in which complaints will be received. This email ID will be shown to the Employees on their E-Posh dashboard in addition to the Complaint Raising functionality. Employees can use this email ID to directly get in touch with the Committee. The Email notifications of all the events will also be received on this email ID.
    
*   **Complaint Auto Response**\- If you keep the complaint auto response button on or enabled, then an automatic message will be triggered to the employees who raise the complaints. It is to acknowledge the receipt of their complaints.
    
*   **Response Content-** It is the email content that is triggered automatically in response to the employees complaints when received. It is triggered when complaint auto response is kept on. You can edit/change the message by clicking on the ‘**Edit Icon’** on its right > **change the content > save it.**
    
    ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F9iSissQUhtObtXWCMHI4%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f32a601&sv=2)
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F5zTXZaX2T4SNnkaODOkw%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=374faca5&sv=2)

**Note-** In case you want to know in details about the Act against Sexual Harassment of Women at Workplace, Click on **‘Here’** on the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FrzXpjCtCnmlB9dCD1GFR%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfb19e07&sv=2)

**Step 4:** After filling up all details, click '**Save**'. The set-up will be done successfully.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FVCf2fEekRwJpb9fKAcLP%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b411a45&sv=2)

**Link:**[https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=EPOSH&submodule=eposhsettingsarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=EPOSH&submodule=eposhsettings)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.2-how-to-allocate-roles-to-employees-in-e-posh)

1.2 How to Allocate Roles to Employees in E-posh?

**Path:** Cloud Login > ESS Setting > Profile Info > Role Allocation > Select Module as E-Posh > Select Role > Search > Give Access.

**Step 1:** Log in to the '**Cloud**' portal and go to '**ESS Setting**' menu, Select '**Profile Info**' tab and then '**Role Allocation**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FIDviEGVGoYlMW24RN99f%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=533b1239&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FpA9DBB27EiZnBmb2S4Ve%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7def7a6a&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select '**Module**' as '**E-Posh**' from the drop-down, select the desired '**Role**' to which you want to give access and click on ‘**Search**’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F18YzXiusbkjnKLtIsaTx%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4e5ec20&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Enable '**Access**', by ticking the required fields.

There are 3 categories to give access to:

*   **Complaint List-** Access to complaint List is only given to the E-posh committee members and chairperson to check or track the progress of Complaints.
    
*   **Dashboard-** Access to dashboard is compulsory as employees will raise complaint from their dashboard.
    
*   **My Complaints-** Access to My complaints is compulsory as this will enable employees to view the status of their complaints.
    
    ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FFvDwgdypJM2Q1L0v9euv%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13fd23e9&sv=2)
    

Or

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FFVKtB1R3bn5mTNleKCPn%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a093118&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Then click on ‘**Save**’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FRlkgCAcRmoGtfIonywji%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2260ab3&sv=2)

**Link:**[https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=RoleAllocationarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=RoleAllocation)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.3-how-to-raise-a-complaint)

1.3 How to Raise a Complaint?

You can raise a complaint from your ESS portal for self or for any colleague of yours by following the path and process mentioned below:

**Path:** ESS portal login of self > E-posh > Dashboard > Dashboard Tab > Raise Voice > Fill In details (For Self or Co-worker) > Submit.

**Step 1:** Log in to the '**ESS**' portal of self, select '**E-posh**' and go to the '**Dashboard**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FKFt6jGfdVn27J7SQ1kNn%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfa4aa00&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Click on ‘\*\*Dashboard’\*\*tab and select '**Raise Voice**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FXFmV7hUt2JbzxctwbImA%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bbed46&sv=2)

**Step 3: Fill in Details:**

*   **For Self-** It means the harassment incident has occurred with you and for that you want to raise a complaint.
    

If you want to raise complaint for self, then fill the details such as:

*   **Hide my identity**\- Tick on it, if you don’t want your name to be reflected in complaint or leave it unticked, if you want your name to be reflected in the complaint.
    
*   **Offender(s)-** You can add one offender or multiple offenders name in this section
    
*   **Type of Incident**\- You can choose the type of incident from the list of incidents provided as per POSH Act. You can also check the details of types of incident by clicking on **‘i Icon’** in yellow beside it. Choose the type as per your need. You can also choose multiple types, in case your incident resembles with 2-3 types or all types mentioned in the option.
    
*   **Date & Time**\- mention the date and time when the incident has occurred with you.
    
*   **Evidence Upload**\- It is not a mandatory field, so you can either skip it or attach any proof or document to support your complaint.
    
*   **Incident Details**\- Here you can mention the details of incident occurred with you.
    
    ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FnaTN6SxtzwbQlLUI8iiJ%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f8d7146&sv=2)
    
*   **Co-Worker-** Choosing co-worker specifies that you are raising the complaint on behalf of other worker with whom an incident has occurred and they are reluctant to complain due to fear, stress or other issue.
    

In case you want to raise the complaint for a co-worker, fill in the details such as:

*   **Victim(s)-** Name of the victim or victims with whom harassment has occurred.
    
*   **Offender(s)-** You can add one offender or multiple offenders name in this section
    
*   **Type of Incident**\- You can choose the type of incident from the list of incidents provided as per POSH Act. You can also check the details of types of incident by clicking on **‘i Icon’** in yellow beside it. Choose the type as per your need. You can also choose multiple types, in case your incident resembles with 2-3 types or all types mentioned in the option.
    
*   **Date & Time**\- mention the date and time when the incident has occurred with you.
    
*   **Evidence Upload**\- It is not a mandatory field, so you can either skip it or attach any proof or document to support your complaint.
    
*   **Incident Details**\- Here you can mention the details of incident occurred with your co-worker.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FxdEd7RgYPZRmm0kdncrG%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8839f25&sv=2)

\*\*Step 4:**Click** ‘Submit’\*\*to raise the complaint.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FQphI73NZVDNSN6aP1twF%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec64d1be&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.4-how-to-track-my-complaints-or-the-complaints-raised)

1.4 How to Track My Complaints or the Complaints Raised?

**Path**: ESS portal login of self > E-Posh > My Complaints > My Complaints Tab >

**Step 1:** Log in to the '**ESS**' portal of self, select '**E-Posh**' menu and go to '**My Complaints**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FTtn70afLW8WLp2cD8R8r%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ffc01f&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Go to ‘**My Complaints’** tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FeGymmslePC8NAs2vCY2s%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=951a2d69&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Here you will view all the details of your complaints, and take actions such as sending reminder to the E posh Committee members. This page has the following elements:

*   You can view Open Tickets by clicking on open tickets, closed tickets or all tickets.
    
*   You can ‘Download’ the report by clicking on the ‘Report’ icon
    
*   You can also ‘Sort’ the complaints as per your requirement.
    
*   Details of Complaint No., incident type, incident date, status of complaint, raise by/for self, agent assigned and action button to send reminder, or close or mark resolved for any complaint, etc.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FlC511inN5pxWP7fWm2k5%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fede4ab6&sv=2)

Step 4: After Clicking the **‘Action’** button you will land in a page where you can add the following:

*   **Reply-** By clicking on it you can send a message the committee member regarding resolving the complaint, or as a reminder, etc.
    
*   **Status**\- You can change the status of complaint to ‘Open’, ‘Close’ or ‘Resolved’.
    
*   **Back**\- Click it to go back to the **‘My Complaints’** page.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FhGp6neDYzgMxLI54v2eA%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e60628fb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.5-how-can-the-committee-members-track-the-complains)

1.5 How Can the Committee Members Track the Complains?

**Path**: ESS portal Login of Committee Member/Presiding Officer> E-Posh > Complaint List

**Step 1:** Log in to the '**ESS**' portal as a '**Committee Member/Presiding Officer**', Select '**E-Posh**' menu and go to '**Complaint List**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FZPqhg4y6sgSiPhbnHDAy%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a0afc13&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Click on ‘**Complaint List’** Tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F7CKT45ZAKHmiJ9sLCuVh%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1cd62860&sv=2)

**Step 3:** In this page you can view the details of complaints received and you can also edit/change actions being a committee member or chairperson. It has the following elements:

*   You can view Open Tickets by clicking on open tickets, closed tickets or all tickets.
    
*   You can ‘Download’ the report by clicking on the ‘Report’ icon
    
*   You can also ‘Sort’ the complaints as per your requirement.
    
*   Details of Complaint No., incident type, incident date, status of complaint, raise by, agent assigned and action button to send reply to the concerned employee.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FMNJPQsdslAU6j6UHGAa2%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b48b48e4&sv=2)

**Step 4:** You can change the ‘Agent Assigned’ by clicking on it. It can only be done when ‘Agent’ has not been assigned to any particular complaint.

*   **In case You want to assign it to some other committee member**\- Click Assign to then click on Assign button of the selected member.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FYGvBDR3ON8VFeH4Gzqt7%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf9ca58c&sv=2)

*   **In Case you want to assign the case to self**\- Click on Self assign.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FOxCMRnPpJoGzYYMh6m9B%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5771a246&sv=2)

**Step 5:** In case you click the ‘Action Button’, you can do the following:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FGt7ngYIy6xYXnmJXnmpb%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4adef91f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/e-posh#id-1.6-what-is-complaint-timeline)

1.6 What is Complaint Timeline?

Complaint Timeline showcases the complaints based on 3 filter. You can filter the complaints by adding the Complaint ID, or agent name in activity by, or Events.

**Path:** ESS portal Login of Committee Member/Presiding Officer > E-Posh > Complaint List > Complaint Timeline > Filter as per your need > Search.

**Step 1:** Log in to the '**ESS**' portal as a '**Committee Member/Presiding Officer**', Select '**E-Posh**' and go to '**Complaint List**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FZPqhg4y6sgSiPhbnHDAy%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a0afc13&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select '**Complaint Timeline**'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FlisCE2LdSK8eG5PvX7IK%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=103a430e&sv=2)

**Step 4:** '**Filter as per your need**' and click '**Search**'.

*   Complaint ID- Here, you can put the complaint Id number and click on search to view the details of that particular complain.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FzCeOwiAzByniLQSDYBfo%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e87282e2&sv=2)

*   Activity By- Here, you can add the committee member name to view the details of the complaint.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FxkLN5dKsqMzy4iVLmEGs%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91e00c28&sv=2)

*   **Event-** Here, you can add the events from the drop-down which is either- ‘Created’, ‘Assigned’ or ‘Archived’ and click on ‘Search’.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FtYi39W5mkhKuXfk6i7Gj%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7cd10e&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6a191f1a1a05181e2a1a0509010f1e0218071944090507)
