# August 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4RzdntWnsdZFvTqo0azs%252FAugust%25202025.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debeb5446-3e76-43c9-888e-b0d991c34b47&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d701326&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of August 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/august-2025#yearly-cap-on-compensatory-off)

Yearly Cap on Compensatory Off

A new option has been added in Leave Configuration for Compensatory Off (Comp-Off). This lets admins set the maximum number of Comp-Off leaves an employee can take in a year.

*   A setting is available: “Maximum \[x\] leaves of this type are allowed in a year.”
    
*   Example: If the limit is 5, an employee can take up to 5 Comp-Off leaves in that financial year.
    
*   After the limit is reached, the system will block new requests and show a message: “Leave limit is exceeded. Allowed yearly limit is: 5.”
    
*   The check happens instantly when applying, so no extra requests can go through.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrPW9o0mba80ZZR0Tw5kc%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f36eec2&sv=2)

The system shows a message when a leave request goes over the 5-day limit.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FydqJEcDrR4qMV0BKOSZY%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a30aa44&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6PcxPDIoPwz1WJHtMO0y%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39c4b4f4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/august-2025#remarks-for-updated-punch-and-attendance-report)

Remarks for Updated Punch and Attendance Report

We have improved the Modified Punch feature by adding a Remarks field. Now, whenever an employee’s in/out punch is changed, the user can record a reason or note.

*   A Remarks field is shown when editing a punch.
    
*   The remarks are saved with the modified punch details.
    
*   These remarks also appear in the Attendance Summary Report.
    
*   Example: If a punch is changed with the note “Informed I’ll be late but completed working hours”, it will be shown in the Remarks column of the report.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQ098hbtJKKv7WbeILWbK%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c426b88&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDtlXB1srdb3mkHEJZqHx%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcf073f2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/august-2025#orientation-added-to-learning-certificate)

Orientation Added to Learning Certificate

A new option is available in Learning Program → Certification Details to set the certificate orientation.

*   Admins can choose Portrait or Landscape mode for certificates.
    
*   This helps match certificates with company branding and design needs.
    
*   When changing the orientation, the system shows a warning: “Warning: Watermark may shift with orientation. Check format before continuing.”
    
*   This ensures the watermark and layout are checked before finalizing.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ff3QEvUND5fUaRIUJ6kk2%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7da2167&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/august-2025#monthly-headcount-analysis)

Monthly Headcount Analysis

A new report called Monthly Headcount Trend Report has been added under the Headcount section. It shows male and female employee counts month by month.

*   Compare male vs. female headcount across months.
    
*   Filter by status:
    
    *   Active – current employees
        
    *   Inactive – employees who have left
        
    *   All – both active and inactive
        
    
*   The report generates three sheets:
    
    *   Active Data Sheet – detailed view of active employees
        
    *   Inactive Data Sheet – detailed view of inactive employees
        
    *   Overall Headcount Sheet – combined monthly headcount trends
        
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FybXqqsu9I5Zxycklae7v%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a66071f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/august-2025#currency-choice-in-ctc-fields)

Currency Choice in CTC Fields

We have added a currency selection option before entering Current and Expected CTC values.

**Display:**

*   Candidate Profile
    
*   Candidate Cards (Candidate List Page)
    

**Customization:**

*   By default, only INR is enabled.
    
*   Other currencies can be added on request through consultants.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTVn286riOTKu1bOyj5a1%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=279b6626&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FD6Of4fUqZkuq2LyZ2pPB%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ec0286&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEeG2Gccggolc3iLZABPZ%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7484af7&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ffdj2QHPzEQmcXl6GRl2L%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a6fdc62&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/august-2025#dynamic-states-in-candidate-creation)

Dynamic States in Candidate Creation

We have added a dynamic state list that updates automatically based on the selected country.

*   **Current coverage:** India, Australia, and Malaysia
    
*   **Customization:** Additional country–state mappings can be set up on request through consultants.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrViAOossug9Bx4SGDlBE%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2cc58b9&sv=2)

# Transfer Setting | Pocket HRMS

The transfer setting module lets you anytime transfer HR templates like location transfer letters easily. Employee code transfer, ESI location transfer, year-end transfer, etc. becomes easy with Pocket HRMS dashboard.

Stepwise transfer setting is as explained below.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr/transfer-management#pre-requisites)

Pre-requisites:

✔️ Admin credentials

✔️User rights

_**Note**_ _- Kindly contact your Admin/ HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr/transfer-management#how-to-go-with-transfer-management)

**How to go with transfer management?**

**Step 1:** Go to 'Settings'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDls_5XAcqBEqqcko5%252F-MYDmINOVGtTBxywZSU6%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0692aed9-1e0f-4d7f-b30c-ffcbbc25dc47&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fb53cb4&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Proceed to 'HR' column

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDls_5XAcqBEqqcko5%252F-MYDmObTA1ASggweb-LT%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1bed3c2d-c7b4-493a-b3e6-b526ac649f37&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31c7f93&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Transfer Setting' option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDls_5XAcqBEqqcko5%252F-MYDmSOJa1l4UOJqub4o%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dece08660-790e-4e0f-9f92-8c7ab879dc48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf0663c7&sv=2)

Now, a window (as above) appears. Here, fill in all the required details like setting name, transfer type, fields for transfer template, etc. After successfully filling all the details, click on 'Save'.

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to setup transfer setting, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#5f2c2a2f2f302d2b1f2f303c343a2b372d322c713c3032)

# Tax Calculator ESS Portal | Pocket HRMS

The Tax Calculator in the Employee Self-Service (ESS) portal helps employees easily compare the Old Tax Regime and the New Tax Regime to decide which one suits them better.

The tax calculator uses the latest salary processed and declarations to give a precise estimate of how much income tax an employee may have to pay in the financial year.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/tax-calculator-ess-portal#what-does-the-tax-calculator-do)

What does the tax calculator do?

*   Projects annual income based on your processed salary
    
*   Estimates total deductions (as per your declarations)
    
*   Tax calculation according to both regimes
    
*   Calculates Surcharge (if applicable) and 4% Health and Education Cess
    

smHRt suggestion: Based on the above parameter the calculator suggests which regime will help you save more tax

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/tax-calculator-ess-portal#how-is-the-tax-calculated)

How is the tax calculated?

The tax is calculated according to the following factors.

**1\. Gross Total Income**

The calculator checks the number of months the salary is already processed, calculates the average and then projects it for the entire year.

For example,

*   If salary is processed for only April: ₹35,000 → Annual projection = ₹35,000 × 12 = ₹4,20,000
    
*   If salary is processed for April and March: Calculate Average → Annual projection = ₹4,20,000
    

**2\. Standard Deduction**

*   ₹50,000 under Old Regime
    
*   ₹75,000 under New Regime
    

**3\. Declared Deductions**

The Declared Deductions are fetched from employee declarations made via ESS or updated by HR on the cloud portal.

**Note**: Declared deductions are only applicable in the Old Regime.

**4\. Total Income**

Total Income = Gross Income - Standard Deduction - Declared Deductions (if any)

**5\. Tax Slab Applied**

Tax is calculated according to the respective tax regimes as seen below.

Old Regime: Income Range and Tax Rate

*   ₹0 – ₹2,50,000: 0%
    
*   ₹2,50,001 – ₹5,00,000: 5%
    
*   ₹5,00,001 – ₹10,00,000: 20%
    
*   Above ₹10,00,000: 30%
    

New Regime: Income Range and Tax Rate

*   ₹0 – ₹3,00,000: 0%
    
*   ₹3,00,001 – ₹7,00,000: 5%
    
*   ₹7,00,001 – ₹10,00,000: 10%
    
*   ₹10,00,001 – ₹12,00,000: 15%
    
*   ₹12,00,001 – ₹15,00,000: 20%
    
*   Above ₹15,00,000: 30%
    

**6\. Surcharge (if applicable)**

Old Regime: Surcharge Rates

*   ₹50L – ₹1Cr: 10%
    
*   ₹1Cr – ₹2Cr: 15%
    
*   ₹2Cr – ₹5Cr: 25%
    
*   Above ₹5Cr: 37%
    

New Regime: Surcharge Rates

*   ₹50L – ₹1Cr: 10%
    
*   ₹1Cr – ₹2Cr: 15%
    
*   Above ₹2Cr: 25%
    

**7\. Health & Education Cess**

Health and Education Cess is calculated as 4% of the summation of tax and surcharges. 8. Total Tax Payable

**Total Tax** = Tax + Surcharge + Cess

**smHRt Recommendation**

The calculator clearly shows you how much you’ll save under each regime and gives you suggestion with precise number For example, “You will save ₹7,300 if you opt for the New Tax Regime”.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/tax-calculator-ess-portal#why-to-use-the-tax-calculator-tool)

Why to use the tax calculator tool?

The tax calculator gives you:

*   Simple, accurate, and updated with the latest tax rules
    
*   Helps you make smart choices before submitting investment proofs
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6wmGZEO2PlG0wQLyP1BQ%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cbdd4b68&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/tax-calculator-ess-portal#how-can-i-compare-taxes-under-the-old-and-new-tax-regimes-in-the-ess-portal)

How can I compare taxes under the old and new tax regimes in the ESS portal?

**Step 1**: Log into the ESS portal, go to the ‘Profile’ menu and click on the ‘My Tax Details’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDvCvgAXbnYZ91hsCXgbN%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f974e73&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Go to the ‘Tax Calculator’ tab to check the comparison between your ‘Total Tax Payable’ under the Old Tax Regime and the New Tax Regime according to the latest tax rules. The system will also show you the exact amount you can save above the comparison table.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7bXl0Q6TqLjgHVgS60Ha%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b964460&sv=2)

**Note**: The calculated according to the declared deductions and your salary.

**Link**: [https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Payroll/MyTaxDetails?Menu=taxcalculatorarrow-up-right](https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Payroll/MyTaxDetails?Menu=taxcalculator)

**Path**: ESS Portal > Profile > My Tax Details > Tax Calculator

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3b484e4b4b54494f7b4b5458505e4f5349564815585456)

[PreviousData Wizard Setting Transferchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/data-wizard-setting-transfer)
[NextPayroll Maker Checkerchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker)

# July 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzKeHO5VYjQMddSxmSu6V%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Updates%2520July23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b923171-e3df-4ad6-a233-e245ced18d5e&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b088c35e&sv=2)

To deliver the best user experience you need to constantly ensure that your software offers the best. That means continuously improving the features and enabling higher convenience and speed. Here is an overview of our July enhancement in Pocket HMRS endeavour to excellence.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#seamless-auto-log-in-across-companies)

Seamless Auto-Log in Across Companies

Managers can now auto-login to view the candidate shared with them without going in and out of multiple accounts they hold. You can use the ‘Merge Account’ feature to allow manager auto login for multiple companies.

For Example:

Consider, that a manager is logged into the ‘Company A’ account and someone has shared a candidate with him in the ‘Company B’ account. Managers will get Auto Login into the ‘Company B’ account once they click on the shared link.

That eliminates the entire manual process of logging out of ‘Company A’ followed by logging in ‘Company B’ to view the shared candidate information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWiQ7oaIKrEe8v5qm1tZT%252FJuly1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15d14957-0cc7-4866-b7a9-60bdb9b0b057&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9110301&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#effective-recruiter-allocation-by-manager)

Effective Recruiter Allocation by Manager

The final level manager or the last level manager can assign a Recruiter and the new recruiter gets a notification for the same. That ensures that the right recruiters with appropriate skills and expertise are handling specific recruitment tasks.

The prompt notification of the newly assigned responsibility allows them to act quickly. It also creates accountability and transparency as everyone involved knows who is responsible for each task.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCzzj3qwgsfa5iHHvUOza%252FJuly2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7ce43db-7c82-4057-9726-9f78fc65065b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=734ffd38&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#simplified-ess-update-approvals)

Simplified ESS Update Approvals

If an employee has updated any information through the ESS portal that particular change will go for approval to HR. This will make update approvals clutter-free for HR as they will only see the fields where the employee has made some changes from the employee profile.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvzsYEXhg0DCVNYSWtvee%252FJuly3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7568563-25b8-45c2-bf86-4559aa892373&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4689ee6e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#end-to-end-candidate-overview)

End-to-End Candidate Overview

We have updated several tracker reports to give you more insights into the valuable information you seek.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#effective-referral-assessment)

➔ Effective Referral Assessment

With this report, you can track the effectiveness of the company’s [employee referral programarrow-up-right](https://www.pockethrms.com/blog/benefits-of-the-employee-referral-program/)
. The report shows an overview of the candidates that were referred by employees, partners and other members of the company’s network. That makes it easier to assess the quality of candidates referred by internal or external sources.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1xDY5HszL157Z1aHAPpq%252FJuly4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7bf8dfa-9d92-4b68-bd5a-2e8f70eb4c27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4860b35&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#navigate-candidate-progress)

➔ Navigate Candidate Progress

The candidate tracker report provides detailed information on candidates that an organization is considering for various job roles. It helps you to track candidates’ progress through various stages in recruitment. It will help recruiters, managers and other stakeholders to make the hiring process more organized and make informed decisions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FL5gqHOI2bM2aAy7lcPZe%252FJuly5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74002b29-c4ad-4b74-95d8-7c4598b5cf8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f5e9e69&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#transparent-candidate-offers)

➔ Transparent Candidate Offers

This report provides an overview of job offers extended to the candidates during the recruitment process. This helps HR professionals, hiring managers, and other stakeholders involved in the recruitment process to track and manage candidate offers.

This way it becomes easier to maintain transparency and consistency in the job offers while maintaining compliance with relevant regulations as well as company policies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJcwz2LjBKExkEbATv8SU%252FJuly6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D356d96e8-5293-456d-9a8d-58146eb46e26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e326f6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#deadline-oriented-attendance-requests)

Deadline-Oriented Attendance Requests

You can now set a deadline for the number of days within which employees can request Regularization/On duty.

For example, if the limit is set at 5, then an employee can request regularization/on duty within 5 days only and won’t be able to apply for it after that.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FueTf7zLDB3r2jUGGHj7V%252FJuly7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85b9dea5-582f-4ace-8601-cc22fbfa17f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=280add65&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#improved-performance-analytics)

Improved Performance Analytics

Now you will get a better perspective with our updated appraisal reports as we made it more informative and comprehensive by adding more useful data.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#enhanced-performance-report)

➔ Enhanced Performance Report

Now, you’ll find new columns like Parameter Marks, Marks, Calculated Weightage, and Final Rating (the final rating will appear according to the configuration). These changes are designed to make the appraisal reports much clearer and easier to understand.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUW8x47hFfF2VliZH4NKb%252FJuly8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9e77c5c-50f6-4c90-9642-9e6637bb5e30&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c8ecacd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#in-depth-performance-review)

➔ In-Depth Performance Review

In the new detailed report – KPI/Questions, weightage, weighted score, Average Manager Rating, Final Rating, Employee Review, Manager Review, Manager Review 2. That gives you more information on the employee performance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEkWXUdtCUD94FJzIh9bT%252FJuly9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc26bab4b-09af-4575-b10f-47c9535efc9a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f872091&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#complete-appraisal-summary)

➔ Complete Appraisal Summary

The ‘Overall Manager Rating’ column combines and condenses the individual ratings given by managers for different sections or parameters. This single rating provides a holistic overview of the employee’s performance or other evaluated criteria.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FH9Lcs1rBT4qGTcAmYVYV%252FJuly10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77cab4dd-d4c3-4407-8c62-f73fa2237227&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c7d035&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#efficient-overtime-control)

Efficient Overtime Control

The Admin/HR can configure overtime (OT) hours, in the setting for working hours you will see shift timings once you select the shift name. Employees will be eligible for OT once they complete default working hours for selected shifts.

You can set the maximum OT hours allowed in a day. Additionally, you will also get an option to allow a manager to update and approve OT.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8ZmLZO0vVqE0zpYpwUS1%252FJuly11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2168b14-b12d-465f-af91-b3db0c6763da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f917a5f3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#personalize-candidate-data)

Personalize Candidate Data

With our new enhancement HR/Admin now can create custom fields with the ‘Field Creation’ feature. These fields will be reflected in the candidate details page in the ESS once you configure it in the Master field screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FePTqqAtdaMAkS6ydGI6k%252FJuly12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbda8d96f-9da1-4379-aca6-c5cbe59a71b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60df07bd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#personalize-job-data)

Personalize Job Data

Thanks to this improvement, HR/Admin now has the ability to generate custom fields through the “Field Creation” feature. These custom fields will seamlessly appear on the Job Details page within the Employee Self-Service (ESS) portal once you configure it in the Master field screen.

This enhancement streamlines the process of adding more information to job-related details for a smoother experience.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCRdgHqe1mdmxIqui8fPF%252FJuly13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b06edd5-f41a-4182-8505-665fbee76114&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc3da06e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/july-2023#flexi-configuration-for-leave-credits)

Flexi-configuration for Leave Credits

With this enhancement for advanced leave settings, you can set varying frequencies for different leave types. In addition to that you can also set leave credit with constant or varying count. As per the frequency selected the leave types will be created.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6OGmzqN8XRZzngF2Pot1%252FJuly14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79e63e75-6d4f-411b-ae18-3d7655bc0f5e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8a85114&sv=2)

# September  2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQ4oTXPBWmbghL2t4XhF1%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%284%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84503d92-fe55-458b-8719-70fd5f889f4b&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ff0515e&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of September, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#cross-company-manager-in-travel)

Cross Company Manager in Travel

The travel request approval process has been expanded to involve managers from other companies within the same corporate group or umbrella organization.

It allows for centralized control and monitoring of travel requests across multiple companies. This is especially useful for organizations with diverse business units or subsidiaries, ensuring uniformity and adherence to policies.

Cross-company approval streamlines the workflow by eliminating the need for separate approval processes for each company. It saves time and reduces administrative overhead by providing a standardized system for travel approval.

Same Company Manager: Dipti Thakkar (B003) Cross Company Manager: Sandip Raina (REG001)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FpGL7nRQk4jK5u4asjPCH%252FCross%2520Company%2520Manager%2520in%2520Travel.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94437870-9292-4dc8-aa94-5deafb606f5a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc349ed&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#cross-company-manager-in-confirmation)

Cross Company Manager in Confirmation

The dual-layered approval process helps guarantee that the employee's confirmation is well-informed and considers broader organizational needs and specific job requirements.

It enhances the transparency and fairness of the confirmation process, ultimately contributing to better decisions regarding permanent employment for the individual in question.

Same Company Manager: Dipti Thakkar (B003) Cross Company Manager: Sandip Raina (REG001)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZlljfp6sRz46LzguqmAr%252FCross%2520Company%2520Manager%2520in%2520Confirmation.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a7aeba6-320c-4265-a070-518ab64839ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=484d060e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#seamless-signature-addition)

Seamless Signature Addition

With our updated signature option, employees can now draw and type their signatures effortlessly, offering simplicity and flexibility. This user-friendly feature empowers employees to modify their signatures anytime, ensuring accuracy and personalization.

The seamless integration of this feature into the HR approval workflow ensures that every time you update your signature, it automatically goes through the approval process based on the configurations set by HR. As a result, your changes are swiftly reviewed and confirmed, keeping your records up-to-date.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWQF30Cj92sVzz0BdXGQi%252FSeamless%2520Signature%2520Addition.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D464c6352-8286-4bdf-aa76-7915eec48884&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b93588f4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTFPa0KjagemOs76JDDjs%252FSeamless%2520Signature%2520Addition3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D146813dd-bfa4-4c05-952d-3f88b6001af3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=516abeb7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#expense-cycles)

Expense Cycles

With this enhancement, administrators can effortlessly establish specific expense date ranges, which can be paired with corresponding due dates for reimbursement claims. This ensures clarity and precision in your expense cycle, ensuring smooth operations for your entire team.

It allows employees to request claims only within the predefined date ranges. This smart system not only saves time but also ensures that all claims are processed promptly, without any delays or confusion.

This update also offers the ability to set exclusive expenses. This means you can specify certain types of expenses that employees can claim. Once a user claims a specific expense type, the system will not allow any blocked expenses to be requested on the same day. This control is fully customizable through the ‘restrictions’ page in the cloud portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyIgrAq2thBcr88iF2StJ%252FExpense%2520Cycles.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D867d1400-57a2-43cc-9d07-3ff773e194d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2baa256a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#probation-extension-letter-download)

Probation Extension Letter Download

This feature allows employees to download their probation letter in scenarios where their probation is extended, such as:

· when the manager decided to extend the probation and the employee agreed to it.

· when the employee disagrees with the probation extension and approaches their HR, who then extends the probation period.

It enhances efficiency by streamlining the probation extension process, ensuring transparency and trust among employees.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4nFE8qG4HhktSfhVoQPk%252FProbation%2520Extension%2520Letter%2520Download.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6462c5b8-ebe2-4112-885b-9a71ffe661d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4407b66f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1p2V6XYPKdp9XNdKjgux%252FProbation%2520Extension%2520Letter%2520Download1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0b585a5-363c-4496-9074-16e1eb05d238&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8b363a9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#predefined-validity-for-job-approval)

Predefined Validity for Job Approval

This enhancement enables a date range feature on the Job Manager approval page. This new functionality allows for specifying a period during which a specific job approval is valid.

When accessing the approval page, managers can now set a start and end date, effectively establishing a window of time during which the job approval is valid.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgvJLWP8q4Nx8dNA3hWu0%252FPredefined%2520Validity%2520for%2520Job%2520Approval.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b16f40b-8fc3-46a8-a216-76f68612174a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac75eb20&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#smart-ai-powered-recruitment)

Smart AI-Powered Recruitment

With Smart AI-powered recruitment, you can utilize smHRt AI tool to level up the entire recruitment process.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#job-description)

Job Description

HRs can quickly generate job descriptions based on the job title by clicking on the ‘Smart AI’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5aINPEQFkUmA792N7lZ8%252FJob%2520Description.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8e9928e-9178-4682-90a4-8ed4d9c22654&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c09814c1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#interview-questions)

Interview Questions

The HR can also enhance the interview experience with accurate professional and behavioural questions based on the position being offered and the candidate’s profile.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#resume-summary)

Resume Summary

You can summarize candidate profiles with a single click to highlight the relevant details in the ESS portal. Such summaries empower recruiters to swiftly extract vital details from resumes, which accelerates candidate screening, ensures timely responses, and enhances the overall application experience.

By focusing on skills and qualifications, these summaries enable objective evaluations, reduce biases and optimize the shortlisting process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEB2oV9opCD7X2fS60IIY%252FResume%2520Summary.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a66f403-af99-42f5-a0d2-b79125859c07&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=373e3403&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#resume-parsing-by-smart-ai)

Resume Parsing by Smart AI

Resume parsing extracts and organizes essential candidate information from multiple resumes, which can be selected by the user. This functionality significantly reduces manual effort, enabling recruiters to swiftly review and compare numerous applications. Parsing systems categorize details like skills, experience, and education, creating a structured database.

This structured data allows recruiters to quickly find suitable candidates. Additionally, it ensures consistency in candidate evaluation and helps in identifying top talents effectively.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3xHgl1HSq7Hexb7gZTsc%252FResume%2520Parsing%2520by%2520Smart%2520AI.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa3fb805-be80-4d59-be58-29fc5e6f0c77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f210874&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#smart-ai-in-hr-letters)

Smart AI in HR Letters

Smart AI HR letters allow you to instantly generate various templates such as Transfer Letters, Warning Letters, Welcome Letters, and more. It also allows you to generate customized letters according to your needs, saving you time and effort.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGGbhQ0U5fUCUEVbAHzRw%252FSmart%2520AI%2520in%2520HR%2520Letters.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49cb4fe5-534a-4ec0-977f-e394908f3285&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7033b5c1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#set-validity-for-offer-letters)

Set Validity for Offer Letters

With this new feature, when a recruiter sends an offer letter to a candidate, they can set a deadline for the candidate to accept the job. For example, the deadline might be stated as "Offer Letter Acceptance Deadline will be \[date\]."

This feature helps companies create a sense of urgency by ensuring a clear and well-defined timeframe for candidates to respond. It streamlines the hiring process, making it more organized and efficient.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCh3HJNqmg8TDq30fDN7a%252FSet%2520Validity%2520for%2520Offer%2520Letters.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59706509-43cc-4c51-b2ad-a24ce7bd041e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c29564ca&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FfZG5dHKCuUxwmkOUsq75%252FSet%2520Validity%2520for%2520Offer%2520Letters2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc780c63f-b8ce-4e2a-9bd8-04694853ae6a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=564a7e53&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDD1lKqq4cyeLfZpU1UMP%252FSet%2520Validity%2520for%2520Offer%2520Letters3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc1240a4-1bb4-44f8-9627-eaf73922c66e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0470e84&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#multiple-managers-in-appraisal-questions-and-manager-data)

Multiple Managers in Appraisal Questions & Manager Data

The appraisal report has been improved to display data for all managers. The candidates will be able to see responses and ratings by all the managers providing them a comprehensive view for their appraisal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXrplrBM9q33ZGyCzyIgj%252FMultiple%2520Managers%2520in%2520Appraisal%2520Questions%2520%2526%2520Manager%2520Data.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9f76b6c-1b0b-4a5a-aba7-d37fff522aee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=449d6458&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FM8aI76yd8jLnd41qzQJ2%252FMultiple%2520Managers%2520in%2520Appraisal%2520Questions%2520%2526%2520Manager%2520Data2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb1591a5-8a20-446b-bd40-43b463cd8ca9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9106d674&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/september-2023#map-column-in-punch-in-out-report)

Map Column in Punch In-Out Report

We have also introduced a map icon to our punch-in and punch-out reports. Now, users can easily click on the map icon in the report to view their specific punch location on the map. It enables users to visualize employees’ locations directly on the map.

It simplifies tracking employee movements, making it easier to monitor work patterns and ensure everyone is where they are required to be. Understanding the geographical distribution of their workforce helps businesses allocate resources accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtcupxjF0so6aHQa68Qgj%252FMap%2520Column%2520in%2520Punch%2520In-Out%2520Report.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc0b6701-b9ed-476e-95fa-599d2c7adc62&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db3c9782&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FuvJyhnwoxaSBu3LO9oAx%252FMap%2520Column%2520in%2520Punch%2520In-Out%2520Report2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db72cd6e6-2baa-4868-bf89-88ab9a7c8217&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a50c5184&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#70030500001f020430001f131b150418021d035e131f1d)

# December 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoHWfx0x4KSuOUeOFBhci%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%2813%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D400aec9d-6946-463c-85a0-055f6c5b8274&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fedb9cf6&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of November, we have the following enhancements:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/december-2023#approval-based-configuration-for-job-modifications)

Approval-based Configuration for Job Modifications

The latest update in your HRMS software empowers HR/Admin to control job modifications, allowing them to decide whether changes require approval. This ensures a streamlined process, preventing unauthorized modifications as well as secure and organize job updates. It enhances your ability to enforce approval protocols, ensuring the accuracy and reliability of job-related information within the system.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4VEVGkb5vl9VOvei2B17%252FEnhanced%2520Accuracy%2520and%2520Security%2520in%2520Job%2520Changes.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbdb750b4-a648-48aa-9290-f580481a990e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2090d7bd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/december-2023#job-timeline)

Job Timeline

Now, you can easily track a job's history with the new 'Job Timeline' button on the Job Profile page. Admins, HR, or Recruiters can view all job-related activities from creation to approval/rejection, publication, modification, and more.

It provides a comprehensive overview of a job's entire journey. It enhances efficiency, enabling quick access to crucial information, making job management smoother.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0NTmLXhElU8YsXrS50eg%252FMaster%2520Job%2520History%2520with%2520Job%2520Timeline%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9567b44d-e449-4e8a-b329-2c39564bf319&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87704e00&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLgn8rID6vSfAeKxrxKwj%252FMaster%2520Job%2520History%2520with%2520Job%2520Timeline%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f23097b-d32b-4fba-9119-422367680e32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=406aaf12&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/december-2023#custom-field-transfer-from-candidate-to-employee)

‘Custom Field’ Transfer from Candidate to Employee

Automate data transfer from Custom Fields in Candidate Profile to Employee Profile by ensuring matching 'Field Name' and 'Field Type'. Set 'Compulsory' in Configuration field creation for seamless migration, simplifying the process and enhancing data consistency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FuMLOKnnnZyeuMjzxcRKE%252FBoost%2520Accuracy%2520by%2520Field%2520Matching%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6d7f28d-97bf-4031-8e70-75dd54008d85&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec51308a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgSVjIkidBRRKm4uYKTmn%252FBoost%2520Accuracy%2520by%2520Field%2520Matching%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9d467c7-1a89-4791-88c1-302405397230&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93b8d916&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGdy23enor5GI2vNzW8jw%252FBoost%2520Accuracy%2520by%2520Field%2520Matching%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2af96db0-dcac-4f52-9945-86cf32eb5aa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1882ef1b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/december-2023#auto-migration-of-candidate-info-upon-onboarding)

Auto-Migration of Candidate Info Upon Onboarding

Upon onboarding the education and work details saved in the candidate profile can be automatically migrated to the Employment History tab in the Employee Profile. It streamlines onboarding for Admins, HR, and Recruiters, eliminates manual data entry, saves time and ensures accuracy.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1cBsi03vPAwmYuhHNE3w%252FBoost%2520Accuracy%2520by%2520Field%2520Matching%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30f64c4e-8159-4da0-9db4-5d8df016ddac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d6e636a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrCRZx5GgujI0b4oWbRop%252FBoost%2520Accuracy%2520by%2520Field%2520Matching%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db59c388e-5890-446f-9cb7-93ae5247997c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b882deab&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/december-2023#automated-logo-generation-for-offer-letters)

Automated Logo Generation for Offer Letters

When moving a candidate to the 'Offer' stage and you use the CTC Calculator to make an offer, the system now automatically includes the Company Name and Logo in the CTC template sent to the candidate. That provides a professional touch to your communication and ensures a polished and branded presentation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FxzHsV1CFDz2h33Ksk4JV%252FProvide%2520Brand%2520Identity%2520to%2520Offer%2520Letters%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba552b49-766d-41d0-84d7-4174a911398f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7299c03&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fpp6LfBVuBwfWWUtzXz9l%252FProvide%2520Brand%2520Identity%2520to%2520Offer%2520Letters%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91f8716b-4715-410d-a7ef-c7a6ebaf8435&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7df0ae63&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1k7L8yXp0hXmAPGXG7Hx%252FProvide%2520Brand%2520Identity%2520to%2520Offer%2520Letters%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac46f38e-c116-4408-8911-cff06689f15c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2bce3270&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/december-2023#multiple-filters-for-flexible-reporting)

Multiple Filters for Flexible Reporting

Use the reporting system's filter to precisely customize reports and find exactly what you need. That makes them more user-friendly and provides targeted insights. This aids in tracking changes and extracting precise data to enhance decision-making. You will get these filters for various reports such as gratuity, report wizard and compliance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0zE0WGvNYWxbJwjm3LL5%252FFlexible%2520Reports%2520to%2520Focus%2520on%2520What%2520Matters%2520Most%2520-Filters.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D829b5b56-cecf-4d9d-91b4-57776ec0a12d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9765792e&sv=2)

# January 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ffbkb9RUO8xPaOiUGnLL9%252FJanuary%25202025.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d73eb54-0d87-400e-a3fe-7c2e7b9b6d84&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70960dd7&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of January, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#set-it-and-forget-it-auto-approve-or-reject-pending-entries)

Set It & Forget It: Auto-Approve or Reject Pending Entries

Now, you can set rules to automate approval or rejection of pending Regularization and On-Duty entries during time consolidation. All the entries will be automatically approved or rejected accordingly without manager intervention, saving time and boosting efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXfFWWHADeAKtC7m2ADoQ%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d321881&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#set-and-manage-monthly-week-off-limits)

**Set & Manage Monthly Week-Off Limits**

Easily limit the maximum week-offs employees can take each month to ensure compliance with company policies. A simple settings page lets you define the limit, and the system automatically prevents excess week-offs.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAtrpq881EORazwcOAGnY%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8afdeff6&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fvr13hBL3Je8CURLoTFd4%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc68de3c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#flexible-sandwich-rules-for-half-days-deduction)

**Flexible Sandwich Rules for Half-day’s Deduction**

Now, the Sandwich Rule is more flexible! You can choose whether it applies to half-day leaves. Furthermore, you can apply it for any half-day or only when part of a continuous leave pattern. This prevents unnecessary leave deductions, aligns better with company policies, and makes leave management more precise and hassle-free.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FTyv99bLNaLvInjuvZnaR%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=294b7895&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FY3wOZFguooWjTw30DyXc%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8596d004&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#locate-employees-in-seconds-with-filters)

**Locate Employees in Seconds with Filters**

Finding employees just got easier! We've added a filter option that lets you search based on specific criteria, so you no longer have to scroll through long lists. This saves time, improves usability, and makes manual attendance management faster and more efficient for managers and admins.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FiPF69SmCOvYeiVcNlg1M%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd5f616b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMJutZu8J71QEMTKLknfO%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34700114&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#efficiently-assign-weekly-off-by-employees-name-or-code)

Efficiently Assign Weekly off by Employees Name or Code

While in weekly off setting you will get both the Employee Code and Name together in the Employee Code field. Plus, the field is now searchable. You can simply type an Employee Code or Name to quickly find the right employee. This update reduces errors and makes managing weekly offs much smoother for HR and admins.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FNoAaiQDa1XPDFjKjFtap%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dcffa7d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#break-shift-get-control-with-precise-work-hour)

Break Shift: Get Control with Precise Work Hour

Easily manage work hours with break-shift configuration. HR/Admin can enable ‘Break Shift Required?’ to calculate hours using detailed break patterns or a simple first-in/last-out method. Employees can regularize missed punches, check shortfalls or extra hours, and request approvals.

Managers and HR/Admin can approve or reject requests, with mandatory comments for rejections. Missed punches are highlighted for better visibility. Detailed reports provide insights for employees, managers, and HR/Admin, ensuring accurate calculations, smoother workflows, and better tracking.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoWsUvDm6s7e13P3cYnKF%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6ca334b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhAFsmfxjWiyLaPLFV6dr%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a0fa489&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#ensure-employee-consent-for-nominee-details)

Ensure Employee Consent for Nominee Details

The ESS Consent Validation ensures employees confirm their consent before saving nominee details. If the checkbox isn’t checked, an alert prompts them to do so before proceeding.

In the Cloud Portal, the checkbox is pre-checked when submitted via ESS, and HR can manually check it while adding or editing details. For bulk imports, the consent is processed as ‘Yes’ if checked and ‘No’ if unchecked, ensuring smooth handling in all cases.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbNKzhe1KWtHMcnbJKMxe%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30ee73c6&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fm2nN3HgKlsqL8FssQAGy%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8d419f3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#a-sleek-modern-career-page-in-one-click)

**A Sleek, Modern Career Page in One Click**

Give your Career Page a fresh, modern look with our new ‘**Modern’ layout** option. Simply select it from the Layout dropdown in Career Page settings, and enjoy a sleek, updated design that makes a great first impression.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2o2vZMn7D5fuBxpp3rwv%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb21e7b9&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7EWurKrHrwlZcols8H7A%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4142e12&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/january-2025#promotion-updates-made-simple-and-quick)

**Promotion Updates Made Simple & Quick**

Easily manage employee promotions with our new **Promotion Tab**. Update an employee’s **designation, department, or both** in just a few clicks. Once a promotion is added, the changes instantly reflect on their profile. Plus, employees can view their full **promotion history** anytime on the **Employee Self-Service (ESS) portal.**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMZFLgDPPQQIY2tJ8NiDF%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e5fd9657&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIyesAU5DiknyMgHIKkSt%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4019ab75&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOmsgmAAYSGib4G2A8Vuz%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0126422&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4CM8gujCeLPiDmJ1LO0b%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45b6a41d&sv=2)

# June 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fly2yynJhBaMwdJo8vXEB%252FJune%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D292e36cf-4813-4293-90e3-a59a3d59ccbc&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb14ae9f&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of June 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#restriction-on-on-duty-during-week-offs-and-holidays)

Restriction on On-Duty during Week Offs and Holidays

This setting allows HR/Admin to prevent employees from applying for On-Duty on weekly offs and designated holidays. It includes two dropdown options to easily control and configure this restriction.

Dropdowns:

• On Duty Restrict – Holiday (Yes/No)

• On Duty Restrict – Week Off (Yes/No)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVSy5yAy2hxuIORfkEAlO%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49f01642&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#lwf-and-prof.-tax-locations-added-by-default)

LWF and Prof. Tax Locations Added by Default

We’ve now added all LWF and Professional Tax locations to the Pop-Up Data by default. This removes the need to manually create them each time. HR/Admin can now simply choose from 16 pre-defined LWF Locations and 37 pre-defined Prof. Tax Locations while adding or editing employees.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRbL6h77SPTJ05JtGMMyM%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a55b955&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Focxk9nzF3q0faNepBQAs%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85db07e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#gender-field-now-includes-transgender-option)

Gender Field Now Includes ‘Transgender’ Option

Admin/HR can now choose **Transgender** as a gender option, along with **Male** and **Female**, when creating or editing employee profiles.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1bXIWKlBRaou74lpunse%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ce54a27&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#email-notification-for-monthly-attendance-summary)

Email Notification for Monthly Attendance Summary

In the recent enhancement, the system sends each employee a monthly attendance summary email on the set date and time. It includes a link to download their personal Excel attendance report for the month.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fez7Odjq19p2wNC6aQWRM%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1041fdb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUgkb8lqRD0rmGmL5bMqW%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30b4b676&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkgVmykiZO0WgoIHTCuuU%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f443d8b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#improved-email-templates-for-password-reset)

Improved Email Templates for Password Reset

Now a new option is available to send a ‘password generation’ or ‘reset’ email to employees when their Self-Service role is reset. This helps HR inform employees about their password change due to an update in their account (e.g., role change).

Email templates have been updated for the following cases:

*   First-time password generation
    
*   Password reset by Admin/HR
    
*   Password reset requested by the employee
    
*   Password successfully reset by the employee
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwM2zbl89HBBIbMF4L34j%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a575e42e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FizNfwdLUIbccSlonjPmR%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5dc38b1c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7BKFDZmvxVyldYtlF5ov%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7af2c879&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbcrZ6u6atZzc7JM1yBFD%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c317f8a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGQk4NWOzF81oMMsDwhvf%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b22ae82&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#enhancements-in-managing-resignation-and-lwd)

Enhancements in Managing Resignation and LWD

We have enhanced the management of Resignation Date and Last Working Date (LWD) with more control and flexibility. We’ve improved how you manage Resignation and Last Working Dates. You can now:

*   Set how default dates should appear if they fall on a holiday or weekly off
    
*   Allow or restrict Employees, Managers, and HRs from updating the Last Working Date
    
*   Allow or restrict them from updating the Resignation Date
    
*   Control whether these updates are allowed on holidays or weekly offs.
    

All these settings can be managed separately for Employees, Managers, and HRs.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FiqLiLEDwlDXiFnYDa8dQ%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9cacf5f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#control-visibility-of-sub-section-limits-in-tds-page)

Control Visibility of Sub-Section Limits in TDS Page

You can now choose to show or hide the sub-section limit in the TDS Declaration and Proof Entry pages. The limit stays active, but employees won’t see it while filling their declarations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgyoX2kSV2bIlSIyEFsRo%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0ed369b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#improved-worksheet-generation)

Improved Worksheet Generation

In the recent enhancement, you can now generate worksheets for any monthly range within the current financial year. There's also an option to generate them for all employees or only for live/left employees. The system will create the latest Income Tax Processed worksheet based on your selection.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJkvWBy2TFGeMRRzbEHIh%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5277c9fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#added-learning-details-placeholder-to-email-template)

Added Learning Details Placeholder to Email Template

This feature lets you add learning details into email templates using separate placeholders for each field like Learning Name, Duration, Start/End Date, Trainer Type, Learning Head, and Location. These placeholders automatically fill in based on the employee’s scheduled session.

**Example:**

Learning Name: Communication Skills | Duration: 2 Days | Start Date: 08 July 2025

Each field is filled automatically using system placeholders.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FrJip73U0myXnUANiC23P%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=223af564&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#helpdesk-tags-now-shown-on-tickets)

Helpdesk Tags Now Shown on Tickets

In the recent update, both the employees and agents can now see the tags added when a Helpdesk ticket is raised by an employee. The tags are visible on the ticket list page as well as inside the ticket.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKdab9Jj1f4qwX04tYbJ2%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c60360ae&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ff2CYUCm9qm86D5wMN2oS%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa86f347&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/june-2025#confirmation-date-update-in-hr-letters)

Confirmation Date Update in HR Letters

In the recent update a new dynamic field, “Confirmation Approved Date” has been added to the HR Letter template. It shows the actual date when the confirmation was approved by the manager or system, even if it’s different from the scheduled date.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8Zn2ZYGhajpWwz8XU2Yk%252F9%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec25fcb5-be3a-4390-894a-bd9f73c78efa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1371cedb&sv=2)
