# Auto Assign Shift Import Time | Pocket HRMS

The ‘Auto Assign Shift Import Time’ allows users to define specific IN/OUT time ranges for shifts. The system will follow these ranges rather than the default IN/OUT times set in the Shift Details screen. Users can select a shift from a dropdown and configure different IN/OUT time ranges for each shift.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/attendance/auto-assign-shift-import-time#how-does-auto-assign-shift-import-time-work-once-the-in-out-time-ranges-are-set-the-system-works-acc)

**How does ‘Auto Assign Shift Import Time’ work**? Once the IN/OUT time ranges are set, the system works accordingly.

If the employee punch is registered during the defined the In/Out time ranges the system will identify and assign the shift for the punches registered accordingly. This way, the system provides flexibility in assigning different IN/OUT time ranges for different shifts and ensures accurate shift detection and assignment.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/attendance/auto-assign-shift-import-time#how-to-define-in-out-time-ranges-for-the-shifts-so-the-system-will-detect-and-auto-assign-a-shift-to)

How to define In/Out time ranges for the shifts so the system will detect and auto assign a shift to the employee according to the punches?

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal, go to the settings menu and under the ‘Attendance’ tab click on the ‘Attendance Settings’ subtab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FNXNHuBEFzzRS3lpgBvYi%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74c10f9e&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Under the ‘Attendance Settings’ subtab click on the ‘Auto Shift Detect’ option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkTDYGWsq70gUpH17GN9J%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b13a5bff&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the ‘Shift Name’ and from the from the respective dropdown when the time you are to enter fall on the ‘Same Date’ or it fall in the ‘Next Date’ according to the calendar days.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJ05uXOrSiiWmzULiqOfJ%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e200b95f&sv=2)

**Step 4**: Then enter values for the ‘Import IN time Start as’, ‘Import IN time End as’, ‘Import Out time Start as’, and the ‘Import Out time End as’ fields and click on the ‘Save’ button.

The shift IN/Out time ranges will be defined and the system will auto assign a shift to the employee according to the punches

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRMN97GvB8IZuhAcGN3mx%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9293d3a9&sv=2)

**Note**: Please make sure that the details all the IN/Out time fields are entered correctly. As the auto shifts will be assigned according to these IN/Out Time Start and IN/Out Time End field values.

**Path**: Cloud -> Setting -> Attendance -> Attendance setting

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=attendance&submodule=AutoAssignShiftImportTimearrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=attendance&submodule=AutoAssignShiftImportTime)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#780b0d0808170a0c3808171b131d0c100a150b561b1715)

[PreviousAuto Shift Detectchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/attendance/auto-shift-detect)
[NextAnalyticschevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/analytics)

# Custom Reports | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/analytics/report/custom-reports#how-to-generate-custom-reports-from-pocket-hrms)

**How to generate Custom Reports from Pocket HRMS?**

**Overview**

The **Custom Reports** feature in Pocket HRMS allows you to generate specific HR reports that assist with various workforce management tasks. Below are the reports currently available in the HR module and the purposes they serve:

1.  **New Joinee Report:** Tracks detailed onboarding information for newly joined employees, ensuring compliance and smooth integration into the company.
    
2.  **Referral Report:** Provides visibility into employee referrals and the outcomes of the referred candidates, helping to assess the effectiveness of the referral program.
    
3.  **Bad Hire Report:** Identifies employees who have been separated within a short tenure, helping to track bad hires and take corrective actions.
    
4.  **LSA (Leave of Service Absence) Report:** Tracks employee leave cases, focusing on tenure-based leave eligibility and absence details.
    

_Note: More reports will be added to this section in the future to support additional HR needs._

**Step 1: Navigate to the Custom Report Section**

*   Go to: **Cloud → Analytics → Reports → HR → Custom Report**
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FwHUF4bqYRfhsQZjXPVp8%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99d80d4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F1cb33OsJ2hhpLCeMpXJU%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a1cb883a&sv=2)

**Step 2: Select the Module**

*   Choose **HR** as the module to generate reports.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fn44X24UdTZQvIQxrVN4z%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cae43af0&sv=2)

**Step 3: Select the Report Name**

*   Choose the report you want to generate. Currently available reports are:
    
    *   **New Joinee Report**
        
    *   **Referral Report**
        
    *   **Bad Hire Report**
        
    *   **LSA (Leave of Service Absence) Report**
        
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FgMIZ6AsdYZTCE2cYhPtF%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c13c7a30&sv=2)

**Step 4: Select Start Date and End Date**

*   Pick the relevant start and end dates for the report.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FypUnJlwmka4RXpzCklB5%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c91261b&sv=2)

**Step 5: Select Employee Status**

*   Choose which employees to include in the report:
    
    *   **Live**
        
    *   **Separate**
        
    *   **All**
        
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FdC8AvhakiIrBGbgKfUg9%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1885be8a&sv=2)

**Step 6: Generate the Report**

*   Click on the **Download** button to generate the report.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F5ugFF7wQK4x7gjhZjDIk%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25b5b873&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#70030500001f020430001f131b150418021d035e131f1d)

# Data Wizard Setting Transfer | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/data-wizard-setting-transfer#what-is-data-wizard)

What is Data Wizard?

The **Data Wizard** is a tool that helps users **set up and extract reports** based on their preferences. Users can apply **filters and settings** to generate reports exactly how they need them.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/data-wizard-setting-transfer#what-is-the-setting-transfer-feature)

What is the Setting Transfer Feature?

Sometimes, different users in different companies need the **same report settings** to save time and effort. Instead of setting everything up again, the **Setting Transfer feature** allows you to copy existing settings from **one user in a company** to **another user in a different company**.

This ensures **consistency** and makes it easier for teams to work with reports in multiple companies.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/data-wizard-setting-transfer#understanding-the-data-wizard-setting-transfer-screen)

Understanding the Data Wizard Setting Transfer Screen

The image shows the **‘Data Wizard Setting Transfer’** screen, which allows users to transfer report settings from one user to another across different companies.

**Fields on the Screen:**

*   **From User** – The user whose report settings will be copied.
    

In the example, the selected user is '**[\[email protected\]](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
'**.

*   **Setting Name** – The specific report setting that will be transferred.
    

Here, the selected setting is '**Leave Summary'**.

*   **To Company** – The company where the settings will be copied.
    

In this case, the target company is '**Prajwal - First Company'**.

*   **To User** – The user in the target company who will receive the settings.
    

The selected user is '**Prajwal…………@gmail.com'**.

*   **Transfer Button** – Clicking this button will **initiate the transfer** process and apply the selected settings to the target user.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/data-wizard-setting-transfer#how-to-transfer-data-wizard-settings)

How to transfer data wizard settings?

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal, go to the ‘Settings’ menu and under the ‘HR’ tab click on the ‘Data Wizard Setting Transfer’ subtab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbWovdf0yEcQgXQtefU9S%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c577ac41&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Select the user who has the report settings you want to transfer, from the ‘From User’ dropdown.

**Step 3**: From the ‘Setting Name’ dropdown, select the report setting that needs to be copied.

**Step 4**: From the ‘To Company dropdown’. Select the company where the settings should be transferred.

**Step 5**: From the ‘To User dropdown’, select the user in the target company who will receive the settings.

**Step 6**: Review your selections

*   **From User**: The user who has the settings.
    
*   **Setting Name**: The report settings to transfer.
    
*   **To Company**: The company receiving the settings.
    
*   **To User**: The recipient of the settings.
    

**Step 7**: Click the ‘Transfer’ button to finalize the process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtqNnNexcvSY1BqGiTpk0%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffc65e8e&sv=2)

**Path**: Cloud > Settings > HR > Data Wizard Setting Transfer > select details >Transfer

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=hr&submodule=SettingsTransferarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=hr&submodule=SettingsTransfer)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f88b8d8888978a8cb888979b939d8c908a958bd69b9795)

[PreviousFeature Guideschevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides)
[NextTax Calculator ESS Portalchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/tax-calculator-ess-portal)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# February 2026 | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#product-update-february-2026)

Product Update February 2026

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of February 2026, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#shift-information-in-regularization)

Shift Information in Regularization

• The **Attendance Regularization** menu has been enhanced to display **Shift Details** for better clarity. This feature is available on both **Mobile and Web** platforms.

• **Shift Details:** The shift information is now visible in the attendance regularization form, helping users clearly view the **shift timings and related details**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F8WuQ6e10CNcHVF28Z3HI%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57f70dcf&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FDBFNzOIDbaY9QE3Jg0Ou%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=673b7ac3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#punch-in-alert)

Punch-In Alert

1.  The **Punch-In Reminder** feature sends shift-based reminders to employees through the **ESS/Mobile portal**.
    
2.  Notifications can be configured in two ways through the **Go Rule Engine**:
    

*   **Interval-based:** reminders are sent before and after shift start at a fixed interval (e.g., every 10 minutes).
    
*   **Time-based:** HR can set specific times to send reminders.• Reminders are sent only if the employee is assigned to the shift and has **not punched in yet**.• Once the employee **punches in**, the reminders stop automatically.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FS5pgJ08Kwao89HG0YKdo%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35b57084&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#leave-credit-lapse-for-multiple-frequencies)

Leave Credit Lapse for Multiple Frequencies

The **Leave Credit Lapse** feature, earlier available only for **monthly frequency**, has now been enhanced to support **Yearly, Quarterly, and Half-Yearly** frequencies.

\*\*Example:\*\*For **Half-Yearly frequency**, any unused leave balance will **lapse at the end of the half-year**, and the leave balance will be adjusted as per the defined credit cycle.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FmtCyNAX2zQotSZMpsPyV%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92b5b38a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#last-manager-approval-flow-in-pms)

Last Manager Approval Flow in PMS

The **PMS workflow** has been enhanced to include an **Approve/Reject option for the Last Manager**, which was not available earlier.

• If the **Last Manager rejects** the review form, the workflow will return to the **previous manager’s stage** for review and resubmission.

• The **previous manager must review and submit the form again** until it is finally approved by the Last Manager.

• Once the **Last Manager approves the form**, it will be included in the **final appraisal calculation**.

• A **mandatory “Remarks” field** has been added for the Last Manager while approving or rejecting the form to ensure proper justification and transparency.

• The **ratings given by the Previous Manager** will automatically be **copied to the “Last Manager Rating” column** after approval.

• These ratings will also be used in the **PMS reports** for accurate reporting and analysis.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F3qsuMRqqkcTeAmgpMiV2%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db837d23&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#duplicate-employee-check-for-group-companies)

Duplicate Employee Check for Group Companies

The **Duplicate Employee Identification – Group Company** feature helps organizations detect and prevent duplicate employee records across multiple companies within the same group. It ensures data accuracy and maintains consistency in employee information across the system.

• Helps **prevent duplicate employee records** for the same person across multiple companies.

• **Alerts HR** if a possible duplicate is detected while creating or editing an employee profile.

• Maintains **clean and accurate employee data**, reducing errors in payroll and compliance.

• Prevents duplication of key records such as **PAN, PF, and ESI**.

• Enables **better tracking of an employee’s lifecycle** across group companies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FM0J5niPBZfR26Kyta1wD%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70ce80ae&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/february-2026#hr-letter-copy-function)

HR Letter Copy Function

The **HR Letter Copy** feature allows HR teams to copy HR letter templates from one entity to another, including the current entity. This helps maintain consistency and reduces the effort required to recreate the same letters across multiple companies.

• HR can **copy one HR letter at a time** and select **multiple companies**, including the current company, where the letter needs to be copied.

• Option available to **include Header and Footer** while copying the letter.

• A **unique template name** can be assigned to the copied letter, and both the **email body and attachment** will be copied.

• Helps **reduce manual effort** and maintain **consistent HR letter formats** across entities.

• Saves time by allowing HR teams to **replicate complete templates quickly** without recreating them manually.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FxnG2z0ucnaUkYT1bzDKF%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3ec972d&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#acdfd9dcdcc3ded8ecdcc3cfc7c9d8c4dec1df82cfc3c1)

# New Employee | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/new-employee#how-to-add-a-new-employee-or-what-is-the-process-of-new-employee-addition-or-creation)

How to add a new employee or what is the process of new employee addition or creation?

**Step 1**: Log into cloud portal, go to the ‘Employee’ menu and click on the ‘Employee List’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUWFhImYFSp6cnWcqtgIZ%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64fb5e09&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Click on the ‘Employee Wizard’ option at the top of the employee list.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLfYaa0MZooMiOj4bhjrp%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d97a291&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Fill in the details in the respective fields and click on the ‘Save’ button once you filled all the information. The new employee profile will be created.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fv1OZNugFVcetiJJKdbkZ%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b441da2&sv=2)

**Path:** Cloud portal>Employee>Employee List>Employee Wizard>fill in details> Save

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Employee/Employee/EmployeeListarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Employee/Employee/EmployeeList)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f88b8d8888978a8cb888979b939d8c908a958bd69b9795)

[PreviousEmployee Documentchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/employee-document)
[NextEmployee FnFchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/employee-separation-and-release)

# October & November 2024 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzNQ5nBloJAjAYlxAizGw%252FOctober%2520%2526%2520November%25202024.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5793446-e789-497e-b720-acf4ac3c7bd0&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88d38e37&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the months of October & November, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#comp-off-leave-now-with-a-deadline)

Comp Off Leave, Now with a Deadline!

Admins can now restrict employees from applying for Comp Off leave after a specific timeframe from the Comp Off date. That ensures policy compliance and prevents misuse of leave.

**For example,** If the Comp Off date is 13th September and the limit is 30 days, leave can only be applied between 13th September and 12th October. Requests outside this range will be denied.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYoeevjpquw73IBoxqMqx%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f242cfa3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#turn-ot-hours-into-time-off-seamlessly)

Turn OT Hours into Time Off Seamlessly

Introducing configurations to consider OT hours as Comp Off for week offs/holidays. Simply, define OT hour ranges and their corresponding Comp Off counts and system will automatically credit Comp off accordingly. There is no minimum hour limit giving you greater flexibility and saving a ton of time.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHpkV5jx3sOAQ3NMgxJSS%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd806b14&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#revolutionizing-consecutive-leave-management)

Revolutionizing Consecutive Leave Management

With this release, we introduce the following improvements to consecutive leave policies:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#consecutive-leaves-restricted)

Consecutive Leaves Restricted

Employees cannot take consecutive leave days without a break. Promotes balanced leave utilization and appropriate rest periods.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#week-offs-and-holidays-excluded)

Week offs and Holidays Excluded

Week offs and holidays are excluded from consecutive leave calculations. Providing flexibility by not penalizing leaves around company holidays or regular time off.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#same-leave-type-restriction)

Same Leave Type Restriction

The system restricts consecutive usage of the same leave type. Encouraging varied leave usage and identifying potential attendance concerns. These enhancements allow transparent leave administration, supporting employee well-being and operational efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FN86xs1xswn2MhVA2TgaV%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61345b63&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#bell-curve-flexibility-tailor-your-appraisal-process)

Bell Curve Flexibility: Tailor Your Appraisal Process

The Appraisal module has been enhanced to provide greater flexibility and configuration options for the Bell Curve functionality.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#rating-type-configuration)

Rating Type Configuration

Users can select ‘Scale’ with a default range of 1-5 or ‘Weightage’ which displays the Grade % as the rating type for appraisals.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#define-bell-curve-screen)

Define Bell Curve Screen

The graph dynamically updates based on the first three values entered. Users can display either Rating Scale or Grade % in the first column. Strict validation ensures the first three values are in ascending order, with the total Expected % equaling 100%.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#rating-normalization-screen)

Rating Normalization Screen

The Rating Normalization screen will now adapt its columns based on the selected rating type (Scale or Grade %). Normalization calculations align with the chosen configuration. An additional "Count to be Normalized" column provides further insights.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fin6KgDeTsSzOjjbN4FEa%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4ac1b41&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fi1bR1lkBrgFNoEL6FDFV%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6585e134&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FR5QqnSuAMKJetd2lZPvY%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54ef3dcc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#real-time-daily-shift-wise-headcount)

Real-time Daily Shift-wise Headcount

Now, you can get Department and shift-wise headcount reports with details such as the number of employees present on the current day based on the employee punches. You can also export a list of the present and absent employees by selecting a business unit.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FmTUXGa50QG3tuoDx8Msv%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56737e1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#effortless-learning-certificate-customization)

Effortless Learning Certificate Customization

HR can now configure learning certificates more easily by selecting a learning template and mapping fields directly into the certificates. This ensures all key details about the learning program are included. **The Learning fields are as follows:**

Learning Code

*   Learning Name
    
*   Duration
    
*   Start Date
    
*   End Date
    
*   Completion Date
    
*   Learning Head
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6jbyodxD692La1hTkm5Q%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7f1db2f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#a-quick-toggle-to-make-expense-modes-mandatory)

A Quick Toggle to Make Expense Modes Mandatory

HR can now make modes mandatory for specific expense types with a simple toggle key. Once activated, if the employee chooses no mode, the system will block expense submissions on the ESS portal. This will streamline the process and increase efficiency in expense management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fr3Iwch3w4iQnLHcKy6Xt%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e63f93e2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#more-flexibility-in-managing-expense-entries)

More Flexibility in Managing Expense Entries

Our latest UX improvement allows managers to select or deselect individual expense entries as needed. They are no longer restricted to either approve or reject the entry. Now, managers can choose not to take action on specific entries allowing greater flexibility and control.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FleP4MTZi6PD11dYAZTmD%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7df3cde8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#travel-approval-with-editable-amounts-and-disclaimer)

Travel Approval with Editable Amounts & disclaimer

The new travel enhancement lets you add finance approval to travel advance requests. When enabled, all requests need finance approval. The final amounts for travel advances and reimbursements can also edited during finance approval. Plus, an approval note or disclaimer can be added to the approval pages through the travel configuration settings.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnwbMtCK17IWqoHRu00L0%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4319615f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSAOPjOkpH2dRQ56QAnDh%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=585288cc&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fr2B4P7BFgTfPVu5xAF4k%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19fdb0e4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#track-every-category-change-with-ease)

Track Every Category Change with Ease

The category transfer feature is now improved further with visibility of the past transfers. Enabling to easily track all the previous changes.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FugLTEX227mf8T0W1z2vS%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b40a319f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#simplified-sorting-for-hr-separation-data)

Simplified Sorting for HR Separation Data

A filter has been added to the HR Separation Approval page where the HR can filter out the entries based on the combination of the filters defined making it even easier to sort the data and take action on the same.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FsuADmusyaHHkDauI2toP%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f07093f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvbOKtyZV1elw2X6Q5tQk%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cd4b18d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#convenient-filter-in-exit-tracker-report)

Convenient filter in exit tracker report

A filter has been added to the Exit Tracker report where the HR can further filter out the entries based on the combination of the filters defined making it even easier to sort the data.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhzPlzl2gl7GSR0eP8jAd%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=debbbc08&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FeEgqVuTvgkSx53RtNmIV%252Fb16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84b0667b-0f46-4b5e-bf80-cee0bfe720e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c01718dc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#enhanced-layout-for-exit-interviews)

Enhanced Layout for Exit Interviews

The Exit Interview Form has been improved with a panel-wise layout, making it easier for employees to fill out by organizing the questions in a clear, structured format.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fk8vvq3ayqwbSDwbIWgfS%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2eff3473&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhZtnKVxnb2EQ9yiJDYnl%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f99711ca&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#e-posh-empowering-action-against-harassment)

e-POSH: Empowering Action Against Harassment

The e-POSH (Prevention of Sexual Harassment) module is now available on web and mobile. It allows female employees to report sexual harassment incidents at the workplace, either for themselves or co-workers, with an option to keep their identity anonymous. A Complaint Committee can be set up, including a Committee Head and members, who can monitor and take necessary actions through the ESS portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWKgWZwvYwLhW9XaRwNE2%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfb2b8b8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3hOh5aDhE3UPSlt6fj4U%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78146958&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXUwLvHi8nuA6ETCqMFlp%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad2eff73&sv=2)

Simplify FnF with Department Filters

A new filter is added to the FnF Department Head Manager page, allowing you to filter entries by department. This makes it easier to manage and view information by department. The department name is now also displayed in the entries.

Display Last Working Dates for HR Approvals

Now the Last Working Date is shown to the HR while approving the separation entries based on the notice period, the employee's request, and the manager's approval. This enables HR to take quick and informed decision.

Streamline Employee Access


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We have introduced a new module named Employee Access. Here, the managers have been given an option to raise requests on behalf of their subordinates to grant or revoke access on various events like New Joining, Promotion, Separation, etc. Access forms can be created in Form Master and the requests can be raised by Managers in ESS and approved by the IT Team.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRcRk96ha5yma9Gfgqx7F%252FFrame%252097.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7616ad13-e800-47a5-857c-b7c8fac9aa48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67608cab&sv=2)

Key Insights in the Helpdesk Employee Report

The employee report in helpdesk has been enhanced by adding columns like:

*   **Response Received**: Shows when the first response was received after the ticket was created.
    
*   **Last Updated by (Code and Name)**: Displays who last updated the ticket.
    
*   **Last Updated Date and Time**: Shows when the ticket was last updated.
    

Providing comprehensive overview

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2024/october-and-november-2024#easily-copy-forms-across-companies)

Easily Copy Forms Across Companies

Admins and HRs can now copy form templates from one company to another within the same login. Multiple forms from a single module can be copied to several companies at once. For Exit Management and AccessForm modules, if the target company already has a form, the system will notify the user. This update significantly reduces manual effort in creating the same forms for different companies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAvIJu0467McjpasEcuD0%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a5e019f&sv=2)

Simplify CTC Creation with smHRt AI

Admins/HR can now use smHRt AI to easily generate the CTC Template and Annexure Table, or just the Annexure Table. The generated template can be edited, allowing changes to properties like font style, size, and headings.

Know Your Last Working Day at a Glance

# Payroll Maker Checker | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker#what-is-payroll-maker-checker)

What is payroll maker checker?

The Payroll Maker-Checker feature in Pocket HRMS software adds an extra layer of validation to the payroll process. It follows a dual-approval system where one user (Maker) prepares the payroll, and another user (Checker) reviews and approves it before processing.

This ensures accuracy, reduces errors, prevents unauthorized changes, and enhances compliance with company policies and regulations.

With role-based access controls, audit trails, and automated notifications, this module streamlines payroll verification while maintaining transparency and accountability.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker#how-to-give-user-rights-for-the-payroll-maker-role)

How to give user rights for the payroll maker role?

**Path**: Cloud Portal > Settings> Organization> User> ‘View User Rights’ > Category > Payroll > select required categories >Save

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal with admin credentials. Go to the ‘Settings’ menu and under the ‘Organization’ tab, click on the ‘Users’ subtab.

**Step 2**: Click the respective ‘View User Rights’ button for the user to whom you want to give the payroll maker rights.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1OZe3DdoK5w7zArubQhO%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ea500cc&sv=2)

**Step 3**: In the ‘User Rights’ pop-up, tick checkboxes for the required ‘Categories’ and ‘Payroll’ menu options and click on the ‘Save’ button. The user rights will be updated accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVt03rbfxc8giZwlh0p0u%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c067c054&sv=2)

**Note**: You can also [add a new userarrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/users#how-to-create-a-new-user-in-the-cloud-portal)
 if required.

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=organization&submodule=usersarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=organization&submodule=users)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c8bbbdb8b8a7babc88b8a7aba3adbca0baa5bbe6aba7a5)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker#how-to-give-user-rights-for-the-payroll-checker-role)

How to give user rights for the payroll checker role?

**Path**: Cloud Portal (Admin) Settings> Organisation> User> ‘View User Rights’ > Category > Payroll > select required categories >Save

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal with admin credentials. Go to the ‘Settings’ menu and under the ‘Organization’ tab, click on the ‘Users’ subtab.

**Step 2**: Click the respective ‘View User Rights’ button for the user to whom you want to give the payroll checker rights.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQkHGoOBIEIkcW9egMuux%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95c72f2&sv=2)

**Step 3**: In the ‘User Rights’ pop-up, tick checkboxes for the required ‘Categories’ and ‘Payroll’ menu options and click on the ‘Save’ button. The user rights will be updated accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2z5uHEGEClF9gPZ5Zy75%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0f9b39c&sv=2)

**Note**: You can also [add a new userarrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/users#how-to-create-a-new-user-in-the-cloud-portal)
 if required.

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=organization&submodule=usersarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=organization&submodule=users)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#added8ddddc2dfd9edddc2cec6c8d9c5dfc0de83cec2c0)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker#how-to-set-up-payroll-maker-checker-or-approval-matrix-for-payroll-maker-checker)

How to set up payroll maker checker or approval matrix for payroll maker checker?

**Path**: Cloud Portal (Admin) > Settings > Organization > Payroll Maker Checker > click ‘Setting Icon’ > select User, Priority > Save

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal with Admin credentials. Go to the ‘Settings’ menu, under the ‘Organization’ tab click on the ‘Payroll Maker Checker’ subtab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fk51OI6ENeDsa0ZXR5UMd%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa8fddd9&sv=2)

**Step 2**: On the Payroll Maker Checker page click on the ‘Settings Icon’ towards upper right corner of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FNosS8YOA5NfSvJX61RQM%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99ffce39&sv=2)

**Step 3**: ‘Select User’ and enter the ‘Priority’ and click on the ‘Save’ button. The approval matrix user priority will be sent accordingly.

The priority defined will be used to send the processed payroll for approval in that order. Once user with highest priority approves the payroll data, it will be posted.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbAcI0m4nkTQYFZCM8Wsx%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad56992c&sv=2)

**For example**,

*   Payroll data first goes to the Priority - 1 User, after their approval it goes to Priority - 2 User for approval.
    
*   If there is no Priority - 2 User, approval by Priority - 1 user will be considered final and payroll will be posted.
    

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=organization&submodule=PayrollMakerCheckerarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/Index?module=organization&submodule=PayrollMakerChecker%22%20\t%20%22_blank)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#daa9afaaaab5a8ae9aaab5b9b1bfaeb2a8b7a9f4b9b5b7)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker#how-to-submit-processed-payroll-data-for-approval-to-payroll-checker)

How to submit processed payroll data for approval to payroll checker?

After processing [payroll for employees in bulkarrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/payroll-with-attendance#id-5.-how-to-run-process-payroll-or-how-to-run-smhrt-payroll)
 or processing [payroll for a single employeearrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/faqs/cloud-portal/employee/employee-list/payroll#b.-how-to-run-payroll-for-a-single-employee)
, you can go to the smHRt payroll screen to submit payroll data for approval.

**Path**: Cloud Payroll (Payroll Maker) > Settings > Payroll > Utilities > smHRt Payroll > Click here to Send Payroll Data for Approval

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal with Payroll Maker credentials. Go to the ‘Payroll’ menu and under the ‘Utilities’ click on the ‘smHRt Payroll’ option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3JdtTYTsWHlcx7AJijbP%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c6c6626&sv=2)

**Step 2**: On the smHRt payroll screen once you process payroll, click the ‘Click here to Send Payroll Data for Approval’ button at the top of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtGSKsKdFz3N2pjn2up2G%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e84e8bf&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Select Month and year and click on the ‘Excel View’ button to check the processed payroll data on the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0ILf47jchGwGfcGmyb95%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b70e6c3c&sv=2)

**Step 4**: Ensure that the processed payroll data is correct, click the ‘Post’ button and it will be sent for the approval to the payroll checker.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWtCLu56IIWsSQoeXU071%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab4da1b3&sv=2)

**Note**:

*   Payroll data first goes to the Priority - 1 User, after their approval it goes to Priority - 2 User for approval.
    
*   If there is no Priority - 2 User, approval by Priority - 1 user will be considered final and payroll will be posted.
    

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/payroll/PayrollMakerChecker/PayrollApprovalRequestarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/payroll/PayrollMakerChecker/PayrollApprovalRequest)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9feceaefeff0edebdfeff0fcf4faebf7edf2ecb1fcf0f2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/payroll-maker-checker#how-to-check-and-approve-payroll-data-as-payroll-checker)

How to check and approve payroll data as payroll checker?

**Path**: Cloud Portal (Payroll Checker) > Payroll > Utilities > Payroll Approval > click Month-Year > check various payroll reports & data > Approve/Reject

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal with Payroll Ch ecker credentials. Go to the ‘Payroll’ menu and under the ‘Utilities’ click on the ‘Payroll Approval’ option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoRQSUP1VyVw562xlLaVT%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de972952&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Click the Month-Year towards the upper left side of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDIyznicWL5Kv4jzjCow7%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c9289c7&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Review the various reports and dashboard provided by system to verify payroll data and click the ‘Approve’ or ‘Reject’ button as required.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVUpCvJExAOrthZT1vdht%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26424e49&sv=2)

**Note**:

*   If approved, the payroll data will be sent to the next approver if available. Else, it will be posted into the system.
    
*   If click ‘Reject’ button you can enter your remark and click on the ‘Save’ button so the payroll maker can check your comment.
    
*   The rejected, the payroll will not be posted, and the payroll maker will have to re-process and send again for approval.
    

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/payroll/PayrollMakerChecker/PayrollApprovalarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/payroll/PayrollMakerChecker/PayrollApproval)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#fa898f8a8a95888eba8a9599919f8e92889789d4999597)

[NextCustom Working Hour Reportchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/feature-guides/custom-working-hour-report)

# Appraisal V2 | Pocket HRMS

Pocket HRMS makes the performance management experience seamless for both employees and the manager with simple steps.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/performance/appraisal-v2#appraisal-module)

Appraisal Module

In Pocket HRMS we are offering a Performance Management System. This module will allow you to do a performance review of your employees.

We can set performance reviews of the employees- on a monthly, quarterly, half-yearly, and on annual basis.

The appraisal process can be set to 90 degrees, 180 degrees, and 360 degrees by the employer.

*   90 degrees means the manager will rate the employees
    
*   180 degrees means the employee will rate himself and the manager will rate the employee
    
*   360 degrees means the employee will rate himself, the manager will rate the employee and peers will also rate the employee.
    

**We can set up the appraisal process in two different ways in Pocket HRMS.**

1\. You can have a predefined set of parameters and questions on which employees and managers can provide ratings.

2\. You can also allow employees to set their own KPI which needs to be approved by the manager so that the employee and the manager can provide ratings for the same.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/performance/appraisal-v2#configuration-of-the-appraisal-module-in-pocket-hrms)

Configuration of the Appraisal Module in Pocket HRMS

We can do the basic configuration by following the steps below.

**Step 1:** Select the ‘Settings’ menu in the cloud portal

**Step 2:** Click on ‘Appraisal V2’ from the top menu and then select ‘Appraisal Configuration’ from the left-hand side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FW6R3RU64LrMBRCqDwpXh%252FAppraisal%2520module%252020.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96ba360c-9f1f-4765-9510-2f8e9638d034&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b6d65fc&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Set the configuration as explained below:

A) Select the ‘Business Unit’ from the drop-down as Category, Department, or Designation.

*   You can also ask for a customized option.
    
*   Setting ‘Company Id’ means the same Appraisal will be set for all employees in the company.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgxJMzqYCWQ0BmqJFog1t%252FAppraisal%2520module%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D067f33a0-655c-4c99-b17f-a1b9fe64ec81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74dda304&sv=2)

B) Choose the Start date and End date as the requirement.

C) Select a value for ‘Completed Month’

*   The value ‘Completed Month’ allows you to decide the employment months that an employee has to complete for being eligible for the appraisal.
    

D) Select whether the ‘Rating’ is to be set for ‘Scale’ or for ‘Weightage’

E) Set ‘Final Rating Option’ as per your requirement

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FaVVq51l39V5aodZ1kKew%252FAppraisal%2520module%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d9858a6-cdb0-4de9-b1a3-7829866ab766&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4bea322&sv=2)

F) You can select the parallel review option as ‘True’ or ‘False’.

G) ‘Peer expiry days’ can be set as per requirement.

H) You can set ‘Dynamic Flow’ if employees want to set their own KPIs. The flow will go for their manager’s approval.

I) Set the criteria that the employee ‘Eligibility Based On’ according to company policy and requirements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/performance/appraisal-v2#settings-by-admin-or-hr-in-appraisal-module)

Settings by Admin or HR in Appraisal Module

Admin can add the different appraisal stages in Pocket HRMS.

Different appraisal cycles can be set under ‘Appraisal Stages’ such as, monthly, half-yearly, quarterly, and annual.

**Path:** In the ‘Appraisal’ module click on the ‘Appraisal V2’ and select the ‘Appraisal Stages’. Fill in the required fields and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fdv04enOWJhvEQZqHNnMb%252FAppraisal%2520module%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De856697f-bf8a-43ae-8bb6-0e61359da7d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc6ece7d&sv=2)

**Note**: Select 'Yes' from the 'IsActive' field so that employees will be able to submit their review from their ESS portal. If you select 'No', employees won't be able to submit their review for the appraisal.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/performance/appraisal-v2#setting-appraisal-parameters)

Setting Appraisal Parameters

**Path:** In the ‘Settings’ module, select the ‘Appraisal V2’ menu and click on ‘Appraisal Parameter’.

Here you can set multiple parameters with a total weightage of 100.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZYVaF3tWGStzZEAlysvF%252FAppraisal%2520module%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc90b8491-7fa2-45c1-aac5-fc28cf51d879&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6270f47&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/performance/appraisal-v2#setting-appraisal-questions)

Setting Appraisal Questions

**Path:** Go to the ‘Settings’ module, select the ‘Appraisal V2’ menu, and click on ‘Appraisal Questions’.

Fill in the details in the required fields to add questions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRjICwik2QqJCUlZXu6CX%252FAppraisal%2520module%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90f30eed-4c96-4188-846d-8329dda68cf0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b018204d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVscBOdAtSgElbtRZcJco%252FAppraisal%2520module%25206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ef2b6b2-9eab-43c3-a2b7-ea9c7189798e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb0c9390&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b8cbcdc8c8d7caccf8c8d7dbd3ddccd0cad5cb96dbd7d5)

# Payroll Guide | Pocket HRMS

The intuitive payroll module of Pocket HRMS makes it easier and compliant for any organization to process a monthly payout.

Calculation of salary components that include earnings and deductions like arrear, allowance, PTax, LOP, credits, loan, DA, HRA, etc. becomes hassle-free for the payroll department. You can anytime hold payroll for any employee or perform FnF with a click.

Salary payslips, deduction and earning formula creation, conditional earnings, etc. through Pocket HRMS make payroll processing a piece of cake.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide#this-section-will-cover-an-in-detail-guide-to-modules-as-follows)

# SMTP Settings | Pocket HRMS

SMTP (Simple Mail Transfer Protocol) is a setup useful in sending mails at an organisation. Be it internal mailing or external, your email client such as Outlook, Apple Mail, Mailbird, etc. runs on SMTP protocol to send e-mails to the right receiver.

The SMTP from TCP/IP protocol stores and forwards emails through network and prevents cross emails.

This section will help you learn the steps involved in setting up an SMTP protocol on Pocket HRMS.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/initial-company-setup-administration/smtp-settings#how-to-set-up-smtp)

How to set up SMTP?

**Step 1:** Log into the cloud portal, go to the 'Settings' menu and, under the ‘Organization’ tab, click on the 'SMTP Settings' sub-tab. To add new SMTP settings, click on the ‘+’ icon towards the upper left-hand side of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLb2ZfsvvHFjBy27MRNgi%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a86d6bb&sv=2)

**Step 2**: A pop-up will open where you need to fill in the details such as the ‘SMTP Server’, ‘Sender Name’, ‘Sender Email’, ‘BCC’, ‘Priority’ and other mandatory details in the respective fields. Click on the ‘Update Settings’ button and the SMTP settings will be saved.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6qBfF8OuN3MVOkfQv2o3%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b98ccb8&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Alternatively, to use the default SMTP settings, click on the ‘Add Default Settings’ button to autofill the values. Enter the ‘BCC’ value as required. Click on the ‘Update Settings’ button and default values will be saved for your organization.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FuE9FRjgGmMqeuf3wDke6%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1534235&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2d5e585d5d425f596d5d424e464859455f405e034e4240)

[NextTemplates Setupchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/initial-company-setup-administration/templates-setup)

# April 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fm9gFYJUB6O0QcTwzOBc1%252FApril%25202025.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3654eca6-23a2-4ec8-bdf4-3133a3f31759&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4678ad77&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of April 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#manager-details-included-in-reports)

Manager Details Included in Reports

We have updated a new feature where the leave, on-duty and regularization reports will include detailed manager-level information such as individual manager status, approval/action date, and remarks. Earlier, the downloaded report had limited data that reflected the approval status. However, in the new enhancement, user can view and track the multi-level approvals.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fag74W6e6w8K4LgSUk6hW%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2a2ab93&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#timestamp-for-leave-application)

Timestamp for Leave Application

The Leave Approval screen (Manager/Admin view) now shows both the date and exact time a leave request was submitted. Earlier, only the date was shown. This update gives approvers better clarity for making informed decisions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FNwEEjxTRkJH5QOXfLkGi%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87fc5c22&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#yearly-leave-credit-based-on-joining-date)

Yearly Leave Credit Based on Joining Date

Pro-rata and mid-joining leave credit, previously limited to monthly and quarterly frequencies, is now available for yearly leave credits as well. The new setting allows leave to be credited proportionally based on the joining date, or users can define a fixed leave credit for mid-joiners. The system will apply either method based on the selected configuration, offering more flexibility and fairness in leave allocation for mid-year joiners.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4fnzE6kINz7bBcoYvjTO%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f098235b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#late-mark-deduction-applied-across-all-shifts)

Late Mark Deduction Applied Across All Shifts

Earlier, late mark deductions were calculated separately for each shift assigned to an employee. Now, with the recent enhancement of unified late rule deduction, the late marks will be counted cumulatively across all shifts unlike separate deductions per shifts, ensuring fair and consistent deductions for multi-shift employees. This is powered by the Go Rule Engine for better flexibility and easier management.

**Example:**

**Before the update:**

An employee working 10 days in General Shift (allowing 3 late marks) and 10 days in Night Shift (allowing 4 late marks) would get a total of 7 late marks for the month before deductions.

**After the update (with new setting enabled):**

If the monthly limit is set to 4 late marks, the employee will be allowed a total of 4 late marks for the entire month, regardless of shifts worked. Any extra late marks beyond this limit will result in deductions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#enhanced-appraisal-report)

Enhanced Appraisal Report

The Appraisal Detailed Report now shows stage-wise data based on the configured settings. Only defined appraisal parameters appear in the PDF; undefined ones are excluded. If employee ratings aren’t part of the flow or not submitted, their details won’t show under the Evaluator section.

The report also includes the date and time of form submission by the employee and/or manager, depending on the appraisal flow. If the flow includes only the manager, then only the manager’s submission date and time will be displayed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fd6zqS3wXzfuBiBqmhSuH%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50fcfeec&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#external-trainer-tagging)

External Trainer Tagging

Now you can add/tag external trainer details to the learning programs. Earlier only internal trainer details were allowed for tagging however, in the recent enhancement enables uses to tag/add and tag external trainers to both learning programs and individual sessions. You can record key details of external trainers like name, email, contact number, and skills for better tracking and management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkoWZUl0Ts2oxHelMlCS0%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76a32321&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4PGWvuYpJR72JILCqLSW%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=535dc5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#revoking-learning-programs)

Revoking Learning Programs

The learning programs can now be revoked or unassigned to employees with the recent enhancement. Previously, learning programs could only be assigned and cannot be unassigned. The recent update enables admins to unassign upcoming learning programs either individually or in bulk before they begin. However, the learning programs that are in progress cannot be unassigned ensuring its consistency and continuity in the flow.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FxO3f1Mub32Jh3trD4rAM%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d857d65c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#survey-added-to-learning-programs)

Survey Added to Learning Programs

The Survey Module is now integrated with the Learning Module, allowing users to link feedback forms to each learning program. To set this up, choose the 'Learning Program Completion' event when configuring the form.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fj46z0z63nFKPfxWFkpbZ%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d42c228&sv=2)

If no form exists, you can create one directly from the setup screen. Once linked, the form will automatically be sent to employees after they complete their learning program. Employees can fill it out through the ESS Portal, and individual feedback reports are generated as PDFs. Admins can also download consolidated feedback reports in Excel or PDF from the ‘Training Reports’ section in the Cloud Portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fjs3txdurhh1hoayXUerI%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d977ed1b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6ZEfcL7hR3Ns3ScEWVoq%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf7008ea&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#benefit-module-added-to-approval-matrix)

Benefit Module Added to Approval Matrix

We’ve streamlined the approval process by integrating the Benefit Module with the centralized Approval Matrix. Previously, approval managers had to be added manually within the module. Now, you can easily configure and import approval managers directly through the Approval Matrix. This enhancement enables faster, more consistent, and priority-based approval setups—saving time and improving efficiency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAi36yWbqgfVqWP53EjYD%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=962a71f1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#rounding-adjustments-in-ctc-calculator)

Rounding Adjustments in CTC Calculator

We’ve added a Rounding Adjustment Component to all CTC Calculators in the Cloud to handle minor rounding differences that may arise due to decimal precision.

**How It Works:**

*   The Rounding Adjustment Component is available in every CTC Calculator.
    
*   It adjusts small rounding differences (typically between ₹3 and ₹6) that may occur when calculating CTC values.
    
*   These adjustments are automatically made in the Annual section of the selected component.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCiAzhShFqzhVpB5eFPXc%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=896c862d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOD6LSzoa6XUsdrbTYxWp%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edd830fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#assign-dedicated-hr-in-exit-module)

Assign Dedicated HR in Exit Module

We’ve introduced a new enhancement in the Exit Module to support the assignment of Dedicated HRs (DHRs) for employees.

**Key Highlights:**

*   **Dedicated HR Field**: A new field is now available in the employee profile, allowing the Head HR or Admin to assign a Dedicated HR to each employee.
    
*   **Separation Approvals**: When such employees submit a separation request, it will be routed to both the assigned DHR and Head HR for approval.
    
*   **Dedicated HR View:** DHRs have access to a new screen— ‘DHR Separation Approval Data’—which shows only the separation requests of their assigned employees (not company-wide data).
    
*   **Role-Based Access**: Access to this screen is controlled via Role Allocation and DHR assignment.
    
*   **Approval Logic:** The system will process the first approval received—either from the DHR or the Head HR.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fp5ZUVB4uCH5m6349Ksxn%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ba51e15&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#automatic-nps-rate-based-on-tax-regime)

Automatic NPS Rate Based on Tax Regime

A default NPS Rate deduction component has been added. It automatically limits the NPS rate to 14% for employees in the New Regime and 10% for those in the Old Regime. Admins/HR cannot change these limits. This component can also be used in other sections if needed. The restriction is applied when adding or editing employee details.

**Example:**

*   If an employee is in the New Regime, the NPS rate will be automatically set to 14%.
    
*   If an employee is in the Old Regime, the NPS rate will be automatically set to 10%. Admins/HR cannot update these rates beyond the set limits."
    

This feature ensures accurate and consistent NPS deductions based on the applicable tax regime.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FeFjgihHWHFLDVmKrSTKK%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e7c9b01&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/april-2025#re-hire-eligibility-during-employee-separation)

Re-Hire Eligibility During Employee Separation

An option has been added to mark an employee as eligible or not for re-hire during separation. When separating an employee in Cloud or ESS, Admin/HR can select ‘Yes’ or ‘No’ for re-hire eligibility and add mandatory remarks. These remarks will be shown when re-hiring the employee, helping Admin/HR make an informed decision. Additionally, the final settlement (FnF) remarks will also be visible during re-hiring.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fbjy91knewAigkeXk9ZDX%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef402176&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0675737676697472467669656d63726e746b752865696b)
