# smHRt Payroll | Pocket HRMS

Payroll process facility in Pocket HRMS enables seamless processing of smHRt Payroll for all employees, which can be done for a single employee, all employees, or selective employee in one go.

This document contains the following:

Prerequisites

*   Payroll Checklist
    
*   Working of smHRt Payroll
    
*   Payroll workflow with manual Income tax
    
*   Payroll workflow with updated Income tax declaration
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/smhrt-payroll#toc123304783)

Payroll Checklist

Below are the pointers that need to be checked before processing the payroll.

*   Whether the active and inactive employees are updated correctly as of the date in the portal or not.
    
*   Holiday applicability data are correctly updated.
    
*   Monthly input that includes the variables (earning / deductions) & extra duty payment details are correctly updated.
    
*   If we are processing the income tax manually, then the tax value needs to be updated through monthly input.
    
*   All the attendance regularization, on-duty & leave request needs to be approved/reject accordingly.
    
*   Increment details should be up to date in the portal.
    
*   All reliever leave requests received through the helpdesk module should be actioned.
    
*   Roster needs to be updated correctly for the particular month.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/smhrt-payroll#toc123304784)

Working of smHRt Payroll

Path: Cloud Login > Payroll > Utilities > SmHRt Payroll > Select Employees > Select Month & Options > Pre-process Check > Run smHRt Payroll > Save.

**Step 1**: In the Cloud portal select the ‘Payroll’ menu, then ‘Utilities’ tab and click on ‘SmHRt Payroll’ sub tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FcdzEEfDk7gOE4YO9pHmC%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0a18bd4&sv=2)

On the screen of ‘smHRt Payroll Process’ page you can see the payroll processing status of months in a year as described below.

*   Yellow Strip - If payroll processing in ongoing
    
*   Blue Strip - If payroll processing is completed
    
*   Grey Strip - If payroll is yet to be processed
    

**Step 2**: Selecting employees for payroll processing:

1.  Click on the ‘Employee Wise’ tab to enter employee code for a single employee or multiple employees.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzCJ0sDwteLMXIlNBg9Vs%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d82d03d3&sv=2)

1.  Select the ‘Selective Employees’ tab to process payroll according to various employee categories.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZyxVaBHXQlgjrDVdFW2Z%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=221d519c&sv=2)

1.  Click on ‘All Employees” tab to process payroll for all the employees.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMfPi6xUL2jupbci3vFUk%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1f603af&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Select the month and the year for which payroll has to be processed.

*   Time consolidation is used to run monthly attendance with all the prior settings
    

and it runs according to settings for a particular month.

*   Leave posting is used to process and post monthly leaves taken by employee for a particular month. It can be done with single employee as well as with a category of employees. After selecting this, the leave post will be reflected in the employee’s account.
    
*   Payroll Posting is done after the payroll for posting salary slips to individual user’s account. You can view the salary slip by logging in to the ESS portal.
    
*   Monthly input is used to give employee's salary details and any other deduction to be done for that particular month.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbRoA75EZ9CPPgwCpYPDd%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b9ca76&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Tick the ‘perform pre-process check’ (especially for doing the payroll for the first time) to identify any error in the following:

*   Formula
    
*   Configuration
    
*   Data Audit
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWCwLhR3nu7A0ahhV8EWW%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c723cb31&sv=2)

Note: You can click on the ‘Re-Process’ button to run payroll again with the same settings after making some minor changes in payroll-related data.

**Step 5:** On the right-hand side of the screen you should check whether all the parameters are checked for biometric attendance and then click on the ‘Run smHRt Payroll’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJBQoG9VY6WX33fTIObn1%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99c1101e&sv=2)

**Step 6:** You can click on the ‘Save’ button once payroll process is completed.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/smhrt-payroll#toc123304785)

Payroll workflow with manual Income tax

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/smhrt-payroll#toc123304786)

Prerequisites

Ensure that following tasks are done before proceeding to payroll processing.

*   All the monthly input that includes the variables (Earning / deductions) & extra duty payment details are updated.
    
*   Update the increment details for the particular month.
    
*   Income tax values for the particular month are updated.
    

**Step 1**: Freeze the attendance, process the time consolidation for the specific month.

1.  Click on the ‘Attendance’ menu and then on the ‘Transaction’ tab and then ‘Time consolidation all’.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fqukl3j42MesMCYJfLqPg%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f58e8a4e&sv=2)

1.  Select the month and year for payroll process
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3lN6bSaZKNswXADw9ItY%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=760a4452&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Download the generated attendance report to verify the frozen attendance.

Go to ‘Payroll’ then click on ‘Transaction’ and select ‘Time Consolidation All’ to Download the report.

**Step 3**: Process the payroll for the specific month.

1.  Select the ‘Payroll’ then click on the ‘Utilities’ tab and then next on the ‘Payroll process’ subtab.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFtjdMneQajo97HO2d0JL%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=222d050&sv=2)

1.  Select the month and year then select the categories and click on the ‘Process’ button.
    
    ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDj9nL5LLS2tRS4ybJwG8%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bc0108f&sv=2)
    

**Step 4**: Download the salary register.

1.  Click on ‘Analytics’ menu and then select the ‘Data-wizard’ sub-tab.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FE9PpA3axY4tETTOVv4FS%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=369902f2&sv=2)

1.  Click on the ‘Select Settings’ drop down menu then select the month & year and click on download button as shown below.
    

**Step 5**: Post the Pay slip to the ESS portal:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkYpYVHIMjRUxNZIShMkB%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4788cf4&sv=2)

1.  Select the ‘Payroll’ menu then on the ‘Utilities’ tab and the ‘Self-service Post’
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8g0jMgU0tLjSEKzhRqNN%252Fslf%2520srv%2520post.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf16e6bd-e43c-4aaa-a006-014b7890f6cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6068a36f&sv=2)

1.  Select the month & year and click on the ‘Post’ button.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FosAQrJHB93JGNEHTAthL%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=921267b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/smhrt-payroll#toc123304787)

Payroll workflow with updated Income tax declaration

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/smhrt-payroll#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Ensure that following tasks are done before proceeding with payroll processing.

*   All the monthly input that includes the variables (Earning / deductions) & extra duty payment details need to be updated in the system.
    
*   Update the increment details for the particular month.
    

**Step 1**: Close the declaration window for employees:

Click on ‘ESS Settings’ go to ‘Declaration Activation’ menu and then un-select all the check boxes and then click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVrorwObeOameGhicu2Kx%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2555ef48&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Import the tax declaration from the ESS portal through web post.

1.  In Cloud portal click on the ’Income tax’ then on the ‘Utilities’ tab and the ‘Web post’ subtab. Select the second option for importing the declaration values. Then select the month & year and click on the ‘Post’ button.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwEDeJZW1ueJ0U0E2ol5p%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bf3e347&sv=2)

1.  You can also follow path in Cloud portal click on ’Income tax’ then on ‘Utilities’ tab and ‘Web post’ subtab. Select the third & fourth options for importing the proof values & document respectively then select the month & year and click on the ‘Post’ button.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvvyCxdFWpKjEnLHMwMW3%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a6be4c5&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Freeze the attendance, process the time consolidation for the specific month.

Select the ‘Payroll’ and click on the ‘Transaction’ then the ‘Time consolidation all’ select the month & year.

**Step 4**: Download the generated attendance report to verify the freeze attendance.

Click on ‘Payroll’ select ‘Transaction’ menu and ‘Time consolidation all’ and download the report

**Step 5**: Process the payroll for the specific month

1.  Select the ‘Payroll’ go to the ‘Utilities’ tab and select the ‘Payroll Process’ subtab.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUj3uEK05SaxZkyqrhNge%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe42fc41&sv=2)

1.  Select the month & year and categories then click on the ‘Income tax’ checkbox and click on the ‘Process’
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0Imtcxj6ZPDFQhetskLu%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3ba1f03&sv=2)

**Step 6**: Download the salary register

Click on ‘Analytics’ then select the ‘Data-wizard’, click on the ‘Select the settings’ then select the month & year next, click on the ‘Download’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPZo1woqmTY8iDxyNGwv0%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5bba33a2&sv=2)

**Step 7**: Post the pay slip to the ESS portal.

A. Select the ‘Payroll’ then the ‘Utilities’ tab and then the ‘Self-service post’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWlDDUcuJjjGl2gXzvUtV%252FA.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D209905f9-239f-44f6-85ca-bb6aa2925d5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5b54031&sv=2)

B. Select the month & year and click on the ‘Post’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCBpcfLGydeMTHC6IcPjt%252FB.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56b8fc89-d843-41ac-af7a-641d5ad8fb45&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad0975ca&sv=2)

For any queries, kindly connect with us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#25414053565055554a575165554a464e40514d5748560b464a48)

# May 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5hclEC1X3ik1ocbOdS6l%252Fmay%25202025.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd11cdff-455c-42ac-9d4d-bdc993bd0df8&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42ae92e8&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of May 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#enhanced-weekly-off-upload-process)

Enhanced Weekly Off Upload Process

HR/Admin users can upload weekly offs in two ways: week-wise and date-wise, especially when weekly offs are set per employee. Earlier, only date-wise uploads were allowed. Now, users can:

*   Assign weekly offs in bulk using a week-wise format
    
*   Create reusable templates
    
*   Set custom date ranges
    
*   Map Excel columns easily based on format
    

Furthermore, the built-in checks ensure data accuracy, making the process faster and reducing manual work.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fe4HLcZILthEE0FKJ4YtZ%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=555b8330&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#shift-wise-data-now-available-in-monthly-summary)

Shift-wise Data Now Available in Monthly Summary

A new “Show Shift Details” checkbox is now available in the Attendance Monthly Summary Report. When HR/Admin selects it, the downloaded Excel will include each employee’s shift name by date, along with attendance details — making shift verification easier.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1C25IiK0MJMIXHeYWGJ9%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a9408fda&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFP0edAUvHmZcup46hvNu%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9352ae1e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#export-of-appraisal-parameters-and-questions)

Export of Appraisal Parameters and Questions

Admins can now export Appraisal Parameters and Questions in Excel format. The report is generated Business Unit-wise and Stage-wise, based on selected filters, and shows the details configured in the system.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC4rEIm9YcHVV1ZkVSkgX%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2f798c2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjUDUtoNIzrZ4wN6ccdC5%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7373f048&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#multi-trainer-setup-for-learning-sessions-and-enhanced-attendance-setting)

Multi-trainer Setup for Learning Sessions & Enhanced Attendance Setting

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#multiple-trainers-per-session)

Multiple Trainers per Session:

*   Earlier, only one trainer could be assigned to a session.
    
*   Now, you can assign multiple trainers to a single session.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#viewing-access)

Viewing Access:

*   All assigned trainers can view the session under their employee sessions tab.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#attendance-marking-rights)

Attendance Marking Rights:

*   Only one trainer (among the assigned ones) can mark attendance.
    
*   This avoids confusion and ensures only one accurate status (Present or Absent) is recorded.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMqmDYqaqoMGGtLlCCrEB%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fd9d0b0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#progress-monitoring-for-reference-materials)

Progress Monitoring for Reference Materials

Now you can track progress on reference materials in a learning program.

*   Admins can now add multiple reference documents while setting up the program from the Cloud portal.
    
*   Once published, employees can view these materials in the ESS portal under the assigned program.
    
*   Progress starts at 0% and updates as employees click “NEXT” on each material, marking it as read.
    
*   A progress bar shows how much has been completed (e.g., reading 2 of 4 files = 50% progress).
    

This helps both employees and managers monitor engagement and ensure assigned materials are read.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDnXUyfhIV2NzaRuauVrC%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47fa824d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSVDOaLRaFz1vfc22b0xG%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f374cbd1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#detailed-training-overview-report)

Detailed Training Overview Report

We’ve added three new training reports in the Cloud portal:

*   Training Master Report – Full training history with quiz scores and feedback
    
*   Employee Training Card Report – Employee-wise summary with average score
    
*   Training Progress Report – Real-time progress with % completed and time taken
    

You can filter by employee, training name, date, or learning type. Reports are available in PDF and Excel formats with the ease to track quiz marks, grades, feedback, and exam attempts, with color-coded bars to show progress at a glance.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fl7Im6NsiuGvaiKwYcgT1%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dce0d5e&sv=2)

**Training Master Report:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWyORo6zcJlwVVuklskkL%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4742d593&sv=2)

**Employee Training Card:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtcVcJ9vWE5mBsEIEuKqi%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfa853e7&sv=2)

**Training Progress Report:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGQYQMCBJFW1SiVGril4P%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=578def71&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#date-range-filtering-added-to-hr-reports-for-applied-and-expense-dates)

Date Range Filtering Added to HR Reports for Applied and Expense Dates

You can now select a date range for Applied Date and Expense Date in HR reports instead of just one day. This helps you view more entries at once and get accurate results within the valid date range.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#earlier-limitation)

Earlier Limitation:

*   Users could only select a single date for Applied Date and Expense Date, showing data for just one day.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#new-enhancement)

New Enhancement:

*   You can now choose a date range for both fields to view more expense records at once.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#validation-check)

Validation Check:

*   The selected range must be within the actual available dates to ensure accurate results.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7E4Ps8c406J2lv6Qo9U4%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30d5a008&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#track-active-inactive-employees-in-joined-list-report)

Track Active/Inactive Employees in Joined List Report

You can now easily track employee status in the Joined List Report with the added option to view active or inactive records. This enhancement improves visibility and helps in better workforce analysis.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#new-filter-added)

New Filter Added:

*   An Employee Status filter has been added to the Joined List report.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#filter-options-available)

Filter Options Available:

*   Active (Default)
    
*   Inactive
    
*   Both
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#purpose)

Purpose:

*   Enables users to generate the joined employee list based on the selected employee status for more targeted reporting.
    
*   Reports can be downloaded in PDF or Excel format.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7A6TitwEPaCGGr6xa1Zd%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b99f164&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/may-2025#new-separation-type-field-introduced-with-updated-labels)

New Separation Type Field Introduced with Updated Labels

A new field called Separation Type has been added to classify employee exit as ‘Voluntary’ (employee’s choice) or ‘Involuntary’ (otherwise).

The list of options like Resignation, Termination, Absconding is now called Separation Category, and reasons like Better Opportunity or Better Pay are now grouped under Separation Reason.

These options are available to HR during employee separation from both Cloud and ESS.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FsfX4x3zI8GwjYV3VJndf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D362ee201-1908-41df-b9bf-171c763fb1d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e6d5457&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#790a0c0909160b0d3909161a121c0d110b140a571a1614)

# October 2025 | Pocket HRMS

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of October 2025, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#unassigned-shift-and-week-off-email-trigger)

Unassigned Shift & Week Off Email Trigger

This feature automatically sends emails to managers based on Go Rule Engine settings.

*   **Unassigned Shift Alerts:**
    
    *   Sent daily within the configured date range (e.g., 17th–22nd of each month).
        
    *   Lists employees without assigned shifts.
        
    *   Sent to managers as per the Shift Schedule Approval Matrix.
        
    
*   **Week Off Alerts:**
    
    *   Sent after each week ends (Monday–Sunday).
        
    *   Lists employees without assigned week offs.
        
    *   Sent to managers as per the Leave Approval Matrix.
        
    

The email format can be customized in the **Email Template Setup**. Each email includes an **Excel attachment** showing the respective employees.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F9lG5SkERLbZ0Kdnj7B91%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=546ede36&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FfueuR0rvdiQf6jiaqFtO%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62e36381&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#master-absenteeism-report)

Master Absenteeism Report

The report can be generated for the full financial year, with filters for **Live**, **Separated**, or **All** employees. It shows a **month-wise count of absences** based on data from the Time Consolidation process. The report can be **downloaded in Excel, PDF, or Word format**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FpynECzphFjEBY7VnT99R%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2fb046ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#enhanced-permission-flow)

Enhanced Permission Flow

The **Permission Approval Flow** is now available under the **Leave module** for easier access. Managers can **approve or reject** permissions directly from **Leave → Approval**, instead of the Profile section.

Label updates for better clarity:

*   “From Hour – To Hour” → **Time-Based Permission**
    
*   “Single Hour” → **Hourly-Based Permission**
    

Status updates (Approved, Rejected, Skipped) appear **in real time**, and managers can add **remarks** while approving or rejecting.

Permission Configuration:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F62PKD6qLflnK8GKYznSe%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6efe05d4&sv=2)

Approval Time-based UI:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fgi4lSa4nahi2KvNrIDtt%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=819fef0a&sv=2)

Approval Hourly-Based UI:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FxYm7RjMFTuHoToXdnyrP%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=153e737e&sv=2)

View Details UI:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FiCmIbparc5SeXrvZ9cIq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d85125b-b02f-4afa-bbf0-e25229de860c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2535a48&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#final-rating-rounding)

Final Rating Rounding

This feature lets you **show final ratings as whole numbers** instead of decimals using a Go Rule Engine setting.

*   **Rounding logic:**
    
    *   Values ≤ 0.5 → rounded down to the lower whole number.
        
    *   Values > 0.5 → rounded up to the next whole number.
        
    

The rounded rating appears in both **Excel** and **PDF Detailed Reports** on the **ESS portal**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FRVzYLBDEGau6fYmlUyrC%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49f77658&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FtA1p1iIZFgAFRoHQpk9i%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c136b6a&sv=2)

A graph with text and numbers AI-generated content may be incorrect.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#expense-eligibility-override)

Expense Eligibility Override

*   A new **“Enable Eligibility Override”** option is added under **Expense Eligibility** in Cloud. When enabled, employees can **submit claims exceeding** the set limit.
    
*   A **confirmation pop-up** appears in ESS if the amount is higher than eligibility.
    
*   On confirmation, the claim goes to the manager for review. Managers see such claims marked with a **red upward arrow** and a tooltip showing the exceeded amount.
    
*   This ensures **flexibility for genuine claims** while keeping **approval control and transparency**.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fqyi9OivpEbdDYXGfI22t%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab616a3a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FDKPkw0Z99UD3uZGeRppX%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5de07b7a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FifkGBL1lx78vFXmCxVHu%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=391f4f2c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#bulk-expense-control)

Bulk Expense Control

*   A new **Expense Lock screen** allows admins to **lock or unlock expenses in bulk** for a selected date range. Locks can be applied by **Business Unit** and **Expense Type**.
    
*   When locked, employees **cannot submit claims** for that expense type until the period ends.
    
*   Added filters to view **All**, **Locked**, or **Unlocked** expenses.
    
*   Displays key details like **Business Unit**, **Expense Type**, **Lock Date**, and **Status**.
    
*   Added **“Select All Across Pages”** option to apply lock/unlock actions to all records at once.
    
*   This update saves time and ensures **faster period closures** with **better control** over expense data.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FueDupMOYQMQmiqNLK7ek%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=939db15a&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer AI-generated content may be incorrect.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#control-joining-document-access)

Control Joining Document Access

Added a new checkbox **“Show document on ESS and Mobile App”** in the Joining Document window. It is **checked by default**, making documents visible to employees on both platforms.

*   HR/Admin can **uncheck** it to hide specific documents.
    
*   Existing documents can also be updated to change their visibility.
    
*   This gives HR/Admin **better control** over which documents employees can view during onboarding.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Ffqu7w6QKex50qzilpWUJ%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5560346a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#random-quiz-feature-in-learning)

Random Quiz Feature in Learning

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#current-behavior)

**Current Behavior:**

*   All learners can view and attempt every question in a quiz.
    
*   There is no option to randomize or limit the number of questions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#enhanced-behavior)

**Enhanced Behavior:**

Added a new field **“Randomized Quiz Set”** in the quiz configuration. Trainers can set how many questions (out of the total) each learner will see.

Example: If a quiz has 5 questions and the value is set to 3, only 3 random questions will appear. The system automatically selects the questions at random for each learner. Learners see only the randomly chosen questions in their ESS portal.

This update gives trainers **more flexibility**, creates **varied quiz experiences**, and makes learning **more dynamic**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5stf8Qgpp6DooV7zVeXX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df81a7bec-8c81-4c09-bd67-dea76ab96729&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b74eeb67&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlmrF5s9Ppnj2szco2Hky%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D753333e3-c9d7-428c-9360-493cf8146611&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4d4cc55&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#flexible-fnf-no-dues-trigger)

Flexible FnF No Dues Trigger

Added new trigger option Earlier, FnF started **only after separation** (default). But now, HR/Admin can choose when to trigger **FnF No Dues**:

*   *   **On Employee Separation** (default)
        
    *   **On HR Approval** (after HR approves separation)
        
    *   **X Days before LWD** (auto-trigger before last working day)
        
    

**smHRt Recommended:** Use **“X Days before LWD”** for smoother and faster closure.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FwPzmRLiz9d5vJCt8LoEc%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8baaa453&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer AI-generated content may be incorrect.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FLvP6ZaxNIpiGUGUmRsDP%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4dc49423&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#external-cc-in-make-an-offer)

External CC in Make an Offer

Added a new field **“Additional CC Email ID(s)”** in the **Make an Offer** window. Recruiters can now **add external CC recipients** while sending offer letters.

*   **Multiple email IDs** can be entered, separated by commas.
    
*   All added IDs will appear in the **CC section** of the offer email.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FP3poBtsbEyiQY9IufpOD%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8e87b60&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#additional-salary-details-field)

Additional Salary Details Field

Added a new text field **“Additional Info / Salary Benefits”** under **Apply Job** in:

*   **Candidate Creation (ESS – Recruiter view)**
    
*   **Career Portal (Candidate view)**
    

Used to mention **allowances, bonuses, or special benefits**. Helps capture **complete compensation details** during job application.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FX4tmcjbXPDYbHsbcNnrf%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2c80949&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer AI-generated content may be incorrect.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F4CPRDHC1H9JO0KqZxwf0%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1679d94&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer AI-generated content may be incorrect.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/october-2025#ess-disable-setting-after-separation)

ESS Disable Setting After Separation

Added a new control to set **when employee ESS and Mobile App access is disabled after separation**.

Options available:

*   **After X Days:** Access auto-disables at midnight after the set number of days.
    
*   **Instantly:** Access is removed immediately upon separation.
    

Applies to separations from both **ESS and Cloud**. HR can **override the default setting** while processing a separation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fy9MGWbkVT0UzeJ4Ae9Su%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73906d33&sv=2)

A screenshot of a chat box AI-generated content may be incorrect.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FeRrrXU4v0jr5Bo0kCxjb%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1640cf8e&sv=2)

A screenshot of a computer screen AI-generated content may be incorrect.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJ28PwUA1FxhVvxxjqUss%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ba0b010-fbb9-4b40-8671-8b88e010179e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fc19ba0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FmBE2xwzgRCgXhL5puhdS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f62f274-259f-4942-8661-22dc294450c8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d2a2e7e&sv=2)

# Recruitment Setup | Pocket HRMS

Pocket HRMS makes employee recruitment management very easy with required modules at same place. Below are steps involved in configuring recruitment template.

**Step 1:** Go to 'Settings'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDoaZoqHie65LtnIYx%252F-MYDpXlOD_RsDIK7LtcZ%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df96ebe4f-ec18-4b76-8773-abdc28622e90&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d29b6697&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Proceed to 'Recruitment' column.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDoaZoqHie65LtnIYx%252F-MYDp_oBdhoDGOm_U90J%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c223499-58e2-4b67-9f41-658594ec9412&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c432e204&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Recruitment Location' to create new location for hiring process. After editing details, click on 'Save'. You can anytime edit/ delete and enter new address details.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDoaZoqHie65LtnIYx%252F-MYDpcnvJKz8wK8adCLu%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da86925de-4abc-466e-9955-c8756f24a080&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eee53fe8&sv=2)

**Step 4:** 'Career Page' allows you to configure recruitment career page using color theme and layout as required. After selecting required parameters, click on 'Save'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDoaZoqHie65LtnIYx%252F-MYDpfWmjcN9jYmKYnsq%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69c7f492-6c08-4835-bec0-94873ddb9d1a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e26aa16&sv=2)

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to set up recruitment module, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#dfacaaafafb0adab9fafb0bcb4baabb7adb2acf1bcb0b2)

# Device Lock | Pocket HRMS

In the ever-evolving landscape of workplace technology, the need for secure and accountable employee punch systems has never been more critical. Ensuring the integrity of attendance records and preventing unauthorized access are paramount for any organization's operational efficiency and trustworthiness.

In this, we delve into the implementation of an advanced device lock mechanism that not only registers devices seamlessly but also acts as a robust gatekeeper against potential security breaches. From the initial setup of a new device to the prevention of cross-device and cross-employee punch attempts, we explore how organizations can fortify their employee punch systems for a secure and accountable workplace.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/device-lock#how-to-do-settings-for-device-lock-on-a-cloud-portal)

How to do settings for device lock on a cloud portal?

Go to the ESS Setting menu from the left-hand sidebar and under the ‘Profile’ tab click on the ‘Global Settings’ subtab. From the ‘Device Lock’ drop-down click on the ‘Yes’ to activate the device lock function.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0d72rBc0GAH9Sn9PiAT8%252FDevice%2520Lock%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D378f5c33-90e6-4d15-b398-d08f93b4c8a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=459b18b0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/device-lock#how-to-do-initial-device-registration)

How to do initial device registration?

When the new user logs into their ESS app and clicks on the punch button in the unregistered device for 1st time this popup will display i.e. “To punch in, you must first register your device” After clicking on the ‘Submit’ button the device will get registered with this Emp ID and the user can punch after that.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwfwiFFs9mDk3LM4e6ap5%252FDevice%2520Lock%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff18d346-173b-41ca-9983-cd59394f2443&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb0c48bb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/device-lock#preventing-cross-profile-punch-attempts)

Preventing Cross-Profile Punch Attempts

Pocket HRMS registers a profile with a device when a person attempts their first-ever punch. So, when someone tries to punch from a new device for a profile registered with another device they will get a pop-up display i.e. ’Raise a device reset request?’

Once an employee clicks on the ‘Reset’ button, an HR/Admin will receive a notification to reset the device with that employee ID.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWlQqfGVvYEN87hC7v5bv%252FDevice%2520Lock%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2122b73d-3923-4ade-a193-cf129db8b0bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=329d19a8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/device-lock#how-to-reset-employee-device)

How to Reset Employee Device?

When an HR receives a notification for employees request to change their registered device they can easily do that from the ‘Device Lock’ screen. For that log into the cloud portal with the Admin portal and click on the ‘ESS Settings’ from the left-hand side menu bar.

Under the ‘Leave’ tab click on the ‘Device Lock’ subtab. You can use the ‘Search’ to find the employee and unique device registered with it. Once you click on the ‘Reset’ button the system will unregister the present unique device ID, essentially resetting the device connection or association.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fyl7DtID57pU2vAyWEg5A%252FDevice%2520Lock%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ed480a1-7b95-42d0-8604-6174d857bf8e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11059c9d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/device-lock#how-does-the-system-stop-cross-device-punch-attempts)

How does the system stop cross-device punch attempts?

If an Employee attempts to punch from a device that is registered with another Employee ID the system will not allow them to punch and will show a pop-up i.e. “Device already registered with another account. Use the different device for punch”.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUfDLJAtedsAiJDtD76gX%252FDevice%2520Lock%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf6f9055-dd3a-4777-a6ed-74468b4593c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d267d866&sv=2)

[PreviousProfile Infochevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info)
[NextRole Allocationchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/role-allocation)

*   [How to do initial device registration?](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/device-lock#how-to-do-initial-device-registration)

# Self Service Role | Pocket HRMS

Integrated self-service portal helps in empowering employees. Pocket HRMS based ESS system allows you to check pending leave approvals, payslips, upcoming events, track reimbursement, etc. on your own.

The admin can easily set up and activate employee self service portal through dashboard. Once, employee profile is successfully created and added to the dashboard, the admin can follow below mentioned steps to receive login credentials for ESS portal.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/setup-and-activation#how-to-activate-self-service-log-in-for-an-employee)

**How to activate self-service log in for an employee?**

**Step 1:** Go to 'Employee'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDjeVMcZXWOjvjVBAG%252F-MYDk6T3OL1v9qvpz0Mr%252F1%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69ceefbb-d719-4f45-a4f4-a5941381fdd8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae64e5c9&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Follow 'Employee' > 'Employee List'

**Step 3:** Select your employee by clicking on their profile or 'Employee Filter' as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDjeVMcZXWOjvjVBAG%252F-MYDk9z7pFysatzVdM-y%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdc6643d-7722-4e2f-8837-debf51342803&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b93657b6&sv=2)

**Step 4:** After the employee profile appears, find 'Self Service Role' option as shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDjeVMcZXWOjvjVBAG%252F-MYDkDWMAHkd-CPh3RIz%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b074487-8419-4913-9f88-cd68b306e6ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d214a311&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Now, select the role of the employee and click on 'Save'. Upon confirmation, you will get a default password for self-service portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDjeVMcZXWOjvjVBAG%252F-MYDkGUqTcTlYmkCoM4y%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11a31968-db4a-454a-8225-13ef9a8c5369&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffc973e0&sv=2)

Ask employee to login with the new generated password along with company code & Employee code detail

**Path**: Cloud>Employee>Employee List>Profile>Self service Role>Save

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Employee/employee/Profile?employeeID=10941&module=employeepunch&empstatus=1arrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Employee/employee/Profile?employeeID=10941&module=employeepunch&empstatus=1)

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to setup ESS account for employees, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#fc8f898c8c938e88bc8c939f979988948e918fd29f9391)

# Employee Access Workflow | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#employee-access-workflow)

Employee Access Workflow

**The "Employee Access" module in Pocket HRMS transforms the HRMS from just a data storage system into an active platform that manages IT resource access and provisioning for employees.**

Employee Access Module in **Pocket HRMS** helps your organization:

*   Automatically provide IT assets to employees (Laptop, Email ID, VPN etc.)
    
*   Modify access when employees are promoted or transferred
    
*   Revoke access when employees resign or exit
    

Instead of manually informing IT team through emails or calls, the system will:

*   Raise request
    
*   Get approvals
    
*   Notify IT team
    
*   Maintain records of issued assets
    

All within Pocket HRMS itself.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#configuration-of-employee-access-in-cloud-portal)

Configuration of Employee Access in Cloud Portal

**Path:** Cloud > ESS Settings > Profile Info > Employee Access control > Fill in details such as Enabled/disable Employee Access Form, Create or Edit Access form by clicking on Form Master > Click on Add to Add Access Form Scenarios/Triggers > Save

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Cloud portal**, navigate to the **‘ESS Settings’** module from the main menu and Select the **‘Profile Info’** tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FgYQcogD1eNa8BbZdISm3%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0ba6ddd&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Then click on **‘Employee Access Control’**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FojvfvYTozu6OerIH099r%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bec7f19&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Toggle the settings to **Enable** or **Disable** the Employee Access Form as needed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FIqaLW6JIdilCRovwuxUQ%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f473274&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Click on **‘Form Master’** to create a new access form or edit an existing one.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FStdVqpRoUeXANiaHVc5N%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9480d8c&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Click the **‘Add’** button to set up specific **Access Form Scenarios/Triggers** (e.g., triggering an approval workflow when an employee updates their address).

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FkpIAs89Re1jBMm1SO1iK%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52f86bcd&sv=2)

**Step 6:** Click **‘Save’** to apply your new configurations.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FBxjqXhuOFwsdPQoIUcMD%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2b2ce65&sv=2)

**Link:**[**https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=EmployeeAccessControl**arrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=EmployeeAccessControl)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#managers-role-allocation-for-employee-access)

Manager’s Role Allocation for Employee Access

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#managers-role-cloud-portal)

Manager’s Role: Cloud Portal

**Path**: Cloud login > ESS Settings > Profile info > Role Allocation > Module (Profile), Role (Manager) > Search > Enable Employee access by ticking on the same > Save.

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Cloud portal**.

**Step 2:** Navigate to the **‘ESS Settings’** module from the main menu. Select the **‘Profile Info’** tab, then click on **‘Role Allocation’**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FgYQcogD1eNa8BbZdISm3%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0ba6ddd&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FY3pK3LaSsZjV4HXxihgm%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=906bdbd8&sv=2)

**Step 3:** From the dropdown, select **‘Profile’** from the Module dropdown and **‘Manager’** from the Role dropdown. Click **‘Search’** to pull up the specific permission settings for that role and module.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FPcwvd0BqHA7Zil5ijC6E%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de6b6b54&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Locate the **‘Employee access’** setting in the generated list and enable it by ticking the corresponding checkbox.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Ft2019U5qdlEAGB4jz57U%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9e9fd0d&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Click **‘Save’** to apply the new permissions to all users with the Manager role.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FK86fbwiQjz8I8KIBGqw0%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=128e07ba&sv=2)

**Link:**[https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=RoleAllocationarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=RoleAllocation)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#managers-role-ess-portal)

Manager’s Role: ESS Portal

**Path:** ESS > Profile > Employee Access > Manager

**Step 1:** Log in to the **ESS portal** using your manager credentials.

**Step 2:** Navigate to the **‘Profile’** module from the main menu. Select the **‘Employee Access’** section.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F9heeTL2u0thimJ1L2emU%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4369386&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Click on the **‘Manager’** tab or view. This will display the list of employees reporting to you and the specific profile information you are authorized to access or edit.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FCGE1891hBpT1GW1og27R%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b50ae65&sv=2)

**Link**: [https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Profile/EmployeeAccess?Menu=Requestarrow-up-right](https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Profile/EmployeeAccess?Menu=Request)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#it-personnel-role-allocation-for-employee-access)

IT Personnel Role Allocation for Employee Access

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#it-role-cloud-portal)

IT Role: Cloud Portal

Path: **Path**: Cloud login > ESS Settings > Profile info > Role Allocation > Module (Profile), Role (IT) > Search > Enable Employee access by ticking on the same > Save.

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Cloud portal**.

**Step 2:** Navigate to the **‘ESS Settings’** module from the main menu. Select the **‘Profile Info’** tab, then click on **‘Role Allocation’**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FgYQcogD1eNa8BbZdISm3%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0ba6ddd&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FY3pK3LaSsZjV4HXxihgm%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=906bdbd8&sv=2)

**Step 3:** From the dropdown, select **‘Profile’** from the Module dropdown and **‘IT’** from the Role dropdown. Click **‘Search’** to pull up the specific permission settings for that role and module.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F3KBoAgXFnBTuP1whoZUF%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc4e09f0&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Locate the **‘Employee access’** setting in the generated list and enable it by ticking the corresponding checkbox.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FkIXRhe5x7YhQKgBkQeIY%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab6c68f8&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Click **‘Save’** to apply the new permissions to all users with the Manager role.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FGO7FHPGim0l4KvMI3Vk3%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=282cd688&sv=2)

**Link:**[https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=RoleAllocationarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Settings/Employee/ESSIndex?module=Profile&submodule=RoleAllocation)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/ess-setting/employee-access-workflow#it-personnels-role-ess-portal)

IT Personnel’s Role: ESS Portal

**Path:** ESS > Profile > Employee Access > IT

**Step 1:** Log in to the **ESS portal** using your manager credentials.

**Step 2:** Navigate to the **‘Profile’** module from the main menu. Select the **‘Employee Access’** section.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F9heeTL2u0thimJ1L2emU%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4369386&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Click on the **‘IT’** tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FgG42DuS4pt0ak0zkfdPT%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94e93081&sv=2)

**Link**: [https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Profile/EmployeeAccess?Menu=Approvalarrow-up-right](https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Profile/EmployeeAccess?Menu=Approval)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f3808683839c8187b3839c909896879b819e80dd909c9e)

# Pocket HRMS Payroll Process | Pocket HRMS

**Pre-requisites:**

✔️ Admin credentials

✔️User rights

_Note - Kindly contact your Admin/ HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/pocket-hrms-payroll-process#how-to-process-payroll)

**How to process payroll?**

Pocket HRMS also allows you to perform payroll for selective employees like any category or all employees in one click. Explained below are the steps involved in payroll processing.

Path: Cloud Login > Payroll > Utilities > SmHRt Payroll > Select Employees > Select Month & Options > Pre-process Check > Run smHRt Payroll > Save.

**Step 1**: In the Cloud portal select the ‘Payroll’ menu, then ‘Utilities’ tab and click on ‘SmHRt Payroll’ sub tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FcdzEEfDk7gOE4YO9pHmC%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0a18bd4&sv=2)

On the screen of ‘smHRt Payroll Process’ page you can see the payroll processing status of months in a year as described below.

*   Yellow Strip - If payroll processing in ongoing
    
*   Blue Strip - If payroll processing is completed
    
*   Grey Strip - If payroll is yet to be processed
    

**Step 2**: Selecting employees for payroll processing:

1.  Click on the ‘Employee Wise’ tab to enter employee code for a single employee or multiple employees.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzCJ0sDwteLMXIlNBg9Vs%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d82d03d3&sv=2)

1.  Select the ‘Selective Employees’ tab to process payroll according to various employee categories.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZyxVaBHXQlgjrDVdFW2Z%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=221d519c&sv=2)

1.  Click on ‘All Employees” tab to process payroll for all the employees.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMfPi6xUL2jupbci3vFUk%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f1f603af&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Select the month and the year for which payroll has to be processed.

*   Time consolidation is used to run monthly attendance with all the prior settings
    

and it runs according to settings for a particular month.

*   Leave posting is used to process and post monthly leaves taken by employee for a particular month. It can be done with single employee as well as with a category of employees. After selecting this, the leave post will be reflected in the employee’s account.
    
*   Payroll Posting is done after the payroll for posting salary slips to individual user’s account. You can view the salary slip by logging in to the ESS portal.
    
*   Monthly input is used to give employee's salary details and any other deduction to be done for that particular month.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbRoA75EZ9CPPgwCpYPDd%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b9ca76&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Tick the ‘perform pre-process check’ (especially for doing the payroll for the first time) to identify any error in the following:

*   Formula
    
*   Configuration
    
*   Data Audit
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWCwLhR3nu7A0ahhV8EWW%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c723cb31&sv=2)

Note: You can click on the ‘Re-Process’ button to run payroll again with the same settings after making some minor changes in payroll-related data.

**Step 5:** On the right-hand side of the screen you should check whether all the parameters are checked for biometric attendance and then click on the ‘Run smHRt Payroll’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJBQoG9VY6WX33fTIObn1%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99c1101e&sv=2)

**Step 6:** You can click on the ‘Save’ button once payroll process is completed.

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to process payroll, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ccbfb9bcbca3beb88cbca3afa7a9b8a4bea1bfe2afa3a1)

[PreviousLOP Settingschevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/payroll-guide/lop-settings)
[NextIncrementchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/increment)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

# New Company | Pocket HRMS

This option allows you to create a NEW company on the dashboard. Pocket HRMS dashboard can have multiple companies with unique user rights and configuration. The configuration may include salary structure, attendance system, leave rule, etc.

This module of initial setup and administration will help you learn the step-wise procedure to set up and configure new companies on the dashboard.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/initial-company-setup-administration/new-company#how-to-create-a-new-company)

How to create a new company?

**Step 1:** Go to 'Settings'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MY4f1bCFM2vGwUDHH7Z%252F-MY4heG0rQbbwJzvmSUa%252Fnew%2520company%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a76168e-a077-4031-8b75-93607258717a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30d3c08a&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Proceed to 'Company Profile' and click on the '+' sign as shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MY4f1bCFM2vGwUDHH7Z%252F-MY4hjFD-7gtWuJxFwR1%252Fnew%2520company%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c88d4ae-9033-4f6c-a91e-899593e3f6ef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f8714b6&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Upon clicking on the '+' button, a screen asking basic information about the new company will pop-out. Fill in the details like Company name, Company address, Self Service Company Code, and Telephone. Click on 'Create Company'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MY4f1bCFM2vGwUDHH7Z%252F-MY4iLsdgMI2W9T-u_IH%252Fnew%2520company%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70116f04-1d2a-4d35-b4cb-83b88e09affe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2e5a8ed&sv=2)

Now you have successfully created a new company on your dashboard in Pocket HRMS.

_**Note:**_ _If you see any error or need personal assistance in creating a new company, find us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a9dadcd9d9c6dbdde9d9c6cac2ccddc1dbc4da87cac6c4)

[PreviousCompany Setupchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/initial-company-setup-administration)
[NextCategory & Pop-upschevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/initial-company-setup-administration/category-and-mandatory-pop-up-components)

# HR | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr#id-1.-how-to-upload-form16-for-all-employees)

1\. How to upload Form16 for all employees?

Follow the steps below to upload Form 16 for all employees.

*   Download Part A and Part B of Form 16 from TRACES
    
*   Prepare the Files
    
*   Use the Utility to Upload Form 16
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr#step-1-download-part-a-and-part-b-of-form-16-from-traces)

Step 1: Download Part A and Part B of Form 16 from TRACES:

*   Log in to **TRACES** using the employer credentials (you’ll need the TAN login).
    
*   Go to the ‘**Downloads’** and click on the ‘**Form 16’** option.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwlMBJXyjF8392EAYhsBN%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41bd6038&sv=2)

*   Download **Part A** and **Part B** of Form 16 for each employee **without Digital Signature**.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fi3sqWZGULC9xYgxOzjwQ%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b327a06&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr#step-2-prepare-the-files)

Step 2: Prepare the Files:

*   Ensure both Part A and Part B are correctly downloaded in PDF format
    
*   Keep the **digital signature dongle** ready
    
*   Make sure the files Part A files and the Part B files are saved in the separate folders.
    
*   PAN number should be updated for all the employees in the Cloud portal.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr#step-3-use-the-utility-to-upload-form-16)

Step 3: Use the Utility to Upload Form 16:

*   Once you have Part A and Part B are ready, you can let us know to use the utility.
    
*   ‘Select Company’ for ‘Part A’ and ‘Part B’ select folders from the respective fields and click on the ‘Sign And Upload’ button.
    

**Note**: For utility installation, we recommend using a system where the digital signature is already installed.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3RuvYTEJaCR4QLxWShYR%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe907233&sv=2)

*   We will update the utility to upload the Form 16 documents to the employee portal, so employees can access them directly **from their ESS portal**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr#path-for-employees-to-access-their-form-16)

Path for employees to access their ‘Form 16’

*   Employee can log into the ESS portal, go to the ‘Profile’ menu and click on the ‘My Tax Details’ submenu
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSWN0FAkAV1dGwIqsJsv6%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1961e5fe&sv=2)

*   Click on the ‘From 16’ tab and the Form 16 can be downloaded from here.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAb7l7nZAhRjHMeOjHp3T%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1fbf5f3&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2c5f595c5c435e586c5c434f474958445e415f024f4341)

[PreviousUserschevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/organization/users)
[NextTransfer Settingchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr/transfer-management)

Last updated 1 month ago
