# Loan Management | Pocket HRMS

Pocket HRMS software allows you to provide loans to your employees. It can be included as a regular deduction component to their salary.

An admin or HR can select or deselect interest application on a loan. If the admin chooses to deduct loan installment along with interest, the employee then needs to provide monthly installments plus the interest amount.

Whereas, Pocket HRMS dashboard makes it very easy to apply and configure loans for employees and admin respectively.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/loan-management-process#pre-requisites)

Pre-requisites:

✔️ Admin credentials

✔️User rights

_**Note**_ _- Kindly contact your Admin/ HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/loan-management-process#how-to-allow-loan-request-for-employees)

**How to allow Loan request for employees?**

**Step 1:** Go to 'Settings'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB57iajeS4QFQgMDr4%252F1%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db20f6922-81a2-4302-b0ef-5b8611c94f20&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12c91f38&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select 'Payroll'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5FyXtidoExiOeHpZ%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D171dcf73-84ad-48f1-a7b8-d1fb846d8643&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6da00ba2&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Proceed to 'Salary Components' and select 'Deductions' from deduction details as shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5K6i_N4xpHpHTD2w%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8c8c439-d772-45ea-8a8c-c4b5088025d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aca91cf6&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Find 'Loan Deduction' under the deductions column

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5UT6sku1RSX_rvlm%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab6a4d88-7711-45b8-9ac8-a51b95b04b33&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6b35150&sv=2)

**Step 5:** After selecting loan deduction, a page - Field Details & Behavior will open. Fill in the required details and check 'Installment' to allow or disallow loan requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5YRKaeohPCMdsBza%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daab2bd70-e6ca-43bc-82b0-2896fb0ad23e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5288f025&sv=2)

After successfully filling in details, click on 'Save'.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/loan-management-process#how-to-add-a-new-employee-loan)

**How to add a new employee loan?**

**Step 1:** Go to 'Employee'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5aglga39Q9KFEOaB%252F1%2520%281%29%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def5354a6-9bc1-4ec7-8b15-0db81fe6ab25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9c21153&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Follow 'Employee' > 'Employee List'

**Step 3:** Select your employee by clicking on their profile or 'Employee Filter' as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5gI6mCvoDD-t0-9Z%252F1%282%29%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e2c8f51-4c2f-4c04-aabd-a38301a033f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16467d19&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Once the loan applicant's/ employee's profile opens, proceed to the 'Payroll' column.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5koG8Z337f356r19%252F3%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f7aaafd-623e-4292-b508-a72f59f712b9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=365bc80&sv=2)

Now, a page showing loan details will appear. Here you can add new details by clicking on '+' button as shown in the screenshot below.

**Step 5:** Fill in the details like loan date, apply year and date, loan amount, and number of installments. After you have entered all the required data, click on 'Save'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB4FTaQxI0xQR0gZzM%252F-MYB5oStwkHDRdnInhOB%252F4%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc703c125-ffcc-43a7-a3c6-13b11657ed5e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=282ccacb&sv=2)

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to manage loans, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#8af9fffafae5f8fecafae5e9e1effee2f8e7f9a4e9e5e7)

[PreviousIncrementchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll/increment)
[NextIncome Taxchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/income-tax)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Timesheet | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/timesheet#employee-timesheet-report)

Employee Timesheet Report

Using the ‘Employee Timesheet Report’ admin or HR can view the employee’s timesheet data and download it using filters. The reports are available in Excel format and can be downloaded according to Project, Task, Status, Client, and Date.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/timesheet#process-for-timesheet-management)

Process for Timesheet Management

It starts with the employee submitting a ‘Timesheet Entry’ through ‘Timesheet Request’. Their manager will receive the request and can approve or reject it accordingly. In case, there is no manager for the timesheet module, the entry will be auto-approved.

**Path for Employee Report**

ESS > TimeSheet -> EmployeeTimesheetReport > Employee TimeSheetReport

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVwonaA0TqFLOaGnUsHwM%252FTimesheetReport.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bd80be7-ab89-453b-ab39-910364f0574e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0b41eb&sv=2)

Multiple Filters Available to Download Timesheet Reports

1.  Project-Wise Hours Worked Report
    
2.  Project-Wise Employee Worked Report
    
3.  Employee-Wise Project Hours Worked Report
    
4.  Employee Wise Hours Worked Report
    

Also, Admin or HR is able to download All Employee ‘TimeSheetReport’ without any filter.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fw6TldufWdMvDsM1sQpAP%252FTimesheetReport1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8b71092-7eb2-4156-accf-c3e592f25280&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31baa8f0&sv=2)

Here we are going to know about All Employee Timesheet Report in detail

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/timesheet#all-employee-timesheet-report-without-any-filter)

All Employee Timesheet Report without any filter:

Here is the Timesheet report of employees where Admin or HR is able to see All Employee Timesheet Details including Project, Task, Status, Employee Details, Approver Name, and more.

You can see the Project details with respective Tasks and the total time required to complete that task. It also shows the Status of the task and the respective Approver Name.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FxbvIQYxIsI9YQqpYzCuQ%252FTimesheetReport2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7eb8cb2f-56ba-4cdc-b792-627a036d1718&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50f6d2d8&sv=2)

1.  Project-Wise Hours Worked Report:
    

Using Project-wise Hours worked report Admin/HR can map data such as:

• Working hours taken by various projects

• Status of the respective project

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyCrIJnSMx4TLKj9Rfoi9%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbf0f9f5-65d8-4cd1-af7f-b22d91cd0f12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8c610fc&sv=2)

1.  Project-Wise Employee Worked Report:
    

Using Project-wise Employee Worked Report Admin/HR can map the following data

• Various employees working on a particular project

• Working hours by respective employees

• Status of that project

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6SFXjpeR3uED0LFBlDBg%252F22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1999fe3-99fb-4eb1-9dbb-63b6f99f469e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=872e00c&sv=2)

1.  Employee-Wise Project Hours Worked Report:
    

Using the Employee wise project hours worked filter Admin/HR can track the employee tasks.

The Report gives brief information about

• The project that a particular employee is working on • Working hours spent on that particular project

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fjcq5qZd36PrOFVVELWr1%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd504272-2b59-48eb-9332-5156f54278ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5814449f&sv=2)

1.  Employee Wise Hours Worked Report:
    

Using Employee Wise Hours Worked Report Admin/HR is able to see the data of employees with respect to their Working Hours which are entered by employees in the timesheet.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0RB13FF9PHaja3aR4cIa%252F44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a926e3d-d7e7-4369-9a59-924dc4ebd79c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f443c0a&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to view or approve the timesheet entries, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ff8c8a8f8f908d8bbf8f909c949a8b978d928cd19c9092)

[PreviousProjectchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/project)
[NextFnF HRchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/fnf-hr)

# Exit HR | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/exit-hr#how-to-respond-to-employees-resignation-separation-request-as-an-hr)

How to respond to employee’s resignation/Separation Request as an HR?

As an HR you can take following actions for employee separation request.

*   Respond to Employee Separation Request
    
*   Generate Exit Interview Form
    
*   Send No dues form for various departments
    

Log into the ESS portal and click on the ‘Exit’ menu followed by ‘Separation’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ffr4uRWvY8deaBoML1Ob3%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad1abb09&sv=2)

Click on the ‘HR Separation Approval’ tab. HR can also change the last working date for the employee, the employee and other stakeholders will be notified about it.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FO0eT9fd8kIUpnAWAZHzk%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=becbbde6&sv=2)

You can select the checkbox to open exit the interview form for the employee.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIT4Tt5B3et9Y8MQ2hCQt%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b81856df&sv=2)

Now when employee will log into the ESS portal they will see the exit interview form.

Once employee fills the form you can find it under the ‘HR Separation Data’ tab and download Interview Report in Excel and PDF format.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHpE3wGeQbObIdQpyQGJo%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b227ff3&sv=2)

Click on the ‘Details’ button and ‘Separation Data’ Pop-up will open,

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtWFV441TP0DLtcN1MI3n%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d38128ae&sv=2)

Check box for the respective asset to release the asset from the employee. Click on the ’Withdraw’ button to withdraw the resignation. You can change ‘Separation Status’, add remark and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyPTlo4AMKtTgFeoUM4t4%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93541034&sv=2)

Once you click on the save button no dues form will be sent to various departments.

[PreviousFnF HRchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/fnf-hr)
[NextHelpchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/help)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Asset Management | Pocket HRMS

Pocket HRMS provides comprehensive Asset Management to upgrade your experience and give you greater efficiency. This guide provides step-by-step instructions and intuitive interface to simplify asset management and ensure streamlined processes and enhanced productivity.

With the help of this guide, you will learn how to create, categorize and assign assets to employees, and generate detailed reports tailored to your organization's needs.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr/asset-management#how-to-add-asset-category)

How to add Asset Category?

Log into the pocket HRMS cloud portal and click on the ‘Settings’ menu and click on the ‘HR’ tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FEUu2h2UAVqOSt47k2lfn%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f9dce29&sv=2)

Scroll down to select the ‘Asset Info’ submenu to view asset categories.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoT8E27AidhVDrmeSeFUj%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f20199b8&sv=2)

Under asset info you can see existing asset categories and click on the ‘+’ to create a new asset category.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FuM5DIVXS8GGzn4IourZG%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a46d1a80&sv=2)

An ‘Asset Info’ pop-up will appear where you need to enter ‘Title’ and ‘Notification Email’ to create a new asset category. That way you will experience systematic asset management. A notification will be sent to this email every time an asset is assigned to an employee, the person in charge will always stay updated.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FxNumZx0pFhDXwljZ6Qy8%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20bcaab9&sv=2)

Once you click on the ‘Save’ button a new category will be created which will automatically appear under ‘Asset Info’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FsohAuKYbtDX3WGC6yxtr%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5300a8a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/hr/asset-management#how-to-add-assets)

How to add Assets?

To view all the assets in the company you need to click on ‘Settings’ menu and under the ‘HR’ tab and click on the ‘Asset List’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDH7mKmqsECf5NsIwunsF%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ac00c26&sv=2)

If you want to create a new asset you can click on the ‘+’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FkKMGK3nSy3gNE8F2NjC4%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e61be0b5&sv=2)

‘Update Asset’ pop-up will appear which allows you to enter various details about the asset.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F69VmcizB4LJ5IQzGJwLn%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3e34d0f&sv=2)

Choose an asset category from the drop-down so you can add a new asset under it.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fg6a232kgKiBkDR2avBt3%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5049bc33&sv=2)

You also need to enter the details such as ‘Asset Name’, ‘Asset Tag’ and ’Model Name’. This makes every asset unique and helps to easily identify the asset.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUhsJ5yvyXU0YQyXCkX2R%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66ecd63&sv=2)

You can select the ‘Asset Status’ from the drop-down. You can also segregate assets here depending on whether it is broken or have been requested which further improves the asset management process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0Xd2L5nvK3uPkJcc3mLq%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6df2c758&sv=2)

You can also add details such as ‘Serial Number’ and ‘Vendor Name’ to further increase accuracy.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFLaetqR1i7zoXJLV9O3y%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81cadcae&sv=2)

You can also add ‘Purchase Date’, and ‘Default Location’ and also add specific ‘Description’ for the asset if you want. In addition to that you can easily ‘Choose File’ from your computer if you want to ‘Upload Image’ and ‘Attach Invoice’ so, you will ‘Save’ all the essential details at the same place.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ft1ievjFvzXouRpLKm1xN%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=98a94d44&sv=2)

[arrow-up-right](https://youtu.be/Sw-9cnShW4c)

# March 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FGwodnhFtrKoslRt0Exqc%252FMarch%25202025%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ebb38c3-8b42-41bd-96dd-53c8c23d1d15&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c28cebd&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of March, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#quick-attendance-summary-now-in-in-out-reports)

Quick Attendance Summary Now in In-Out Reports

We’ve added a new ‘Show/Hide Summary’ checkbox in the In-Out Details report. When turned on, it shows a clear summary of key attendance data like:

*   Total working hours
    
*   Leaves taken
    
*   Late arrivals and more
    

The summary changes automatically based on the date range and what you’re viewing—whether it’s one employee, a team, or multiple employees. It helps you understand the numbers better and tooltips are available with extra info for each metric.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHmZXoIvuRqkEV8Ny8UX5%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6f3d61d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#advanced-leave-tracking-with-smaller-deductions)

Advanced Leave Tracking with Smaller Deductions

We've improved the leave deduction system to allow for more flexible options. Now, leave can be deducted in smaller incremental portions, 0.25 or 0.75 days based on your company’s leave policy. This update helps ensure leave records are more accurate and better aligned with your organization’s rules. It also works smoothly with attendance and payroll systems, so everything stays in sync.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#apply-on-duty-for-multiple-dates-all-at-once)

Apply On-Duty for Multiple Dates—All at Once

Now user can apply on-duty for multiple dates and also choose the Day Type for each selected date in one go. Based on this, the system will automatically pick the right shift timings.

In addition to that for Night Shifts, there’s a new option to set whether the ‘To Time’ should be considered for the same date or the next day. This gives you more control over how night shifts are managed and saves you time and effort.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8ra6QgnJVhbjT1WRM3rE%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1498f24e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#set-sequence-for-appraisal-questions)

Set Sequence for Appraisal Questions

Now through ‘Order Number’ field, you can set appraisal questions in specific order to be shown in ESS Portal. This makes the appraisal process more organized and easier to follow.

You can assign order numbers while uploading questions in bulk, and the system will keep everything in the right order automatically.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhcP7TkHV99sQHNVD6i6P%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c79a2557&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIswcjSWi4UCnsDI1psXN%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44115ae3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#boosted-accuracy-in-shift-and-punch-management)

Boosted Accuracy in Shift & Punch Management

This enhancement ensures that attendance punches are accurately captured and assigned to the most appropriate shift, while also incorporating flag-based punch recognition for improved attendance management.

**Smarter Auto-Shift Assignment**

When a punch doesn’t match any shift, the system now uses reverse logic to assign the most suitable one.

It checks shifts in order and assigns the first one where punch time is before the shift’s start time.

This works regardless of the existing auto shift detection settings.

For Example:

Punch is at 14:43

Shift A- (08:00–10:00): Punch is after → skipped

Shift B- (20:00–23:00): Punch is before → Shift B → assigned

**Improved Accuracy with Flag-Based Punches**

Instead of just using the first IN and last OUT, the system now reads flag data from punches. This helps in more accurate shift mapping and reporting.

**Better In-Out Punch Import**

Once a shift is assigned, the system records the actual punch time as IN, even if it’s outside the shift range.

OUT time is calculated based on the assigned shift’s logic.

For Example: (continuing the above example)

Assigned shift is ‘Shift B’

IN punch: 14:13 → Recorded as IN

OUT: 08:07 AM (based on shift logic)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FjmjTTvb9xU1Tj1V7l6B6%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21e953d5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#speed-up-with-bulk-delete-for-appraisal-parameters-and-questions)

Speed Up with Bulk Delete for Appraisal Parameters & Questions

Earlier, users had to delete Appraisal Parameters and Questions one by one, which took a lot of time. Now, with our new bulk delete option, users can select and delete multiple Appraisal Parameters and Questions items at once. This improves efficiency by making the process faster and much easier.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FptmUDfnsFrbB4DEajxuE%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bab16465&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fu7MwESn4Tp1CFgliiRev%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ea193e3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#effective-news-display-with-ess-pop-ups)

Effective News Display with ESS Pop-Ups

Now the news updates will be displayed in the pop-up window, so employees won’t miss them in the ESS portal. That ensures that employee gets the updates instantly. Admins can check and select the news items as well as control how and when the news is shown through the settings from the cloud portal. Ensuring that the news is delivered to employees appropriately.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFfSBww8pPZm7Bcq3bWkg%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b071e251&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2hD54VTHQ8TVDRItinj3%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f21d2abe&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#smart-consent-upload-and-review-files-with-ease)

Smart Consent: Upload and Review Files with Ease

Previously, employees couldn’t upload files in the consent settings. Now, we’ve added a file upload feature. This lets employees view the attached document before giving their acknowledgement on the ESS portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJlntoPZ0hMEGnSPa8DM6%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1f2d82d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fk109t65x9t3qrd4zABkv%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4182a135&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#approval-matrix-manager-now-more-insightful)

Approval Matrix Manager: Now More Insightful

The Approval Matrix Manager screen has been updated with some helpful new features that give all the relevant information at a glance

*   **Created Date:** You can now see when each approval entry was added, making it easier to track them.
    
*   **Module Name:** Each entry now shows which module it belongs to, like Attendance Regularization, Daily Working Hours, or Earning Deduction, so it's clearer.
    
*   **Company Info:** Shows if an approver is from the same company or a different one, helping you understand the workflow better.
    
*   **Search & Filter:** A search bar lets you quickly find entries by employee name, module, or priority.
    
*   **Action Buttons:** You can now easily add, export, or delete entries with the new buttons, making the tool more user-friendly.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F61xgDWkU2lK8Yd5devNG%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b31827f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#keep-emails-relevant-exclude-employees-with-ease)

Keep Emails Relevant: Exclude Employees with Ease

A new feature lets administrators choose specific employees and the types of emails to exclude them from. In other words, which employees should not receive certain email notifications. Admins can configure multiple exclusion rules, based on employee’s role, department and specific needs. This helps HR teams send the right messages to the right people, keeping communication focused and relevant.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyyuMm9JJJS1fzzCRkXhd%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fcf5228&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZmfxUixyeP9E21QbD1hE%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8390e5e6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#easily-filter-and-export-finance-data)

Easily Filter and Export Finance Data

Now can can filter finance reports more easily with the new employee-based filter options and export this information. Here is how you can do that.

*   **Choose key employee information**: Bank Account Number, Blood Group, Branch, Category, Employee ID, Cost Centre, Department and Designation.
    
*   **Set your own filter rules:** Use AND/OR conditions to combine filters. Also, you can add multiple filters easily with the ‘Insert Row’ option.
    
*   **Export Your Data:** Search, view, and export the filtered results to Excel.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnZeo585oUSCtl7AhUULN%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7bcac024&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/march-2025#everyone-notified-every-step-of-the-exit)

Everyone Notified, Every Step of the Exit

Multiple new reminder events have been added to the Exit Notification Settings. Employees will now get automatic email alerts for each event. Admins and HRs can also set up email notifications for others involved—like Managers, HRs, and Department Heads—making the exit process smoother and more organized.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fw9PfeNtIpkUUigthILWd%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fbbc1c8&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#45363035352a373105352a262e20312d3728366b262a28)

# Currency Option | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/hire/currency-option#id-1.-currency-option-for-salary-ctc)

1\. Currency Option for Salary (CTC)

A new currency selection feature has been added, allowing you to choose the preferred currency before entering Current and Expected CTC values. It helps organizations capture salary details in the currency they actually use. This will further help global teams to enter pay in the right currency.

By default, the system continues to display values in **INR**. However, users can now select alternate currencies before entering Current and Expected CTC amounts. Additional currencies can be enabled for your organization with consultant support. Please contact us in case you need more flexibility or currency option in your system.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/hire/currency-option#how-to-set-currency-option)

How to Set Currency Option?

You can view and set the currency option through two different paths:

1.  When Candidates sets it for self.
    
2.  When HR/Admin Sets it
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/hire/currency-option#hlk208323914)

When Candidate Sets Currency Option:

Candidates can set the currency option for self by following the path below:

**Path:** Visit the Company’s Career Page > Apply for your desired Job > Fill in the details > Proceed > fill details > change the currency option > Apply.

**Step 1:** Visit career page, click on ‘Apply’ for your desired Job. Then it will take you to job application page, fill in all the details (Name, Dob, email, etc), and click proceed. Then, change the currency option and click on ‘Apply’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlSY0lkjtSSoThnX8L5X6%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c619e88&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FOB2Fx0NJS35msFUy9v6V%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e5c2cdd&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9qyEUyq5eyE2v7mN9q0r%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8d8f4aa&sv=2)

**Link**: Career Page of your Company

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/hire/currency-option#when-hr-admin-sets-currency-option)

When HR/Admin sets Currency Option:

Follow the path below when. HR/admin/recruiter sets the currency:

**Path:** ESS login > Hire > Candidate > Candidates> Edit Icon > Apply for Job > Change the currency option > save.

**Step 1:** Login to ESS portal, go to ‘Hire’ menu, and select ‘Candidate’ sub-menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FHMBGBvvRqJW1z30F9Jvr%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2cd2133&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Candidates’ tab, and click on the ‘Edit icon’ below the employee card.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLWH3GeGwPRT1VJhrdxZ6%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8369914&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the ‘Apply for Job’ option and change the currency option as per your requirement. Then click on ‘Save’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDtz7oIE5XGmATQkSFMaZ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4998acd&sv=2)

**Link:** [https://ess.pockethrms.com/Recruitment/Transaction/Candidate?Menu=EditCandidate&CanId=1511arrow-up-right](https://ess.pockethrms.com/Recruitment/Transaction/Candidate?Menu=EditCandidate&CanId=1511)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/hire/currency-option#where-will-be-currency-option-visible)

It will be visible in two places:

1.  In Candidate Profile

1.  Candidate Cards (Candidate List Page)
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fps9nu1EyUMgBKfpKmjgl%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93a1aa6f&sv=2)

# January 2026 | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#product-update-january-2026)

Product Update January 2026

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#auto-comp-off-expiry)

Auto Comp-Off Expiry

Earlier, the comp-off lapse had to be processed manually through a separate screen. This has now been automated. Based on the configured lapse days, eligible comp-off balances will automatically expire after the defined period, removing the need for manual action and ensuring timely and accurate balance updates.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F1O37wg62W363IoNIgxsC%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21556fdd&sv=2)

**Comp off Lapse Days Configuration:**

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fsz2gyu5QKX6eocK7iqsb%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=753d784b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#leave-balance-extraction)

Leave Balance Extraction

The Leave Balance screen now includes a Download (Excel) option. Earlier, users could only view team leave balances on the screen. With this update, managers and HR users can export leave balance details to Excel for easier review, sharing, and offline record-keeping.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FHjMCGJSt7zDCRbIS4ja5%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16dd796&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#manager-break-shift-report)

Manager Break Shift Report

The Break Shift Report in the ESS Portal allows managers to view and download break-shift attendance details of their direct reporting employees.

Managers can select one or multiple employees, choose an optional date range, and generate the report in either of the following formats:• Alternate In/Out Punches• Dedicated In/Out Flags

If no employee is selected, the report includes all employees under the manager. If no date range is selected, all available data is considered.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FpNSxFpXNSpuKLTfiAg2m%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c972107c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#unpunched-report-email-upgrade)

Unpunched Report – Email Upgrade

The Continuous Unpunched Report email has been enhanced to include more employee details when someone has not punched in for three consecutive days.

In addition to Employee Code and Name, the email now also shows:• Reporting Manager Name• Location• Department• Category

This helps stakeholders quickly identify the employee and take necessary action without checking the system separately.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FnShx1EIRk9V7MPFfKTlI%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b57d67d6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#pms-stage-activation-alert)

PMS Stage Activation Alert

A new notification feature has been added in PMS to inform employees when a stage becomes active in the workflow. Once a stage is activated, the system automatically notifies the relevant employees, ensuring better visibility, timely action, and smoother communication throughout the PMS cycle.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F1QmVErV292vJ8Od6dSgC%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf9641b1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#custom-event-notifications)

Custom Event Notifications

*   Added configurable email and ESS notifications for key events like Profile Updates and Device Reset Requests.
    
*   Automatically informs HR, approvers, and employees when an action is triggered or completed.
    
*   Prevents unnoticed profile changes and pending device reset requests.
    
*   Reduces manual follow-ups and dependency on HR calls.
    
*   Minimizes attendance and payroll issues caused by delays.
    
*   Improves transparency, response time, and overall employee experience.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FLkgboZcXizRZ0Zq0fgnG%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d26c4010&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FiYhTy6pi2kFkOy26Y9ot%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa98787&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2026/january-2026#draft-option-for-travel-and-reimbursement)

Draft Option for Travel & Reimbursement

*   Added a **Save as Draft** option for Travel and Reimbursement Requests, allowing employees to save entries without submitting them.
    
*   Employees can partially fill details and continue later without losing data.
    
*   Draft requests are shown separately under **Drafted Entries**.
    
*   Employees can edit or delete drafts before final submission.
    
*   Only complete requests are submitted to approvers, reducing errors and rework.
    
*   Improves flexibility, accuracy, and overall user experience.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F51uuMyPGFWnqiNMIPLQj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d7c4138-a55f-4019-86a0-1300d4c566b8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbcc671b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPWvHs91ZzlF0z7QDMdFW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03f9cd4e-f667-431e-81e5-eb6f07bc9d81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f805400&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FlGPcvLFlPhe82dEALtE0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f036c4b-6b67-4d0b-91b9-a52198968ad8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b8e0c46&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9eedebeeeef1eceadeeef1fdf5fbeaf6ecf3edb0fdf1f3)

# Income Tax | Pocket HRMS

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/analytics/report/income-tax#id-2.-how-to-download-export-income-tax-declaration-details-report)

1\. How to download/export income tax declaration details report?

Before downloading any TDS or Tax reports make sure the default year is set correctly for the year you want to download the report. Follow the process in the link mentioned below to change the default financial year.

[![Logo](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Ficon%252FsgcFodd2iFFEXCwR0BrQ%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9c622b4-4b96-4e1e-8d75-1127189759bd&width=48&height=48&sign=5c056a2b&sv=2)Income Tax | Pocket HRMSdocs.pockethrms.comarrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/faqs/cloud-portal/settings/income-tax#id-8.-how-to-change-the-default-financial-year)

**Path**: Analytics>Reports>Income Tax>Declaration Details Export>select Category/Month>Entry Type (Declaration/Proof)>Select Tax Section as required>Export Excel (download)

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal, go to the ‘Analytics’ menu and click on the ‘Report’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7D4FjTVKYGDdjcuQjVgv%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec67cf57&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Under the ‘Income Tax’ tab, click on the ‘Declaration Details Export’ submenu. Select the details such as Category, Month, Year, Entry Type (Declaration/Proof) and Tax Section from the respective fields as required and click on the ‘Export Excel’ button and the income tax declaration report will be downloaded accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoL5Frld5HOglbjbIVOJi%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ca69a2e&sv=2)

**Link**: [https://www.figma.com/design/mSQQU8o4zS2R7dCDfR1GPu/Shital?node-id=991-9&node-type=frame&t=sZol1t5zcNcrOrU7-0arrow-up-right](https://www.figma.com/design/mSQQU8o4zS2R7dCDfR1GPu/Shital?node-id=991-9&node-type=frame&t=sZol1t5zcNcrOrU7-0)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9deee8ededf2efe9ddedf2fef6f8e9f5eff0eeb3fef2f0)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/analytics/report/income-tax#id-8.-how-to-download-income-tax-proof-details-report)

2\. How to download income tax proof details report?

Before downloading any TDS or Tax reports make sure the default year is set correctly for the year you want to download the report. Follow the process in the link mentioned below to change the default financial year.

[![Logo](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Ficon%252FsgcFodd2iFFEXCwR0BrQ%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9c622b4-4b96-4e1e-8d75-1127189759bd&width=48&height=48&sign=5c056a2b&sv=2)Income Tax | Pocket HRMSdocs.pockethrms.comarrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/faqs/cloud-portal/settings/income-tax#id-8.-how-to-change-the-default-financial-year)

**Path**: Analytics > Reports > Income Tax > Declaration Details Export > select details > Proof > User/Authorised Entry > tick ‘Tax Section’ > Export Excel

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal, go to the ‘Analytics’ menu and click on the ‘Report’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FQxNfl3aUOpwstem0Emkr%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bc9e0441&sv=2)

**Step 2**: under the ‘Income Tax’ tab, click on the ‘Declaration Details Export’ subtab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoEdJ2TtvOKBgvVmHq39S%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43000f6c&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Select Category, Month, Year, Proof, User/Authorized Entry options as required.

Tick the checkboxes for the ‘Tax Section’ as required and click the ‘Export Excel’ button and the report will be downloaded accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXlPVs3tkBUjbTZQyKX4B%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b68f7852&sv=2)

**Note**: Proof entry is available only in the Excel format and not in PDF format.

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Reports/Report/Index?module=incometax&submodule=DeclarationDetailsExportarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Reports/Report/Index?module=incometax&submodule=DeclarationDetailsExport)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e89b9d9898879a9ca898878b838d9c809a859bc68b8785)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/analytics/report/income-tax#id-10.-how-to-check-the-income-tax-declaration-in-one-excel-sheet-for-the-all-employees)

3\. How to Check the Income Tax Declaration in One Excel Sheet for the All Employees?

Before downloading any TDS or Tax reports make sure the default year is set correctly for the year you want to download the report. Follow the process in the link mentioned below to change the default financial year.

[https://docs.pockethrms.com/faqs/cloud-portal/settings/income-tax#id-8.-how-to-change-the-default-financial-yeararrow-up-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/faqs/cloud-portal/settings/income-tax#id-8.-how-to-change-the-default-financial-year)

To download the income tax declaration of all the employees in one Excel sheet, please follow the below path:

**Path:** Cloud > Analytics > Report > Income tax > Declaration detail export > Fill in details such as category, month, year, entry type (declaration), at least one selection from the ‘Tax Section’> Click Export Excel.

**Step 1:** Login to ‘Cloud portal’, go to ‘Analytics’ menu, and select ‘Report’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKoztuf0YzSIQZzf5nKfW%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7f4dc83&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Income tax’ tab, click on ‘Declaration Detail Export’, fill in details such as ‘Category’, ‘Month’ (for which you want the declaration Excel), ‘Year’ (for which you want the declaration Excel), ‘Entry Type’ (click on radio button of declaration), at least one selection from the options in ‘Tax Section’ and click ‘Export Excel’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDBbuMLKJvmrbXkK5Hw5Z%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d6b4425&sv=2)

**Note:** You can find the Excel file in the download location of your system.

Link:[https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Reports/Report/Index?module=incometax&submodule=DeclarationDetailsExportarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Reports/Report/Index?module=incometax&submodule=DeclarationDetailsExport)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e2919792928d9096a2928d818987968a908f91cc818d8f)

# April 2023 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9dzb1isv6jpHrJfwcXIQ%252FPocket%2520HRMS%2520Monthly%2520Updates%2520%285%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D855eafc6-25d0-4569-9d58-061dd74d69bd&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24a32d1d&sv=2)

Pocket HRMS Product Update April 2023

Pocket HRMS has always been committed to consistent improvement. This April we present you our latest updates that will improve your user experience further.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-1.-employee-joining-insights)

1\. Employee Joining Insights

The month-wise joining chart in Pocket HRMS provides a visual representation of the number of new employees who joined the organization every month in graphical format.

Makes it easier for HR to grasp information and asset trends quicker so they can take suitable action. For example, they might discover that certain months consistently have higher turnover rates, prompting a closer look at onboarding or retention strategies.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYF0jZX9QQVp6NTeCvOHf%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68af61e0-60c0-4acd-a035-a86a7ec9c93b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=618ef76b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-2.-viewing-increment-records-easily)

2\. Viewing Increment Records Easily

These new fields allow HR to easily view details related to the last incremented date, the month in which the last increment occurred, and the effective date of the increment. This improved visibility helps HR professionals stay up-to-date with critical employee compensation data.

The 'Increment Register' feature allows HR to download all incremented data in a structured format saving time and effort.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F5KRUCgmOzTcBUzU8xpWt%252F2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3448d99c-cc93-4917-9ba7-c56f1e9cc0cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6516447c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-3.-personalise-tickets-priority-and-status)

3\. Personalise Ticket’s Priority and Status

When the ticket is created, the user is redirected to the ticket information page as shown below. On this page, the user can change the priority and status of the ticket according to their requirement. The user can see the agent assigned to the ticket. The user and agent can also communicate with each other regarding the issue.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1TjJJaYGFtnkjHWP11JH%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d44326e-2718-47a3-be80-48fae80ceaeb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d44844c&sv=2)

*   Coming back to the My Ticket List page, the open tab shows the list of all the tickets raised by the employee. The status will be shown as either open, in progress or reopen. Similarly, the closed tab shows the list of tickets having the status as resolved and closed.
    
*   The user can also filter the tickets using the filter option and get the data according to their requirements such as Ticket ID, Title, Status, Priority, and Tag Name.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FeDdBCx0xKjLaDj9kizbs%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1f17f78-e38f-471f-bed8-d4fb46012183&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b70e36f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-4.-convenient-bulk-asset-mapping)

4\. Convenient Bulk Asset Mapping

The bulk asset mapping feature in Pocket HRMS allows users to map multiple assets to multiple employees. This feature is designed to save time and effort by avoiding the need to map assets to each employee separately. It's a powerful tool for HR professionals, allowing them to efficiently manage assets and streamline their workflows.

Note: If it is available, it will fill all the fields automatically. If you have multiple devices in the same category you can select the asset name to write a note for it and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwgH7KSt7NN1AfOZtspHw%252F4.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc690fff6-b1dd-44fe-8063-0c6005d56b5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21cd94dc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-5.-enhanced-assets-history)

5\. Enhanced Assets History

We added new functionality in the employee module in which users would see ‘Assets History’. HR will have better visibility into the history of assets assigned to employees. This enhanced tracking helps in preventing asset misplacement or loss.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLHbNnIkyhsrzANiCb3df%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa33eeab-09b8-46f7-a253-2f148f5b6b7d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5470af0d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-6.-easy-asset-insights)

6\. Easy Asset Insights

In this enhancement, the user would be able to view the “Assets Report” in the ESS portal. They will be able to view the current assets and history of assets in the “My Assets” tab. The feature makes it convenient for them to access information reducing the need for employees to contact HR or other departments for asset-related inquiries.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-7.-simplified-filters)

7\. Simplified Filters

With the Generic Filter options, HR can easily narrow down the list of employees based on various criteria such as Employee Status, Department, Designation, and more. This simplifies the payroll posting process, making it quicker and more efficient. HR staff can easily select and process payroll for specific groups of employees, saving time in payroll preparation.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F70dhWpHeF4UtchUa0BWb%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c0449f0-1352-4ed2-adbc-a8feb9a8f34b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cefea46&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-8.-effortless-approval-management)

8\. Effortless Approval Management

As a view-only Manager in the appraisal, the user should be able to Review the Appraisal form and Approve/Reject it, so that the appraisal is finalised.

*   Review Appraisal Settings should be enabled for a review process.
    
*   Approval/ Reject will not impact the current appraisal process as it is for review purposes only.
    
*   Review Approve and reject can only be done after the appraisal process is completed or else the system will give validation.
    
*   The status of the review whether Approve/Reject including remarks will be displayed in the Admin Detailed Report.
    
*   The remark option is optional for both approval and rejection
    

Appraisal Entries of the employees’ active stage will be displayed on the Employee Appraisal Page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FLAlwcFMRITbmQcW1oUr2%252F7.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9fdd9812-0838-4d3c-a2f7-835c0e30f9d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42dc7475&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-9.-travel-module-in-mobile-app)

9\. Travel Module in Mobile APP

The travel module in the mobile ESS app allows employees to create travel requests, get them approved, and track travel details like ‘Travel from’, ‘Travel to’, the Purpose of travel, Departure date, Arrival date, Accommodation expenses, Miscellaneous expenses, Other details and more.

This streamlines the entire process and also removes manual paperwork ensuring data accuracy and reducing the risk of financial discrepancies. That results in quicker decision making keeping everyone informed and maintaining transparency.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDkLXLQhRuqhDCZLasqD7%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc54416b0-fb89-4b39-89cc-7afee25d6d8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c34f350&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-10.-improved-ticket-management-with-sorting)

10\. Improved Ticket Management with Sorting

The group manager can download the reports of all the tickets received in the group and can also download the reports for all the unassigned tickets by going to the ‘Unassigned Ticket Report’ tab and then applying the required filters. This makes it easier for them to efficiently manage and track the progress of tickets related to their team or department.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoaOxcENoYiVcEaQMS0A0%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd913d04f-228d-48d1-bed2-ff19b5498001&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=164d555b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJ6vX9iqJKP10dW5zHrlq%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3db766e4-33e6-4b69-94da-3ef23984e82f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e7680ec&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-11.-transparent-managerial-insights)

11\. Transparent Managerial Insights

With our new update in the Confirmation Module, when the 1st level manager confirms an employee, their review, recommendation, and date are visible to the 2nd level manager which streamlines the confirmation process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8uX8HWaHrlxXUQsCLdnO%252F11.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da283a903-2ef0-4140-8855-376d3c61fd3f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f3503f2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2023/april-2023#id-12.-simplified-talent-management)

12\. Simplified Talent Management

The skill repository serves as a centralized database for storing information about the skills of employees. This makes it easy for HR managers and other relevant stakeholders to access and update skill-related information in one place

In Pocket HRMS, the skill repository is likely to be a centralized database that stores information about the skills of employees for example HTML, and CSS. The repository may include details such as the employee’s skills. HR managers can use this information to create personalized development plans for each employee and identify skill gaps and areas for improvement.

There are multiple beneficial features as described below.

• Set skills in the job title.

• Name the Skill Set

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FuRV4qgFJROH9y0O3aFFO%252F12.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a369494-d7e0-4318-a7f6-2a6fc1be06bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=908036f4&sv=2)

• User will get to set skill for the job as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAWrqlfwZq6yrTDYebwD1%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11d59fe9-d224-4ffe-996a-4f96907982df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dec8f11f&sv=2)

• User can find the details of the particular Skill Set by clicking the eye icon.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FM8U84Ve2V5QEdrtzNKYE%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07004ded-a26e-47e2-9f73-65ec276d36fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=205cfca6&sv=2)

• Managers can approve data with the skill set

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2qm8wD8gFbphQnoIUH5H%252F15.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09643ab1-e0c5-4894-bea0-95f2e94f83aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=508153ed&sv=2)

· After creating a job, the user will also receive an e-mail

· After clicking on Rate, A skill option, the user can rate a candidate as shown screenshot below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FydAlQwOrr6LnTdG0U0ZM%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D632763aa-5d62-4d36-b9ce-2508ac3a4207&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62f1f29c&sv=2)

· On the Career page, the user will get the all job details with the Skill Description.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDe32JrEQUcav6do1OUg4%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b3e2ee4-e350-4e6a-9784-28ab122168c8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf298cc&sv=2)

· User can also track the activity record of the candidate in the candidate Timeline

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPsPAZPUrJckXJmJOsHuv%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40d3b1b7-eb4d-40a8-beb8-bfe212918984&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e3a79ee&sv=2)

· The candidate’s skill details will reflect on a particular employee profile after onboarding.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSV6RXU2BcHJCm5GCtkmd%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dddd30237-7e01-4997-a35d-6f4030c2d3ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5954a594&sv=2)

# Accept/Reject Offer | Pocket HRMS

**Introduction**

This page will help you with the steps to accept or reject the offer letter using the candidate’s self-service portal.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/candidate-self-service-portal/accept-reject-offer#pre-requisites)

Pre-requisites:

✔️ Credentials

✔️User rights

_Note - Kindly contact your HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/candidate-self-service-portal/accept-reject-offer#how-to-accept-or-reject-the-offer-letter)

**How to accept or reject the offer letter?**

**Step 1:** Open the email received on your personal email ID and follow the provided link. Use the credentials provided in the email to login.

**Step 2:** Once logged in, select the ‘CTC/Offer Letter’ tab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MaSXLNNFOjxBszQIrxM%252F-MaSYGRVKo7NgAcSRH4m%252Faccept-reject-offer-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4708f0be-b0c4-4db0-9971-af24087185a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7162a37&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Click on the ‘Accept Offer’ or ‘Reject Offer’ buttons respectively to either accept or reject the offer.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MaSXLNNFOjxBszQIrxM%252F-MaSYR758NChvJNb9GXg%252Faccept-reject-offer-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D719254e8-39dd-4c68-9f4f-949be6d77f1b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6af51b2&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to accept or reject the offer, kindly contact your HR.**_

[PreviousLog Inchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/candidate-self-service-portal/login)
[NextUpload Documentschevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/candidate-self-service-portal/upload-documents)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Face Recognition | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/face-recognition#face-recognition)

Face Recognition

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/face-recognition#how-to-upload-face-for-face-recognition)

How to Upload Face for Face Recognition?

**Path:** Login to Pocket HRMS 2.0 mobile app > Go to Leave > Face Recognition > Read the details > Confirm and start > Upload Photos (center view, right profile and left profile) > Upload

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Pocket HRMS 2.0 mobile app**.

**Step 2:** Navigate to the **‘Leave’** module from the main menu. Then Select the **‘Face Recognition’** option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FQ0xvCNV9JsJZSL1SDqpM%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2c5259b&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Carefully **read the ‘Set Up Guide’ details** and instructions provided on the screen regarding facial capture. Tap on **‘Confirm and start’** to begin the camera capture process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FAlgNSuWQpwonaXBxyBEf%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c47f32db&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Follow the on-screen prompts to capture and **upload photos** of your face from three specific angles:

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F1GgJHtN0XGhNcmYOiBp2%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c9428fd&sv=2)

*   Centre view
    
*   Right profile
    
*   Left profile
    
    ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FA34MzsWFhOvBPDncc3kX%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86553114&sv=2)
    

**Step 5:** Once all three angles are captured successfully, tap **‘Save face images’** to submit your facial data to the system.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FBU3BZkpWYqAGJl11rshG%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=748cd5bc&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#295a5c5959465b5d6959464a424c5d415b445a074a4644)

[PreviousSet Addresschevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/request/set-address)
[NextMy Reportchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report)
