# Group Configuration | Pocket HRMS

**How to create groups for the Help Desk:**

**Step 1:** Select 'ESS Settings' from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqJrg25D6Bb6Ymh6jAvol%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72e26eb1-8503-4b52-8ccc-837b663b9b2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1f31f97&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘HelpDesk’ tab inside the ESS Settings page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzNPuCBYOKxPvG4iHovEl%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c34540d-a5bd-4d66-ad94-ee68b227a57f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb9d95d2&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Groups Page' tab from the tabs section to the left of the HelpDesk page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWSzl5n2twT4vBgfcy8d6%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bd70611-dc18-49a4-b846-dcf9ca27f0ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea5db2d5&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select ‘+’ icon as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F0e59gFW7tS2nrDeTkFFZ%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92602947-07cf-47a9-8b62-df07dde64499&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b72c881f&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Enter the relevant details and select the 'Save' button to create a new group.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCiOM7sApBXjyco21Zipy%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6b776cb-db8e-4124-b47d-f65bdd023efa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77f41930&sv=2)

**How to edit groups for the Help Desk:**

**Step 1:** Select 'ESS Settings' from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqJrg25D6Bb6Ymh6jAvol%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72e26eb1-8503-4b52-8ccc-837b663b9b2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1f31f97&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘HelpDesk’ tab inside the ESS Settings page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzNPuCBYOKxPvG4iHovEl%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c34540d-a5bd-4d66-ad94-ee68b227a57f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb9d95d2&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Groups Page' tab from the tabs section to the left of the HelpDesk page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FWSzl5n2twT4vBgfcy8d6%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bd70611-dc18-49a4-b846-dcf9ca27f0ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea5db2d5&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the edit icon corresponding to the group that needs to be edited.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FdWo4O29aDjirtNLEaZ6Q%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2b002bd-7d64-42a4-b4a9-ed2455cfc0e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b660a49&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Change the relevant details and select the 'Save' button to edit the selected group.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fu1Fim3ApW9ev7SGWuNWD%252FHelpDesk%2520GroupConfig%25207.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc50411de-cc7a-49cb-92ce-9389455d98a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70c0ec15&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to configure the groups for the Help Desk, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#85f6f0f5f5eaf7f1c5f5eae6eee0f1edf7e8f6abe6eae8)

# Travel | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/travel#travel-module-admin)

Travel Module – Admin

The Travel Management module of Pocket HRMS is an advanced suite of multi-functional features that automates the management of employee travel. The travel module make it a smooth experience for all the stakeholders involved. This document aims to guide you on all the functions of travel module.

Let us start with setting up the module according to company’s requirement.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/travel#how-to-set-travel-module)

How to set travel module?

Log in to Cloud portal, click on the ‘ESS Settings’ menu. Go to the ‘Travel’ tab followed by clicking on the ‘Travel Master’ subtab and click on the ‘+’ icon.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fkb85bmFMr2rCKVUf8qzw%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac707406&sv=2)

A ‘Travel Master’ pop-up will open, from the ‘Select Travel Master’ drop-down you can to select option such as,

1.  Purpose of Travel,
    
2.  Mode of Travel, &
    
3.  Other Miscellaneous.
    

You can ‘Select Travel Master’ add ‘Description’ and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fb686xj15YarqvTUGDBlq%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2292be24&sv=2)

1.  Adding ‘Purpose of Travel’
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FG6tmm1eynvgF969NJ8PB%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e9a1fd4&sv=2)

1.  Adding ‘Mode of Travel’
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVqstwVyo3tkY48VTh76D%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b41aba7&sv=2)

1.  Adding ‘Other Miscellaneous’
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSdJcHBVg14eBpZ36BEgk%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=148167ee&sv=2)

You will find these under the ‘Travel Master’ once you save it.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fcj37rN91cHl1XGQIPGWQ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=250db76f&sv=2)

From a dedicated ‘Travel Form Builder’, you can customize the travel request and reimbursement requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fb3SSk8SyP5P86CcetTpq%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d65789e&sv=2)

Next, you can go to ‘Travel Notification Settings’ option to set the manager for travel and add their email id for the travel notifications.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoVpgP719HNfW4bMVstU2%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d92ab9d5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/travel#how-can-admin-access-employee-travel-report)

How can admin access employee travel report?

Admin can access employee’s travel report easily on the ESS portal. For this go to ‘Travel’ menu and click on the ‘Employee Report’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3a5dKPMU10VRYCiP4JRJ%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=188e0d39&sv=2)

Under the ‘Travel Report’ tab you get various customization options. You can start will applying ‘Filter’ from the drop down and then select the date range and click on the search button. The system also allows you to ‘Select Employee’ individually by entering their employee code.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIhuV5h0pYXUTtBV4Rlkx%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24489504&sv=2)

Here you can click on quick access buttons for ‘Travel Details’ and ‘Reimbursement Details’ as well as click on a download icon to download ‘Reimbursement Attachment’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fpf1HpyluXzwixUAS0eOW%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd9579c9&sv=2)

View details by clicking on the ‘Travel Details’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnK9WxuT6MxgHmDcDlV6F%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f07413c7&sv=2)

The system allows you to easily ‘Print’ or ‘Download Excel’ report by using respective buttons.

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3c4f494c4c534e487c4c535f575948544e514f125f5351)

[PreviousExpensechevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/expense)
[NextHelp Deskchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/helpdesk)

Last updated 1 month ago

# On duty | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/request/on-duty#on-duty)

On-Duty

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/request/on-duty#how-to-apply-on-duty-in-pocket-hrms-2.0-application)

How to Apply On-duty in Pocket HRMS 2.0 Application?

Path: Login to mobile app of Pocket HRMS 2.0 > click on plus sign > Select Apply On-duty/WFH > Fill in the details such as (Date, Day type, time range, On duty type, remarks) > Save Request.

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Pocket HRMS 2.0 mobile app**.

**Step 2:** Tap on the **plus sign (+)** icon, which is typically located on the home dashboard for quick actions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FYGXF0uB5ZflWxpjZo4fe%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3cb0377&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the **‘Apply On-duty/WFH’** option from the menu that appears.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fdi50OOXPlSp33S5ezwKU%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ccd8f3a7&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Accurately fill in the required details for your request, which include:

*   **Date:** Select the specific date for your request.
    
*   **Day type:** Specify whether you are requesting a full day or a half day.
    
*   **Time range:** Enter your expected working hours for that day.
    
*   **On duty type:** Choose the appropriate category from the dropdown (e.g., Work From Home, Client Visit, Training).
    
*   **Remarks:** Add a brief reason or any necessary context for your manager.
    

**Step 5:** Tap **‘Save Request’** to formally submit your application for approval.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FpUeWcmVvaGuoZ3HLy8VT%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a34ac547&sv=2)

**Alternate way:**

**Path:** Login to mobile app of Pocket HRMS 2.0 > click on 3 horizontal lines > Leave menu > Request > Select Onduty/Wfh Tab > > Fill in the details such as (Date, Day type, time range, On duty type, remarks) > Save Request.

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Pocket HRMS 2.0 mobile app**.

**Step 2:** Tap on the **three horizontal lines** (hamburger menu) located at the top left corner of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FtcC6cS5S8AsMXKD1m88m%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61209cc9&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the **‘Leave’** module from the menu and tap on **‘Request’**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FfqFjpq89eeYCQfoTmBZS%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dccb727&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select “On duty/Work from home’ tab

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fb5CGnlgyNya4yZBXVA2B%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e166ea7d&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Accurately fill in the required details for your request, which include:

*   **Date:** Select the specific date for your request.
    
*   **Day type:** Specify whether you are requesting a full day or a half day.
    
*   **Time range:** Enter your expected working hours for that day.
    
*   **On duty type:** Choose the appropriate category from the dropdown (e.g., Work From Home, Client Visit, Training).
    
*   **Remarks:** Add a brief reason or any necessary context for your manager.
    

**Step 6:** Tap **‘Save Request’** to formally submit your application for approval.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FpUeWcmVvaGuoZ3HLy8VT%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a34ac547&sv=2)

**Note:** You can also view the details of previous on-duty application and approvals by clicking on **‘View Previous Entries’**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FL3fXlVUbILigMe4XDqfq%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96b45693&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fmtb8x0gEoeQHwWk3DquZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ac9fa3d-fd96-4e76-8f2f-2eb6d21a6c3d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6560f2c&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#33404643435c414773435c505856475b415e401d505c5e)

# Create & Publish Jobs | Pocket HRMS

**Introduction**

This page provides the steps for creating and publishing a new job opening.

**Pre-requisites**

✔️ Admin credentials

✔️ User rights

_**Note:**_

*   _Kindly contact your Admin/HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._
    
*   _You will be required to assign a Job Manager before proceeding._
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/recruiter/recruitment-management/create-and-publish-jobs#how-to-create-a-new-job-opening)

**How to create a new job opening?**

**Step 1:** Select ‘Hire’ and then ‘Jobs’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fjq6wfH83lvh6ujf7i5kM%252FCreate%2520Job%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9642fec-1f55-4047-b191-f9638ab46f03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbfad2fc&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Job List’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCe3INfcxVOiXM9VJb2B0%252FCreate%2520Job%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De681a395-ac95-43bd-9e3d-a9e06ddba3ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acbde895&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Click on the ‘+ Add’ button to the top right corner.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FqK0Zl7X44UwXSgJtBiHu%252FCreate%2520Job%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D135db268-ace5-442a-aaf2-2e8c68f0f9fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=23f84f0a&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Enter the required details, upload the documents for ‘Job Summary’ and ‘Others’ if required and click on the ‘Save & Continue’ button to proceed. The job will be added to the ‘Job List’ page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZBJtPTRvWaVUbFL3FaSu%252FCreate%2520Job%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0440286f-59d8-4587-aba8-6695fe780370&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84c2fc7d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9WTJjeccRZREX3GGZSg3%252FCreate%2520Job%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bbc218a-3a2b-4590-b939-740257f33201&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8e1144e&sv=2)

_**Note:**_

*   _If the ‘Manager Approval’ option is set, the created job will be displayed in the ‘Pending Approval’ modal box from where, you can check whether the job has been approved by the manager or not._
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2xYtoiKKbBQSMAPITrBQ%252FCreate%2520Job%25206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b81e918-36ea-4252-952a-0284803e038e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df1000c8&sv=2)

*   _The newly created jobs defaults to ‘Unpublished’ status. Click on the ‘Unpublish’ quick filter to view the created job and make sure to sort the list as ‘Newest First’ to display the newest jobs at the top of the list._
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMaR0R1uTAaxQbsMn1ZTr%252FCreate%2520Job%25207.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D422c0d69-46c8-4039-895e-17ee59c19e51&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2927ff33&sv=2)

*   _You can also filter the jobs as per your requirement by clicking on the ‘Filter’ button and clicking on the ‘Apply’ button after setting the required parameters._
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJG9pFOsYpPirjwEfmPZO%252FCreate%2520Job%25208.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D049d2e4d-9252-4d86-b7ba-696c51e808ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91962c01&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhdA1iOILd6E7MKcJyZou%252FCreate%2520Job%25209.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc873d5d-9e8f-4c06-99af-33335e3cd063&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81ad62ea&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/recruiter/recruitment-management/create-and-publish-jobs#how-to-approve-a-newly-created-job)

**How to approve a newly created job?**

**Step 1:** Select ‘Hire’ and then ‘Jobs’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbZG3kZqoyL3OZyBeUoTG%252FApprove%2520Job%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ef64374-7244-43b5-82b1-59b6f8a479ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79d77cd5&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Job Manager Approval’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKL3tEdrLnXq6TUGohryH%252FApprove%2520Job%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4390249b-9755-4d57-aea4-0238548a477f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c8f7bd4&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the ‘View Details’ button adjacent to the job.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSkr0te3rzqFPOIzQvsCX%252FApprove%2520Job%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba898a42-5d66-4dae-9189-0d2e1fa77c0d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=116fd93f&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Enter the remarks and click on the ‘Approve’ or ‘Reject’ button to approve or reject the job respectively.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSQNla3nhhitAH3bdS2qR%252FApprove%2520Job%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38236e90-5340-45f1-b556-7968683c0148&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65a2d027&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/recruiter/recruitment-management/create-and-publish-jobs#how-to-publish-a-newly-created-job)

**How to publish a newly created job?**

**Step 1:** Select ‘Hire’ and then ‘Jobs’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FcxB4ErO51p6lsgGb6Fd5%252FPublish%2520Job%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D555f7c78-64cc-4aa5-b8ff-3b6bb80697d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbe0d460&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Job Outline’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FRG8udeVF5PBkdHHkgTiO%252FPublish%2520Job%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9869a0ed-ef00-4f76-b692-1b14004ffd73&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6deacf83&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the ‘UnPublished’ button at the top to filter the jobs that are not published.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F6AawWE3q1ImvqofxVZLc%252FPublish%2520Job%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7efbf328-58a8-4d83-8696-f3d7cf0d7630&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c09115b&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the ‘Publish’ drop-down option adjacent to the job that you wish to publish.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbOd9IiZxE4tbv1bplN6z%252FPublish%2520Job%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b909ac1-e688-431d-9809-38730e2115d4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5606a8c8&sv=2)

_**Note:**_

*   _You can publish, unpublish, and archive jobs using the steps above and selecting the corresponding option from the drop-down menu._
    
*   _You can also click on the ‘Career Page’ button if you wish to view the published job._
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F75PwSJ9jmQxAKDYBAvMh%252FPublish%2520Job%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1ee3cad-aa1e-44ef-9503-5ecf14e1695f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b2813a&sv=2)

*   _You can also click on the ‘Add to Website’ button if you wish to add the job to your company’s official website. You will be provided the embed code that you can paste into your website to embed the job._
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMdvFDOKbbD4PmRj3xLj8%252FPublish%2520Job%25206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ca7aed4-2a9e-48b7-a514-37094d427a6c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10a89c97&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4L2BE9I5WTcwiIA45HHg%252FPublish%2520Job%25207.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da75ff53d-4703-4b55-bb27-d27c861eafd3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e302f472&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to create, publish or edit a new job opening, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#15666065657a676155657a767e70617d6778663b767a78)

# Employee FnF | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/employee-separation-and-release#full-and-final-f-and-f)

Full and Final (F&F)

This section will explain how you can separate, and process the full and final settlement. You will also learn how to release employee or activate an employee.

**Note-** Release Employee signifies activating an employee or making them re-join.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/employee-separation-and-release#a-how-to-separate-or-exit-employees)

**A) How to Separate or Exit Employees?**

Follow the path below to separate or exit an employee:

**Path:** Cloud Login > Payroll > Transaction > Separation > Fill in the Details > save.

**Step 1:** Login to the cloud portal, go to ‘Payroll’ menu and Under ‘Transaction’ sub-menu, select the ‘Separation’ option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCBW3QbCXzCMGNQBRzENt%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26a00ec9&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Fill in all the details such as ‘Employee’, ‘Separation type’, ‘Separation Category’, ‘Separation Reason’, ‘Last Working Date’, ‘Resignation Date’, ‘Disable Self Service Login’, ‘Employee Rehire’, ‘Employee Rehire Remark’, and click on ‘Save’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FhCM3SR4HJJN2m9M1gn9Z%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22632f5c&sv=2)

If you want to check the employees who have left the organization, then click on ‘Left Employees’. All the details such as ‘Name of employee’, ‘Employee code’, ‘Date of Joining’, ‘Date of Separation’ and ‘Reason of separation’ of separated employees will be reflected.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F1hBel3PkFwRRurNeIgZr%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b23a6fa&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FA20GLERxZkdFzL1oCuJu%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=459155d7&sv=2)

**Link:** [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Payroll/Transaction/separationarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Payroll/Transaction/separation)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/employee-separation-and-release#b-how-to-release-or-activate-separated-employee)

B) How to Release or Activate Separated Employee?

To release or active separated employee, follow the path below:

**Path:** Cloud login > Payroll > Transaction > Release Employee > Fill in the details > Save

**Step 1:** Login to cloud portal, go to ‘Payroll’ menu, Under the ‘Transaction’ sub-menu select ‘Release employee’ option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FCOjgYp5HhPzb4Lr6lgE2%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c664bfe&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Fill in the details such as separated employee name you want to re-join in ‘Employee’ section. The system will automatically fetch all details. Then, fill the ‘Release Date’ (date in which employee will re-join) and click on ‘Release’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FbnYXTkpOl49lvxbk0P9Q%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eabd9663&sv=2)

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Payroll/Transaction/separationReleasearrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Payroll/Transaction/separationRelease)

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to separate employees, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e5969095958a9791a5958a868e80918d978896cb868a88)

[PreviousNew Employeechevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/new-employee)
[NextApproval Matrixchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/approval-matrix)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Leave Opening | Pocket HRMS

**Pocket HRMS** allow users schedule interviews, process onboarding, etc. with just a few clicks. It is an end-to-end Human Resource Management System. Every HR responsibility like creating job templates, scheduling interview rounds, shortlisting candidates, generating offer letter, etc. can be handled easily with this software.

When new employees join the company, we update the Employee Master and follow it with Leave

Opening for the employees. We can do this in a couple of ways in Pocket HRMS-

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/leave-opening#leave-opening-manual-entry)

Leave Opening Manual Entry

In case the Admin wants to make Leave Entry for the database employees, follow this process-

1.  Login to Pocket HRMS on next.pockethrms.com
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXEK5ddMhhMRV71f1vn3r%252F2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72100ce9&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Employee →** Select **Employee List** and click on the required Employee
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FyKYieOkJVcRqX0a1b3Iv%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdd9618d&sv=2)

1.  In the Employee Profile, select the **Leave** Tab. From here you can see the types of leaves available. You can easily set Leave opening by selecting the **Three Dots** Symbol on each of the leave types
    
2.  Now, you can enter the Leave Opening and Credit details. Click Save and repeat the process for other leave types as required.
    
3.  You are done. Great Work!
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fb5lAyRS97Xjgtm9ZD2WZ%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31d3151e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/leave-opening#leave-opening-import)

Leave Opening Import

Pocket HRMS also allows you to set Leave Opening for multiple employees simultaneously by importing Excel Files (.xlsx format only). The process is very simple and user-friendly. Let us see how we can use Leave Opening Import tool-

1.  Login to next.pockethrms.com
    
2.  Select **Leave →** Under **Import**, choose **Leave Opening**
    
3.  In the new page, we will first setup the setting. We will be using the **Sample Excel File** as an example which can be downloaded from this page itself.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FeQvYyD6aL4WRgNmpe4d3%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b6ce029&sv=2)

1.  Click on Add New and type a setting Name. Select Add to finalize the setting name.
    
2.  Fill the appropriate fields as per your excel file. We have filled the data as per the sample excel file mentioned earlier.
    
3.  Click on Save Settings. Now, the setting is ready to be used.
    
4.  Let’s come back to Leave Debit Import Utility or just hit Refresh. Select your setting and the fields will auto load.
    
5.  Upload the excel file and sheet name will be selected automatically. You can also change the sheet name as desired.
    
6.  Click Upload File and we’re done!
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvpfaYZOfO17F0DU44une%252F14.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2ce4720&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJ1nVVfuIBs8jF11vYJXV%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=babf71be&sv=2)

Remember that you do only need to setup a setting once to reuse whenever you require for future use.

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b3c0c6c3c3dcc1c7f3c3dcd0d8d6c7dbc1dec09dd0dcde)

[PreviousLeave Debitchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/leave-debit)
[NextLeave Debit Entrychevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/leave-debit-entry)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Health | Pocket HRMS

Through health module of Pocket HRMS dashboard you can keep track of employee health parameters. The HRMS allows you to set health related questions and frequency of tracking easily.

The employees then answer the set questions on set frequency to help HR/ admin know their health status. Stepwise procedure to set health module is explained below.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/health#how-to-set-health-module)

**How to set health module:**

**Step 1:** Go to 'Settings'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDz70J49zom83QY0Hr%252F-MYDzQF0nHuhepEr18uc%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd66ae95-14dc-4039-867f-978a64caf5a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f9b4bfa&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Proceed to 'Health' module

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDz70J49zom83QY0Hr%252F-MYDzTvymidoHokdBf3K%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74ab3828-df7c-4336-b3d2-6774400eca9d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4aaf0d75&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Settings' option. Here you can enable or disable the module. Also, you can set frequency and select day to track employee health.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDz70J49zom83QY0Hr%252F-MYDzZIM7nIyOhtvLj9z%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80a2fcf7-4103-420f-a67d-bc7d064de3b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bb9469f&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select 'Field Creation' option. This option helps you create health-related questions to be asked to your employees.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDz70J49zom83QY0Hr%252F-MYDzlEGIKz0cuhD5RKS%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdc44207-eee2-423b-a50b-fdbe1ce9ee39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=828425f9&sv=2)

_If you are unable to create health templates or facing similar issue, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2f5c5a5f5f405d5b6f5f404c444a5b475d425c014c4042)

[PreviousRecruitment Setupchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/recruitment-setup)
[NextSurveychevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/survey)

# Biometric system | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/mobile-app/leave/biometric-system#introduction)

Introduction

Biometric system for attendance management makes it accurate and foolproof for the HR and payroll department to operate. Minimized errors and accurate attendance data are some prime benefits of biometric attendance management.

Automated biometrics in managing attendance include fingerprint attendance, iris scanners, etc. Pocket HRMS allows easy integration of biometric system with its attendance management system and makes payroll easy.

Employees can also provide their log data through punching system available on mobile self-service app as shown in screenshot below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoqGSkgmhgjPG9oPLJCPn%252FLeave%2520%2526%2520Attendance%2520Mobile%2520App%2520-%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ab07df3-afd0-4557-be20-9ba40b4d587c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13cc3afa&sv=2)

To learn more - [Biometric Attendance Systemarrow-up-right](https://www.pockethrms.com/biometric-attendance-system/)

_**Note: Steps can only be performed by employees with authorized access. If you are unable to perform the aforementioned steps, kindly contact your HR/ manager.**_

[PreviousLeavechevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/mobile-app/leave)
[NextLeave and Attendance Mobile Appchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/mobile-app/leave/mobile-app)

# Leave Details | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report/leave-details#leave-details)

Leave Details

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report/leave-details#how-to-check-leave-details-in-pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app)

How to check Leave Details in Pocket HRMS 2.0 Mobile App?

**Path:** Login to mobile app of Pocket HRMS 2.0 > click on 3 horizontal lines (Hamburger menu) > > Leave > My Reports > Leave Details

**Step 1:** Log in to the Pocket HRMS 2.0 mobile app and click on the 3 horizontal lines (Hamburger menu) on the top left.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F60nlfF17YanVdrFagBF8%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40c5e990&sv=2)

**Step 2:** From the menu list, select the ‘Leave’ module, then Navigate to the ‘My Reports’ section within the Leave module.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FInfxhtbLIvKYcX3AvqNn%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef6acefc&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Click on ‘Leave Details’ to view the comprehensive report of your leave records.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FKIzwIDdu0eNN0HiP8Xa1%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f52ac365&sv=2)

**Note:** Leave details displays various leaves applied in the current month along with the detailing such as:

*   Type of leave: Earned leave, PL, EL or optional leave etc.
    
*   From date- To Date
    
*   Half/full day leave
    
*   No. of days
    
*   Status: If the leave is approved, or pending.
    
    ![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FelekCzjP5vQIaY7ma8b0%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e175693c&sv=2)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report/leave-details#filter-icon)

Filter Icon

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FODZ2446V4W8IpEzCQS62%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=831be0d1&sv=2)

It allows you to filter any specific leave. Click on the filter icon and fill in details such as ‘Report Type’, ‘Leave Type’, ‘From date-to Date’, and click on ‘Search’ to get the report for your required leave.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FNbJLPe5eQIBDEVKzWMcZ%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de3dc7ea&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9deee8ededf2efe9ddedf2fef6f8e9f5eff0eeb3fef2f0)

# FnF HR | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/fnf-hr#how-to-check-no-dues-responses-from-all-departments)

How to Check No dues responses from all departments?

You can check the all the responses from all the departments. For that go to the ‘F&F’ menu and click on the ‘Approval’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fphbe12M5k8wPPN9ylbkR%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55fd9ada&sv=2)

Under the ‘Full Final Approval’ tab you will find the entries click on the ‘View’ button against employee’s name, and you will see forms filled by different departments.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FmnWmrO3rsiMzctnyXZhn%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c298a73e&sv=2)

Here you will also find the forms filled by various departments as well as a form for HR department for which you can select your response and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fs59BSkewbseeQpegjTGt%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=230ae255&sv=2)

Once it is saves you have to open the entry again

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwyB3Ku7029Aw5dbIhbfi%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc0e765e&sv=2)

and click on the ‘Submit button and it can be accessed from the cloud portal.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FF2GJrVEstRLEtSw3BsIo%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e530dcd3&sv=2)

# Email Templates | Pocket HRMS

Email module of Pocket HRMS dashboard helps you create and customize HR templates in clicks.

Automated HR template generation helps make employee handling and HRM less time-consuming. Given below are steps involved in editing HR email templates.

**How to create new email templates?**

**Step 1:** Go to 'Settings'

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDyYTl0mRJgc8nMMc7%252F-MYDyzUv9-L8lNWxwcWM%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D074f6a92-1b5b-40c8-b61a-5a6e7e4ac153&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7165ad13&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Proceed to 'Organization' module

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDyYTl0mRJgc8nMMc7%252F-MYDz1pHkIqbIGRiI7r4%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54057b6a-75c6-4c5d-9114-5c0dd35d068a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=800d02a9&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Email Templates' option

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYDyYTl0mRJgc8nMMc7%252F-MYDz4nTWDa0tLFIB_j_%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccb4965b-5e72-4cb6-8112-b937c158a204&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e5e4a0c&sv=2)

Here, you can preview and edit email templates like payslip, Form16, password reset email, etc.

_**Note: If you are unable to configure HR templates, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0d7e787d7d627f794d7d626e666879657f607e236e6260)

# Expense | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/finance/expense#how-approve-expense-claims-as-a-finance-person)

How approve expense claims as a finance person?

As a Finance person, you need to log into the ESS portal and click on the ‘Finance Approval’ under the ‘Expense’ menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8lJKN4KSqRO7qOWCI8rn%252FFinance%2520Approval%2520subtab.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0bad7757-6d66-4ddd-9529-cd1a4189d15e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5783a24&sv=2)

Under the ‘Finance Approval’ tab select the ‘Month’ and click on the ‘Search’ button. The expense requests will appear, click on the ‘Details’ button for more information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FXIcu7v51QGr8Xxi6M00k%252FFinance%2520requests.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7dcb0c46-9dcd-47b2-8754-2f5a096672cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7521a56&sv=2)

The ‘Expense Details’ pop-up will open, you can edit the ‘Finance Amount’ and scroll left to ‘Approve’ or ‘Reject’ the request. Enter the ‘Finance Remark’ and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F99ixHD6tc8oOlikBNsne%252FExpense%2520Details%2520pop%2520up.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14aaaaa9-e767-421d-a62f-620bb7f7f29d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91f593cb&sv=2)

# Bulk Category Transfer | Pocket HRMS

This feature allows you to **bulk transfer employee categories using an Excel file**, whereas previously, this process had to be completed **individually for each employee**.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/bulk-category-transfer#how-to-do-bulk-category-transfer)

How to do Bulk Category Transfer?

**Path:** Cloud Login > Employee > Import > From select import template, click on Category Transfer Import from drop down > Download category transfer import sample file > Make changes in the downloaded Excel as per your requirement and save it > Select or Add setting name > Import template (import the Excel file that you have saved after making changes) > Fill the starting and ending row > Map the components as per you Excel file > Save settings > Upload File.

**Step 1:** Log in to the **Cloud portal**. Navigate to the **‘Employee’** module, select **‘Import’**.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FQXzvz1fXpZQeYznV3Zel%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37359d5&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Click on ‘**Select Import Template’** and select **‘Category Transfer Import’from drop-down and click** the option to **‘Download category transfer import sample file’** to get the standard template.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FglZgOsNvRhvpejI8iFK5%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a7dbfbf&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Open the downloaded Excel sheet, fill in the required employee and category transfer details as per your requirements, and save the file to your computer.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Ffwc8J2QhVEi7SNbYzP5i%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b181884a&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Return to the portal and select an existing **‘Setting Name’** from the dropdown menu, or type to add a new one.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FCocUsHBMUj2n6n8D5XNC%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da7578b5&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Click on **‘Import Template’** to browse and select the Excel file you just prepared and saved in your system.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FuW1ILAYhFCuZjE8rIedk%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5024257a&sv=2)

**Step 6:** Specify the **Starting Row** and **Ending Row** so the system knows exactly where your data begins and ends in the spreadsheet.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fs0MVQ3O2io2W09mnvPt4%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fbb26ca&sv=2)

**Step 7:** **Map the components** by carefully matching the system fields to the corresponding column headers in your Excel sheet.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FufbTSiELHnMSUmzHTSlC%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=757a7d80&sv=2)

**Step 8:** Click **‘Save Settings’** to store this configuration for future use. Finally, click **‘Upload File’** to execute the bulk transfer.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2Fphd7k2pSIbwB6yzN5NFe%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a19eac42&sv=2)

**Link**: [https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Employee/Employee/EmployeeImport?import=1#arrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Employee/Employee/EmployeeImport?import=1#)

[arrow-up-right](https://youtu.be/PLzYoZ4QBoQ)
For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f88b8d8888978a8cb888979b939d8c908a958bd69b9795)

[PreviousGeo Location Employee Tagging Bulk Importchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/geo-location-employee-tagging-bulk-import)
[NextPayrollchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/payroll)

Last updated 5 days ago

# Income Tax - New Financial Year | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/income-tax/income-tax-new-financial-year#how-to-change-the-financial-year-for-income-tax-calculations)

**How to change the financial year for income tax calculations?**

**Step 1**: Go to 'Income Tax' > 'Utilities' > 'Year End Transfer'.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB3QzDbjFIPduhLn-j%252F-MYB3fQ2Gs5XFpQ2jc0a%252F12041.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c1d8527-972e-48d1-9ad1-880d8ab70c6c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=503296ec&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select the checkboxes for the companies and click on the 'Transfer' button to complete the process.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYB3QzDbjFIPduhLn-j%252F-MYB3jXmwyanXUgHNt76%252F12042.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62215d71-8d36-4bf0-b68b-107548178b59&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e38d062a&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to transfer the income tax calculations to the next financial year, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#93e0e6e3e3fce1e7d3e3fcf0f8f6e7fbe1fee0bdf0fcfe)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/income-tax/income-tax-new-financial-year#how-to-do-the-challan-entry)

How to do the Challan Entry?

Log into the cloud portal, click on the ‘Income Tax’ menu and then select the ‘Transaction’ sub-menu followed by the ‘[Challan Entryarrow-up-right](https://cloud.pockethrms.com/Itax/transaction/challanentry)
’ option.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FfNqwf946Lrhf11LIoNNG%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6dab623&sv=2)

Click on the ‘+’ button to add the month-wise challans. A pop-up window will open.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FPesog7cz9lwF7Nh6yT0O%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5abe68c9&sv=2)

Fill in the details in the form and click the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZiag7dXtC4GRW68K9U8O%252Fetds%2520challan.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d65e3af-eddb-4bc7-9046-89d605606151&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4eae26e2&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

# Attendance | Pocket HRMS

**Introduction**

This page provides the steps for approving the attendance regularization requests from your employees. You will be able to do this process using any of the following 4 methods:

*   ESS
    
*   Mobile App
    
*   App Notification
    
*   Email
    

_Note - Kindly contact your Admin/ HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/manager/leave-attendance-on-duty/approving-rejecting-attendance-regularization#how-to-approve-reject-attendance-regularization-requests-using-ess-portal)

**How to approve/reject attendance regularization requests using ESS Portal?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal with your manager credentials. Select ‘Leave’ and then ‘Approval’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqU9HSVC7rPVb823VZ%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bfc713c-a6e9-4dc7-bf44-394a2f4b3ef1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94a2d7e9&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Attendance Regularization’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUCHdYTgF7TCe-5v-%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D144023a7-f491-4a58-ac81-68ef3a5bab8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=90b65f42&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Optionally, search for the employee’s name.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUGo9jhIWfQyUE253%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbff1c795-f084-416a-ad81-58fef8cee6fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3210118&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the ‘From Date’ and ‘To Date’ between which you need to regularize the attendance entries.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUK_3xMByXCrGzRZR%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39c7d13b-be85-4971-bdc1-b6ab5234fa16&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f8b5bce&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Select the ‘Search’ button to start searching for the regularization requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUNHN8jztotgJiB2w%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D206292bb-392c-49c6-8e7c-a8de9f817523&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91191a38&sv=2)

**Step 6:** Select the bullet points / radio buttons next to each request’s row to accept or reject the requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUQbeFmU4gTnRByHe%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbaace01b-cb03-4404-bb75-375c36c36ac3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=975aebad&sv=2)

**Step 7:** Alternatively, you can select the check box next to ‘ACCEPT’ or ‘REJECT’ to approve or reject all of the requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUTdtPE5xdnU4_ZCY%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De80d59b4-7617-4578-9b07-6f90fd22f636&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2b2156&sv=2)

**Step 8:** Once you are satisfied with the selections, select the button ‘Save’ to confirm the changes.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqUYHgvWzdzXc1YtHY%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-ESS-8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbdf1619a-9530-4fad-bacf-44553e52478c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15becd9f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/manager/leave-attendance-on-duty/approving-rejecting-attendance-regularization#how-to-approve-reject-attendance-regularization-requests-using-the-pocket-hrms-mobile-app)

**How to approve/reject attendance regularization requests using the Pocket HRMS Mobile App?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal with your manager credentials. Log into the ESS portal with your manager credentials. Open the side menu by tapping on the ‘Hamburger Menu Icon’ and select the option ‘Leave’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqVYxV-0nDwm0f8Vev%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-App-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db416321a-a95e-4e27-843c-db5a0ac2f40a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b492fc3&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Tap on the option ‘Approval’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqVaSGlRs-e6xIhvAc%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-App-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6b5ae91-1c06-4213-9fdd-44d8d59192f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7bc39fc&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Tap on the ‘Attendance Regularization’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqVeFYLvEdiR9p3XTc%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-App-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48034e65-9421-4e2f-9043-d8f206bf4317&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cbb39765&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Tap on the filter button at the bottom right and select the relevant filters and then tap on ‘Search’ button to find the requests.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqVgpA8-fnOI9G-3Rf%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-App-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D742e7b7f-1362-4e3b-a8f5-0a13bd79f4e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=738377df&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Approval: Tap on the ‘Approve’ button corresponding to each request to approve it and get the ‘Success’ notification at the bottom of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqVr-nlIR0gWUERcCm%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-App-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D221455f8-fc4c-4114-ac40-0ad1d635331a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e18985d&sv=2)

**Step 6:** Rejection: Tap on the ‘Reject’ button corresponding to each request to reject it and provide the reason for the same in the pop-up menu and select ‘Ok’ to confirm your selection.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqVuKfSGvMcZ5x6dg0%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-App-6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f8947f9-6023-4f1c-a587-e6241f9e6d4e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92fb14ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/manager/leave-attendance-on-duty/approving-rejecting-attendance-regularization#how-to-approve-reject-attendance-regularization-requests-using-the-app-notification)

**How to approve/reject attendance regularization requests using the app notification?**

**Step 1:** Tap on the bell icon at the top right corner of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqWlU2j3EKzufjKpQ0%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Notfcn-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c1ca594-3891-4418-9e0f-7a64985c9385&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad59b683&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Tap on the regularization request notification titled, ‘Regularization Pending’

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqWniYV_VvmcD69tjw%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Notfcn-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c7f2654-f807-4e7c-a2ca-a89118e66148&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=823ca5f2&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Approval: Tap on the ‘Approve’ button corresponding to the request to approve it and get the ‘Success’ notification at the bottom of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqWqxReXGNaWgCK4Tj%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Notfcn-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da938ed86-846e-401a-8d11-317192bedf8b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c78d1bce&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Rejection: Tap on the ‘Reject’ button corresponding to the request to reject it and provide the reason for the same in the pop-up menu and select ‘Ok’ to confirm your selection.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqWtuBVkLdcp_OWYik%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Notfcn-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fd48044-9f60-481f-9dd4-cdc44adbb3dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6e5c481&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/manager/leave-attendance-on-duty/approving-rejecting-attendance-regularization#how-to-approve-reject-attendance-regularization-requests-using-your-official-email)

**How to approve/reject attendance regularization requests using your official email?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal with your manager credentials. You will get an attendance regularization approval email with the ‘Approve’ and ‘Reject’ links.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqXZDGQgxLXAM4C6wq%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Email-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2719ec61-9aec-47f5-a0a6-07d79d38a890&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=851fb9ea&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Approval: On clicking the ‘Approve’ link, a new window or tab will open where you can enter any remarks and click on ‘Approve’ button to approve the request.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqXao76Fbk2A8KWfxb%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Email-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D225b5f89-1df0-41b0-b821-0690588b7381&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f36be113&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Rejection: On clicking the rejection link, a new window or tab will open where you need to enter the reason for rejection and click on ‘Save’ to reject the request.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqREQKk4z3RLKvrnSr%252F-MkqXdDMlyDOI3wGaN-O%252FAttendance%2520Regln-Approve-Email-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1154488a-1dc8-485a-af0e-9fe1444cbcbc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26b58476&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/manager/leave-attendance-on-duty/approving-rejecting-attendance-regularization#how-to-generate-your-teams-attendance-regularization-report-in-the-ess-portal)

**How to generate your team’s attendance regularization report in the ESS portal?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal with your manager credentials. Select ‘Leave’ and then ‘My Team Report’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqvY_ANXWATDamcbZx%252F-Mkqxk7i8m7hFl4Dcd6M%252FAttendance%2520Regln-MyTeamReport-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc036545d-e3e0-4ab6-b275-9f06ce522d4d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1de3bcd5&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Attendance Regularization’ tab at the top. In some cases, depending on your screen resolution, it might be under the ‘More’ menu at the end of the tabs section.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqvY_ANXWATDamcbZx%252F-MkqxmqAxh_LJZH64zc0%252FAttendance%2520Regln-MyTeamReport-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2a1ee32-3fd6-4c4d-99bb-e2bb5c1a1ff9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8ae07e7&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Search for the employee’s name, the type of regularization as well as the period for which you need to generate the report. Once selected, select the ‘Search’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkqvY_ANXWATDamcbZx%252F-MkqxpR7H6DUSdNLZ5q2%252FAttendance%2520Regln-MyTeamReport-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9519910-73ae-40f6-a561-a7edd0ed2a52&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d81b7935&sv=2)

**Note:** If you are unable above steps, kindly contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a1d2d4d1d1ced3d5e1d1cec2cac4d5c9d3ccd28fc2cecc)

# Candidate Onboarding | Pocket HRMS

This page provides the steps for onboarding a candidate.

**Pre-requisites**

✔️ Admin credentials

✔️ User rights

_**Note:**_ _Kindly contact your Admin/HR for rights if you are not able to perform the steps below._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/recruiter/recruitment-management/candidate-onboarding#how-to-onboard-a-candidate)

**How to onboard a candidate?**

**Step 1:** Select ‘Hire’ and then ‘Recruiter’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FfpnzNc2e4yFbKdhBnj4t%252FOnboarding%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3538f579-5af0-4ba2-bed8-fdfc8def18a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da3a11bc&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Candidate Onboarding’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgRZefeQWMArAT0BG5MqK%252FOnboarding%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1054e127-dcc5-4605-8d47-070a8f458201&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ea8e5ca&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Enter the ‘Employee Code’ and click on the ‘Add’ button against the employee that is being onboarded.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FwXsV59POIhltIS0A7GIw%252FOnboarding%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7e43c47-273b-40f7-8c5e-8f9c52567ef7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d945acde&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Enter the required details, tick the ‘Send Password Reset Email’ checkbox and click on the ‘Add Employee’ button to send the email to the candidate with the ESS portal login credentials and the URL.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F7lggX0klG4d7AJeAKuxl%252FOnboarding%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcd8e488-2eba-4f23-bf4a-3b7cfb190c8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df1f61fc&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to onboard any candidate, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#5e2d2b2e2e312c2a1e2e313d353b2a362c332d703d3133)

[PreviousCandidate Documentation Approvalchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/recruiter/recruitment-management/candidate-documentation-approval)
[NextRecruitment Overviewchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/recruiter/recruitment-management/recruitment-overview)

# Employee Document | Pocket HRMS

This page explains how you can add new joining documents for employees to submit once they are onboarded.

Once you successfully add document requirements, employees can submit them through their self-service portal.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/employee-document#how-to-add-edit-employee-document)

**How to add/ edit employee document?**

**Step 1**: Go to settings

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYAnp6yPYOUaue4Z6G2%252F-MYAo3Q6rBwF02RuZwZu%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb1109a5-993e-40dd-9414-d218efe96632&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96c747d&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Proceed to the 'HR' column

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYAnp6yPYOUaue4Z6G2%252F-MYAo97iqtp6Zk5Wqmdv%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f13a7ae-9d4f-4e9c-a4bd-29f9df5a3de2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19615ae3&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'Joining Document'. Here, you can add a new requirement by clicking on '+' button. Also, you can edit/ delete any document as shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MYAnp6yPYOUaue4Z6G2%252F-MYAoEVdBgL1jPlgV6Zk%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df55e3bea-bc93-4445-a410-5f264400c71f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7d19845&sv=2)

_**Note:**_ _If you are unable to create employee documents, kindly contact us at_ [_\[email protected\]_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f0838580809f8284b0809f939b958498829d83de939f9d)

[PreviousOn-boardingchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/on-boarding)
[NextNew Employeechevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/employee-management/new-employee)
