# February 2025 | Pocket HRMS

![Page cover](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fn4Iq8KoXFkrTend2wcJu%252FJanuary%25202025%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a5f9d92-0608-4c9a-982a-1221f0ef9f73&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e906d0d&sv=2)

We are thrilled to present our Monthly Update, with enhanced user-friendly tools to elevate your HR experience. Our commitment to innovation and efficiency drives us to bring you seamless updates that transform your HR processes. For the month of February, we have the following enhancements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#monthly-count-report-more-clarity-better-decisions)

Monthly Count Report: More Clarity, Better Decisions

We’ve added a Monthly Count Report to the Attendance module, making it easier to track and analyse attendance.

*   **Detailed Insights**: View punch records (Biometric, Web, etc.), attendance regularization, and leave status.
    
*   **Better Visibility**: Easily track present and absent days for a specific period.
    
*   **Flexible Data Access**: Retrieve attendance data for any selected month and year.
    
*   **Excel Export**: Download reports in Excel for deeper analysis.
    
*   **Advanced Filtering**: Use multiple filters to refine report generation.
    

This update provides accurate and flexible attendance reporting, helping HR and management make informed decisions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FnedmWgaEqGBAre6YuF2o%252FFrame%2520147.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11b0667d-54c2-4765-b1c9-7b7a4e7c5ef7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32f971cf&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FUEwmB0uBGpRpVRdLWUcK%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d78601ce&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#prevent-overlapping-deductions-in-sandwich-leave)

Prevent Overlapping Deductions in Sandwich Leave

Now you get an option to ensure that sandwich deduction will not be applied when ‘Working Hour’ or ‘Invalid Leave Deduction Rule’ are applicable. You can simply click the checkboxes to exclude these scenarios being calculated in the sandwich rule deduction. This removes confusion and unnecessary deductions.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FJvr0FPc6yVfbd5mivAlW%252FFrame%2520148.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f659354-8e1a-48e0-a120-98ea67e197f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67f1a3e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#repeat-employee-detail-for-better-clarity)

Repeat Employee Detail for Better Clarity

We have added a ‘Repeat Data Format’ checkbox to enhance our monthly summary report further. Selecting this checkbox ensures that the Code, Name, Category, Department, and Designation will be replicated and displayed against all entries. So, you get a consistent and structured report, making it easier to analyze and interpret data.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FByUwCS9Zzm9Cud048j8q%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c75c518b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ff8K3hWpmWjdLh9UGA2ZP%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d666c048&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIdnNrgxISJRQkQRZpwIp%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9dd3391&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#flexible-leave-deductions-for-unassigned-shift)

Flexible Leave Deductions for Unassigned Shift

Ensure employees aren’t paid for unassigned shifts unless a leave deduction rule applies. HR/Admins can set accurate deduction rules, choose leave type (Paid/Unpaid), apply Half-Day or Full-Day deductions, and control weekend/holiday deductions. If leave is exhausted, the system deducts an alternative type. This ensures fair and accurate payroll management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F3ySMITJad51Ld9UW27lH%252FM4%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2143ba33-a0b7-417e-aed3-a9538fec1be3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da8ad084&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#quarterly-leave-credit-made-flexible-for-mid-joiners)

Quarterly Leave Credit Made Flexible for Mid-Joiners

The **Pro-rata & Mid-Joining Leave Credit** feature now supports **Quarterly Frequency**. This allows proportionate or fixed leave credits for mid-joiners within a quarter, ensuring flexible and fair leave allocation. The system applies either **pro-rata credit** or a **fixed mid-joining credit**, based on your settings.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FoJ5qVjdrOeLZ5GePOfpd%252FFrame%2520146%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1e4ccd1-7780-47d6-a474-048b00f5d9dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3776ede&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#customized-hr-letters-made-simple)

Customized HR Letters Made Simple

Now along with the custom predefined template the system allows you to create custom HR letters under the newly added option ‘Others’. Selecting the template type as ‘**Others’ from the dropdown** allows you to name and define your own template.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FiUjyT71lBoJBGvsxXowN%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c74dca9d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#easily-view-tax-details-in-a-pop-up)

Easily View Tax Details in a Pop-Up

We have changed the way an employee can view the description of the Tax Sections on their declaration page. As compared to earlier where the description was being shown in a tool tip hover, it is now shown in a pop-up enhancing the readability of the same.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDgsIQM9xl9KHCjQ6i46e%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2017c56&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FtdrLMEJY4X4V51YQmlsh%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db0f957&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#boost-action-in-confirmation-with-multi-level-reminder-cc)

Boost Action in Confirmation with Multi-Level Reminder CC

With the help of a simple drop down, you can add senior managers (Level 2, Level 3, HR, Admin) according to your company’s hierarchy to be CC’d in the 2nd and 3rd reminder emails for employee confirmation.

That means if the 1st level manager doesn’t act over the 1st reminder the selected seniors will also get notified in 2nd and 3rd reminder emails ensuring accountability and prompt action.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F9l4DW9xKMo97jTlTrFDZ%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86c18d97&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#approve-today-separate-on-the-last-working-day)

Approve Today, Separate on the Last Working Day

HR can now pre-approve resignation requests with a future Last Working Day (LWD) instead of waiting until the actual date. The system will automatically separate the employee on the approved LWD. For example, if the LWD is 21/03/2025, the employee will be separated on 22/03/2025 in the morning.

HR can also track Manager and Department Head approvals more efficiently with our new structured view. Additionally, they have the option to immediately separate an employee by updating the LWD to today.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F4wUZAikH6pr0pORm3OvY%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab62e940&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fq4CFn7D6tMq0ydhFDIUB%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5005b071&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FZBGGjZgtNZK86jNFIvGK%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0571c75&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#multi-company-fnf-approvals-made-easy)

Multi-Company FnF Approvals Made Easy

HRs can now assign cross-company department heads for Full & Final approvals, either individually or in bulk. Department heads will also see the company name for approvals received, keeping them well informed and improving FnF management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFTmP6MA42WwZJUx6JvEI%252FFrame%2520137.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd98de1a9-ce8b-437c-a698-ac3e3011cce2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e487baf8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#customize-career-page-branding)

Customize Career Page Branding

Now the Admin/HR can decide whether or not to show the company name on the career page along with the company profile. This enhancement will be useful for the customers who host the Pocket HRMS career page on their websites.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzUfkYSPnc5B3IqqMX0K2%252Fm11%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6fea1290-78c7-4506-90ea-4576e7364a8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=962663fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#instant-payslip-notifications)

Instant Payslip Notifications

Now, simply toggle to ensure that your employees will receive an email and ESS notification when their payslips are posted. Admin/HR can enable or disable these notifications during the Web Post. Providing ease, efficiency and convenience to everyone.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FfpW0xWoQXBFizilOMqdA%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fe26253&sv=2)

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FMJp1mfRs2a48KZVn2iWf%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcf8430a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#double-check-payroll-with-maker-checker)

Double-Check Payroll with Maker-Checker

We’ve added Maker-Checker functionality to smHRt Payroll! Now, you Can assign a Maker who is responsible for processing the payroll. In addition to that, there can be multiple checkers, who can review and approve it before finalization. This feature adds an extra layer of checks to eliminate possibilities for errors.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FVCMd8tiM9tUks08INsph%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486bcc6d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/product-updates/updates-2025/february-2025#lock-attendance-data-for-payroll-accuracy)

**Lock Attendance Data for Payroll Accuracy**

A new feature lets you disable Attendance Payroll Components from manual edits in Monthly Input screens. This ensures that only approved data will go to Payroll, preventing unauthorized changes.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FYTEy1wcUjlaCc8pDhSgn%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2dec41d&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#1e6d6b6e6e716c6a5e6e717d757b6a766c736d307d7173)

# In Out Raw Details | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report/in-out-raw-details#in-out-raw-details)

In Out Raw Details

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report/in-out-raw-details#how-to-get-in-out-raw-details-report-from-pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-application)

How to get In Out Raw Details Report from Pocket HRMS 2.0 Mobile Application?

**Path:** Login to mobile app of Pocket HRMS 2.0 > click on 3 horizontal lines (Hamburger menu) > Leave > My Reports > In Out Raw Details

**Step 1:** Log in to the Pocket HRMS 2.0 mobile app.

**Step 2:** Tap on the three horizontal lines (hamburger menu) located at the top left corner of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2F60nlfF17YanVdrFagBF8%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40c5e990&sv=2)

**Step 3:** From the side menu, select the ‘Leave’ module. Navigate to the ‘My Reports’ section within the leave menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FInfxhtbLIvKYcX3AvqNn%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef6acefc&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select ‘In Out Raw Details’ to view your punch information.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%2Fblobs%2FQjlNPU7klSfcfu1lkPyr%2FUnknown%2520image&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55a41c2c&sv=2)

It includes the following:

*   Date and
    
*   Time
    

Of every day punch In and punch out

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/pocket-hrms-2.0-mobile-app/leave/my-report/in-out-raw-details#filter-icon)

Filers the specific Report type of specific date of your need

Click on filter icon> Fill in the date range > search

# Role Allocation | Pocket HRMS

Pocket HRMS allows flexibility you to provide access to various modules and features under it for various roles according to the company policies. You follow steps below for various role allocation activities as needed.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/role-allocation#how-to-give-access-rights-to-various-modules-and-features-to-particular-role)

How to give access rights to various modules and features to particular role?

**Step 1**: Log into the cloud portal, go to the ‘ESS Settings’ menu and under the ‘Profile Info’ tab and click on the ‘Role Allocation’ subtab.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FcR01jGh2GLFCdFZON6Xl%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a44537e1&sv=2)

**Step 2**: From respective fields ‘Select Module’ for which you want to give access to the particular role.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fw3SDiAg7bB6g7iwZWDGj%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87a07455&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Then ‘Select Role’ for which you want to give access to selected module and click on the ‘Search’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2vrxB0Esv3gKM5RTTfCi%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e32b4030&sv=2)

**Step 4**: Once you have selected the module and role click on the ‘Search’ button. The options/features for the respective module will appear.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FBCf1yLNg1KMCNm04qJE9%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d38ebae0&sv=2)

**Step 5**: You can select options and the list of features will appear under it. Select the checkboxes for various features for which you want to give access, similarly if you want to remove access untick the respective checkboxes. Click on the ‘Save’ button and access to selected features will be allocated for the particular role.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzjzzG8rYnBUo9c9DNhVG%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b070c01&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/profile-info/role-allocation#example-1)

Example 1:

We select the module as ‘Leave’ and role as ‘Manager’ and click on the ‘Search’ button. We select the checkbox for the ‘Approval’ and select options such as leave, OT approval, On Duty/Work From Home’ and more for which approval rights to be given to the ‘Manager Role’ and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FY2c14AOkdTDlLfTiFtWQ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1eda14ad&sv=2)

Example 2:

We select the module as ‘Expense’ and the role as ‘Finance’ and click on the ‘Search’ button. Under the various fields such as approval, request, My trip and more we select the option for which you want to give right to the ‘Finance Role’ according to your company policies and click on the ‘Save’ button.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FvrVWjQuXkfkR5INqUF9j%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5f3a959&sv=2)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#4a393f3a3a25383e0a3a2529212f3e2238273964292527)

# Leave Credit | Pocket HRMS

Pocket HRMS offers a comprehensive leave module that allows you to take care of all your leave management needs and customize it for the needs of your company. Here is a simple guide that walks you through the various functions of the module and how you can utilize Pocket HRMS to streamline your leave management process.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/leave-credit#leave-credit)

Leave Credit

The leave credit feature can be used to credit a particular type of leaves to the employees and set various parameters for it as described below.

First you need to log into the Pocket HRMS cloud portal with admin credentials. Now, you can click on the ‘**Setting’** menu towards the bottom of the left-hand side bar.

That will take you to the screen below, select the ‘**Leave’** tab from the top and then ‘**Leave Credit**’ from the subtab as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzVmyjiYx7CvJmCIboWok%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f567c3a&sv=2)

This takes you to ‘**Leave Credit Monthly’** window, you can do various settings described in detail below.

*   Click on the ‘**Monthly**’ radio button to set criteria for monthly leave credits.
    
*   From the ‘**Category**’ drop-down menu, you should select the employee category for which leave credit criteria will apply. That way admin can ensure that the setting you do will be applicable to only for a selected employee category while existing settings for other employee categories stay unaffected.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FcenkohNGoUb6UcK3x2Ib%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dd67e26&sv=2)

*   From ‘**Leave**’ drop down menu select the type of leave for which you want to set the leave credit criteria for. Here, you can set different parameters for various types of leaves you have configured in the system. That way you can ensure differentiation in rules for particular type of leave.
    
*   For example, rules for crediting casual leave will differ from crediting sick leave.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F8vvSiWjsjXB0bGiW5POi%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22c447fd&sv=2)

*   From option ‘**a**’ drop-down select criteria based on which the leaves employees will get the leave credit such as their joining date, birth date, anniversaries and much more.
    

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FKTZO0sWcsQqMugrFjwB9%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e1e4be5&sv=2)

*   In option ‘**b**’, fill the sum of opening leaves and leave credits in the text box provided. This setting will ensure that the monthly leave credit and opening does not exceed this limit.
    

This feature allows you to limit maximum leave balance which is beneficial in many ways. It controls liability that company has for unused leaves, don’t allow employees to take unreasonable amount of leaves at the same time so you can avoid staffing shortage. It also encourages employees to take regular breaks which helps in building healthy work-life balance.

*   In option ‘**c**’, enter the number of leaves to be credited every month.
    

The option allows you to establish a standardized leave policy across the organization. This ensures consistency and transparency in leave entitlements for all employees.

*   In option ‘**d**’ select the rounding rule for leave credit, so the system will do the rounding accordingly. You can also select option ‘NIL’ if you don't want to use rounding.
    

Rounding rules ensure that leave credits are calculated consistently, and accurately for all employees. It also avoids discrepancies that might arise due to variations in leave accrual calculations. Employees gets clear understanding of their available leave balances. The consistent leave data generated by the system supports better reporting and analytics.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FAoisWS1hWOFGzQIjCpnl%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d0b85b7&sv=2)

*   In option ‘**e**’ you can enter the formula or change it by clicking the ‘Leave Credit Formula’ button set the formula and click on ‘Save changes’ button so the system will calculate monthly leave credit based on this formula.
    

The ability to set up a leave credit formula allows your company to customize leave accrual calculations to company’s specific needs and policies. This flexibility ensures that the system works in alignment with your organization's unique structure and requirements.

If your company has complex leave accrual rules based on factors like tenure, job role, or other variables, the formula feature can handle these calculations accurately reducing the time and effort required for manual calculations

Plus, if policies change over time, updating the formula is more efficient than modifying individual leave accrual records for each employee.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FFtEHLHUfMnzsQgALSzFJ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1a051c6&sv=2)

In option ‘**f**’ select the checkbox if you don’t want to credit leave for the employee's first month of joining. When the checkbox is checked the system will exempt the employees for their first month.

Often, new employees are placed on a probationary period during their initial months. Exempting leave credits for the first month acknowledges this period and prevents unnecessary accruals before an employee's status is confirmed. The checkbox automates this process, saving HR time and reducing errors also simplifying tracking and calculations.

*   In option ‘**g**’ you can select the text box to apply pro rata so the system can credit the leaves by pro rata.
    

Pro rata calculations ensure that leave credits are proportionate to an employee's actual service duration. Useful for employees joining or leaving the company in the middle of the year.

By applying pro rata calculations, the system accurately reflects the leave entitlement of employees based on the exact time they have been with the company. This prevents overestimating or underestimating leave balances.

*   In option ‘**h**’ check the box if you want to set different criteria for employees who are joining the company in the middle of month.
    

After checking the box, you will get an option **‘**Mid Joining Days’ to set a value to define mid joining as greater than equal to the set number of days. You can set the number of leave to be credited for mid joining employees in the field against ‘Leave Credit Days for Mid Joining’.

Enabling the option to set different criteria for employees who join the company in the middle of the month provides them with an appropriate number of leave days based on their actual working days in the month. This option allows you to customize leave benefits to your company's unique requirements. The automated calculation gives you correct calculations and avoids possible disputes and confusion over the leave credit.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2PRotp2Nrr8PeRuvCUV2%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b963e7fa&sv=2)

*   In option ‘**i**’, you can enter the formula for leave credit eligibility in the given field or set formula by clicking on the “Leave Credit Eligibility’ button. Based on this formula the system will decide if the employee is eligible to receive the leave credit.
    

With the ability to define a formula you can customize leave credit eligibility based on various factors. If company policies change, the formula can be adjusted accordingly providing you additional flexibility. It also ensures precise leave balance projections, enabling better workforce planning and resource management.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FDUg4WVMrlFejAd2XGqBz%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80f3530c&sv=2)

*   In option ‘j’ can be used to set what would be the cut off value.
    

Setting a cut-off value can provide your company with more control and flexibility over how leave credits are allocated to employees. So, the employees who meet or exceed the specified criteria will receive the allocated leave credits, while those who fall below the cut-off value may receive a different amount or no credits.

Allocating leave credits to employees who meet the criteria also reduces the overall leave-related financial burden.

*   Click on the ‘Save’ button so the system will store the criteria you chose and use it to credit leaves for your employees.
    

[PreviousConfigurationschevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/configuration-and-reports)
[NextLeave Debitchevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/cloud-configuration/leave/leave-debit)

# Leave | Pocket HRMS

Leaves are an integral part of employment. As a result, it is a necessity and is authorized by the company as a part of the employee’s employment contract. Hence, Pocket HRMS helps you in easy management of employee leaves.

**This section will cover an in-detail guide to the leave management process.**

*   Requesting Leave
    
*   Check Status
    
    *   ESS
        
    *   Mobile App
        
    *   App Notification
        
    
*   Cancel Leave Request
    
*   Report
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-apply-for-leaves-using-ess-portal)

**How to apply for leaves using ESS Portal?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal, select ‘Leave’ and then ‘Request’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2KImQZ-2YjCjbKby%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8e8a67d-3007-4312-871f-a1d667e89e70&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8340d448&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select the ‘Leave’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2N-ccv8GM0eikpS7%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db26de46e-bac4-48d8-a618-4a9a72072cd5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bf0ff20&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the type of leave from the drop-down menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2PIzzlTYNKaqOKX2%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9883acb-ec3a-4946-93bd-90d81e236922&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f461fa5a&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the start date and end date as well as the duration of the same.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2S1143wbXkIk8peZ%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De61fb2c7-a960-4d75-9552-d56687a67e37&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd5d35c&sv=2)

**Step 5:** State the reason for the leave and select whether you are going out of the station.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2UaA4rc8D46hz8F3%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37f45064-c541-4892-926f-6ca267c4fd77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53d2b12b&sv=2)

**Step 6:** Optionally, you can provide a vacation address and contact number.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2X3iNTH4o8Uqeohh%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3097c13-3f14-4be8-9814-072417a55dae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=962fe586&sv=2)

**Step 7:** Select the button ‘Add’ to apply.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr2ZZvwrBWiN_mV0hd%252FLeave-Apply-ESS-7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31aecccd-9ccf-44cf-a5f3-120afc07f38c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d636cbe5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-apply-for-leaves-using-the-ess-mobile-app)

**How to apply for leaves using the ESS Mobile App?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS mobile app, open the left side menu by tapping on the ‘Hamburger Menu Icon’ (3 Lines) and select the option ‘Leave’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3Vhjw-DWigGnEoUj%252FLeave-Apply-App-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1964025b-552c-4d7c-8c3a-9bea8aec4489&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8ea176a&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Tap on the option ‘Request’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3YfXtRkvksUwATAi%252FLeave-Apply-App-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2924dbbd-8f3a-48e0-9ab0-15dc395fa19d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70699e84&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Tap on the ‘Leave’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3a_AqY80ODwqUInu%252FLeave-Apply-App-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e0ec987-2df2-4c7f-9ea6-0a64965e6124&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8a88bae&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the start date and end date as well as the duration of the same.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3eF7oN4eGVaQXjxp%252FLeave-Apply-App-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5d97c19-e772-4f34-8d9a-cf155e1fead2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcddfa58&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Select the type of leave, and the reason for leave and mention whether you are going out of station.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3gdVGDVMsR_s8qcP%252FLeave-Apply-App-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D139a9a5f-bdb4-4940-a47a-b50c573785ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc4960c&sv=2)

**Step 6:** Optionally, you can provide a vacation address and contact number if you are going out of station.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3ig9K1EfR-Tnosbb%252FLeave-Apply-App-6.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f45f86c-e820-4eef-b27b-77a4ed48d172&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=581d26c2&sv=2)

**Step 7:** Tap on the ‘Save’ button to apply.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr-ULwOWwsbTyjaFlw%252F-Mkr3kqjwL42pdorHZB3%252FLeave-Apply-App-7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D014c971f-cbec-4b1b-99f2-bbf38708a6b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=718fc7a5&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-check-leaves-request-status-using-ess-portal)

**How to check leaves’ request status using ESS Portal?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal, select ‘Leave’ and then ‘My Report’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr8sSDDgvjECsLgZO8%252FLeave-Status-ESS-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4f57873-a7f6-4293-b26f-64e54232babd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e03069f4&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘Leave Details’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr8vHcW-66OGOKKj8r%252FLeave-Status-ESS-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bb042eb-8b1a-4405-bdcd-79fc28f0d751&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=730a856a&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Your previous leaves are displayed here.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr8xLOE9MH-haTRssJ%252FLeave-Status-ESS-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78ccb060-ea6a-4a06-8bbe-158f7c96afc2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d018e6dc&sv=2)

**Step 4:** If you wish so, you can select the relevant filters at the top and select the ‘Search’ button to find the status of a particular leave.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr94nnScWzD4zdVvnc%252FLeave-Status-ESS-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca3baf40-1525-47b8-824a-bdb45ecc00d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=994b7190&sv=2)

**Step 5:** You will also be able to find further details about a particular leave by selecting the corresponding button under the ‘Leave Type’ column.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr97Xt07557CsDamJ8%252FLeave-Status-ESS-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D463a592d-6f9e-44a4-b9cc-494bf9365396&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44ed51ab&sv=2)

**How to check leaves’ request status using ESS Mobile App?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS mobile app, open the left side menu by tapping on the ‘Hamburger Menu Icon’ (3 Lines) and select the option ‘Leave’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr9ewzWH_r9c5yRq_1%252FLeave-Status-App-1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65cd41f2-1b73-4cb3-a038-f1271207f4d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=917b9b61&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Tap on the option ‘My Report’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr9hG19-dPtQp21mqz%252FLeave-Status-App-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df80914a9-37ba-43d3-8243-c151c66fb882&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63a51e62&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Tap on the ‘Leave Details’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr9jtmMQi2n10seCaz%252FLeave-Status-App-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fe2854c-ec1e-4186-9386-cb9bf8d53bda&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d181ae0&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Your previous leaves in the current financial year are displayed here.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr9m7cUWvWQISSjICa%252FLeave-Status-App-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a9660f4-1f8d-4a2b-90dd-7d7b0f5882f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=68108998&sv=2)

**Step 5:** If you wish so, you can select the filter button at the bottom right and select the relevant filters and then tap on ‘Search’ button to find the status of a particular leave.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-Mkr9oRQunilyFgriPyP%252FLeave-Status-App-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29f384a3-f3a5-45ca-9062-5d5cadf8acd6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e827af1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-check-leaves-request-status-using-ess-mobile-app-notification)

**How to check leaves’ request status using ESS Mobile App Notification?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS mobile app, tap on the bell icon at the top right corner of the screen.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-MkrANqJ_aYegUOu4sK1%252FLeave-Status-Notfcn-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f6c9baa-39c6-44d6-8a8d-7a1fc89226fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e50e5c9&sv=2)

**Step 2:** You will be able to view whether your leave request has been approved or rejected based on the notifications titled ‘Leave Accepted’ or ‘Leave Rejected’

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-Mkr7Ne83wuKN48vWBqS%252F-MkrASveJ1abUpidxZNI%252FLeave-Status-Notfcn-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47c60e90-08f4-4086-8715-b4e6c69655b8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48b45587&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-cancel-leave-requests-from-the-ess-portal)

**How to cancel leave requests from the ESS portal?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal, select ‘Leave’ and then ‘Request’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrAVUt9eX3SL4d6sYg%252F-MkrBUBCoOF6oV1up_qI%252FLeave-Cancel-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfffab24c-0700-432b-a120-d61576d2d901&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=544fd8b6&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select the ‘Leave’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrAVUt9eX3SL4d6sYg%252F-MkrBWoRZjFov7_usnfR%252FLeave-Cancel-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1aa4ab1-a880-403d-ae66-d0468747341c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d502575d&sv=2)

**Step 3:** You will be able to view the previously applied leaves at the bottom of the page under the table titled ‘Previous Leaves’.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrAVUt9eX3SL4d6sYg%252F-MkrBZ8j3ARG20TQFYFb%252FLeave-Cancel-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60e0bf80-24be-457f-bcc9-74fd97349193&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcaba47f&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the ‘Cancel’ button under the ‘Action’ column corresponding to the leave that you wish to cancel and select ‘OK’ on the pop-up to confirm your selection.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrAVUt9eX3SL4d6sYg%252F-MkrBal5Fd52iV9egdNC%252FLeave-Cancel-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57bf896b-3b5e-4be1-82ad-c26b508a2dd4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64141492&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-generate-your-own-leave-report-from-the-ess-portal)

**How to generate your own leave report from the ESS portal?**

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal, select ‘Leave’ and then ‘My Report’ from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrBkRwEQAYCGkx__ak%252F-MkrCf_NKcn9EAC0s73s%252FLeave-MyReport-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30cc7204-a529-4a32-8970-2c286fef46c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7062edb&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select the ‘Leave Details’ tab at the top.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrBkRwEQAYCGkx__ak%252F-MkrChricL-XwLnjfGqj%252FLeave-MyReport-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db425de97-bbe7-44dc-9a61-875438df783d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b95ef1a&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Your previous leaves are displayed here.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrBkRwEQAYCGkx__ak%252F-MkrCk-IFPmsSUafEf9n%252FLeave-MyReport-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f1b4010-91ac-42b1-b072-f976131750d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e69e3b2&sv=2)

**Step 4:** If you wish so, you can select the relevant filters at the top and select the ‘Search’ button to find the status of a particular leave.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrBkRwEQAYCGkx__ak%252F-MkrCmSKrJ2FOyuEFyHh%252FLeave-MyReport-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd43742d0-06c0-4f95-9b97-22855801abf7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1db3b744&sv=2)

**Step 5:** You will also be able to find further details about a particular leave by selecting the corresponding button under the ‘Leave Type’ column.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252F-MkrBkRwEQAYCGkx__ak%252F-MkrCpfKy8vEdpCHOlCO%252FLeave-MyReport-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c7f5f21-150b-4c0a-9a06-6fa27334b70a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8c0ecd6&sv=2)

**Note**: If you are unable to follow above steps, kindly contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#aad9dfdadac5d8deeadac5c9c1cfdec2d8c7d984c9c5c7)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/leave#how-to-check-my-geo-tracking-details-from-the-ess-portal)

How to check my geo-tracking details from the ESS portal?

**Step 1:** Log into the ESS portal, go to the ‘Leave’ menu and click on the ‘Geo-tracking’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FzpS9XYBhNTJ33VlQzUtH%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c4ecd92&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Click on the ‘Geo Track Employee’ tab, ‘Choose Employee’ and the date from the respective fields.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Feb8Pnj0rTl8eI5nbgMLN%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2276386e&sv=2)

The geo-tracking details will appear for the selected date and you can see the ‘location pins’ on the map.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Ft47sDciorryoc0ccih8C%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fd42979&sv=2)

For any queries, connect with us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2a595f5a5a45585e6a5a4549414f5e4258475904494547)

[PreviousLeave Attendance & On Dutychevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty)
[NextAttendancechevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/employee/leave-attendance-and-on-duty/attendance-regularization)

# Profile | Pocket HRMS

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/profile#how-to-check-permission-entries-as-an-hr-or-admin)

How to check permission entries as an HR or admin?

**Step 1**: Log into the ESS portal with manager rights, go to the ‘Leave’ menu and click on the ‘Approval’ submenu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252Fc3h8dqE1YWIiTAEEjhfh%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=859e970c&sv=2)

**Step 2**: Go to the ‘HR Approval’ tab, select ‘Module’ as ‘Selfservice Permission’, select Date Range and click on the ‘Search’ button. The permission entries will appear.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FgTkpN13WaXMqy7QwaHXA%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=efc2aaed&sv=2)

**Step 3**: Select radio button from the ‘Approve’ or ‘Reject’ column for the respective entry and click on the ‘Save’ button.

The permission request will be accepted or rejected accordingly.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252F2NjqWzT2pOqWlmkpExnJ%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3dde6b8&sv=2)

**Path**: ESS Portal with HR log in>Profile>Approval>HR Approval>Module-Selfservice Permission >Select Date Range>Search>Approve/Reject>Save

**Link**: [https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Profile/EmployeeApprovals?Menu=managerapprovearrow-up-right](https://ess.pockethrms.com/Employee/Profile/EmployeeApprovals?Menu=managerapprove)

For any queries, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#7605030606190402360619151d13021e041b055815191b)

[PreviousAdminchevron-left](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin)
[NextLeavechevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/ess-portal/admin/leave)

# Adding Tags | Pocket HRMS

**How do you create tags for the Help Desk?**

**Step 1:** Select 'ESS Settings' from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC9QuiAxanncHJDWPcqBM%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D729af1ab-8df8-4018-80e6-ad902fb84598&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30aaa844&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘HelpDesk’ tab inside the ESS Settings page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC7KK86IgQsPmV2BjEWRY%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2b97fd0-36d9-4531-8140-6eeb67a91fa7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4084ccd7&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select 'HelpDesk Tag' tab from the tabs section to the left of the HelpDesk page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FF078orR7uvIf1kb3T58U%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f3c9319-b3f4-41aa-a482-e659077697a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ad7de2f&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select ‘+’ icon as shown below.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FSRCK1UDgmVa1rT7s5nRT%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2880161b-fee3-4ab7-b3c6-6c3c5606b96c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5a52071&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Enter the name of the tag and select the 'Save' button to create a new HelpDesk Tag.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FR0f9n7VhcE4MiUSKQEH0%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3d5ad3c-1b49-4e07-9ac9-51db90b73ba1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=179f7320&sv=2)

**How to edit tags for the Help Desk:**

**Step 1:** Select 'ESS Settings' from the left side menu.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC9QuiAxanncHJDWPcqBM%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D729af1ab-8df8-4018-80e6-ad902fb84598&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30aaa844&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Select ‘HelpDesk’ tab inside the ESS Settings page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FC7KK86IgQsPmV2BjEWRY%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2b97fd0-36d9-4531-8140-6eeb67a91fa7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4084ccd7&sv=2)

**Step 3:** Select the 'HelpDesk Tag' tab from the tabs section to the left of the HelpDesk page.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FF078orR7uvIf1kb3T58U%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f3c9319-b3f4-41aa-a482-e659077697a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ad7de2f&sv=2)

**Step 4:** Select the edit icon corresponding to the tag that needs to be edited.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIZuZvNVZCE3ie78EOpCU%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4e226fb-174e-402f-a349-9855efa96aba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59353369&sv=2)

**Step 5:** Enter the name of the tag and select the 'Save' button to edit the name of the selected HelpDesk Tag.

![](https://docs.pockethrms.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4282324958-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MXep_PEmh8mDPVWj49x%252Fuploads%252FIIZuTRRt5Cz7lPgpPKVg%252FHelpDesk%2520Tags%25207.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd787a78a-2630-4240-b145-7462c5535954&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=807c2988&sv=2)

_**Note: If you are unable to add or edit tags, kindly contact us at**_ [_**\[email protected\]**_envelope](https://docs.pockethrms.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3c4f494c4c534e487c4c535f575948544e514f125f5351)

[NextReminder Settingschevron-right](https://docs.pockethrms.com/hr-and-admin-portal/ess-configurations/helpdesk/reminder-settings)
